# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Efficient Semi-Automated Material Microstructure Analysis Using Deep Learning: A Case Study in Additive Manufacturing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13831)
*Sanjeev S. Navaratna,Nikhil Thawari,Gunashekhar Mari,Amritha V P,Murugaiyan Amirthalingam,Rohit Batra*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于主动学习（active learning）的半自动图像分割流程，针对增材制造（additive manufacturing）数据集，通过结合U-Net卷积神经网络、交互式用户标注界面和代表性核心集图像选择策略，显著提升了分割性能并减少了人工标注工作量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料图像分割对于缺陷识别和结构-性能关联至关重要，但由于材料处理与测试条件差异导致的显著异质性，传统图像处理技术难以捕捉复杂特征，深度学习也因高质量标注数据稀缺而难以泛化，现有方法依赖费时且难以扩展的人工专家标注。

Method: 提出半自动主动学习分割流程，集成U-Net卷积神经网络、交互式用户标注校正界面和代表性核心集图像选择策略。主动学习工作流通过将用户校正的分割结果纳入训练池来迭代更新模型，同时评估了三种子集选择策略：手动选择、不确定性驱动采样和提出的基于嵌入的最大最小拉丁超立方采样（SMILE）方法。

Result: SMILE策略在六轮优化中始终优于其他方法，将宏观F1分数从0.74提升至0.93，同时减少约65%的人工标注时间。分割后的缺陷区域通过耦合分类模型进一步分析，基于微观结构特征对缺陷分类并将其映射到相应的增材制造工艺参数。

Conclusion: 所提框架在保持可扩展性和鲁棒性的同时显著减少了标注工作量，广泛适用于多种材料系统的图像分析。该方法通过主动学习和智能样本选择策略，有效解决了材料图像分割中的异质性和标注数据稀缺问题。

Abstract: Image segmentation is fundamental to microstructural analysis for defect identification and structure-property correlation, yet remains challenging due to pronounced heterogeneity in materials images arising from varied processing and testing conditions. Conventional image processing techniques often fail to capture such complex features rendering them ineffective for large-scale analysis. Even deep learning approaches struggle to generalize across heterogeneous datasets due to scarcity of high-quality labeled data. Consequently, segmentation workflows often rely on manual expert-driven annotations which are labor intensive and difficult to scale. Using an additive manufacturing (AM) dataset as a case study, we present a semi-automated active learning based segmentation pipeline that integrates a U-Net based convolutional neural network with an interactive user annotation and correction interface and a representative core-set image selection strategy. The active learning workflow iteratively updates the model by incorporating user corrected segmentations into the training pool while the core-set strategy identifies representative images for annotation. Three subset selection strategies, manual selection, uncertainty driven sampling and proposed maximin Latin hypercube sampling from embeddings (SMILE) method were evaluated over six refinement rounds. The SMILE strategy consistently outperformed other approaches, improving the macro F1 score from 0.74 to 0.93 while reducing manual annotation time by about 65 percent. The segmented defect regions were further analyzed using a coupled classification model to categorize defects based on microstructural characteristics and map them to corresponding AM process parameters. The proposed framework reduces labeling effort while maintaining scalability and robustness and is broadly applicable to image based analysis across diverse materials systems.

</details>


### [2] [From Artefact to Insight: Efficient Low-Rank Adaptation of BrushNet for Scanning Probe Microscopy Image Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14850)
*Ziwei Wei,Yao Shen,Wanheng Lu,Ghim Wei Ho,Kaiyang Zeng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于扩散模型（diffusion model）的轻量级修复框架，专门用于扫描探针显微镜（SPM）图像的伪影去除。通过微调少于0.2%的BrushNet权重，该框架在单GPU上实现了与完整重训练相当的精度，显著提升了图像质量指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扫描探针显微镜（Scanning Probe Microscopy, SPM）虽能提供纳米级分辨率，但常受线扫描丢失、增益诱导噪声、针尖卷积和相位跳变等结构化伪影影响。现有方法多将SPM伪影去除视为孤立的去噪或插值任务，而基于生成式修复（generative inpainting）的视角尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 本文引入了一个专为科学灰度图像设计的基于扩散的修复框架。通过使用秩约束低秩适应（rank constrained low rank adaptation, LoRA）微调少于0.2%的BrushNet权重，仅利用从739个实验扫描中提取的7390个伪影-干净图像对来适应预训练的扩散模型。

Result: 在即将公开的SPM InpBench基准测试中，LoRA增强模型将峰值信噪比（Peak Signal to Noise Ratio, PSNR）提升了6.61 dB，并将学习感知图像块相似度（Learned Perceptual Image Patch Similarity, LPIPS）相对于零样本推理降低了一半。该模型匹配或略微超越了完整重训练的精度，且可在单GPU而非四张高显存显卡上训练。

Conclusion: 该方法能泛化到包括高度、振幅和相位在内的多种SPM图像通道，忠实地恢复细微结构细节，并抑制了从自然图像先验继承的幻觉伪影。这一轻量级框架实现了对不可替代SPM图像的高效、可扩展恢复，为扩散模型在纳米尺度成像分析中的更广泛应用铺平了道路。

Abstract: Scanning Probe Microscopy or SPM offers nanoscale resolution but is frequently marred by structured artefacts such as line scan dropout, gain induced noise, tip convolution, and phase hops. While most available methods treat SPM artefact removal as isolated denoising or interpolation tasks, the generative inpainting perspective remains largely unexplored. In this work, we introduce a diffusion based inpainting framework tailored to scientific grayscale imagery. By fine tuning less than 0.2 percent of BrushNet weights with rank constrained low rank adaptation (LoRA), we adapt a pretrained diffusion model using only 7390 artefact, clean pairs distilled from 739 experimental scans. On our forthcoming public SPM InpBench benchmark, the LoRA enhanced model lifts the Peak Signal to Noise Ratio or PSNR by 6.61 dB and halves the Learned Perceptual Image Patch Similarity or LPIPS relative to zero-shot inference, while matching or slightly surpassing the accuracy of full retraining, trainable on a single GPU instead of four high-memory cards. The approach generalizes across various SPM image channels including height, amplitude and phase, faithfully restores subtle structural details, and suppresses hallucination artefacts inherited from natural image priors. This lightweight framework enables efficient, scalable recovery of irreplaceable SPM images and paves the way for a broader diffusion model adoption in nanoscopic imaging analysis.

</details>

# cond-mat.other [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Terahertz cavity hybridization of collective proteins vibrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14476)
*Elsa Perez-Martin,Laurent Bonnet,Songlin Fang,Jelle Bannink,Elwin Vrouwe,Cedric Bray,Frederic Teppe,Sandra Ruffenach,Elodie Strupiechonski,Zhedong Zhang,Jeremie Torres*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究展示了在室温下，光泵浦R-藻红蛋白（R-phycoerythrin）支持相干亚太赫兹振动模式，这些模式与微流控腔中的太赫兹腔光子发生杂化，实现了强集体耦合，为腔工程振动光谱和无标记生物传感开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合光-物质态（hybrid light-matter states）已改变光子学领域，但在生物系统中利用驱动集体振动实现此类态仍具挑战。本研究旨在探索生物分子系统中集体振动与腔光子杂化的可能性。

Method: 采用室温下光泵浦的R-藻红蛋白（R-phycoerythrin）蛋白质，在微流控腔平台（microfluidic cavity platform）中研究其亚太赫兹振动模式与受限太赫兹腔光子的杂化。通过光谱分析和微观非平衡分析（microscopic nonequilibrium analysis）评估耦合特性。

Result: 观测到光谱双峰结构、功率和浓度依赖的谱重分布以及线宽变窄，表明腔修饰耗散（cavity-modified dissipation）。耦合强度呈现集体平方根N标度（collective square-root of N-scaling），合作性和分裂-线宽比超过1，符合强集体耦合（strong collective coupling）特征。弗罗利希极化子态（Frohlich polariton state）的弛豫时间尺度为1-10微秒。

Conclusion: 太赫兹腔可作为稳定和控制集体分子振动动力学的平台，为腔工程振动光谱（cavity-engineered vibrational spectroscopy）、无标记生物传感（label-free biosensing）以及复杂生物分子系统中能量传输的光子控制开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Hybrid light-matter states have transformed photonics, yet their realization with driven collective vibrations in biological systems remains an open challenge. Here we show that optically pumped R-phycoerythrin proteins at room temperature support coherent sub-terahertz vibrational modes consistent with Frohlich condensation, and that these modes hybridize with confined terahertz cavity photons in a microfluidic cavity platform. The resulting spectra exhibit a resolved doublet, power- and concentration-dependent redistribution of spectral weight, and linewidth narrowing indicative of cavity-modified dissipation. Quantitative analysis reveals collective square-root of N-scaling of the coupling strength, with cooperativity and splitting-to-linewidth ratios exceeding unity, consistent with the onset of strong collective coupling driven by the vibrational molecular mode. A microscopic nonequilibrium analysis further indicates that the relaxation timescale toward the Frohlich polariton state is on the order of 1-10 microseconds. These findings identify terahertz cavities as a platform for stabilizing and controlling collective molecular vibration dynamics and open opportunities for cavity-engineered vibrational spectroscopy, label-free biosensing and photonic control of energy transport in complex biomolecular systems.

</details>


### [4] [Demonstration of AI-Assisted Scientific Workflow on Canonical Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14888)
*Kin Hung Fung*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文展示了一个完全可复现的AI辅助科研工作流程，通过经典基准问题验证了AI在推导、实现、验证、可视化和论文准备等方面的辅助能力，为可信AI在技术研究中的应用提供了具体模板。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为广泛的物理、数学和计算机科学读者展示一个完全可复现的AI辅助科研工作流程。其动机不是提出新的科学发现，而是通过经典基准问题验证AI作为科研助手的实用性，为可信AI在技术研究中的应用提供具体模板。

Method: 方法包括四个核心组件：分析组件从一维量子谐振子出发，推导其无量纲形式，并通过有限差分特征对验证精确的Hermite函数基准；数值偏微分方程组件求解具有已知模态解的热方程和通过制造解验证的Poisson问题，并进行显式收敛性研究；逆建模组件通过非线性最小二乘法拟合合成阻尼振荡数据，并通过自助重采样量化参数不确定性；计算科学组件比较稠密和稀疏特征值求解器，对比直接和迭代稀疏线性求解器，并仔细解释机器相关的时间数据。

Result: 结果表明，当代AI已经能够作为科研副驾驶（scientific copilot）在推导、实现、验证、可视化和论文准备等方面提供有用帮助，前提是每个阶段都受到基准理论、显式验证和透明工件的约束。该演示的相关性不在于底层科学的新颖性，而在于为技术研究实践中可信AI使用提供了具体模板。

Conclusion: 论文证明，在受到基准理论、显式验证和透明工件约束的条件下，当代AI能够作为有效的科研副驾驶。该工作为可信AI在技术研究实践中的应用提供了一个具体、可复现的模板，强调了验证和透明度在AI辅助科研中的重要性。

Abstract: We present a fully reproducible demonstration of an AI-assisted scientific workflow designed for a broad physics, mathematics, and computer-science readership. The initial project artifact stack was generated from one single user prompt and then reviewed and curated for submission by the human author. Rather than claiming a new scientific discovery, the manuscript uses canonical benchmark problems with exact, manufactured, or independently checkable answers. The analytical component starts from the one-dimensional quantum harmonic oscillator, derives its dimensionless form, and validates finite-difference eigenpairs against exact Hermite-function benchmarks. The numerical partial-differential-equation component solves a heat equation with a known modal solution and a Poisson problem verified by a manufactured solution, with explicit convergence studies. The inverse-modeling component fits synthetic damped-oscillation data by nonlinear least squares and quantifies parametric uncertainty by bootstrap resampling. The computational-science component compares dense and sparse eigensolvers and contrasts direct and iterative sparse linear solvers, with careful interpretation of machine-dependent timing data. Taken together, the results show that contemporary AI can already serve as a useful scientific copilot for derivation, implementation, validation, visualization, and manuscript preparation, provided that each stage is constrained by benchmark theory, explicit verification, and transparent artifacts. The demonstration is therefore relevant not because the underlying science is novel, but because it offers a concrete template for trustworthy AI use in technical research practice.

</details>


### [5] [Measuring impurity-induced shifts in Coulomb crystallization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14980)
*Mingyao Xu,Aaron A. Smith,Leonid Prokhorov,Vera Guarrera,Giovanni Barontini*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究通过激光冷却的Ca⁺晶体掺杂可控数量的Xe¹²⁺高电荷离子，测量了杂质对强相互作用离子系统中库仑结晶（Coulomb crystallization）阈值的影响，发现低浓度时阈值不变，高浓度时发生明显交叉转变后近似线性增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在实验测量杂质如何影响强相互作用离子系统中的库仑结晶（Coulomb crystallization）阈值，这对于理解多组分库仑物质（multicomponent Coulomb matter）中的杂质效应至关重要，特别是在白矮星（white dwarfs）和中子星（neutron stars）的结晶模型中。

Method: 采用激光冷却（laser cooled）的Ca⁺晶体掺杂可控数量的Xe¹²⁺高电荷离子（highly charged ions），通过实验室测量研究杂质浓度对结晶阈值的影响，并进行补充测量分析其微观机制。

Result: 发现低杂质浓度时结晶阈值保持不变，但当杂质含量足够大时出现明显交叉转变（crossover），之后阈值近似线性增长；补充测量表明这种全局效应源于杂质周围的晶体局部钉扎（local pinning）。

Conclusion: 测量结果提供了将杂质效应纳入多组分库仑物质模型的实验途径，对白矮星和中子星的标准结晶模型具有重要影响，为强耦合等离子体（strongly coupled plasmas）和恒星结晶研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We report a laboratory measurement of how impurities shift Coulomb crystallization in a strongly interacting ionic system. This is achieved by using laser cooled Ca$^+$ crystals doped with a controlled number of Xe$^{12+}$ highly charged ions. We find that the crystallization threshold is unchanged at low impurity concentration, but shows a clear crossover once the impurity content becomes sufficiently large, after which the shift grows approximately linearly. Complementary measurements reveal that this global effect originates from a local pinning of the crystal around the impurities. We further show how the measured shift could impact standard models of crystallization in white dwarfs and neutron stars. Our results provide an experimental route to incorporating impurity effects into models of multicomponent Coulomb matter, relevant to stellar crystallization and strongly coupled plasmas.

</details>


<div id='quant-ph'></div>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Higher order Magnus expansions for two-level quantum dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13821)
*Chen Wei,Frank Großmann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了单轴驱动下一般含时二能级系统的马格努斯展开（Magnus expansion），通过su(2)李代数将其分解为无对易子形式，并应用于Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana模型和半经典Rabi模型，证明三阶近似可获得与精确解几乎完美一致的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究单轴驱动下一般含时二能级系统的马格努斯展开，旨在获得无对易子形式的分解表达式，并验证其在具体物理模型中的适用性和收敛性。

Method: 利用su(2)李代数将马格努斯展开分解为无对易子形式，通过适当的绘景变换（picture transformations）并强制底层模型的对称性来保证展开的收敛性，分别应用于Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana模型和半经典Rabi模型。

Result: 对于研究的两个模型，三阶近似产生与精确解析结果几乎完美一致的结果；在半经典Rabi模型中，绝热绘景下的二阶马格努斯近似在整个参数范围内都能产生几乎精确的结果。

Conclusion: 马格努斯展开在单轴驱动二能级系统中具有良好适用性，通过适当的数学处理和对称性约束可保证收敛性，三阶近似已能获得高精度结果，为相关量子系统研究提供了有效工具。

Abstract: We investigate the Magnus expansion for a generic time-dependent two-level system under single-axis driving. By virtue of the \(\mathfrak{su}(2)\) Lie algebra, the expansion is decomposed into a commutator-free form. To illustrate the usefulness of the gained expression, we then revisit the Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana model, with a focus on non-adiabatic transitions as well as the Stokes phase. In addition, the semiclassical Rabi model is systematically treated by determining the Floquet quasienergy up to different orders. We demonstrate how to employ suitable picture transformations as well as on how to enforce the symmetry of the underlying model in order to guarantee convergence of the expansion as well as to achieve satisfactory agreement with the exact results. For both models that we studied it turns out that a third order approximation yields results that are in next to perfect agreement with exact analytical ones. Surprisingly, in the case of the semiclassical Rabi model, even the second order Magnus approximation in the adiabatic picture produces almost exact results over the whole parameter range.

</details>


### [7] [Revisited Quantification of the Resource Theory of Imaginarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13980)
*Yue Han,Naihong Hu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了三种虚性度量在典型量子通道下的衰减行为，从单量子比特系统扩展到两量子比特系统，并推广了最大虚态、虚功率和去虚功率的概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究虚性资源理论（resource theory of imaginarity）中不同虚性度量在量子通道作用下的衰减特性，从单量子比特系统扩展到高维系统，以更全面理解虚性在量子信息处理中的行为。

Method: 方法包括：分析三种虚性度量（$l_1$-norm-based imaginarity measure、imaginarity robustness、imaginarity relative entropy）在三种典型量子通道（dephasing、generalized amplitude damping、phase-amplitude damping）下的衰减行为；将分析扩展到两量子比特系统，研究关键两量子比特态在两量子比特通道下的虚性衰减趋势；推广最大虚态概念到可分两量子比特态；将虚功率和去虚功率定义从单量子比特通道扩展到作用于可分两量子比特态的两量子比特通道。

Result: 研究结果包括：获得了任意单量子比特纯初始态在三种典型量子通道下三种虚性度量的衰减行为；分析了两量子比特系统中关键态在两量子比特通道下的虚性衰减趋势；成功将最大虚态概念推广到可分两量子比特态；将虚功率和去虚功率定义扩展到两量子比特通道；计算了多种常见两量子比特通道的虚功率和去虚功率。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了虚性度量在量子通道下的衰减特性，成功将虚性资源理论的概念从单量子比特系统扩展到两量子比特系统，为理解虚性在高维量子系统中的行为提供了理论基础，并计算了常见两量子比特通道的虚功率特性。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the decay behaviors of three imaginarity-related metrics, specifically the $l_1$-norm-based imaginarity measure, imaginarity robustness, and imaginarity relative entropy, for arbitrary single-qubit pure initial states under three typical quantum channels: dephasing, generalized amplitude damping, and phase-amplitude damping. Furthermore, we extend our analysis to higher-dimensional systems by examining the decay trends of the aforementioned imaginarity metrics for several key two-qubit states under two-qubit channels. We also generalize the concept of the maximal imaginary state (originally defined for single qubits in the resource theory of imaginarity) to separable two-qubit states. In addition, we extend the definitions of imaginary power and de-imaginary power for single-qubit channels to two-qubit channels acting on separable two-qubit states. Finally, we compute the imaginary and de-imaginary powers for several common two-qubit channels.

Method: 论文扩展了张量分解方法在含时薛定谔方程动力学模拟中的应用，重点关注支持低秩表示的张量链（tensor-train）和Tucker张量分解。概述了用于捕捉量子动力学的TDVP、TDVP-2和BUG时间积分算法。

Abstract: Classical simulations of quantum computing devices generally become intractable as the number of qubits increases. This is due to the exponential growth of the quantum state vector and the associated increase in computational effort. However, when entanglement within the system is limited, rank-adaptive tensor decomposition techniques can be employed to mitigate the exponential scaling. This paper broadens the application of tensor decomposition methods to dynamical simulations of Schrödinger's equation where the Hamiltonian is time-dependent, e.g., to study quantum computing devices subject to time-dependent control pulses. We focus on the tensor-train and Tucker-tensor decompositions that both support low-rank representations, and present an overview of the TDVP, TDVP-2, and BUG, time-integration algorithms for capturing quantum dynamics. ### [9] [Quantum Dynamical Entropy and non-Markovianity: a collisional model perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14015)
*Giovanni Nichele,Fabio Benatti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了开放量子系统中非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）现象的物理机制，通过Alicki-Lindblad-Fannes（ALF）熵分析系统-环境联合动力学，在碰撞模型（collisional model）中建立了ALF熵与环境统计特性参数的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解开放量子动力学中非马尔可夫现象背后的物理机制需要研究系统-环境联合动力学的统计特性。仅从开放系统的约化动力学层面无法实现这一目标，因为约化动力学是通过消除环境自由度获得的。

Method: 通过考虑仅涉及开放系统可观测量（observables）的多时间关联函数（multi-time correlation functions）来研究系统-环境相互作用。这些关联函数构成了量子随机过程理论和Alicki-Lindblad-Fannes（ALF）熵的基础。在碰撞模型中，通过将有限能级系统耦合到无限经典自旋链（infinite classical spin chain）来获得耗散动力学。

Result: 在碰撞模型中，ALF熵可以被显式计算。结果表明，ALF熵依赖于表征环境统计特性的参数，并且可以与开放量子系统中记忆效应（memory effects）的激活和超激活（activation and super-activation）相关联。

Conclusion: ALF熵为量子系统提供了类似于Kolmogorov-Sinai熵对经典系统的动力学熵产生度量。通过多时间关联函数和ALF熵分析，可以揭示开放量子系统中非马尔可夫现象的物理机制，特别是记忆效应与环境统计特性之间的关系。

Abstract: Accessing the physical mechanisms behind non-Markovian phenomena in open quantum dynamics requires the study of the statistical properties of the joint system-environment dynamics. This is impossible at the level of the reduced dynamics of the open system alone as the latter is obtained by suitably eliminating the environment. The task is instead made possible by considering multi-time correlation functions involving observables of the open system, only: the open system-environment interactions turn them into global ones thus building up correlations between the two systems. Multi-time correlations form the basis of both the theory of quantum stochastic processes and of the Alicki-Lindblad-Fannes dynamical entropy (ALF entropy for short). This latter quantity provides for quantum systems a measure of the dynamical entropy production as the Kolmogorov-Sinai entropy does for classical systems. In the case of a collisional model whereby the dissipative dynamics of a finite-level system is obtained by its coupling to an infinite classical spin chain, the ALF entropy can be explicitly computed. It turns out to depend on the parameters characterizing the statistical properties of the environment and can be related to the activation and super-activation of memory effects in the open quantum system.

*Giovanni Nichele,Fabio Benatti*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 获得了开放系统ALF熵（open-system ALF entropy）的精确表达式，该表达式明确依赖于环境相关性（environment correlations）。极端情况表明，从环境到系统的信息流对应于熵产生消失，类似于可逆有限量子系统。

Abstract: The Alicki-Lindblad-Fannes dynamical (ALF) entropy measures the rate at which new information is gathered about a quantum system by inspecting its long-time evolution. We propose an extension of the ALF entropy to open quantum dynamics as a measure of back-flow of information from the environment. Such a proposal is stronger than the existing ones based only on the open system reduced dynamics. In the case of a qubit collisionally coupled to a classical spin chain, we obtain an exact expression for the $\textit{open-system ALF entropy}$ explicitly depending on the environment correlations. An extreme case shows how the information flow from environment to system corresponds to vanishing entropy production as for reversible finite quantum systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 推导的涨落和耗散核满足涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relations），其谱结构揭示了与动力学卡西米尔效应（dynamical Casimir effect）粒子产生机制的直接联系。通过半经典运动方程和量子场论in-out形式计算辐射能量，验证了镜面机械能耗散与场中粒子产生能量之间的平衡。

Conclusion: 成功建立了光机系统的微扰闭时路径理论框架，揭示了运动镜面与量子场相互作用的物理本质。涨落-耗散关系的满足和能量平衡的验证表明该理论自洽地描述了辐射压力反作用效应与动力学卡西米尔效应粒子产生之间的内在联系。

Abstract: We present a perturbative closed-time-path (in-in) formulation of an optomechanical system in which a quantum field interacts with a moving mirror via radiation pressure. We derive the effective action governing the dynamics of the moving mirror, incorporating the full back-reaction of the cavity field. These effects are encoded in fluctuation and dissipation kernels, that we show satisfy fluctuation-dissipation relations, and whose spectral structure reveals a direct connection with the underlying physical mechanism responsible for the back-reaction, that is particle creation by the dynamical Casimir effect. By deriving the semiclassical equations of motion for the moving mirror, and computing the energy radiated into the field within the in-out formalism of quantum field theory, we verify the energy balance between the mechanical energy dissipated by the optical back-reaction forces acting on the mirror and the energy carried by the particles created in the field.

### [12] [Finite path integrals on stochastic branched structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14136)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机源于物理学中作用量（action）与统计力学中熵（entropy）都具有变分性质的相似性，探索将经典作用量与统计熵相统一的可能途径，为量子与经典描述提供共同的理论框架。

Method: 方法基于分支流形（branched manifold）上有限路径集合构建时空轨迹统计模型，为每个分支流形配置定义香农熵（Shannon entropy），并提出经典作用量与此熵成正比的假设，由此推导出维克旋转（Wick-rotated）版本的路径积分。

Result: 推导出的维克旋转（Wick-rotated）路径积分保持有限性，在微观层面展现量子干涉（quantum interference）效应，在宏观尺度呈现经典确定性（classical determinism）。该模型通过非均匀幅度权重分配路径，并将波函数坍缩（wave function collapse）解释为熵最大化（entropy maximization）的结果。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a statistical model of spacetime trajectories based on a finite collection of paths organized into a branched manifold. For each configuration of the branched manifold, we define a Shannon entropy. Given the variational nature of both the action in physics and the entropy in statistical mechanics, we explore the hypothesis that the classical action is proportional to this entropy. Under this assumption, we derive a Wick-rotated version of the path integral that remains finite and exhibits both quantum interference at the microscopic level and classical determinism at the macroscopic scale. In effect, this version of the path integral differs from the standard one because it assigns weights of non-uniform magnitude to different paths. The model suggests that wave function collapse can be interpreted as a consequence of entropy maximization. Although still idealized, this framework provides a possible route toward unifying quantum and classical descriptions within a common finite-entropy structure.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究结果表明：1）在具有公平划分的图随机游走中，Szegedy量子化与聚合操作的条件得到满足；2）通过柏拉图立体（Platonic solids）、N维超立方体（N-dimensional hypercube）上的离散时间经典/量子游走、自由群（free groups）的Cayley图等多个案例验证了理论结果。

Abstract: Given random walk on a graph, the corresponding discrete-time quantum walk can be constructed using the method proposed by Szegedy. On the other hand, given a partition of the set of states of a Markov chain, one can study the corresponding aggregated process. We extend the aggregation technique to the level of quantum Markov chains. We provide conditions under which application of these two operations - Szegedy's quantization and aggregation - give the same result. In particular, we show that the conditions are satisfied in the case of the random walk on graphs equipped with equitable partitions. We present several examples, which include the classical/quantum walks on Platonic solids. We discuss also relation of discrete-time classical/quantum walks on $N$-dimensional hypercube and the Ehrenfests urn model with $N$ particles. We apply our technique for of discrete-time walks on Cayley graphs of free groups. We also compare our results with those obtained using Cantero-Moral-Velazquez uniformization of unitary matrices.

### [14] [Mixed-State Entanglement in a Minimal Model of Quantum Chaos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14292)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合副本技巧（replica trick）与模型的时空对偶性（space-time duality），确定了部分转置约化密度矩阵（partially transposed reduced density matrix）的精确谱。通过广泛的数值模拟验证了结果对一般初始态的普适性。

Result: 平坦谱结构导致早期时间纠缠负性（entanglement negativity）、奇熵（odd entropy）和Rényi互信息（Rényi mutual information）之间的精确关系。数值结果显示，对于等三分区，所有纠缠度量在晚期时间饱和到Haar随机值；对于不等三分区，Rényi互信息和纠缠负性在晚期时间消失，表明相应约化密度矩阵可因子化。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamics of quantum correlations in many-body systems is a central problem in non-equilibrium quantum physics. We study the spread of mixed-state entanglement in a minimal model of quantum chaos, the kicked field Ising model. By combining the replica trick with the space-time duality of the model, we determine the exact spectrum of the partially transposed reduced density matrix. The resulting flat spectrum leads to exact relations between entanglement negativity, odd entropy and Rényi mutual information at early times. Numerical results further demonstrate that for equal tri-partitions and at late times, all entanglement measures saturate to the Haar-random values. In contrast, for unequal tri-partitions Rényi mutual information and negativity vanish at late times, implying that the corresponding reduced density matrix is factorizable. Extensive numerical simulations also show that the relation remains quantitatively valid for generic initial states, leading us to conjecture it for all initial states and all times.

### [15] [Exact characterizations for quantum conditional mutual information and some other entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14650)
*Zhou Gang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提供了量子信息论中互信息（mutual information）的精确数学表征，解决了强次可加性定理（strong subadditivity）在互信息较小时寻找最优恢复信道（recovery channel）的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当量子互信息为零时，可以使用Petz恢复映射（Petz recovery map）重构量子信道；但当互信息较小时，需要定义最优恢复信道。为此，需要互信息的精确数学表征。

Result: 提供了互信息的精确表征，控制是尖锐的（sharp），没有改进空间，即无论互信息（或余项）大小都提供等式。表征适用于互信息及其他熵。

Conclusion: 通过将熵定义转化为显式构造项的求和，获得了互信息的精确数学表征，这有助于在互信息较小时定义最优恢复信道。

Abstract: Lieb and Ruskai's strong subadditivity theorem, which shows that the conditional mutual information must be nonnegative, is fundamental in quantum theory. It has numerous applications, such as in quantum error correction. When the mutual information is zero, the Petz recovery map can be used to reconstruct the quantum channel. When the mutual information is small, one seeks to define an optimal recovery channel. To this end, a mathematical characterization of the mutual information is desirable. We address this problem by providing an exact characterization of the mutual information, along with characterizations for other entropies. Our controls are sharp, leaving no room for improvement, in the sense that we provide equalities, regardless of whether the mutual information (or remainder) is small or large. We transform the definitions of these entropies into a summation of explicitly constructed terms, and the definition of each term obviously demonstrates the desired positivity/convexity/concavity. The summation converges rapidly and absolutely in a chosen elementary norm.

Motivation: 研究旨在探讨简并高阶导数系统中经典等价性是否必然延伸至量子动力学，特别是通过玻姆力学框架分析幽灵哈密顿量的动力学行为。

Method: 采用玻姆力学（Bohmian mechanics）方法，使用高斯波包推导相应的引导方程（guidance equations）、中心与宽度演化以及量子势（quantum potential），并比较幽灵哈密顿量与经典等价替代表述的双哈密顿量对。

Result: 玻姆轨迹（Bohmian trajectories）能够直接诊断相干性、波包形变和量子-经典分离，并表征了有界、准半经典、螺旋和逃逸等不同动力学区域。虽然两种经典等价描述产生相同的经典轨迹，但导致不同的玻姆轨迹和沿这些轨迹评估的量子势。

Conclusion: 经典等价性不一定延伸至玻姆量子动力学，这揭示了简并高阶导数系统中存在具体的量子模糊性（quantum ambiguity）。玻姆轨迹为相干性和波包形变提供了直接的动力学诊断工具。

Abstract: We develop a Bohmian analysis of a two-dimensional ghost Hamiltonian and its mapping to the degenerate Pais-Uhlenbeck model. Using Gaussian wavepackets, we derive the corresponding guidance equations, the centre and width evolution, and the quantum potential. We use these quantities to characterise bounded, quasi-semiclassical, spiral, and runaway regimes. The Bohmian trajectories provide a direct dynamical diagnostic of coherence, packet deformation, and quantum-classical separation. We then compare a bi-Hamiltonian pair consisting of the ghost Hamiltonian and a classically equivalent alternative formulation. While the two descriptions produce identical classical trajectories, they lead to different Bohmian trajectories and different quantum potentials evaluated along those trajectories. This demonstrates that classical equivalence need not extend to Bohmian quantum dynamics and identifies a concrete quantum ambiguity in the degenerate higher-derivative system.

</details>

Conclusion: 结论表明，电路量子电动力学平台为研究监测多体动力学提供了可行实验路径，特殊分束器电路展现出独特的临界行为，且相关特征在现有技术条件下可观测。

Abstract: We propose a route to study monitored many-body dynamics in multimode bosonic systems using circuit quantum electrodynamics. In this experimental setting, we construct several bosonic models comprising brickwork circuits built from beam-splitter gates, local parity measurements, and optional on-site Hubbard interactions, and diagnose their monitored dynamics via ancilla purification and a learnability-based probe. Under parity measurements, generic gate sets exhibit behavior that is largely consistent with a conventional measurement-induced phase transition, while a special class of beam-splitter circuits shows an apparent critical-like high-measurement regime in which purification times scale linearly with system size. We show that for realistic noise, gate, and measurement rates, these signatures are observable with near-term circuit QED hardware.

### [18] [Characterization of Radiation-Induced Errors in Superconducting Qubits Protected with Various Gap-Engineering Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13460)

TL;DR: 该研究评估了能隙工程（gap engineering）对超导量子比特（superconducting qubits）辐射抗性的影响，通过暴露量子比特阵列于α粒子和电子辐射源，发现能隙工程能减少相关错误并加速准粒子（quasiparticle）恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能粒子撞击会导致约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions, JJs）附近准粒子密度增加，从而引发相关错误（correlated errors），这些错误难以通过传统纠错码修复。先前实验通过增大结两侧超导能隙差（superconducting gap energy）来减少相关错误，本研究旨在系统评估能隙工程的效果。

Method: 将transmon量子比特阵列暴露于两种辐射源：来自²⁴¹Am源的α粒子（alpha-particles）和来自脉冲直线加速器（pulsed linear accelerator）的电子。测量了空间和时间相关的T₁错误以及时间相关的T₁和T₂错误，评估了约瑟夫森结附近能隙工程（δΔJJ）和电容/地平面能隙工程（δΔM1）的影响。

Result: α粒子辐射导致空间和时间相关的T₁错误，支持强子宇宙射线（hadronic cosmic rays）是先前观测到的10⁻¹⁰错误底限的主要贡献者。电子辐射导致时间相关的T₁和T₂错误。具有更强约瑟夫森结能隙工程的量子比特阵列表现出更少的相关T₁错误，而更大的δΔM1能加速T₁和T₂错误的恢复时间，归因于准粒子被捕获到电容/地平面。

Conclusion: 能隙工程能有效减少超导量子比特中的辐射诱导相关错误，约瑟夫森结处的能隙工程降低错误严重性，而电容/地平面的能隙工程加速准粒子恢复。研究构建的准粒子动力学模型与观测结果定性一致，为提升量子比特的辐射抗性提供了策略。

Abstract: Impacts from high-energy particles cause correlated errors in superconducting qubits by increasing the quasiparticle density in the vicinity of the Josephson junctions (JJs). Such errors are particularly harmful as they cannot be easily remedied via conventional error correcting codes. Recent experiments reduced correlated errors by making the difference in superconducting gap energy across the JJ larger than the qubit energy. In this work, we assess gap engineering near the JJ ($δΔ_{\mathrm{JJ}}$) and the capacitor/ground-plane ($δΔ_{\mathrm{M1}}$) by exposing arrays of transmon qubits to two sources of radiation. For $α$-particles from an $^{241}$Am source, we observe $T_1$ errors correlated in space and time, supporting a hypothesis that hadronic cosmic rays are a major contributor to the $10^{-10}$ error floor observed in Ref. 1. For electrons from a pulsed linear accelerator, we observe temporally correlated $T_1$ and $T_2$ errors, this measurement is insensitive to spatial correlations. We observe that the severity of correlated $T_1$ errors is reduced for qubit arrays with a greater degree of gap engineering at the JJ. For both $T_1$ and $T_2$ errors, the recovery time is hastened by an increased $δΔ_{\mathrm{M1}}$, which we attribute to the trapping of quasiparticles into the capacitor/ground-plane. We construct a model of quasiparticle dynamics that qualitatively agrees with our observations. This work reinforces the multifaceted influence of radiation on superconducting qubits and provides strategies for improving radiation resilience.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统理论在凝聚态物理和量子技术中至关重要，但Schwinger-Keldysh场理论的数值求解面临时间步数立方标度的限制，特别是在系统与环境时间尺度广泛分离的情况下尤为严重。

Result: 该方法能够同时捕捉低温非马尔可夫性（low-temperature non-Markovianity）和由更快环境尺度产生的重整化效应（renormalization effects）。

Abstract: The theory of open quantum systems addresses how coupling to external degrees of freedom modifies observables and quantum coherence, a situation central to fundamental condensed-matter research and emerging quantum technologies. Schwinger-Keldysh field theory is a natural framework for both open- and nonequilibrium quantum systems in terms of functional integrals. However, its numerical solution is limited by a cubic scaling with the number of time steps. This is particularly prohibitive for scenarios with widely separated time scales, as is often the case for system and environmental scales. We consider a damped quantum harmonic oscillator as a toy model to study a separation-of-scales ansatz based on Hadamard regularization. A time-stepping algorithm for the Kadanoff-Baym equations on the slow system time-scale is presented that captures both low-temperature non-Markovianity and renormalization effects arising from the much faster environment scale.

### [20] [Distance learning from projective measurements as an information-geometric probe of many-body physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13485)
*Oleksii Malyshev,Simon M. Linsel,Fabian Grusdt,Annabelle Bohrdt,Eugene Demler,Ivan Morera*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于距离学习（distance learning）的量子多体系统分析方法，通过单神经网络判别器无监督地估计量子态间的统计距离，用于识别不同关联主导的区域和相变临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代量子模拟器能够生成大量单次投影"快照"，为量子多体系统研究提供了丰富数据。传统方法通常通过学习和聚类量子态的低维表示来重建相图，本研究旨在绕过表示学习，直接从快照推断量子态间的成对距离。

Method: 采用距离学习（distance learning）方法，使用单一神经网络判别器无监督地估计Csiszar f-散度（Csiszar f-divergences）——分布间的统计距离。该方法将推断的发散极限与Fisher信息度量（Fisher information metric）联系起来，并分析其有限尺寸标度。

Result: 生成的聚类揭示了具有不同主导关联的区域，这些区域通常与（但不限于）传统定义的物相重合。该方法成功恢复了各种系统中的相界，包括具有传统局域序参量、非局域拓扑序和高阶关联的系统，并定量匹配了已知的临界行为。

Conclusion: 距离学习作为一种多功能的信息几何探针，能够识别量子多体物理中的主导关联。通过分析到适当参考快照分布的距离，可以确定所发现聚类内的主导关联模式，为量子多体系统研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: The ability of modern quantum simulators--both digital and analogue--to generate large ensembles of single-shot projective "snapshots" has opened a data-rich avenue for the study of quantum many-body systems. Unsupervised machine learning analysis of such snapshots has gained traction, with numerous works reconstructing phase diagrams by learning and clustering low-dimensional representations of quantum states. Here, we forgo such representation learning in favour of distance learning: we infer the pairwise distances between quantum states--already sufficient for clustering--directly from snapshots. Specifically, we use a single neural discriminator to estimate Csiszar f-divergences--statistical distances between distributions--in an unsupervised manner. The resulting clusters reveal regimes with different dominant correlations, often coinciding with, but not limited to, conventionally defined phases of matter. Beyond phase-diagram exploration, we connect the infinitesimal limit of the inferred divergences to the Fisher information metric and analyse its finite-size scaling. This yields critical exponents of the discovered transitions and enables snapshot-based analysis of universality classes. We apply distance learning to a diverse set of systems characterised by conventional local order parameters (1D transverse-field and 2D classical Ising models), non-local topological order (extended toric code), and higher-order correlations (fermionic t-J model on a triangular lattice). In all cases, we correctly recover boundaries between distinct correlation regimes and, where applicable, quantitatively match established critical behaviour. Finally, we show that distances to suitably chosen reference snapshot distributions help identify the dominant correlations within the discovered clusters, positioning distance learning as a versatile information-geometric probe of quantum many-body physics.

Abstract: For decades, Hermiticity was considered an immutable axiom of quantum mechanics, essential for ensuring real energies and unitary evolution. This perspective has shifted radically, driven by the realization that non-Hermitian Hamiltonians provide a powerful effective description of open quantum systems, granting access to unique phenomena such as Exceptional Points and the Non-Hermitian Skin Effect. In this Perspective, we chart the trajectory of this field, moving from its established foundations in single-particle, linear models to the emerging frontier of interacting many-body systems. We first clarify the physical origins of non-Hermitian dynamics, distinguishing between mean-field approximations, conditional "no-click" evolution, and exact Liouvillian dynamics. We then focus on the rich phenomenology arising from the interplay of non-Hermiticity and interactions. We discuss interaction-induced topological phases, the generalization of skin effects to the many-body Hilbert space, and the distinct signatures of dissipative quantum chaos and complexity. Finally, we highlight collective phenomena in nonlinear regimes, including skin solitons and dissipative phase transitions. We also comment on measurement-induced entanglement transitions and their relation to non-Hermitian spectra and topology. By synthesizing these diverse developments, we provide a roadmap for the future of non-Hermitian physics.

### [22] [Quantum Process Realization of LDPC Code Dualities and Product Constructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13538)
*Shuhan Zhang,Deepak Aryal,Yi-Zhuang You*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种统一框架，将经典LDPC码的多种构造（包括Kramers-Wannier对偶、张量积和校验积）实现为由辅助比特初始化、局部幺正算符和投影测量组成的量子过程，并利用ZX-演算进行图解表示和电路提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在建立经典纠错码（classical error-correcting codes）变换与量子过程之间的系统联系，特别是将Kramers-Wannier对偶性（Kramers-Wannier duality）、张量积（tensor product）和校验积（check product）等构造统一到量子电路框架中。

Method: 采用ZX-演算（ZX-calculus）进行图解表示，并开发系统算法提取量子电路。核心框架基于经典LDPC码的物理内容由其Tanner图（Tanner graph）相关的算子代数（operator algebra）捕获，码变换对应这些代数之间的映射。

Result: 成功将Kramers-Wannier对偶性解释为规范固定（gauging），张量积和校验积对应耦合层构造（coupled-layer constructions），其中层间耦合和投影实现了堆叠算子代数（stacked operator algebras）的商运算（quotient）。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一个统一框架，连接了码变换、量子电路以及不同物质量子相（quantum phases of matter）之间的映射关系。

Abstract: We realize a broad class of code constructions, including Kramers-Wannier duality, tensor product, and check product, as quantum processes consisting of ancilla initialization, local unitaries, and projective measurements. Using ZX-calculus, we represent these transformations diagrammatically and provide a systematic algorithm for extracting quantum circuits. Central to our framework is the observation that the physical content of a classical LDPC code is captured by the operator algebra associated with its Tanner graph, and that code transformations correspond to maps between such algebras. Kramers-Wannier duality then admits a natural interpretation as gauging, while tensor and check products correspond to coupled-layer constructions in which interlayer coupling and projection implement a quotient on stacked operator algebras. Together, these results establish a unified framework connecting code transformations, quantum circuits, and mappings between distinct quantum phases of matter.

Result: 在20个基准测试实例中，单次混合尝试在1秒内产生高质量解，其中14个案例匹配基态能量（ground-state energy）。在相同运行时间内，基于CPU的求解器（包括模拟退火、模因禁忌搜索和EasySolve）未能达到HSQC获得的解质量，而增强的并行回火方法和GPU加速求解器ABS3达到或超越了该性能。

Abstract: We perform an end-to-end benchmark of a hybrid sequential quantum computing (HSQC) solver for higher-order unconstrained binary optimization (HUBO), executed on IBM Heron r3 quantum processors to evaluate the potential of current quantum hardware for combinatorial optimization with sub-second end-to-end runtimes. All reported runtimes include the complete pipeline--from preprocessing to QPU execution and postprocessing--under strict wall-clock accounting. Across 20 benchmark instances, a single hybrid attempt produces high-quality solutions in less than one second, matching the ground-state energy in 14 cases. At the same runtime, CPU-based solvers, including simulated annealing, memetic tabu search, and EasySolve, do not reach the value obtained by HSQC, whereas an enhanced parallel tempering method and the GPU-accelerated solver ABS3 reach or surpass it. These results show that HSQC, executed on a single QPU, can achieve performance competitive with strong classical solvers running on 128 vCPUs or 8 NVIDIA A100 GPUs, while also providing a reproducible system-level benchmark for tracking progress as quantum hardware and hybrid sequential workflows improve.

Motivation: 近期量子设备通常产生噪声通道产生的混合态而非完美纯态，因此需要研究在噪声条件下的量子优势。多体非定域性和上下文性（contextuality）的贝尔定理可作为证明量子优势的基准。

Method: 研究考虑具有对称性保护拓扑序（symmetry-protected topological order, SPT）的一维多体系统的热混合态。使用最小纠缠典型热态算法（minimally entangled typical thermal states algorithm）分析多体上下文性游戏（many-body contextuality game）的有限尺寸实例。

Result: 量子优势在混合态中由扭曲弦序参数（twisted string order parameters, SOP）和对称性表示期望值的组合测量。量子优势在非零临界温度下持续存在，且该临界温度对系统尺寸相对稳健。量子获胜概率由与一维簇态（1D cluster state）的全局保真度下界给出。

Conclusion: 该上下文性游戏可为近期实验设备中创建长程序（如SPT态）的能力提供操作意义基准，表明这些态在可扩展方式下仍可用于证明噪声硬件的真正"量子性"。

Abstract: Bell theorems of many-body nonlocality and contextuality serve as a benchmark for proving quantum advantage in that a quantum computer outperforms a classical computer for a certain problem. In practice, however, near-term quantum devices do not prepare perfectly pure states but rather mixed states produced from noisy channels. We investigate noisy quantum advantage by considering thermal mixed states of one-dimensional many-body systems with a symmetry-protected topological (SPT) order. In the pure-state (or zero-temperature) case, these states are known to be useful for measurement-based quantum computation, and to outperform classical computers in a many-body contextuality game, provided string order parameters (SOPs) of SPT are sufficiently large. Here, we show that quantum advantage in mixed states is measured by a combination of twisted SOP and symmetry representation expectation values. Using the minimally entangled typical thermal states algorithm, it is demonstrated that quantum advantage persists to a nonzero critical temperature for finite-sized instances of the many-body contextuality game. While this critical temperature goes to zero in the thermodynamic limit, it is relatively robust to system size, suggesting that these states remain useful for demonstrating genuine "quantumness" of noisy hardware in a scalable fashion. Finally, we show that the quantum winning probability is lower bounded by the global fidelity with the 1D cluster state, so that our contextuality game can provide an operational meaning to benchmark the capacity to create long-range order like SPT states in near-term experimental devices.

</details>


### [25] [Quantum Correlations and Entanglement in Generalized Dicke-Ising Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13693)
*Santiago F. Caballero-Benitez*

TL;DR: 本文开发了光-物质DMRG算法，研究高Q腔中量子自旋链与腔场耦合系统的超辐射相变，发现光诱导多模结构可调控量子纠缠和长程序自旋向列态。

Method: 利用光与相互作用物质之间的增强耦合，通过新开发的光-物质DMRG（Light-Matter DMRG）算法研究强相互作用自旋链中涌现超辐射模式的性质。该方法可有效模拟横向伊辛链（transverse Ising chain）与腔光耦合的实验可行推广模型。

Result: 研究发现系统可诱导由泵浦光定制的多模结构，产生丰富可测信号。在向超辐射相（superradiant phases）转变时，涌现具有长程序（long range order）的量子自旋向列态（quantum spin nematic states）和磁振子对（magnon pairs）。腔场可优化不同光诱导模式间的自旋纠缠，用于量子关联态的量子态工程（quantum state engineering）。

Conclusion: 该方法可高效模拟局域和长程耦合的量子自旋系统，研究涌现序和强量子关联物理。所开发算法同样适用于其他混合量子系统（hybrid quantum systems）的高效建模。

Abstract: Quantum systems inside high-Q cavities offer an excellent testbed for the control of emergent symmetries induced by light and their interplay with quantum matter. Recently several developments in cavity experiments with neutral atoms and other quantum objects such as ions motivate the study of their quantum correlated properties and their entanglement to tailor and control the behavior of the system. Using the enhanced coupling between light and interacting matter we explore the properties of emergent superradiant modes using our newly developed Light-Matter DMRG algorithm with strongly interacting spin chains. We explore a experimentally viable generalization of the transverse Ising chain coupled to the cavity light where it is possible to induce multimode structures tailored by the light pumped into the system. We find a plethora of scenarios can be explored with clear and accesible measurable signatures. This allows to study the physics of emergent orders and strong quantum correlations with quantum spins where the local and long range coupling can be efficiently simulated. We find that quantum spin nematic states with long range order and magnon pairs emerge as the transitions to superradiant phases take place. Notably, we show the cavity field allows the optimization of entanglement between spins for different light induced modes which can be used for quantum state engineering of quantum correlated states. Our methods can be used to model other hybrid quantum systems efficiently.

### [26] [Thermodynamics of a biophotomimetic nonreciprocal quantum battery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15268)
*Trishna Kalita,Manash Jyoti Sarmah,Himangshu Prabal Goswami*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于细菌捕光复合体架构的全功能非互易量子电池理论模型，通过亚辐射和超辐射态实现功能分配，并引入单模腔辅助存储，研究了包括存储、泄漏、功提取、通量和功率在内的完整热力学性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于受细菌捕光复合体（bacterial light-harvesting complexes）架构启发的非互易量子电池设计需求，旨在探索量子光学态在能量存储系统中的功能角色分配，并建立完整的量子电池热力学性能分析框架。

Method: 方法包括：1）将集体量子光学亚辐射态（subradiant states）和超辐射态（superradiant states）赋予功能性角色；2）引入单模腔（unimodal cavity）辅助能量存储；3）从针对电池几何结构定制的有效非厄米哈密顿量（effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）获得跃迁速率；4）将跃迁速率输入主方程（master equation）以解析时间演化。

Result: 研究发现：1）不同环尺寸存在优化点，每个尺寸在其特定能量功能上达到峰值；2）环与中心系统之间的强耦合（strong coupling）增强了电池存储能量的能力，但降低了功率输出能力；3）功提取（ergotropy）超过容量并随系统尺寸增加线性趋近容量，存在一个在强耦合下消失的最优小尺寸区域。

Conclusion: 结论表明，基于细菌捕光复合体架构的非互易量子电池模型能够实现完整的热力学功能，系统尺寸和耦合强度对存储能力与功率输出存在权衡关系，功提取性能随系统尺寸呈现线性增长趋势，为量子电池设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We propose a theoretical model of a fully functional nonreciprocal quantum battery inspired by the architecture of bacterial light-harvesting complexes. We assign functional roles to collective quantum optical subradiant and superradiant states and introduce a unimodal cavity to assist storage. The transition rates are obtained from an effective non-Hermitian Hamiltonian, tailored to the battery geometry which are fed into a master equation to unravel the time evolution. We investigate the complete thermodynamic performance including storage, leakage, ergotropy, work extraction, flux, and power. We observe optimization at different ring sizes, each peaking at its specific energetic function. Strong coupling between the ring and central system enhances the battery's ability to store energy but reduces the ability of power output. The ergotropy exceeds capacity and approaches it linearly with increasing system size, with an optimal small-size regime that disappears under strong coupling.

### [27] [Analog-Digital Quantum Computing with Quantum Annealing Processors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15534)
*Rahul Deshpande,Majid Kheirkhah,Chris Rich,Richard Harris,Jack Raymond,Emile Hoskinson,Pratik Sathe,Andrew J. Berkley,Stefan Paul,Brian Barch,Daniel A. Lidar,Markus Müller,Gabriel Aeppli,Andrew D. King,Mohammad H. Amin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在超导量子退火处理器中实现了模拟-数字量子计算，通过辅助量子比特实现任意基矢的初始化和测量，扩展了量子退火处理器的操作类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子退火处理器通常统一控制量子比特，均匀衰减量子涨落，这简化了控制要求但限制了可用操作类别。本研究旨在扩展量子退火处理器的功能类别。

Method: 在高度多路复用的超导量子退火处理器中执行模拟-数字量子计算（analog-digital quantum computing），利用固定多体哈密顿量演化，在弱耦合区域可用有效XY模型描述，并通过辅助量子比特实现任意基矢的初始化和测量。

Result: 展示了多个基础应用：不同初始化和测量基矢下的单量子比特和双量子比特相干振荡、符合理论预期的多量子比特量子行走（quantum walk）与费米子色散（fermionic dispersion），以及无序链中的安德森局域化（Anderson localization）。

Conclusion: 这些实验为量子计算和量子模拟开辟了广泛的新可能性，极大地扩展了商用量子退火处理器的应用范围。

Abstract: Quantum annealing processors typically control qubits in unison, attenuating quantum fluctuations uniformly until the applied system Hamiltonian is diagonal in the computational basis. This simplifies control requirements, allowing annealing QPUs to scale to much larger sizes than gate-based systems, but constraining the class of available operations. Here we expand the class by performing analog-digital quantum computing in a highly-multiplexed, superconducting quantum annealing processor. This involves evolution under a fixed many-body Hamiltonian that, in the weak-coupling regime, is well-described by an effective XY model, together with arbitrary-basis initialization and measurement via auxiliary qubits. Operationally, this is equivalent to implementing single-qubit gates at the beginning and end of an analog quantum evolution. We demonstrate this capability with several foundational applications: single-qubit and two-qubit coherent oscillations with varying initialization and measurement bases, a multi-qubit quantum walk with fermionic dispersion in line with theory, and Anderson localization in a disordered chain. These experiments open the door to a wide range of new possibilities in quantum computation and simulation, greatly expanding the applications of commercially available quantum annealing processors.

### [28] [Simulating the Open System Dynamics of Multiple Exchange-Only Qubits using Subspace Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15577)
*Tameem Albash,N. Tobias Jacobson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）的子空间蒙特卡洛方法（Subspace Monte Carlo method），用于模拟多比特交换编码（exchange-only, EO）量子比特的开放系统动力学。该方法通过测量每个EO比特的z轴总自旋分量，将密度矩阵表示维度从8²ⁿ降低到3²ⁿ，并结合随机编译（randomized compiling）将相干误差转换为随机误差，从而高效模拟包含复位泄漏（reset-if-leaked）电路的测量结果相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在交换编码（exchange-only, EO）量子比特的开放系统动力学模拟中，传统方法面临维度爆炸问题。EO编码中三个组成自旋的z轴总自旋投影量子数在交换操作下保持不变，但在开放系统（或多比特失准）设置中，不同量子数状态会发生相干和非相干混合，需要更高效的模拟方法。

Method: 提出子空间蒙特卡洛方法（Subspace Monte Carlo method），在每个逻辑量子操作后测量每个EO比特的z轴总自旋分量，使不同自旋投影量子数状态的相干混合退相干。每个EO比特具有确定的自旋投影量子数，n个比特的密度矩阵可用维度3²ⁿ的向量表示（而非8²ⁿ），外加维度n的向量标记每个比特的量子数。

Result: 当模拟电路通过噪声扭转（twirl the noise）将相干误差转换为随机误差时，该动力学近似保持对真实动力学的忠实性，这可通过随机编译（randomized compiling）实现。该方法用于研究包含复位泄漏（reset-if-leaked）电路的测量结果相关性如何受CNOT实现选择的影响，例如使用6个EO比特的多轮贝尔态稳定电路。

Conclusion: 子空间蒙特卡洛方法为多比特交换编码量子比特的开放系统动力学提供了一种高效的模拟框架。通过降低表示维度和利用噪声扭转特性，该方法能够有效研究复杂量子电路（如贝尔态稳定电路）中测量结果的相关性，特别适用于分析不同CNOT实现对系统行为的影响。

Abstract: We propose a Monte Carlo based method for simulating the open system dynamics of multiple exchange-only (EO) qubits. In the EO encoding, the total spin projection quantum number along the $z$-axis of the three constituent spins remains unchanged under exchange operations, in contrast to the open system (or multi-qubit miscalibration) setting where coherent and incoherent mixing of states with different quantum numbers occurs. In our approach, we choose to measure the total spin component along the $z$-axis of each EO qubit after every logical quantum operation, which decoheres coherent mixtures of states with different spin projection quantum numbers. Independent simulations thus give different trajectories of the system in the associated subspaces, so we refer to this method as the Subspace Monte Carlo method. With each EO qubit having a definite spin projection quantum number, the density matrix of $n$ qubits can be represented by a vector of dimension $3^{2n}$, instead of $8^{2n}$, with an additional vector of dimension $n$ to label the quantum number of each qubit. We show that this approximation of the dynamics remains faithful to the true dynamics when the simulated circuits twirl the noise, converting coherent errors to stochastic errors, which can be achieved using randomized compiling. We use this simulation approach to study how correlations in measurement outcomes of circuits with reset-if-leaked gadgets, such as a multi-round Bell state stabilization circuit that uses 6 EO qubits, are affected by the choice of CNOT implementations.

</details>


### [29] [Benchmarking quantum simulation with neutron-scattering experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15608)
*Yi-Ting Lee,Keerthi Kumaran,Bibek Pokharel,Allen Scheie,Colin L. Sarkis,David A. Tennant,Travis Humble,André Schleife,Abhinav Kandala,Arnab Banerjee*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了使用50量子比特超导量子处理器对量子材料进行定量模拟的能力，通过与KCuF₃的中子散射实验数据对比，验证了量子计算在强关联系统模拟中的可靠性，并建立了可扩展的量子-经典混合计算框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计算的核心目标之一是实现量子材料的真实模拟。尽管量子处理器在规模和保真度方面进展迅速，但尚不清楚故障容错前（pre-fault-tolerant）设备能否在其有限的量子门预算内进行定量可靠的材料模拟。

Method: 研究采用量子-经典混合工作流（quantum-classical workflow）计算动力学结构因子（dynamical structure factors, DSFs），使用最多50个量子比特的超导量子处理器模拟KCuF₃（无隙Luttinger液体系统）和具有次近邻相互作用及强各向异性的1D XXZ Heisenberg模型。

Result: 量子模拟结果与KCuF₃的中子散射实验测量进行了定量比较，通过多个指标验证了模拟准确性，并分析了电路深度和保真度对模拟精度的影响。扩展模拟产生了具有能隙的激发谱，可用于描述CsCoX₃化合物在Néel温度以上的行为。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一个计算量子材料动力学结构因子的框架，适用于经典计算难以处理的强纠缠和长程相互作用区域，使得量子模拟能够直接与实验室测量结果进行对比验证。

Abstract: A central goal of quantum computation is the realistic simulation of quantum materials. Although quantum processors have advanced rapidly in scale and fidelity, it has remained unclear whether pre-fault-tolerant devices can perform quantitatively reliable material simulations within their limited gate budgets. Here, we demonstrate that a superconducting quantum processor operating on up to 50 qubits can already produce meaningful, quantitative comparisons with inelastic neutron-scattering measurements of KCuF$_3$, a canonical realization of a gapless Luttinger liquid system with a strongly correlated ground state and a spectrum of emergent spinons. The quantum simulation is enabled by a quantum-classical workflow for computing dynamical structure factors (DSFs). The resulting spectra are benchmarked against experimental measurements using multiple metrics, highlighting the impact of circuit depth and circuit fidelity on simulation accuracy. Finally, we extend our simulations to 1D XXZ Heisenberg model with next-nearest neighbor interactions and a strong anisotropy, producing a gapped excitation spectrum, which could be used to describe the CsCoX$_3$ compounds above the Néel temperature. Our results establish a framework for computing DSFs for quantum materials in classically challenging regimes of strong entanglement and long-range interactions, enabling quantum simulations that are directly testable against laboratory measurements.

### [30] [Automorphisms of Stokes multipliers in higher-order WKBJ theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13332)
*Josh Shelton,Samuel Crew,Christopher J. Lustri*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 该论文研究了线性微分方程和积分问题WKBJ分析中出现的渐近超级数的斯托克斯现象和高阶斯托克斯现象，通过自同构框架和参数化Alien演算来捕捉这些现象，并以燕尾问题为例展示了四分量WKBJ系统的完整结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究线性微分方程和积分问题WKBJ分析中出现的渐近超级数（transseries）的斯托克斯现象（Stokes phenomenon）和高阶斯托克斯现象（higher-order Stokes phenomenon, HOSP）。这些现象在渐近分析中具有重要意义，特别是在处理发散展开时。

Method: 引入了一个自同构（automorphisms）框架，该框架作用于发散展开的斯托克斯常数（Stokes constants），通过晚期项展开（late-late-term expansions）和参数化Alien演算（parametric Alien calculus）来解释这些现象。该方法应用于一个典型范例：从突变理论（catastrophe theory）中的燕尾问题（Swallowtail problem）出发，该问题包含四个WKBJ分量。

Result: 获得了燕尾问题的完整斯托克斯线结构（Stokes line structure）和自同构。研究表明，在具有四个或更多WKBJ分量的系统中，与高阶斯托克斯现象相关的自同构本身可以在另一个高阶斯托克斯线上改变值，这发生在不同高阶斯托克斯线相交时。同时论证了对于五个或更多WKBJ分量的超级数，不会出现额外的特殊行为。

Conclusion: 论文建立了一个系统框架来捕捉渐近超级数中的高阶斯托克斯现象，揭示了在四分量WKBJ系统中自同构值变化的机制，并确定了这种现象在更高维度系统中的行为界限。

Abstract: We consider the Stokes phenomenon and higher-order Stokes phenomenon (HOSP) of formal asymptotic transseries arising in the WKBJ analysis of linear differential equations and integral problems. We introduce a framework of automorphisms that act on the Stokes constants of the divergent expansion, explained via late-late-term expansions and parametric Alien calculus, to capture this phenomenon. Our method is applied to a paradigmatic example: we obtain the full Stokes line structure and automorphisms for the Swallowtail problem from catastrophe theory, which contains four WKBJ components. We demonstrate that, in a system with four or more WKBJ components, the automorphism associated with the HOSP can itself change value across another higher-order Stokes line, which occurs when different higher-order Stokes lines intersect. We then argue that no additional special behaviour emerges for transseries with five or more WKBJ components.

</details>

### [31] [PolyMon: A Unified Framework for Polymer Property Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13303)
*Gaopeng Ren,Yijie Yang,Jiajun Zhou,Kim E. Jelfs*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: PolyMon是一个统一的聚合物性质预测框架，整合了多种聚合物表示方法、机器学习模型和训练策略，通过系统评估为机器学习在聚合物领域的应用提供了可扩展的基础平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物性质的准确预测对材料设计至关重要，但面临数据稀缺、聚合物表示方法多样以及缺乏对建模选择的系统评估等挑战。现有方法分散且缺乏统一比较标准。

Method: PolyMon框架整合了多种聚合物描述符和图形构建策略，支持从表格模型到图神经网络（graph neural networks）的广泛模型，并包含多保真学习（multi-fidelity learning）、Δ学习（Δ-learning）、主动学习（active learning）和集成学习（ensemble learning）等灵活训练策略。

Result: 使用五个关键聚合物性质作为基准，通过系统评估揭示了不同表示方法和模型对预测性能的影响。案例研究展示了如何在一致的工作流程中应用不同训练策略来利用有限数据并整合物理模型信息。

Conclusion: PolyMon为基于机器学习的聚合物性质预测的基准测试和进展提供了全面且可扩展的基础平台，其代码已在GitHub上开源，促进了该领域的标准化和可重复性研究。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of polymer properties is essential for materials design, but remains challenging due to data scarcity, diverse polymer representations, and the lack of systematic evaluation across modelling choices. Here, we present PolyMon, a unified and accessible framework that integrates multiple polymer representations, machine learning methods, and training strategies within a single, accessible platform. PolyMon supports various descriptors and graph construction strategies for polymer representations, and includes a wide range of models, from tabular models to graph neural networks, along with flexible training strategies including multi-fidelity learning, Δ-learning, active learning, and ensemble learning. Using five key polymer properties as benchmarks, we perform systematic evaluations to assess how representations and models affect predictive performance. These case studies further illustrate how different training strategies can be applied within a consistent workflow to leverage limited data and incorporate physical model derived information. Overall, PolyMon provides a comprehensive and extensible foundation for benchmarking and advancing machine learning-based polymer property prediction. The code is available at github.com/fate1997/polymon.

</details>


### [32] [Brush-mediated angular constraints reshape structure, rigidity, and percolation in colloidal depletion gels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13596)
*Ziye Zhuang,Robert A. Campbell,Paniz Haghighi,Safa Jamali,Ali Mohraz*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过调控表面接枝聚合物刷密度，在胶体凝胶中实现了非中心力的涌现，从而显著改变凝胶结构和力学性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体凝胶等软无序固体的力学性能不仅取决于粒子间吸引力强度，还受约束粒子运动的力对称性影响。传统方法通过粒子各向异性、表面粗糙度或斑块相互作用引入非中心力，但这些方法掩盖了非中心力的独立作用。

Method: 研究采用几何保持的最小化方法，通过降低表面接枝聚合物刷密度在胶体凝胶中实现涌现的非中心力。结合实验、模拟和平均场理论，分析非中心约束对结构和力学性能的影响。

Result: 低刷密度下，部分刷相互渗透在粒子接触处引入有效的角弯曲刚度，抑制局部致密化，稳定低配位网络，产生高度分支的凝胶结构。非中心约束重组了跨尺度的结构和力学，使凝胶边界偏移，弹性模量提高近三倍。

Conclusion: 表面刷密度可作为软颗粒物质中编程相互作用对称性的通用控制参数，对无序系统中的刚性、渗流和机械设计具有重要意义。

Abstract: Colloidal gels, like many other soft and disordered solids derive their mechanical properties not only from the strength of interparticle attraction, but also from the symmetry of the forces that constrain particle motion. While non-central interactions are known to profoundly alter rigidity and elasticity, they are typically introduced through particle anisotropy, surface roughness, or patchy interactions, obscuring their independent role. Here we demonstrate a minimal and geometry-preserving route to emergent non-central forces in colloidal gels by reducing the density of surface-grafted polymer brushes. At low brush density, partial brush interpenetration introduces an effective angular bending rigidity at particle contacts, despite fully isotropic particle geometry. This emergent constraint suppresses local densification, stabilizes low-coordination networks, and produces highly ramified gel structures with enhanced elasticity. Combining experiments, simulations, and mean-field theory, we show that these non-central constraints reorganize structure and mechanics across length scales, shifting gelation boundaries and increasing the elastic modulus by nearly a factor of three. Our results establish surface brush density as a generic control parameter for programming interaction symmetry in soft particulate matter, with implications for rigidity, percolation, and mechanical design in disordered systems.

</details>

*Qinghao Mao,Michael van der Naald,Abhinendra Singh,Heinrich M. Jaeger*

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种约束计数模型（constraint-counting model），通过引入约束比（constraint ratio）作为关键控制参数，能够统一描述致密悬浮液在剪切下的粘度剧增现象，为剪切增稠材料提供了预测性建模框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密悬浮液在剪切作用下观察到的粘度剧增现象，对理解微观接触力学如何转化为宏观流动阻力构成了重大挑战。当前缺乏能够自然整合摩擦和维度因素的理论框架来解释这一现象。

Method: 借鉴干颗粒堵塞物理（dry granular jamming physics）的思想，引入约束计数模型，将接触分为锁定（locked）和非锁定（non-locked）两类，定义约束比（constraint ratio）作为单一状态变量来衡量每个粒子的平均机械约束强度。

Result: 该模型能够自然整合摩擦和维度因素，无需额外假设即可实现流变学数据（rheological data）在通用主曲线（universal master curve）上的坍缩。通过将约束比识别为关键控制参数，为剪切增稠材料提供了统一描述框架。

Conclusion: 该约束计数模型框架为剪切增稠材料的预测性建模（predictive modeling）和理性设计（rational design）提供了统一路径，通过单一状态变量约束比成功解释了微观接触力学到宏观流动阻力的转化机制。

Abstract: The dramatic viscosity increase observed in dense suspensions under shear poses a major challenge in our understanding of how microscopic contact mechanics translate into macroscopic flow resistance. Here, we introduce a constraint-counting model that incorporates friction and dimensionality naturally without additional assumptions and allows for collapsing of rheological data onto a universal master curve. In this model, we borrow ideas from dry granular jamming physics and classify contacts as either locked or non-locked to define a single state variable, the constraint ratio, which measures the average strength of mechanical constraint per particle. By identifying the constraint ratio as the key control parameter, our framework provides a unifying route toward predictive modeling and rational design of shear-thickening materials.

### [34] [Splitting probabilities of confined active particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13621)
*Sarafa A. Iyaniwura,Zhiwei Peng*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过后向福克-普朗克方程（backward Fokker-Planck equation）分析了活性粒子（active particles）在受限域中的分裂概率（splitting probability），包括一维区间和二维波纹通道，揭示了通道几何、粒子活性和手性对逃逸概率的调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性粒子表现出自推进（self-propulsion）特性，其输运行为与被动布朗运动（passive Brownian motion）有本质区别。在受限或结构化域中，活性强烈影响逃逸概率和首次通过行为（first-passage behavior），理解这些效应对于描述生物微环境、微流控装置和异质介质中的输运至关重要。

Method: 研究利用后向福克-普朗克方程（backward Fokker-Planck equation）分析活性粒子在受限域中的分裂概率。对于一维情况，推导了各种渐近区域（asymptotic regimes）的解析解；对于小纵横比的波纹通道，发展了菲克-雅各布斯约化（Fick-Jacobs reduction）以获得沿轴向的有效输运方程；对于有限纵横比情况，则通过数值方法表征分裂动力学。

Result: 研究展示了通道几何、粒子活性和手性（chirality）如何调控通过不同边界的逃逸可能性。在波纹通道中，小纵横比情况下获得了有效的轴向输运方程，而有限纵横比情况下的分裂动力学通过数值方法得到表征。

Conclusion: 研究结果为复杂环境中活性物质（active matter）的输运提供了定量预测，并强调了限制（confinement）与活性之间的相互作用（interplay）。这些发现对于理解受限环境中活性粒子的输运行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: Active particles exhibit self-propulsion, leading to transport behavior that differs fundamentally from passive Brownian motion. In confined or structured domains, activity strongly influence escape probabilities and first-passage behavior. Understanding these effects is essential for describing transport in biological microenvironments, microfluidic devices, and heterogeneous media. In this work, leveraging the backward Fokker--Planck equation, we investigate the splitting probability of active particles in confined domains, focusing on both a one-dimensional interval and a two-dimensional corrugated channel. Analytical solutions are derived for the one-dimensional case in various asymptotic regimes. In corrugated channels with small aspect ratios, we develop a Fick--Jacobs reduction that yields effective transport equations along the axial direction, whereas for finite aspect ratios, the splitting dynamics are characterized numerically. We demonstrate how channel geometry, particle activity, and chirality modulate the likelihood of escape through different boundaries. Our results provide quantitative predictions for the transport of active matter in complex environments and highlight the interplay between confinement and activity.

Our study thus provides additional evidence for an underlying unity among various theoretical frameworks and for the presence of quantitative relations between the characteristic properties emphasized by these models. ### [39] [Air Drag Controls the Finite-Time Singularity of Euler's Disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14520)
*Benjamin G. Thorne,Ahmad Zareei,Kausalya Mahadevan,Shmuel M. Rubinstein,Ariel Amir*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过高速成像实验揭示了欧拉圆盘（Euler's disk）在停止前运动中的主要耗散机制：在接近奇点（singularity）的后期阶段由空气粘性阻力主导，而在早期阶段则由滚动摩擦主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圆盘侧立旋转至停止的运动是有限时间奇点（finite-time singularity）的经典案例，但其主导耗散机制仍存在争议。本研究旨在澄清欧拉圆盘奇点背后的耗散机制，并对光滑表面低载荷下的滚动接触系统有更广泛的意义。

Method: 采用立体高速成像（stereoscopic high-speed imaging）技术，研究不同质量和半径的圆盘在不同表面的动力学行为。通过质量依赖性分析、部分真空环境测量以及使用钢环进行几何控制等实验方法，验证耗散机制。

Result: 研究表明，在接近奇点的后期运动由边界层剪切产生的空气粘性阻力（viscous air-drag）主导，这通过质量依赖性、真空实验和几何控制得到证实。早期阶段则主要由滚动摩擦（rolling friction）主导，在玻璃表面观察到与圆盘质量呈亚线性缩放（sublinear scaling）的意外现象，表明存在基于粘附的滚动阻力（adhesion-based rolling resistance）。

Conclusion: 该研究明确了欧拉圆盘奇点背后的耗散机制：后期阶段空气粘性阻力主导，早期阶段滚动摩擦主导。这些发现不仅澄清了经典力学问题，也对光滑表面低载荷条件下的滚动接触系统具有更广泛的启示意义。

Abstract: The motion of a disk spinning to rest after being tipped on its side is a classic example of a finite-time singularity, yet the dominant dissipation mechanism governing this process remains debated. Using stereoscopic high-speed imaging, we study the dynamics of disks with varying mass and radius on different surfaces. We show that the late-time motion near the singularity is governed by viscous air-drag arising from shear in the boundary layer beneath the disk, as evidenced by the mass dependence of the dynamics, measurements in a partial vacuum, and a geometric control using a steel ring. At earlier times, dissipation is dominated by rolling friction, which on glass exhibits an unexpected sublinear scaling with disk mass, suggesting an adhesion-based rolling resistance. These results clarify the dissipation mechanisms underlying the singularity of Euler's disk and have broader implications for rolling-contact systems operating under low loads on smooth surfaces.

In contrast, pronounced aerotactic migration toward the oxygen-supplying wall emerges as the density increases. Analyzing the temporal evolution of this bacterial distribution reveals that the aerotactic response is driven by a self-generated oxygen gradient induced by collective respiration. Our diffusion-advection model of bacteria and oxygen, accounting for aerotactic migration, hydrodynamic attraction to the walls, and respiration, quantitatively reproduces our experimental observations and provides valuable insights into bacterial self-organization within complex environments.

*Eamon Dwight,D. Candela*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过数值模拟发现，软摩擦颗粒的无热随机堆积体能够存储任意波形，并在后续解压时以时间反转顺序回忆该波形，这一效应依赖于颗粒间的摩擦作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无热随机介质在压缩过程中形成内部接触时的波形记忆能力，探索这类系统作为信息存储介质的潜在应用。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，研究软摩擦颗粒（soft frictional grains）在缓慢压缩过程中对施加的小幅时变剪切波形的存储机制，分析摩擦模型的影响。

Result: 104个颗粒的堆积体能够以100%准确率回忆128种不同波形，对512种波形的分类准确率超过90%；该效应依赖于颗粒间摩擦，但与摩擦模型的某些细节无关。

Conclusion: 波形记忆效应可能存在于其他形成内部接触的无热随机介质中，如皱褶薄片（crumpled sheets）和巢状纤维组件（nest-like fiber assemblies）。

Abstract: Using numerical simulations it is shown that a random, athermal pack of soft frictional grains will store an arbitrary waveform that is applied as a small time-dependent shear while the system is slowly compressed. When the system is decompressed at a later time, an approximation of the input waveform is recalled in time-reversed order as shear stresses on the system boundaries. It is shown that this effect depends on friction between the grains, and is independent of some aspects of the friction model. By systematically increasing the complexity of the stored waveform, it is found that a pack of $10^4$ grains can recall any one of 128 different waveforms with 100% classification accuracy and 512 different waveforms with over 90% classification accuracy, as measured by a neural net trained only on the inputs. This type of waveform memory might be observable in other types of athermal random media that form internal contacts when compressed such as crumpled sheets and nest-like fiber assemblies.

</details>


### [42] [Dissipative self-assembly of colloidal suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14637)
*Jason Conradt,Eric M. Furst*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 顺磁胶体悬浮液在强磁场中表现出动力学阻滞（kinetic arrest）。通过周期性开关磁场的耗散过程，悬浮液自组装形成致密且动态的稳态相。基于畴伸长、α-和轮廓形状以及相分离程度，通过k-means聚类分析构建相图，识别出六种特征结构区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究顺磁胶体（paramagnetic colloids）悬浮液在强磁场中的动力学阻滞现象，探索通过周期性开关磁场这一耗散过程诱导自组装形成稳态相的行为。

Method: 采用k-means聚类分析（k-means clustering analysis）构建相图，基于畴伸长、α-形状、轮廓形状和相分离程度等参数。同时使用平衡平均场磁静能计算（equilibrium mean-field magnetostatic energy calculation）对自组装畴形状进行建模。

Result: 识别出六种特征结构区域：无结构相、阻滞结构、片状结构、带状结构、尖峰相和瞬态流体-流体区域。进一步报告了畴的分布和排列，以及结果的普适性。磁静能计算预测了由样品限制驱动的高度各向异性结构的意外出现。

Conclusion: 通过周期性开关磁场的耗散过程，顺磁胶体悬浮液能够自组装形成多种稳态相结构。平衡平均场磁静能计算成功解释了自组装畴形状，并预测了由样品限制驱动的高度各向异性结构的形成。

Abstract: Suspensions of paramagnetic colloids exhibit kinetic arrest in strong magnetic fields. Through a dissipative process of toggling the field on and off, suspensions self-assemble into dense and dynamic steady-state phases. Based on the domain elongation, alpha- and contour-shapes, and degree of phase separation, we construct a phase diagram using a k-means clustering analysis. We identify six characteristic structural regimes: a structureless phase, an arrested structure, sheets, ribbons, a spiky phase, and a transient fluid-fluid regime. We further report the distribution and alignment of domains and the generality of the results. We model self-assembled domain shapes using an equilibrium mean-field magnetostatic energy calculation, which predicts the surprising emergence of highly-anisotropic structures driven by the sample's confinement.

### [43] [Molecular Origin of UV-Induced Irreversible Phase Changes in a Chromonic Liquid Crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14725)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究（Nastishin et al., 2018）发现UV照射能改变DSCG（disodium cromoglycate）的相图，使向列相转变为向列-各向同性双相态，但该现象的分子起源尚不明确。本研究旨在阐明这种相图偏移的分子机制。

Method: 采用液相色谱-质谱联用技术（liquid chromatography-mass spectrometry）鉴定DSCG的UV诱导光降解产物。结合原位X射线散射（in situ X-ray scattering）和偏光光学显微镜（polarized optical microscopy）的综合方法，分析降解产物对DSCG自组装的影响。

Result: 研究确定了DSCG在UV照射下产生的特定光降解产物。这些降解产物破坏了DSCG聚集体的自组装，导致相图中各向同性区和双相区扩大，从而解释了先前观察到的相图变化现象。

Conclusion: 色氨酸液晶（chromonic liquid crystals）的自组装及其相行为对微小的化学变化高度敏感。这一发现为光控软物质自组装提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: Aqueous solutions of disodium cromoglycate (DSCG), a representative model system for chromonic liquid crystals, exhibit temperature- and concentration-dependent phase behaviors spanning isotropic, nematic, and columnar phases, as well as their coexistence regions. Nastishin et al. (2018) reported that UV irradiation can alter the phase diagram, transforming a nematic phase into a nematic-isotropic biphasic state due to weakened molecular attractions, accompanied by a slow post-irradiation relaxation. Here, we revisit this phenomenon and elucidate the molecular origin of this phase diagram shift: the UV-induced photodegradation of DSCG into specific photodegradation products, which we identify using liquid chromatography-mass spectrometry. Through an integrated approach combining in situ X-ray scattering and polarized optical microscopy, we demonstrate that these degradation products disrupt the self-assembly of DSCG aggregates, thereby expanding the isotropic and biphasic regions in the phase diagram. These findings demonstrate that chromonic assemblies and their phase behaviors are highly sensitive to minor chemical alterations, providing a potential route toward light-controlled self assembly of soft matter.

### [44] [Cage Breaking Far from Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14973)
*Jared Popowski,Nico Schramma,Edan Lerner,Maziyar Jalaal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过三圆盘受限主动物质模型，揭示了活性如何微观重塑笼状环境：低活性时熵景观呈双稳态，高活性时边界出现受挫团簇的亚稳态，当持续长度匹配粒子半径时笼打破最快，二维扩展显示概率流循环并破坏细致平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主动物质（active matter）在被动物质会堵塞和减速的条件下仍能流动和屈服，因为自推进（self-propulsion）显著调节了粒子从局部笼状结构（cages）的逃逸。然而，活性如何微观重塑笼状环境以产生这种效应仍不清楚。

Method: 研究采用一个最小主动物质模型：三个可区分的自推进圆盘（self-propelling disks）在圆形约束（circular confinement）下。该简单设置允许构建重排的熵景观（entropic landscape）并与平衡对应物精确比较。

Result: 低活性时景观有效呈现双稳态（bistable），高活性时在边界出现与受挫团簇（frustrated clusters）相关的额外亚稳态盆地（metastable basins）。笼打破在持续长度（persistence length）匹配粒子半径时最快，将几何微观尺度与活性玻璃（active glasses）的增强动力学联系起来。二维扩展显示循环概率电流（circulating probability currents），马尔可夫态描述表明细致平衡（detailed balance）在连续景观动力学和粗粒度熵盆地间跃迁中均被破坏。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解活性如何重塑致密非平衡物质（dense nonequilibrium matter）中的笼状约束、弛豫和不可逆性提供了最小微观框架。

Abstract: Active matter can flow and yield under conditions where passive matter jams and slows down, as self-propulsion significantly modulates particle escape from local cages. How activity microscopically reshapes the caging environment to produce this effect, however, remains poorly understood. Here we study a minimal active-matter model of cage breaking: three distinguishable self-propelling disks under circular confinement. This simple setting allows us to construct an entropic landscape for rearrangements and to compare it exactly with its equilibrium counterpart. At low activity the landscape is effectively bistable, whereas at high activity it develops additional metastable basins associated with frustrated clusters at the boundary. We quantify the system's departure from equilibrium and show that cage breaking is fastest when the persistence length matches the particle radius, linking a geometric microscopic scale to the enhanced dynamics of active glasses. Extending the landscape to two dimensions reveals circulating probability currents, and a Markov-state description shows that detailed balance is broken both in the continuous landscape dynamics and in the coarse-grained transitions between entropic basins. Our results provide a minimal microscopic framework for understanding how activity reshapes caging, relaxation, and irreversibility in dense nonequilibrium matter.

### [45] [Polarization Plasticity of Ferroelectric Nematics: a case of Electrostatic Frustration in Simple Planar Electrode Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15012)
*Stefano Marni,Federico Caimi,Luca Casiraghi,Jordan Hobbs,Calum J. Gibb,Richard Mandle,Giovanni Nava,Tommaso Bellini*

TL;DR: 铁电向列相液晶在平行金属电极限制下，当外加电压低于饱和阈值时，系统进入极化可塑性区域，表现为反极性管状畴结构，其中极化保持平衡值但方向交替排列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电向列相液晶（ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals）因其自发的体极化特性，在表面耦合或限制条件下容易产生束缚电荷积累与极性有序不相容的挫败状态。这种状态在简单的平行未涂层金属电极结构中尤为明显。

Method: 研究采用平行未涂层金属电极结构，测量极化电荷与外加电压的关系。通过分析电压低于饱和阈值时的系统行为，建立了包含反极性管状畴（antipolar tubular domains）和纯极化反转壁（pure polarization-reversal walls）的理论模型。

Result: 当外加电压ΔV低于饱和阈值Vsat时，电极上积累的极化电荷与外加电压成正比，且Vsat与电池厚度无关。在此区域，系统进入极化可塑性区域（polarization plasticity），向列相有序性保持，指向矢垂直于电极，但极化减小以抵消内部电场。

Conclusion: 观察结果与系统分裂为从电极到电极延伸的介观尺度反极性管状畴模型一致，其中极化保持其无约束平衡值，由纯极化反转壁分隔。在此区域，束缚电荷反转的动力学变得与外加电压ΔV无关。

Abstract: Because of their spontaneous bulk polarization, ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals can be easily brought by surface coupling or confinement in a state in which the accumulation of bound charges becomes incompatible with polar order, creating frustration. This condition also occurs in the simplest cells with parallel uncoated metal electrodes where we find that the polarization charge accumulating on the electrodes is proportional to the applied voltage for $ΔV< V_{sat}$, a threshold value independent of cell thickness. We show that below $V_{sat}$, frustration drives the system into a regime of polarization plasticity, in which nematic ordering is preserved and the nematic director remains perpendicular to the electrodes, while instead the polarization is reduced to cancel the internal electric field. In this regime, the kinetics of bound charge reversal becomes independent from $ΔV$. The observations are consistent with a model in which the system splits into antipolar tubular domains of mesoscale diameter extending from electrode to electrode, in which the polarization retains its unconstrained equilibrium value, separated by pure polarization-reversal walls.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cells are defined by lipid membranes that differ in their structure across the tree of life. While the membranes of most bacteria and eukaryotes consist of single-headed bilayer lipids, the membranes of archaea are composed of mixtures of single-headed bilayer lipids and double-headed bolalipids. Archaeal bolalipids can adopt straight or u-shaped conformations, enabling them - together with bilayer lipids - to control whether membranes form bilayer or monolayer structures. Yet, the physical principles governing archaeal membranes remain largely unexplored, especially how membrane structure couples to externally imposed curvature during membrane remodeling. Here, we perform coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations of toroidal vesicles to systematically probe the effects of all relevant combinations of mean and Gaussian curvatures on shape stability and lipid organization. We find that soft bilayer membranes can sustain all curvatures induced, whereas rigid bolalipid monolayer membranes either transition to different vesicle shapes or rupture. Bilayer-mimicking u-shaped bolalipids and bilayer lipids are spatially accumulated in regions of high mean membrane curvature independent of Gaussian curvature. Our work identifies curvature-composition coupling as a physical signature of archaeal membrane remodeling.
