### [47] [A mechanical bifurcation constrains the evolution of cell sheet folding in the family Volvocaceae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15171)
*Valens Tribet,Pierre A. Haas*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了绿藻家族Volvocaceae中形态发生（morphogenesis）的机械分岔（mechanical bifurcation）如何约束其进化路径。研究发现，Pleodorina californica（64个细胞）的简单细胞楔形波（wave of cell wedging）驱动翻转（inversion），而Volvox（400-50000个细胞）需要更复杂的细胞形状变化程序。中间细胞数（256个）物种的缺失与机械分岔导致的翻转限制相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索机械不稳定性（mechanical instabilities）是否能够驱动或约束发育过程中形态发生的进化。具体关注Volvocaceae家族绿藻的胚胎细胞片翻转过程，试图解释为何缺乏中间细胞数（256个）的物种，以及不同物种采用不同翻转策略的进化原因。

Method: 基于Pleodorina californica（64个细胞）的翻转过程，建立了连续介质模型（continuum model），将驱动翻转的细胞形状变化建模为弹性表面内在曲率（intrinsic curvature）的变化。使用异速生长观察（allometric observations）和Volvocaceae细胞分裂模型，将参数外推至256个或更多细胞的情况。

Result: 模型中的机械分岔预测翻转仅在参数空间的子集中可能实现。P. californica的参数落入该可能子集，但外推至256个或更多细胞的参数则不在其中。这解释了为何缺乏中间细胞数的物种，并表明Volvox更复杂的翻转策略是规避此分岔的进化必然。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，Volvox的复杂翻转策略是为了规避机械分岔而产生的进化必要性。这更广泛地揭示了机械分岔如何能够驱动形态发生的进化，为理解发育过程中形状形成的进化约束提供了机械学基础。

Abstract: The processes of morphogenesis that give rise to the shapes of organs and organisms during development are often driven by mechanical instabilities. Can such mechanical bifurcations also drive or constrain the evolution of these processes in the first place? We discover an instance of these constraints in the green algae of the family Volvocaceae. During their development, their bowl-shaped embryonic cell sheet turns itself inside out. This inversion is driven by a simple wave of cell wedging in the genus Pleodorina (16-128 cells) and more complex programmes of cell shape changes in Volvox (~400-50000 cells). However, no species with intermediate cell numbers (256 cells) have been described. Here, we relate this gap to a mechanical bifurcation: Focusing on the inversion of Pleodorina californica (64 cells), we develop a continuum model, in which the cell shape changes driving inversion appear as changes of the intrinsic curvature of an elastic surface. A mechanical bifurcation in this model predicts that inversion is only possible in a subset of its parameter space. Strikingly, parameters estimated for P. californica fall into this possible subset, but those that we extrapolate to 256 or more cells using allometric observations and a model of cell cleavage in Volvocaceae do not. Our work thus suggests that the more complex inversion strategies of Volvox are an evolutionary necessity to obviate this bifurcation and indicates more broadly how mechanical bifurcations can drive the evolution of morphogenesis.

### [48] [Topological localisation and motility of active knots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15591)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡活性聚合物为研究DNA和染色质等生物聚合物在分子马达作用下的行为提供了最小化框架。研究旨在探究受控拓扑结构的活性环状聚合物中，结类型如何定性决定其非平衡行为。

Method: 研究分析了具有不同拓扑结构的活性环状聚合物，特别关注了环面结（torus knots）和扭转结（twist knots）两类拓扑家族。通过考察其切线场（tangent fields）的对称性质，研究了活性力沿链的排列方式。

Result: 研究发现活性诱导了不同拓扑家族的相反局域化响应：环面结系统性地去局域化并膨胀，而扭转结则收紧并保持局域化。活性环面结表现为软手性自推进粒子，表现出由拓扑手性固定的明确手性持续性运动；而无手性结则无净手性。

Conclusion: 结作为可变形拓扑准粒子（deformable topological quasiparticle），其形态和推进方式由拓扑结构选择。这些结果为设计具有可控形态和涌现运动模式的可编程软手性粒子（programmable soft chiral particles）提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: Nonequilibrium active polymers provide a minimal framework to investigate biopolymers such as DNA and chromatin under the action of molecular motors. Here we study active ring polymers with controlled topology and show that knot type qualitatively determines their nonequilibrium behaviour. We find that activity induces opposite localisation responses in different topological families: torus knots systematically delocalise and inflate, whereas twist knots tighten and remain localised. We trace this divergent behaviour to the distinct symmetry properties of their tangent fields, which control the alignment of active forces along the chain. We show that topology also governs internal and emergent dynamics. Active torus knots behave as soft chiral self-propelled particles exhibiting persistent motion with a well-defined handedness fixed by their topological chirality. In contrast, achiral knots show no net handedness. The knot thus acts as a deformable topological quasiparticle whose morphology and propulsion are selected by topology. These results suggest potential routes toward programmable soft chiral particles with controllable morphology and emergent motility modes.

### [49] [Nonequilibrium energetics of sensing and actuation by a smart active particle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15602)
*Luca Cocconi,Benoît Mahault,Lorenzo Piro*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个自导向粒子（self-steering particle）的最小模型，将稳态熵产率分解为运动、驱动和感知成本，揭示了即使是最简单的具身导航（embodied navigation）也存在的能量簿记结构，并发现了连接能量消耗与定位精度和路径跟随性能的帕累托前沿（Pareto fronts）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能主动代理（smart active agents）必须在不同功能间分配有限的能量资源，但基础的热力学权衡（thermodynamic trade-offs）仍未被充分理解。研究旨在揭示即使是最简单的具身导航（embodied navigation）也存在的能量簿记结构。

Method: 引入了一个具有内部极性线索传感器（internal polarity-cue sensor）的自导向粒子（self-steering particle）最小模型，该传感器与外部环境场耦合。将稳态熵产率（steady-state entropy production rate）分解为运动（locomotion）、驱动（actuation）和感知（sensing）成本。

Result: 发现了连接能量消耗与定位精度（localisation precision）和路径跟随性能（path-following performance）的帕累托前沿（Pareto fronts）。这表明反馈控制的主动运动（feedback-controlled active motion）受到定量热力学边界（quantitative thermodynamic bounds）的约束，这些边界在不同任务几何结构中持续存在。

Conclusion: 该分离揭示了即使是最简单的具身导航（embodied navigation）也存在的能量簿记结构。反馈控制的主动运动（feedback-controlled active motion）受到定量热力学边界（quantitative thermodynamic bounds）的约束，这些边界在不同任务几何结构中持续存在。

Abstract: Smart active agents must allocate finite energetic resources across distinct functions, yet the underlying thermodynamic trade-offs remain poorly understood. Here, we introduce a minimal model of a self-steering particle with an internal polarity-cue sensor coupled to an external environmental field, decomposing its steady-state entropy production rate into locomotion, actuation, and sensing costs. This separation exposes an energetic bookkeeping structure underlying even the simplest form of embodied navigation. The emergence of Pareto fronts linking energetic expenditure to localisation precision and path-following performance shows that feedback-controlled active motion is constrained by quantitative thermodynamic bounds that persist across distinct task geometries.

</details>

### [50] [Projected Sensitivity of Paleo-Detectors to Dark Matter Effective Interactions with Nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13629)
*Dionysios P. Theodosopoulos,Katherine Freese,Chris Kelso,Patrick Stengel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了古探测器（paleo-detectors）对暗物质（dark matter）探测的理论预测，基于非相对论有效场论（NREFT）框架，评估了其对弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）与原子核相互作用的灵敏度，并与传统实验进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 古探测器通过读取天然矿物中暗物质诱导的核反冲径迹来直接探测暗物质，利用地质时间尺度上的暴露替代传统实验所需的大质量探测器。研究旨在扩展先前对标准自旋无关相干散射和自旋相关散射的理论预测。

Method: 在非相对论有效场论（Non-Relativistic Effective Field Theory, NREFT）框架下，考虑同位旋标量（isoscalar）耦合到核子的弹性散射和非弹性散射，评估古探测器的灵敏度。考虑了宇宙成因、天体物理和放射性本底，并研究了代表性读出方案和多种目标矿物。

Result: 对于1 GeV-10 GeV的暗物质质量，古探测器对所有NREFT算符的WIMP-核相互作用的灵敏度均优于传统实验，且基本独立于读出方案或目标矿物。对于10 GeV-5 TeV的质量范围，古探测器对多个NREFT算符的灵敏度与传统实验相当或更好，具体取决于读出方案和目标矿物。

Conclusion: 古探测器在宽质量范围内对暗物质探测具有显著优势，特别是在低质量区域（1-10 GeV）对所有NREFT算符都表现出优越灵敏度，为暗物质直接探测提供了有前景的新技术途径。

Abstract: Paleo-detectors are a proposed experimental technique for direct detection (DD) of dark matter (DM) via the read-out of DM-induced nuclear recoil tracks in natural minerals. The large detector mass required for the sensitivity of conventional DD experiments to rare events is replaced by the exposure of paleo-detectors to DM-induced nuclear recoils over geological timescales. In this paper, we extend previous theoretical predictions for canonical spin-independent coherent and spin-dependent scattering (proportional to $A^2$ and the spin of the nucleus, respectively). We estimate the sensitivity of paleo-detectors to interactions between weakly interacting massive particle (WIMP) DM and nuclei within the framework of a Non-Relativistic Effective Field Theory (NREFT), considering isoscalar couplings to nucleons for both elastic and inelastic scattering. Taking into account cosmogenic, astrophysical and radiogenic backgrounds, we project the 90% confidence-level (CL) upper limits on the isoscalar NREFT coupling constants for both scattering types. We consider representative read-out scenarios and examine several target minerals. The projected sensitivities of paleo-detectors are compared with the 90% CL limits from the XENON100, LUX-ZEPLIN, and PandaX-II experiments, as well as with the 95% Bayesian credible region of the 2D marginalized posterior distribution from SuperCDMS. For DM masses from 1 GeV-10 GeV, paleo-detectors are projected to have sensitivity superior to that of conventional experiments for WIMP-nucleus interactions via all NREFT operators, largely independent of read-out scenario or target mineral. For DM masses from 10 GeV-5 TeV, we find that the sensitivity of paleo-detectors is projected to be comparable to or better than that of conventional experiments for WIMP-nucleus interactions via several NREFT operators, depending on the read-out scenario and target mineral.

</details>


### [51] [Searching for Unparticles with the Cosmic Microwave Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13486)
*Oliver H. E. Philcox,Guilherme L. Pimentel,Chen Yang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究暴胀（inflation）的"非粒子（unparticle）"模型，其中暴胀子与强耦合共形场论（conformal field theory）弱混合。通过开发神经网络因子化方案和最优CMB估计器，将161个不可分离模板压缩为7个可因子化形式，并应用于Planck数据，未发现新物理证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多场暴胀模型通常假设粒子间相互作用可微扰处理，而强耦合模型提供了有趣替代方案，可能产生新颖的暴胀现象学。非粒子场景中暴胀子与强耦合共形场论弱混合，可能产生独特的非高斯特征。

Method: 开发了一套工具库，包括神经网络因子化方案（neural-network factorization schemes）和最优宇宙微波背景（Cosmic Microwave Background, CMB）估计器。该流程将161个不可分离模板压缩为仅7个可因子化形式，信噪比损失可忽略。将模型应用于Planck数据进行分析。

Result: 在1≤Δ≤9范围内，发现最大信噪比为1.2σ，表明无新物理证据。首次对满足修正一致性条件的正交双谱（orthogonal bispectrum）给出CMB约束：f_NL^orth* = -12±12。虽然许多非粒子模型与单场形状简并，但接近半整数的Δ值具有非常不同的形状。

Conclusion: 非粒子模型在接近半整数的共形标度维度（conformal scaling dimension）Δ值时表现出独特形状，为未来发现提供了有趣通道。开发的方法可直接应用于其他类型模板，激励探索超越标准弱耦合范式（weakly-coupled paradigm）的模型。

Abstract: Multi-field models of inflation typically assume that interactions between particles can be treated perturbatively. Strongly-coupled models provide an intriguing alternative and may offer novel inflationary phenomenology. We study the "unparticle" scenario, where the inflaton is weakly mixed with a strongly-coupled sector, specified by a (gapless) conformal field theory. For certain choices of conformal scaling dimension, $Δ$, the exchange of unparticles leads to distinctive non-Gaussian features in the primordial curvature distribution, including bispectra with enhanced squeezed limits and oscillations close to the equilateral regime. Efficiently analyzing these models using Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data is a challenge since the shapes are non-factorizable in momenta and often highly degenerate with single-field self-interactions. Here, we overcome these limitations using a library of tools, including neural-network factorization schemes and optimal CMB estimators. Our pipeline condenses 161 non-separable templates into just 7 factorizable forms, with negligible loss of signal-to-noise. We apply the model to the \textit{Planck} data, asking two key questions: (1) can we detect unparticles? (2) can we distinguish them from single-field self-interactions? Across $1\leq Δ\leq 9$, we find a maximal signal-to-noise of $1.2σ$, implying no evidence for new physics. We also place the first CMB constraints on the modified consistency-condition-satisfying orthogonal bispectrum with $f^{\rm orth^*}_{\rm NL} = -12\pm12$. While many unparticle models are degenerate with single-field shapes, values of $Δ$ close to half-integers have very different shapes, offering an intriguing future discovery channel. The methods developed herein can be directly applied to other classes of templates, motivating the exploration of models beyond the standard weakly-coupled paradigm.

</details>


### [52] [Smoking-gun signatures of bounce cosmology from echoes of relic gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13924)
*Mian Zhu,Yi-Fu Cai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文报告了非奇异反弹宇宙学中遗迹引力波（gravitational waves）的新特征：由于收缩相的存在，有效势产生双峰结构，导致引力波谱在高频区出现独特的振荡模式，类似于量子力学中的共振隧穿效应（resonant tunneling effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非奇异反弹宇宙学（non-singular bounce cosmologies）中遗迹引力波的独特特征，为实验检验这类早期宇宙模型提供新途径。与暴胀（inflation）等其他宇宙学情景相比，反弹宇宙学中的收缩相会产生可观测的引力波特征。

Method: 分析非奇异反弹宇宙学中控制原初引力波演化的有效势 $M_p^2 a^{\prime \prime}/a$，该势在标准膨胀相之前的收缩相中形成双峰结构。研究双峰间的引力波干涉效应，类比量子力学中的共振隧穿效应。

Result: 发现遗迹引力波谱在高频区呈现独特的振荡模式，这是非奇异反弹宇宙学区别于暴胀等其他宇宙学情景的特征性信号。计算表明该引力波谱的振幅足够高，能够达到当前和未来引力波探测器的灵敏度范围。

Conclusion: 非奇异反弹宇宙学中的遗迹引力波振荡特征为实验检验这类早期宇宙模型提供了有前景的方法，使相关预测具有可证伪性，为探索早期宇宙新物理开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We report a novel feature of relic gravitational waves (GWs) in non-singular bounce cosmologies that is testable in light of GWs astronomy. In non-singular bounce cosmologies, the effective potential $M_p^2 a^{\prime \prime}/a$ that governs the evolution of primordial GWs contains two peaks due to the existence of contraction phase prior to the standard expansion phase. Accordingly, relic GWs interference between the two peaks, resulting in a distinctive oscillatory feature in the spectrum, analog to the resonant tunneling effect in quantum mechanics. As a result, the GWs spectrum exhibits an oscillatory patterns on high frequecy regime, distinctive to other cosmological scenarios such as inflation. We show that the amplitude of GWs spectrum is high enough to reach the sensitivity of current and forthcoming GWs instruments, making our predictions falsifiable. Hence, our finding offers a promising way to experimentally test the non-singular bounce scenarios and search for new physics in early universe cosmologies.

</details>


### [53] [Inflation without an Inflaton III: non-Gaussian signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15036)
*Mariam Abdelaziz,Marisol Traforetti,Daniele Bertacca,Raul Jimenez,Sabino Matarrese,Angelo Ricciardone*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究分析了"无暴胀子的暴胀"框架中的原初非高斯性，发现标量扰动由原初引力波在二阶产生，导致非高斯性是该机制的内在预测，但其幅度在CMB尺度上可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索"无暴胀子的暴胀"框架中原初非高斯性的特性，该框架中标量扰动由原初引力波在二阶产生，非高斯性是该机制的内在预测，需要系统分析其统计特性。

Method: 研究方法包括计算相应的标量双谱，推导标量势三点的相关贡献，并在精确德西特背景上对爱因斯坦引力中的原初引力波进行数值评估。

Result: 研究发现双谱与标量功率谱存在结构差异，双谱对数依赖于暴胀结束设定的紫外截断，形状在压缩构型中增强，但幅度在标量功率谱归一化到观测值后强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 结论表明该机制在CMB尺度产生的非高斯性可忽略不计，远低于当前观测灵敏度，这为"无暴胀子的暴胀"框架提供了重要的理论约束。

Abstract: We investigate primordial non-Gaussianity in the Inflation without an Inflaton (IWI) framework, where scalar perturbations are generated at second order by primordial gravitational waves in Einstein gravity on an exact de Sitter (dS) background. Since scalar modes are produced nonlinearly from tensor modes, non-Gaussianity is an intrinsic prediction of the mechanism. We compute the corresponding scalar bispectrum, derive the relevant contribution to the three-point function of the scalar potential, and evaluate its shape numerically. We find that, unlike the scalar power spectrum, the bispectrum depends logarithmically on the ultraviolet cutoff set by the end of inflation, indicating a structural difference between the two- and three-point statistics in this scenario. Its shape is enhanced toward squeezed configurations, but its amplitude becomes strongly suppressed once the scalar power spectrum is normalized to the observed value. The resulting non-Gaussianity at CMB scales is therefore negligibly small, well below present observational sensitivity.

</details>


### [54] [Cosmological peculiar velocities in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14511)
*Chris Clarkson,Roy Maartens*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文重新审视了协变扰动理论中星系本动速度的晚期演化，驳斥了协变方法预测比标准方法更强本动速度增长的观点，证明两种方法在一致应用时给出相同结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期有研究声称1+3协变方法（1+3 covariant approach）预测的本动速度（peculiar velocities）增长显著强于标准度规扰动理论，理由是协变处理是完全相对论性的而标准处理本质上是牛顿式的。本文旨在澄清这一误解。

Method: 采用1+3协变扰动理论（1+3 covariant perturbation theory）重新分析星系本动速度的晚期演化，通过一致处理耦合的协变方程组，并与标准度规扰动理论结果进行比较。

Result: 当协变方程被一致应用时，1+3方法精确复现了标准扰动理论关于本动速度增长的结果。近期研究中声称的更强增长规律源于对耦合协变系统的不一致处理，即将场方程约束的项当作独立源处理。

Conclusion: 标准本动速度处理方法是正确且完全相对论性的，不会导致异常的大尺度流动（bulk flows）或表观加速膨胀（apparent accelerated expansion）。关于协变方法预测更强本动速度增长及可模拟尘埃宇宙中加速膨胀的主张存在概念混淆。

Abstract: We reconsider the late-time evolution of galaxy peculiar velocities in the 1+3 covariant approach to cosmological perturbation theory. It has recently been claimed that this approach predicts substantially stronger growth of peculiar velocities than standard metric-based perturbation theory -- on the grounds that the covariant treatment is fully relativistic whereas standard treatments are effectively Newtonian. We show that this is not the case. When the covariant equations are applied consistently, the $1+3$ approach reproduces exactly the standard perturbative result for peculiar-velocity growth. The stronger growth laws claimed in recent work arise from an inconsistent treatment of the coupled covariant system, in which terms constrained by the field equations are treated as if they were independent sources. Further claims are made that the stronger bulk flows can mimic accelerated expansion in a dust universe. We argue that these claims rest on a confusion between the kinematics of an arbitrarily chosen observer congruence and the physical expansion of the matter congruence traced by galaxies. We conclude that the standard treatment of peculiar velocities is correct and fully relativistic~-- and does not lead to anomalous bulk flows or to apparent accelerated expansion.

</details>

*Nandan Roy,Prasanta Sahoo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: CosmoDS是一个在Cobaya框架内用于宇宙学模型背景水平研究的工具包，通过动力系统分析（dynamical system analysis）来研究非线性系统，特别关注暗能量模型的稳定性和演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动力系统分析是研究非线性系统的强大数学方法，在宇宙学中被广泛用于研究不同宇宙学模型的稳定性和演化，特别是涉及暗能量的模型。该工具包旨在为宇宙学模型约束提供一个动力系统分析框架。

Method: CosmoDS工具包在Cobaya框架内实现，提供基于动力系统公式的宇宙学模型约束框架。该工具包直接与Cobaya接口集成，允许用户利用Cobaya中已实现的复杂统计和推断工具进行宇宙学参数估计和模型分析。

Result: 开发了一个专门用于宇宙学背景水平研究的工具包，实现了动力系统分析与Cobaya框架的直接集成，为宇宙学模型分析提供了新的计算框架。

Conclusion: CosmoDS工具包通过将动力系统分析与Cobaya的统计推断能力相结合，为宇宙学模型研究提供了一个强大的集成分析平台，特别适用于暗能量模型的稳定性和演化研究。

Abstract: We present a toolkit, CosmoDS, designed to study cosmological models at the background level using dynamical system analysis within the Cobaya framework. Dynamical system analysis is a powerful mathematical approach for studying nonlinear systems and is widely used in cosmology to investigate the stability and evolution of different cosmological models, particularly those involving dark energy. In this code, we provide a framework for constraining cosmological models using a dynamical system formulation. Most importantly, the toolkit is directly integrated with the Cobaya interface, allowing users to take advantage of the sophisticated statistical and inference tools already implemented in Cobaya for cosmological parameter estimation and model analysis.

### [56] [Luminosity-Temperature Relation as a Probe for Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15077)
*Antonino Del Popolo,Saeed Fakhry,David F. Mota*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究通过改进的半解析框架，利用星系团的光度-温度（L-T）关系作为诊断工具，测试修正引力（MG）理论，发现低质量系统在MG模型中表现出更陡的L-T斜率，且这些特征无法被传统天体物理过程模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于利用星系团的光度-温度（luminosity-temperature, L-T）关系作为探针，测试修正引力（modified gravity, MG）理论，特别是f(R)引力和对称子（symmetron）模型，以区分广义相对论与屏蔽修正引力理论。

Method: 采用改进的半解析框架，整合了角动量获取（angular momentum acquisition）、动力学摩擦（dynamical friction）和激波加热（shock heating）过程，基于修正的间断平衡模型（modified punctuated equilibrium model），并将预测结果与流体动力学模拟和观测数据进行对比。

Result: 研究发现大质量星系团基本保持屏蔽状态，遵循标准ΛCDM预测，而低质量系统（kT ≲ 1-2 keV）在MG情景中表现出系统性偏离，呈现更陡的L-T斜率。这些特征无法被反馈或角动量效应等传统天体物理过程模拟，后者主要影响归一化而非曲率。

Conclusion: L-T关系可作为区分广义相对论与屏蔽修正引力理论的稳健诊断工具，在星系群尺度上具有最强的区分能力。归一化约化χ²分析显示，MG模型与观测数据的吻合度显著优于ΛCDM模型，多个实现获得极佳拟合，而ΛCDM模型表现最差。

Abstract: We investigate the luminosity-temperature ($L$-$T$) relation of galaxy clusters as a probe for testing modified gravity (MG) theories, focusing on $f(R)$ gravity and symmetron models. Using an improved semi-analytic framework that incorporates angular momentum acquisition, dynamical friction, and shock heating within the modified punctuated equilibrium model, we compare predictions against hydrodynamical simulations and observational data. While massive clusters remain largely screened and follow standard $Λ$CDM predictions, low-mass systems ($kT \lesssim 1-2$ keV) exhibit systematic deviations characterized by steeper $L$-$T$ slopes in MG scenarios. Crucially, we demonstrate that these signatures cannot be mimicked by conventional astrophysical processes such as feedback or angular momentum effects, which primarily affect normalization rather than curvature. Our results establish the $L$-$T$ relation as a robust diagnostic tool for distinguishing general relativity from screened MG theories, with the strongest discriminatory power emerging at group scales accessible to current and future X-ray surveys. Moreover, a normalized reduced $χ^2$ analysis of the $L$-$T$ relation shows that MG models provide significantly better agreement with observational data than $Λ$CDM, with several realizations achieving excellent fits while the $Λ$CDM model consistently performs worst.

</details>


### [57] [When One-Parameter Dark Energy Makes Neutrinos Physical Again](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15422)
*Weiqiang Yang,Eleonora Di Valentino,Eric V. Linder,Sibo Zhang,Supriya Pan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 研究发现，在特定单参数暗能量状态方程下，中微子质量后验分布可恢复正值，表明数据指向暗能量的物理特性而非广泛简并性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前ΛCDM宇宙学数据暗示中微子质量和为负值，这存在理论矛盾。研究旨在探索是否必须采用双参数暗能量状态方程才能使中微子质量恢复正值。

Method: 研究系统考察了多种具有特定物理特性的单参数暗能量状态方程，分析它们对中微子质量后验分布的影响，并与双参数模型进行对比。

Result: 某些单参数暗能量状态方程足以使中微子质量后验恢复正值，表明数据指向特定物理特性而非参数简并。所需特性为高红移处的幻影暗能量（phantom dark energy）并在低红移处穿越w=-1。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，中微子质量负值问题可通过特定物理特性的单参数暗能量模型解决，无需引入更复杂的双参数模型，这为理解暗能量本质提供了新视角。

Abstract: A puzzling implication of current data interpreted in the $Λ$CDM cosmology is the preference for a negative sum of neutrino masses. Moving to $w_0w_a$CDM brings an appreciable fraction of the neutrino mass posterior back to positive values, while the constant equation-of-state dark energy case $w$CDM does not. We investigate a variety of one-parameter dark energy equations of state (DE EoS), each variation with particular physical properties, to understand whether a two-parameter DE EoS is required to bring the neutrino mass positive. The conclusion is that certain one-parameter DE EoS can suffice, implying that the data are pointing toward physical characteristics rather than a broad degeneracy. The required characteristics are identified as phantom dark energy at high redshift, crossing $w=-1$ at lower redshift.

### [58] [Probing Gravitational-Wave Four-Point Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15514)
*Martina Ciprini,Maria Lucia Marcelli,Gianmassimo Tasinato*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了原初随机引力波背景（SGWBs）的非高斯特征，重点关注由矢量涨落二阶产生的引力波四阶关联函数（trispectrum），并分析了其观测意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机引力波背景（SGWBs）为早期宇宙物理和暗区动力学提供了重要探针。大多数研究集中于功率谱，但高阶关联函数中编码了信号的统计特性信息，特别是非高斯特征能帮助区分宇宙学与天体物理起源。

Method: 研究在矢量涨落二阶产生宇宙学随机引力波背景的框架下，开发了表征高阶引力波关联函数的工具，计算了代表性的四阶关联函数，这些函数对引力波三谱（trispectrum）产生连通贡献。

Result: 研究发现三谱振幅与引力波功率谱的平方成正比，并在特征折叠动量构型（folded momentum configurations）中达到峰值，反映了非线性源的结构。连通三谱对两点重叠缩减函数（overlap reduction functions）的方差有贡献，包括脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays）相关的Hellings-Downs曲线。

Conclusion: 非高斯随机引力波背景统计量为探测引力波背景起源提供了互补可观测量，有助于区分宇宙学与天体物理源。研究还构建了地基干涉仪测量连通三谱的最优估计器。

Abstract: Stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds (SGWBs) of primordial origin offer a powerful probe of early-Universe physics and possible dark-sector dynamics. While most searches focus on the GW power spectrum, additional information is encoded in higher-order correlators that characterize the statistical properties of the signal. In this work we study non-Gaussian features of a cosmological SGWB generated at second order by vector fluctuations, a class of sources well motivated in early-Universe scenarios. Within this framework we develop tools to characterize higher-order GW correlators and compute representative four-point functions that generate a connected contribution to the GW trispectrum. We show that the trispectrum amplitude scales as the square of the GW power spectrum and peaks in characteristic folded momentum configurations, reflecting the structure of the nonlinear source. We then explore the observational implications. First, we demonstrate that the connected trispectrum contributes to the variance of two-point overlap reduction functions, including the Hellings-Downs curve relevant for pulsar timing arrays. We then construct the optimal estimator to measure the connected trispectrum with ground-based interferometers. Our results highlight how non-Gaussian SGWB statistics provide a complementary observable to probe the origin of GW backgrounds and to distinguish cosmological from astrophysical sources.

### [59] [Microscopic geometric theory for gapped excitations in fractional topological fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13489)
*Yuzhu Wang,Bo Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种描述分数量子霍尔（fractional quantum Hall）相中所有带隙激发的几何框架，揭示了多个具有实验意义的基本理解。该框架建立了Laughlin相中多个自旋2的类引力子激发与无理Haffnian共形场论中非阿贝尔准空穴之间的对偶关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为分数量子霍尔相中的所有带隙激发提供统一的几何描述，揭示其基本物理特性并探索实验验证的可能性。研究动机源于理解拓扑量子态中高自旋中性模式的几何起源及其与共形场论结构的深层联系。

Method: 通过几何框架描述带隙激发，构建Laughlin相中多个高自旋中性模式的微观波函数。这些模式源于拓扑基态的高阶几何形变，并渐近地存在于Gaffnian共形希尔伯特空间内。研究分析了这些高自旋模式之间的散射过程。

Result: 建立了ν=1/3 Laughlin相中多个自旋2类引力子激发与无理Haffnian共形场论非阿贝尔准空穴之间的希尔伯特空间对偶关系。证明了分数量子霍尔相的完整多体希尔伯特空间可以通过此类几何形变的叠加生成，为所有带隙激发提供了具体的几何解释。

Conclusion: 所有带隙激发都可以通过拓扑基态的几何形变来理解，支持了分数量子霍尔相中激发的统一几何解释。研究推测这些高自旋模式可能具有较长的寿命，并提出了相应的实验探测方法。

Abstract: We propose a geometric description of all gapped excitations in fractional quantum Hall phases that reveals several fundamental understandings with experimental consequences. These include a duality between the Hilbert space of multiple gapped ``graviton-like" spin 2 excitations at $ν=1/3$ Laughlin phase, and that of non-Abelian quasiholes of an irrational Haffnian conformal field theory. This leads us to construct microscopic wave functions for multiple higher-spin gapped neutral modes in the Laughlin phase. Carrying spin $s \ge 2$, they emerge from higher-order geometric deformations of the topological ground state, and live within the Gaffnian conformal Hilbert space asymptotically. We show that the full many-body Hilbert space of an FQH phase can be generated from superpositions of such geometric deformations, supporting a concrete geometric interpretation of all gapped excitations. We analyse the scattering between these higher spin modes and conjecture that they can have a long lifetime, and propose methods for their experimental detection.

### [60] [Effective band-projected description of interacting quasiperiodic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13548)
*Flavio Riche,Raul Liquito,Bruno Amorim,Eduardo V. Castro,Pedro Ribeiro,Miguel Gonçalves*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过二阶能带投影方法，在一维准周期窄带系统中成功再现了相互作用导致的相图，包括Luttinger液体到电荷密度波相的转变，以及强准周期性下的准分形电荷密度波区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索一维窄带系统中电子相互作用与准周期性之间的相互作用，重点关注基态和低能激发特性。这对比了传统平移不变平带系统中一阶能带投影的成功与准周期环境下的差异。

Method: 采用能带投影作为低能有效方法，发现仅包含相互作用强度一阶项的投影无法再现关联相图。通过微扰地纳入二阶带间贡献，构建了有效的哈密顿量，并与密度矩阵重整化群计算结果进行定量比较。

Result: 二阶能带投影有效哈密顿量定量再现了精确相图，包括Luttinger液体到电荷密度波相的转变，以及强准周期性下的准分形电荷密度波区域。该框架还用于研究低能中性激发和光学电导率，识别了不同相区的动态特征。

Conclusion: 研究确立了二阶能带投影作为关联准周期窄带系统的可靠工具，并为研究超越一维的相互作用准周期和莫尔材料提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: We study the interplay between electronic interactions and quasiperiodicity in a one-dimensional narrow-band system, focusing on ground-state and low-energy excitation properties. Using band projection as low-energy effective approach, we show that a projection restricted to first order in the interaction strength fails to reproduce the correlated phase diagram. This contrasts with the standard success of first-order band projection in translationally invariant flatband systems and highlights the essential role of virtual processes involving remote bands in quasiperiodic settings. By incorporating second-order interband contributions perturbatively, we obtain an effective Hamiltonian that quantitatively reproduces the exact phase iagram previously obtained using density matrix renormalization group calculations, including the transition between a Luttinger liquid and a charge-density-wave phase and the crossover to a quasifractal charge-density-wave regime at strong quasiperiodicity. We further use this controlled framework to investigate low-energy neutral excitations and the optical conductivity, identifying clear dynamical signatures distinguishing the different phases. Our results establish second-order band projection as a reliable tool for correlated quasiperiodic narrow-band systems and suggest a promising route for studying interacting quasiperiodic and moiré materials beyond one dimension.

Method: 开发了一种无符号问题（sign-problem-free）的费米子-光子混合量子蒙特卡洛算法，该算法可推广到更复杂的腔体强关联模型。

Conclusion: 该方法可推广应用于更复杂的腔体强关联模型研究，为探索腔体量子材料中的新奇量子现象提供了有效计算工具。

Abstract: In cavity quantum materials, entangling strongly correlated electrons with quantum light provides a unique opportunity to explore novel quantum phases and phase transitions absent in conventional solid-state materials. In this study, we develop a sign-problem-free fermion-photon hybrid Quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) algorithm, and use it to systematically investigate the ground-state phase diagram of a two-dimensional cavity Hubbard model. It is shown that the interplay between the electron correlation and photon condensation gives rise to intriguing quantum phases ({\it e.g.} superradiant antiferromagnetic and chiral/$π$-flux states), and different quantum phase transitions, such as a first-order superradiant phase transition and a continuous phase transition with Gross-Neveu universality class. The methodology can be readily generalized to more complicated cavity strongly correlated models.

### [62] [Entanglement Rényi Negativity across the Finite-Temperature Transition in the O(3) Universality Class](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13711)
*Dong-Xu Liu,Yi-Ming Ding,Zhe Wang,Zheng Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过大规模量子蒙特卡洛模拟，首次研究了三维海森堡反铁磁体中O(3)相变处的第三Rényi负性，发现热涨落完全破坏了零温下的长程纠缠，但负性的温度导数仍遵循比热的精确标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限温度相变中量子纠缠的命运仍是一个开放问题，特别是在连续对称性破缺的情况下，零温下的戈德斯通模式会产生长程关联。本研究旨在探索热临界点处量子纠缠的行为特征。

Method: 采用大规模量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，研究三维海森堡反铁磁体（Heisenberg antiferromagnet）中O(3)相变处的第三Rényi负性（third Rényi negativity）。这是首个针对具有连续对称性的热临界点的此类研究。

Result: 研究发现：1）负性在临界点呈现纯面积律（pure area law），次领头阶常数项在统计不确定度内消失，表明热涨落完全破坏了零温下的长程纠缠；2）尽管负性本身无奇异行为，但其温度导数遵循比热（specific heat）的精确标度律，得到临界指数-α/ν=0.190(1)和1/ν=1.350(5)，与O(3)普适类精确一致。

Conclusion: 研究确立了量子纠缠对热临界性"视而不见"，但其热力学导数编码了完整的普适标度行为，揭示了纠缠与经典相变之间意想不到的联系。同时证明Rényi负性在具有连续对称性的系统中仍能有效屏蔽经典关联。

Abstract: The fate of quantum entanglement at finite-temperature phase transitions remains an open question, particularly for continuous symmetry breaking where zero-temperature Goldstone modes generate long-range correlations. Using large-scale quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we investigate the third Rényi negativity across the O(3) transition in the three-dimensional Heisenberg antiferromagnet. The first such study for a thermal critical point with continuous symmetry. We uncover two fundamental results. First, the negativity exhibits a pure area law at the critical point, with the subleading constant term vanishing within statistical uncertainty. This demonstrates that thermal fluctuations completely destroy the long-range entanglement present at zero temperature. The divergent classical correlation length leaves no imprint on quantum entanglement itself. Second, despite this absence of singular behavior in the negativity, its temperature derivative follows the exact scaling of the specific heat, yielding critical exponents -α/ν=0.190(1) and 1/ν=1.350(5) in precise agreement with the O(3) universality class. Our work establishes that while quantum entanglement is blind to thermal criticality, its thermodynamic derivatives encode the full universal scaling, revealing an unexpected connection between entanglement and classical phase transitions. Furthermore, this also provides further evidence that Rényi negativity can still effectively shield classical correlations in systems with continuous symmetry.

</details>


### [63] [Pressure induced redistribution of oxygen hole states in La$_{4}$Ni$_{3}$O$_{10}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13808)
*Guiwen Jiang,Liang Si,George A. Sawatzky,Mi Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过密度泛函计算和多轨道多原子团簇精确对角化，研究了三层La₄Ni₃O₁₀的局域低能电子态。发现在常压下，两个额外空穴分别形成Zhang-Rice单态和三维自旋极化子；高压下则形成不同的电荷和自旋有序态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索三层镍酸盐La₄Ni₃O₁₀的局域低能电子态，特别是通过对比常压和高压条件下的电子结构变化，揭示其与双层La₃Ni₂O₇体系的相似性。

Method: 采用密度泛函计算（density functional calculations）和多轨道多原子团簇精确对角化（multi-orbital, multi-atom cluster exact diagonalization）方法，包含局域交换和库仑相互作用，通过最小Ni₃O₁₄团簇模型进行研究。

Result: 常压下，两个额外空穴分别形成：1) 中心NiO₂层中的Zhang-Rice单态（ZRS）与d_{x²-y²}轨道；2) 主要占据两个层间O p_z轨道的反键组合，并与三个NiO₂层的d_{z²}轨道形成的三维自旋极化子（3SP）杂化。高压下，两个空穴分别集中在外层和内层，形成不同的ZRS或面内3SP构型。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了La₄Ni₃O₁₀在常压和高压下不同的电荷和自旋有序态，并强调了其与双层La₃Ni₂O₇体系在电荷和自旋有序状态方面的相似性，为理解多层镍酸盐的电子结构提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Using density functional calculations and multi-orbital, multi-atom cluster exact diagonalization that includes local exchange and Coulomb interactions, we explored the local low-energy electronic states of trilayer La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ via a minimal Ni$_3$O$_{14}$ cluster. We find that, at ambient pressure, starting with all three Ni being nominally 2+ valence, one of the two extra holes is localized in the central NiO$_2$ layer forming a Zhang-Rice singlet (ZRS) with $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital. The other hole mainly occupies the antibonding combination of the two interplane O $p_z$ orbitals and thereby hybridizes with an out-of-plane three-spin-polaron (3SP) formed by the $d_{z^2}$ orbitals of three NiO$_2$ layers. In this way, the in-plane spin orientation alternation is carried by the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbitals of two outer layers with interlayer antiferromagnetic correlation. Simultaneously, the central layer is insulating like with negligible magnetic moment. At high pressure, however, the two extra holes are concentrated on one of two outer layers and the inner layer separately forming the ZRS with $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbitals or in-plane 3SP with neighboring cluster. We highlight the similarities between the bilayer La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ and trilayer La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ via possible charge and spin ordered states suggested by our cluster results.

</details>

Just above room temperature, this compound undergoes a structural phase transition from the high-temperature trigonal $P\bar{3}m1$ $(a=b=a_0$ and $c=c_0)$ to the low-temperature monoclinic $I2/a$ phase $(a \approx \sqrt{3}a_0$, $b=a_0$, $c \approx 2c_0$ and $β\approx 90.6^\circ)$. According to thermodynamic and nuclear magnetic resonance measurements, it experiences a phase transition into a canted antiferromagnetic state at $T_N = 21~\mathrm{K}$. ### [65] [Disentangling Tensor Network States with Deep Neural Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14425)
*Chaohui Fan,Bo Zhan,Yuntian Gu,Tong Liu,Yantao Wu,Mingpu Qin,Dingshun Lv,Tao Xiang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出神经张量网络态（νTNS），一种结合深度神经网络与张量网络架构的变分多体波函数拟设。该方法在自旋-1/2 J₁-J₂海森堡模型上实现了最先进的变分能量，并支持该模型在J₂/J₁=0.5处存在无能隙量子自旋液体基态的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种紧凑且高表达能力的表示方法，用于描述强关联量子多体系统。传统方法在处理高度纠缠的量子态时面临挑战，需要新的架构来更有效地表征这些复杂系统。

Method: 方法核心是神经张量网络态（νTNS）框架，其中神经网络作为波函数的解纠缠器（disentangler），将物理自由度转换为纠缠度大幅降低的重整化变量。重整化态随后通过回流张量网络（back-flow tensor network）进行高效编码。具体实现采用卷积神经网络与矩阵乘积态（matrix product states）相结合的方式。

Result: 在具有周期性边界条件的20×20方格晶格上，对自旋-1/2 J₁-J₂海森堡模型（J₂/J₁=0.5）获得了最先进的变分能量。自旋、二聚体和晶格关联的有限尺寸标度分析显示幂律衰减，未观察到磁序或价键长程有序，这与该点存在无能隙量子自旋液体（gapless quantum spin-liquid）基态一致。

Conclusion: νTNS框架具有灵活性，可自然扩展到其他神经网络和张量网络结构，为研究强关联量子多体系统提供了一个通用平台。该工作展示了深度神经网络与张量网络架构结合在量子多体问题中的潜力。

Abstract: We introduce Neural Tensor Network States ($ν$TNS), a variational many-body wave-function ansatz that integrates deep neural networks with tensor-network architectures. In the $ν$TNS framework, a neural network serves as a disentangler of the wave-function, transforming the physical degrees of freedom into renormalized variables with much less entanglement. The renormalized state is then efficiently encoded by a back-flow tensor network. This construction yields a compact yet highly expressive representation of strongly correlated quantum states. Using convolutional neural networks combined with matrix product states as a concrete implementation, we obtain state-of-the-art variational energies for the spin-$1/2$ $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg model on the square lattice at the highly frustrated point $J_2/J_1=0.5$, for systems up to $20\times 20$ with periodic boundary conditions. Finite-size scaling of spin, dimer, and plaquette correlations exhibits power-law decay without magnetic or valence-bond long-range order, consistent with a gapless quantum spin-liquid ground state at that point.This $ν$TNS framework is flexible and naturally extensible to other neural and tensor-network structures, offering a general platform for investigating strongly correlated quantum many-body systems.

</details>


### [66] [Variance reduction for forces and pressure in variational Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14521)
*David Linteau,Saverio Moroni,Giuseppe Carleo,Markus Holzmann*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了降低蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）估计器方差的简单实用策略，重点针对电子系统中的原子力和压力计算，展示了这些方法在高压金属氢系统中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蒙特卡洛估计器在计算原子力、压力等物理量时常面临方差较大的问题，特别是在变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）计算中，这限制了计算的精度和效率。

Method: 针对Pulay型贡献，提出了基于Metropolis接受率（Metropolis acceptance ratio）的改进方法，将方差幂律发散（power-law divergence）减弱为对数发散；对于Hellmann-Feynman力，推导了适用于周期系统的紧凑型方差降低估计器。

Result: 改进方法显著降低了估计器方差，通过廉价正则化（regularizations）进一步抑制了异常值，代价是引入可控的小偏差；方法已成功应用于包含百余原子的高压金属氢系统的神经量子态（neural quantum states）描述。

Conclusion: 所提出的方差降低策略简单实用，不仅适用于原子力和压力计算，还可推广到对关联函数（pair-correlation）、角分布函数（angular-distribution functions）等其他可观测量，以及分子动力学（molecular dynamics）等其他方法。

Abstract: We present simple and practical strategies to reduce the variance of Monte Carlo estimators. Our focus is on variational Monte Carlo calculations of atomic forces and pressure in electronic systems, although we show that the underlying ideas apply more broadly to other observables, like pair-correlation and angular-distribution functions, and other methods, including molecular dynamics. For Pulay-type contributions, we show that a minor modification based on the Metropolis acceptance ratio softens the power-law divergence of the variance to a logarithmic one, and that inexpensive regularizations can further suppress outliers at the price of a controlled small bias. For Hellmann-Feynman forces, we derive compact variance-reduced estimators for periodic systems that are straightforward to implement in standard Monte Carlo codes. The approach is illustrated for high-pressure metallic hydrogen with more than a hundred atoms described by neural quantum states, including an application to molecular dynamics driven by the improved forces.

</details>


### [67] [Microwave spin resonance in epitaxial thin films of spin liquid candidate TbInO3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14545)
*Sandesh S. Kalantre,Johanna Nordlander,Margaret A. Anderson,Julia A. Mundy,David Goldhaber-Gordon*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究使用共面超导谐振器（coplanar superconducting resonators）探测候选量子自旋液体材料TbInO3薄膜的磁激发，通过微波技术测量传统体材料技术无法探测的低体积样品，揭示了该材料在极低温下的极端磁阻挫特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL）作为由晶格连接性导致的磁有序阻挫和量子涨落共同作用产生的奇异量子态，在实验上难以通过序参量直接识别。研究旨在开发适用于低体积薄膜样品的测量技术，以诊断阻挫自旋系统的基态性质。

Method: 采用共面超导谐振器探测外延生长的TbInO3薄膜的磁激发，借鉴电路量子电动力学（circuit quantum electrodynamics）领域的微波技术，测量传统体材料技术无法适用的低体积样品。通过自旋共振信号提取面内磁化率，并进行晶体场分析。

Result: 从自旋共振信号提取的面内磁化率表明，磁有序在低至20 mK的温度下仍存在极端阻挫，比居里-外斯能量尺度（Curie-Weiss energy scale）低两个数量级。晶体场分析识别了构成基态的双重态本征态，由于非本征铁电性（improper ferroelectricity），Tb磁矩分裂为具有不同g因子的两类，反映了每个格点的局域晶体场环境。

Conclusion: 自旋轨道耦合、晶体场、磁阻挫和非本征铁电性独特地结合，共同塑造了TbInO3的磁基态。该工作建立了使用超导谐振器探测阻挫磁体薄膜的测量技术，并应用该技术构建对TbInO3磁性的连贯理解。

Abstract: Minimizing the energy of a many body system tends to favor order, but classical frustration and quantum fluctuations destabilize that order. The tension between these effects can produce exotic quantum states of matter. Quantum spin liquid (QSL) states emerge in models of localized magnetic moments where the crystal lattice connectivity frustrates ordering, and the exchange interaction of neighboring spins strengthens quantum fluctuations. Experimentally identifying a QSL in a real material is challenging from the lack of an order parameter. Piecing together evidence from varied techniques is necessary for diagnosing the nature of the ground state -- QSL or otherwise -- of a frustrated spin system. In this work, we use coplanar superconducting resonators to probe magnetic excitations in epitaxially grown thin films of a spin liquid candidate TbInO3. Adapting microwave techniques from the field of circuit quantum electrodynamics, we measure responses of these thin films whose volume is too low for applying conventional bulk techniques. In-plane susceptibility extracted from the spin resonance signal indicates extreme frustration of magnetic order down to 20 mK, over two orders of magnitude lower than the Curie-Weiss energy scale. Through a crystal field analysis, we identify the doublet eigenstates comprising the ground state. As a consequence of improper ferroelectricity, Tb moments split into two flavors with distinct g-factors reflecting the local crystal field environment of each site. Spin-orbit coupling, crystal fields, magnetic frustration and improper ferroelectricity distinctively combine to shape the magnetic ground state of TbInO3. This work establishes a measurement technique using superconducting resonators to probe thin films of frustrated magnets, and applies this technique towards building a coherent understanding of the magnetic properties of TbInO3.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和晶体轨道哈密顿布居（Crystal Orbital Hamilton Population, COHP）计算相结合的方法。重点对SmTi₃(Sb,Sn)₄系列进行详细表征，并简要探讨其他稀土化合物（Ce, Pr, Nd, Gd）的(Sb,Sn)固溶范围和磁性可调性。

Conclusion: (Sb,Sn)协同对可用于稳定LnTi₃(Sb,Sn)₄结构，同时提供调控磁性的手段，为开发具有化学、磁性和电子可调性的新型金属间化合物提供了潜在途径。该工作展示了通过合金化策略实现材料多维度性质调控的有效性。

Abstract: Here we present our synthesis and characterization of the LnTi$_3$(Sb,Sn)$_4$ (Ln: Ce, Pr, Nd, Sm, Gd) family of cleavable kagome metals. We use a combination of first-principles density functional theory (DFT) and Crystal Orbital Hamilton Population (COHP) calculations to show that (Sb,Sn) alloying has a stabilizing effect on the structure by adjusting the Fermi level, filling bonding states, depopulating antibonding states, and adjusting the density-of-states (DOS) towards local minima, an effect we call ``synergistic doping.'' The tunable Fermi level also has a profound effect on the magnetism, which we demonstrate through a detailed characterization of the SmTi$_3$(Sb,Sn)$_4$ series. The series hosts multiple magnetic ground states resulting from competing magnetic interactions that are tunable by the (Sb,Sn) ratio. While the focus of this work is on SmTi$_3$(Sb,Sn)$_4$, we briefly comment on the (Sb,Sn) solubility range and the conferred magnetic tunability in the other rare-earths compounds (Ln: Ce, Pr, Nd, Gd) as well. Our work demonstrates how the (Sb,Sn) synergistic pair can be used to stabilize the LnTi$_3$(Sb,Sn)$_4$ structure while simultaneously providing a means to tune the magnetism, ultimately providing a potential route to develop new intermetallics with chemical, magnetic, and electronic tunability.

### [69] [Evidence for ferroaxial order in 1T-TiSe$_2$ via elastoresistivity measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14613)
*Qianni Jiang,Ezra Day-Roberts,Benito Gonzalez,Awadhesh Das,Darius H. Torchinsky,Turan Birol,Rafael M. Fernandes,Ian R. Fisher*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过弹阻测量（elastoresistivity）探测1T-TiSe₂中的铁轴序（ferroaxial order），发现电荷密度波态中的异常非对角线性弹阻响应，并构建了铁轴序的有效共轭场，揭示了铁轴磁化率在临界温度附近的发散行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐藏序（hidden order）作为难以被传统探测手段发现的对称性破缺态，对于理解复杂量子相至关重要。铁轴序（ferroaxial order）是一种破坏镜面对称性但保持时间反演和反演对称性的隐藏序，实验探测极具挑战性。

Method: 研究采用弹阻测量（elastoresistivity measurements）来探测铁轴序参数和铁轴磁化率（ferroaxial susceptibility），并构建了对称性破缺应变ε_{x²-y²}和ε_{xy}的适当组合作为铁轴序的有效共轭场（effective conjugate field）。同时进行了详细的弹热测量（elastocaloric measurements）。

Result: 在1T-TiSe₂的电荷密度波（CDW）态中观测到异常的非对角线性弹阻响应，这为铁轴序提供了确凿证据。通过扫描有效场，观察到与铁轴畴壁（ferroaxial domain walls）运动相关的弹阻迟滞行为。某些非线性弹阻系数在临界温度以上发散，与铁轴磁化率在T_CDW~200K附近的发散一致。弹热测量还揭示了在T_CDW以下数十开尔文处存在额外的相变。

Conclusion: 该研究为1T-TiSe₂有序态的对称性提供了新见解，并确立了弹阻测量作为探测隐藏序及其对称性的有力工具。铁轴序的发现有助于理解长期未得到全面认识的电荷密度波序。

Abstract: The study of spontaneous symmetry breaking and electronic order is fundamental in condensed matter physics. Hidden order, symmetry-breaking states that elude conventional probes, potentially plays a crucial role in understanding complex quantum phases in a wide range of materials. Ferroaxial order, a state characterized by broken mirror symmetries while maintaining time-reversal and inversion symmetries, is one of the hidden orders that have proven most challenging to detect experimentally. Here, we demonstrate a new approach for investigating both the ferroaxial order parameter and ferroaxial susceptibility using elastoresistivity measurements. We do this for 1T-TiSe$_{2}$, a material that exhibits charge density wave order that has eluded comprehensive understanding for a long time. These measurements reveal an anomalous off-diagonal linear elastoresistivity in the CDW state. We discuss why this provides a smoking gun for ferroaxial order. Furthermore, we construct an appropriate combination of the symmetry-breaking strains $ε_{x^2-y^2}$ and $ε_{xy}$ that acts as an effective conjugate field for the ferroaxial order, and demonstrate how sweeping this effective field in the CDW state results in a hysteretic behavior of the elastoresistivity, associated with the movement of ferroaxial domain walls. Finally, we reveal a divergence of certain nonlinear elastoresistivity coefficients above the critical temperature, and discuss how this is consistent with a divergence of the ferroaxial susceptibility near T$_{\rm{CDW}}$ $\sim$ 200K. Our study also includes detailed elastocaloric measurements, which reveal the presence of an additional phase transition several tens of Kelvin below T$_{\rm{CDW}}$. Our results provide new insight into the symmetry of the ordered state in 1T-TiSe$_2$ and establish elastoresistivity as a powerful probe of hidden order and its symmetry.

### [70] [Ferroaxial and nematic transitions in the charge density wave phase of 1T-TiSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14614)
*Sarah Edwards,Elliott Rosenberg,Ilaria Maccari,Jiaqin Wen,Chaowei Hu,Xiaodong Xu,Jong-Woo Kim,Philip J. Ryan,Rafael M. Fernandes,Fernando de Juan,Maria N. Gastiasoro,Jiun-Haw Chu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究澄清了1T-TiSe₂中电荷密度波（CDW）的对称性破缺本质，发现其并非手性态而是铁轴性（ferroaxial）态，同时揭示了在铁轴性CDW内部存在旋转对称性破缺不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1T-TiSe₂材料中观察到的电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）是否具有手性特征（即自发破缺镜面和反演对称性）存在长期争议，先前实验报告了相互矛盾的结果，需要澄清其对称性破缺的本质。

Method: 采用对称性分辨的弹性电阻率（symmetry-resolved elastoresistivity）测量技术，检测自发出现的本征非对角弹性电阻率系数，这些系数满足反对称关系；同时进行弹性热（elastocaloric）测量以确定相变时序。

Result: 识别出体对称性破缺为铁轴性（ferroaxial），即破缺垂直镜面但保留反演对称性；检测到满足反对称关系的本征非对角弹性电阻率系数，提供了宏观电环矩（electric toroidal moment）的明确体输运特征；铁轴序起始于CDW相变稍下方，随温度进一步降低，发散的向列相（nematic）敏感性信号表明铁轴性CDW内部存在独特的旋转对称性破缺不稳定性。

Conclusion: 1T-TiSe₂中提出的"手性"CDW实际上是中心对称的铁轴性态，这一发现调和了先前表面敏感观测与体对称性约束之间的矛盾，解决了关于该材料CDW相对称性破缺本质的长期争议。

Abstract: Charge density waves (CDWs) with multi-component order parameters can break unexpected symmetries through the interplay of nearly degenerate instabilities. In the widely investigated material 1T-TiSe$_2$, a central question is whether the observed CDW has a chiral character, which would manifest as the spontaneous breaking of mirror and inversion symmetries. Previous experiments have reported conflicting results about the broken symmetries in the CDW phase of 1T-TiSe$_2$. Here, we resolve this controversy by identifying the bulk broken symmetry as ferroaxial, corresponding to the breaking of vertical mirrors while preserving inversion symmetry. Using symmetry-resolved elastoresistivity, we detect the spontaneous emergence of intrinsic off-diagonal elastoresistivity coefficients that satisfy an antisymmetric relation ($m_{xx-yy,xy} \approx -m_{xy,xx-yy}$), providing an unambiguous bulk transport signature of a macroscopic electric toroidal moment. Simultaneous elastocaloric measurements reveal that the onset of ferroaxial order occurs just below the CDW transition. As the temperature is lowered further, a diverging nematic susceptibility signals a distinct rotational symmetry-breaking instability inside the ferroaxial CDW state. Our findings demonstrate that the proposed ``chiral'' CDW in 1T-TiSe$_2$ is actually a centrosymmetric ferroaxial state, reconciling previous surface-sensitive observations with bulk symmetry constraints.

Method: 结合磁输运测量、量子振荡、中子衍射和第一性原理计算（ab initio calculations）等多种实验与理论方法。通过磁输运表征反常霍尔效应，量子振荡揭示费米面重构，中子衍射探测磁结构，第一性原理计算提供理论支持。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个受挫磁体平台用于调控反常霍尔效应，阐明了交换相互作用和自旋织构在量子输运中的主导作用。同时为设计利用涌现自旋织构动力学的非常规自旋电子学系统提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The interaction between conduction electrons and localized magnetic moments profoundly influences the electrical and magnetic properties of materials, giving rise to a variety of fascinating physical phenomena and quantum effects. Here, we discover a giant anomalous Hall effect (AHE) in a frustrated Eu-based magnet, exhibiting a giant anomalous Hall conductivity (AHC) of 31000 Ω-1cm-1 and a remarkable anomalous Hall angle (AHA, tanθH) of 12 %--surpassing conventional mechanisms (either intrinsic or extrinsic) by two orders of magnitude. Combining magnetotransport, quantum oscillations, neutron diffraction and ab initio calculations, we establish that the giant AHC originates from fluctuating spin chirality skew scattering, generated by indirect Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida (RKKY) interactions of Eu-4f moments. Simultaneously, Hund's coupling of itinerant electrons and localized Eu-4f spins triggers giant exchange splitting, evidenced by temperature-dependent Fermi surface reconstruction. This work establishes a frustrated magnetic platform for engineering the AHE and elucidates the governing role of exchange interactions and spin textures in quantum transport, while also providing a framework for designing unconventional spintronic systems that harness emergent spin-texture dynamics.

### [72] [Non-Abelian fractional Chern insulators from an exactly solvable two-body model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14722)
*Joseph R. Cruise,Alexander Seidel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一类晶格哈密顿量，其单粒子谱包含任意数量的精确简并平带（flat bands），这些平带在晶格上重现了前p个朗道能级（Landau levels）的解析结构。结合局域玻色接触相互作用后，这些模型成为分数陈绝缘体（FCIs）的精确可解无阻挫母哈密顿量，实现了阿贝尔和非阿贝尔部分子量子霍尔态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在构建能够精确捕捉连续朗道能级解析结构的理想化晶格模型，同时保持与指数局域跳跃的兼容性。这为研究陈数（Chern number）C > 1的分数陈绝缘体提供了新框架，并实现了多朗道能级物理的精确可解晶格实现。

Method: 研究构建了一类特殊的晶格哈密顿量，其单粒子谱包含任意数量的精确简并平带，这些平带在晶格上重现了前p个朗道能级的解析结构。通过结合局域玻色接触相互作用，这些模型成为分数陈绝缘体的精确可解无阻挫母哈密顿量。研究还使用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法验证了模型的预期零模计数。

Result: 通过精确对角化确认了模型变体稳定玻色Jain-21态以及非阿贝尔22-和33-态的预期零模计数，这些态分别预期支持Ising型和Fibonacci型任意子（anyons）。该构造为多朗道能级物理提供了精确可解的晶格实现，并为研究陈数C > 1的分数陈绝缘体提供了新框架。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一类能够精确重现连续朗道能级解析结构的理想化晶格模型，同时保持与指数局域跳跃的兼容性。这一构造不仅实现了多朗道能级物理的精确可解晶格实现，还为研究具有更高陈数的分数陈绝缘体提供了新框架，特别是能够稳定阿贝尔和非阿贝尔部分子量子霍尔态。

Abstract: We construct a class of lattice Hamiltonians whose single-particle spectrum consists of an arbitrary number of exactly degenerate flat bands that reproduce the analytic structure of the first $p$ Landau levels restricted to the lattice. When combined with local bosonic contact interactions, these models become exactly solvable frustration-free parent Hamiltonians for FCIs that realize both Abelian and non-Abelian parton quantum Hall states. Using exact diagonalization, we confirm the expected zero-mode counting for variants of the model stabilizing the bosonic Jain-21 state as well as the non-Abelian 22- and 33-states, which are expected to support Ising- and Fibonacci-type anyons, respectively. Our construction provides an exactly solvable lattice realization of multi Landau-level physics and offers a new framework for studying FCIs with Chern number $C > 1$. More broadly, it supplies a family of idealized lattice models that capture the analytic structure of continuum Landau levels while remaining compatible with exponentially local hopping.

### [73] [Neural network backflow for ab-initio solid calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14775)
*An-Jun Liu,Bryan K. Clark*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究成功将神经网络回流（NNBF）方法扩展至从头算固态材料，通过两阶段剪枝策略管理庞大的构型空间，在多种固态基准测试中达到最先进精度，包括一维氢链、二维石墨烯和三维硅材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确模拟扩展周期性系统是凝聚态物理学的核心挑战。虽然神经量子态（NQS）为此任务提供了表达性波函数，但面临可扩展性问题。本研究旨在将神经网络回流方法应用于从头算固态材料，解决现有方法的局限性。

Method: 基于分子可扩展优化框架，引入两阶段剪枝策略管理构型空间扩展：利用计算成本低、物理信息丰富的重要性代理，将精确的NNBF振幅评估仅分配给最相关的行列式。该方法显著提高了优化效率、能量估计和收敛性。

Result: 在一维氢链中，NNBF匹配或超越了密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）和辅助场量子蒙特卡洛（AFQMC）方法，在耦合簇方法失效的强关联键断裂区域保持稳健，并能平滑外推至热力学极限。进一步展示了计算二维石墨烯和三维硅基态势能曲线的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 该框架在多种固态基准测试中实现了最先进的精度。消融研究验证了剪枝策略的计算节省效果，并强调了NNBF能量对基组的依赖性。该方法成功解决了神经量子态在扩展周期性系统中的可扩展性问题。

Abstract: Accurately simulating extended periodic systems is a central challenge in condensed matter physics. Neural quantum states (NQS) offer expressive wavefunctions for this task but face issues with scalability. In this work, we successfully extend the neural network backflow (NNBF) approach to ab-initio solid-state materials. Building on our scalable optimization framework for molecules [Liu et al., PRB 112, 155162 (2025)], we introduce a two-stage pruning strategy to manage the massive configuration space expansions: by utilizing a computationally cheap, physics-informed importance proxy, we devote exact NNBF amplitude evaluations solely to the most relevant determinants, significantly improving optimization efficiency, energy estimation, and convergence. Our framework achieves state-of-the-art accuracy across diverse solid-state benchmarks. For 1D hydrogen chains, NNBF matches or surpasses DMRG and AFQMC, remains robust in strongly correlated bond-breaking regimes where coupled-cluster methods fail, and smoothly extrapolates to the thermodynamic limit. We further demonstrate its scalability by computing ground-state potential energy curves for 2D graphene and 3D silicon. Finally, ablation studies validate the computational savings of our pruning strategy and highlight the dependence of the NNBF energies on basis sets.

### [74] [Study of the triangular-lattice Hubbard model with constrained-path quantum Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14808)
*Shu Fay Ung,Ankit Mahajan,David R. Reichman*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文对三角晶格哈伯德模型（triangular-lattice Hubbard model）进行了约束路径蒙特卡洛（constrained-path Monte Carlo, CPMC）基准测试，展示了对称性适应（symmetry-adapted）试探波函数对于定量精度的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在评估CPMC方法在强关联、受挫系统（frustrated systems）中的性能，特别是针对三角晶格哈伯德模型在不同填充度和U值下的表现，为研究此类系统中的竞争基态（competing ground states）提供实用途径。

Method: 采用约束路径蒙特卡洛方法，使用对称性适应试探波函数（symmetry-adapted trial wave functions），并与精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group）结果进行基准比较。

Result: 在半填充（half-filling）以外，基于自由电子的简单试探波函数能保持基态对称性，能量偏差小于1%；而在半填充时，中等到大U值区域的强受挫（strong frustration）需要对称性投影试探波函数（symmetry-projected trials）才能达到可比精度。

Conclusion: 由于CPMC与对称性投影结合的计算成本随系统尺寸多项式增长，该方法为研究强关联受挫系统中的竞争基态提供了实用途径，其中对称性适应试探波函数对于定量精度至关重要。

Abstract: We benchmark constrained-path Monte Carlo (CPMC) on the triangular-lattice Hubbard model for several fillings and $U$ values and show that symmetry-adapted trial wave functions are essential for quantitative accuracy. Away from half-filling, simple free-electron-based trials that preserve the ground state symmetry yield energy deviations $\lesssim 1\%$ from exact diagonalization and density matrix renormalization group results. At half-filling, strong frustration in the intermediate to large $U$ regimes necessitates symmetry-projected trials to reach comparable accuracy, where both free-electron and symmetry-broken Hartree-Fock trials incur substantial constraint bias. Since the computational cost of CPMC with symmetry projection scales polynomially with system size, our results motivate its use as a practical route for studying competing ground states in strongly correlated, frustrated systems.

</details>


### [75] [Lee-Yang Zeros and Pseudocritical Drift in J-Q Néel-VBS Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15116)
*Chunhao Guo,Zhe Wang,Danhe Wang,Zenan Liu,Haiyuan Zou,Zheng Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过计算李-杨零点（Lee-Yang zeros）的标度行为，研究J-Q模型中奈尔（Néel）反铁磁体与柱状价键固体（columnar valence-bond solid）之间的量子相变，发现该转变具有弱一级相变特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: J-Q模型为研究奈尔反铁磁体与柱状价键固体之间的量子相变提供了无符号问题（sign-problem-free）的计算框架。需要深入理解该相变的本质特性，特别是其属于连续相变还是一级相变。

Method: 采用随机级数展开量子蒙特卡洛（stochastic series expansion quantum Monte Carlo）方法，通过在复源场存在下对临界点附近构型进行重加权（reweighting），计算李-杨零点的标度行为。该方法在二聚化海森堡模型和棋盘J-Q模型中进行了基准验证。

Result: J-Q模型中李-杨零点的标度行为随系统尺寸增大呈现显著系统性漂移，表明存在扩展的赝临界（pseudocritical）区域。SO(5)序参量场的有效标度维度随尺寸减小，在热力学极限下趋于消失，这种行为低于2+1维幺正相对论共形场论（unitary relativistic conformal field theory）的标量幺正界限（scalar unitarity bound）。

Conclusion: 李-杨零点的标度分析支持奈尔-价键固体（Néel-VBS）相变属于弱一级相变（weakly first-order transition）的解释。有限尺寸李-杨零点可作为J-Q模型中赝临界性和相变阶数的灵敏、对称性分辨的诊断工具。

Abstract: Square-lattice J-Q models provide a sign-problem-free setting for probing the quantum phase transition between Néel antiferromagnet and columnar valence-bond solid. We analyze this transition through the scaling of Lee-Yang zeros, computed within stochastic series expansion quantum Monte Carlo by reweighting configurations sampled near criticality in the presence of complex source fields. Benchmark studies of the dimerized Heisenberg model and the checkerboard J-Q model validate the method, yielding stable O(3) critical scaling in the former and clear spacetime-volume scaling in the latter, as expected for a first-order transition. Applying the same analysis to the J-Q models, we find a pronounced and systematic drift of the leading-zero scaling with increasing system size, consistent with an extended pseudocritical regime. The Lee-Yang scaling implies an effective scaling dimension of the SO(5) order-parameter field that decreases with size and is consistent with vanishing in the thermodynamic limit. Such behavior lies below the scalar unitarity bound of any unitary relativistic conformal field theory in 2+1 dimensions and enforces inverse spacetime-volume scaling of the zeros, the hallmark of a first-order transition. These results support a weakly first-order interpretation of the Néel-VBS transition and establish finite-size Lee-Yang zeros as a sensitive, symmetry-resolved diagnostic of pseudocriticality and transition order in the J-Q family.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: α-MnTe表现出显著的电子非均匀性，表明纳米尺度表征对于确保altermagnet材料在电子应用中的可靠使用至关重要。

Abstract: Altermagnets exhibit spin-split electronic bands like ferromagnets, yet they are magnetically compensated like collinear antiferromagnets. Altermagnets thus combine the benefits of ferromagnets and antiferromagnets, opening routes to tailored materials and applications. However, reported bulk signatures such as the anomalous Hall response in candidate altermagnets have been inconsistent across samples, suggesting that inhomogeneity may affect their functionality in electronic devices. Here, we use low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy to map the local electronic landscape of $α$-MnTe on atomically flat cleaved single crystals. We resolve two distinct electronic regions. In Region A, the chemical potential lies near the valence-band edge and varies by $\sim$100 meV on the nanometer length scale. In Region B, the chemical potential lies near the middle of a wider band gap. We further identify an incommensurate charge modulation with periodicity (2.5$\pm$0.1)$a$, observed exclusively in Region A. Our work establishes that $α$-MnTe can exhibit significant electronic non-uniformity, suggesting that nanoscale characterization is essential for its reliable use in electronic applications.

Result: 该框架能够统一描述不同维度的拓扑序：在二维情况下恢复已知的幺正模张量范畴（unitary modular tensor categories），在更高维度下自然引出真正的高范畴结构。这表明现有分类方案应重新解释为内在∞-范畴对象的低范畴阴影实现。

Conclusion: 本文提出拓扑相理论需要哥白尼式转向（Copernican turn）：许多现有分类方案应被视为内在∞-范畴对象的低范畴阴影实现。该统一框架为理解拓扑序提供了更基础的高范畴视角，为后续研究对称保护拓扑序（symmetry-protected topological order）和对称富化拓扑序（symmetry-enriched topological order）奠定基础。

Abstract: In the series of papers Motivic GUT Part I: Grand Unified Theory of Topological Order, Motivic GUT Part II: Grand Unified Theory of Symmetry-Protected Topological Order, and Motivic GUT Part III: Grand Unified Theory of Symmetry-Enriched Topological Order, we propose a unified framework for gapped topological phases based on the Grothendieck-Kitaev-Lurie motivic yoga. In the spirit of Grothendieck's rising sea, we argue that the classification problem can only be properly addressed after identifying the correct higher-categorical ambient space in which its full richness appears. In this first part, we propose a unified definition of gapped topological order in spatial dimension $d$ in terms of unitary fusion $(\infty,d)$-categorical data, considered up to Morita equivalence. For $d=2$, this framework recovers unitary modular tensor categories. For $d>2$, it naturally leads to genuinely higher-categorical structures. This suggests a Copernican turn in the theory of topological phases: many existing classification schemes should be reinterpreted as lower-categorical shadow realizations of intrinsically $\infty$-categorical objects.

Abstract: This work presents a comprehensive investigation of the structural, magnetic, and electronic properties of the double perovskite Ba$_2$CoMoO$_6$ (BCMO). Single crystals were grown via floating-zone and Czochralski techniques and characterized using a set of complementary methods. X-ray absorption spectroscopy at the Co~$L_{2,3}$ edges provides insight into the local electronic structure, revealing spin-orbit and crystal-field splitting effects; cluster-model calculations constrained by the XAS spectra yield a Landé $g$ factor $g = 4.52$, consistent with a spin-orbit-entangled $J_\mathrm{eff} = \tfrac{1}{2}$ ground state. Surface photovoltage spectroscopy reveals a strong optical response with a prominent feature at $2.65$~eV. These findings advance the understanding of face-centered cubic lattice antiferromagnets with strong spin-orbit coupling and suggest the technological promise of BCMO for spintronic and energy-conversion applications.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过引入关联跳跃相互作用（correlated hopping interaction）产生涌现准粒子，采用适当的相干态基矢推导配分函数的高斯路径积分表示，并利用标准多体技术（如微扰图论或平均场理论）系统处理高斯极限的偏离。

Abstract: We propose an interacting model that is exactly solvable in any spatial dimension and gives rise to a Fermi liquid (FL) featuring a pseudogapped (PG) single-particle spectral function and a vanishing quasiparticle (QP) weight at half-filling, without invoking Mott physics. The PG originates from a purely fermionic mechanism through emergent QPs arising from a correlated hopping interaction. By employing an appropriate coherent-state basis, we derive a Gaussian path-integral representation of the partition function, which enables systematic treatments of deviations from the Gaussian limit using standard many-body techniques, such as diagrammatic perturbation theory or mean-field theory. We explicitly demonstrate and discuss several properties of the exactly solvable limit on the square lattice, including the mechanism for temperature-dependent PG opening, the singular behavior of the self-energy, the violation of the Luttinger sum rule, and the role of Luttinger and Fermi surfaces. Finally, we explore quantum phase transitions between PG-FLs and Landau FLs.

### [80] [Conditioning on a Volatility Proxy Compresses the Apparent Timescale of Collective Market Correlation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14072)
*Yuda Bi,Vince D Calhoun*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 该研究解决了表观慢集体动力学的归因问题：观察到的持续性（persistence）是内在的，还是来自持久驱动因素？通过VIX耦合的Ornstein-Uhlenbeck模型分析S&P 500滚动相关矩阵，发现VIX代理（proxy）吸收了大部分表观慢动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决表观慢集体动力学的归因问题：观察到的持续性（persistence）是内在的（intrinsic）还是继承自持久驱动因素（persistent driver）。这一问题对于理解金融时间序列中的长期相关性具有重要意义。

Method: 采用VIX耦合的Ornstein-Uhlenbeck模型分析S&P 500 60天滚动相关矩阵（237只股票，2004-2023年）。通过贝叶斯信息准则（Bayesian Information Criterion, BIC）比较模型拟合效果，并进行自相关匹配的安慰剂场（placebo fields）、不相交周重构（disjoint weekly reconstructions）和六个锚定时间序列保留集（anchored chronological holdouts）等稳健性检验。

Result: VIX耦合模型将有效弛豫时间（relaxation time）从298天减少到61个交易日，BIC改进ΔBIC=109。仅使用log(VIX)的信息残差（informational residual）保留了大部分增益（ΔBIC=78.6），而机械VIX代理（mechanical VIX proxy）单独使用未改善拟合。安慰剂场检验失败，周重构仍支持场耦合模型，样本外优势得以保持。

Conclusion: 在测试的随机类（stochastic class）内，基于观察到的VIX代理的条件化（conditioning）吸收了大部分表观慢动力学。更强的隐变量扩展（hidden-variable extensions）仅得到部分支持，表明VIX在解释金融相关性持久性方面具有重要作用。

Abstract: We address the attribution problem for apparent slow collective dynamics: is the observed persistence intrinsic, or inherited from a persistent driver? For the leading eigenvalue fraction $ψ_1=λ_{\max}/N$ of S\&P 500 60-day rolling correlation matrices ($237$ stocks, 2004--2023), a VIX-coupled Ornstein--Uhlenbeck model reduces the effective relaxation time from $298$ to $61$ trading days and improves the fit over bare mean reversion by $Δ$BIC$=109$. On the decomposition sample, an informational residual of $\log(\mathrm{VIX})$ alone retains most of that gain ($Δ$BIC$=78.6$), whereas a mechanical VIX proxy alone does not improve the fit. Autocorrelation-matched placebo fields fail ($Δ$BIC$_{\max}=2.7$), disjoint weekly reconstructions still favor the field-coupled model ($Δ$BIC$=140$--$151$), and six anchored chronological holdouts preserve the out-of-sample advantage. Quiet-regime and field-stripped residual autocorrelation controls show the same collapse of persistence. Stronger hidden-variable extensions remain only partially supported. Within the tested stochastic class, conditioning on the observed VIX proxy absorbs most of the apparent slow dynamics.

</details>

### [81] [Nahm Poles and 0-Instantons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13805)
*Marco Usula*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了渐近双曲4-流形上的自对偶0-联络（0-瞬子），证明了其渐近展开的对数光滑性，并发现首个对数项的系数（0-瞬子阻碍张量）是一个与背景共形度量的Weyl曲率相关的共形不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于对渐近双曲4-流形上自对偶0-联络（0-instantons）的渐近行为分析。这些联络在共形无穷远处发展出均匀奇异性，并在边界点处渐近于$H^4$上的"Nahm pole"模型解。

Method: 方法受到Poincaré-Einstein度量的Fefferman-Graham展开启发，研究这些0-瞬子的渐近展开。通过分析渐近展开的对数光滑性，识别出首个对数项的系数作为关键不变量。

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了渐近展开是对数光滑的；首个对数项的系数（称为0-瞬子阻碍张量）是与背景共形度量的Weyl曲率相关的共形不变量；该不变量消失当且仅当0-瞬子在规范变换下光滑。

Conclusion: 研究还表明，如果度量在三级近似下渐近于Poincaré-Einstein度量，则重整化Yang-Mills能量是明确定义的共形不变量，且等于共形无穷远处的负Chern-Simons不变量。

Abstract: We study self-dual 0-connections, or 0-instantons, on asymptotically hyperbolic 4-manifolds. These connections develop a uniform singularity along the conformal infinity, and are asymptotic, at each point of the boundary, to a "Nahm pole" model solution on $H^4$. Examples include the Levi-Civita spin connections on $S^+$ over spin Poincaré-Einstein 4-manifolds. Inspired by the Fefferman-Graham expansion for Poincaré-Einstein metrics, we study the asymptotic expansion of these 0-instantons. We prove that the expansion is log-smooth, and that the coefficient of the first log term - which we call the 0-instanton obstruction tensor - is a conformal invariant related to the Weyl curvature of the ambient conformal metric. We then show that this invariant vanishes if and only if the 0-instanton is smooth modulo gauge. Finally, we study the renormalized Yang-Mills energy: we prove that, if the metric is asymptotically Poincaré-Einstein to third order, then this energy is a well-defined conformal invariant, and equals the negative Chern-Simons invariant of the conformal infinity.

</details>

### [82] [Shapes are not enough: CONSERVAttack and its use for finding vulnerabilities and uncertainties in machine learning applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13970)
*Philip Bechtle,Lucie Flek,Philipp Alexander Jung,Akbar Karimi,Timo Saala,Alexander Schmidt,Matthias Schott,Philipp Soldin,Christopher Wiebusch,Ulrich Willemsen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CONSERVAttack的新型对抗攻击方法，旨在利用高能物理（high energy physics）中模拟与数据之间未被标准验证检测到的剩余偏差空间，同时提出了相应的防御策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管高能物理实验中对物理系统不确定性（systematic uncertainties）进行了严格测试，并通过控制区域（control regions）进行数据与模拟的分布比较，但物理动机的指导和特定区域限制并不能保证所有可能的偏差来源都被考虑。因此需要探索剩余偏差空间对机器学习输出的影响。

Method: 提出CONSERVAttack对抗攻击方法，该方法在不确定性界限内生成一致的对抗扰动（adversarial perturbations），能够规避标准验证检查，同时成功欺骗底层模型。该方法专门针对模拟与数据之间假设性偏差的剩余空间进行攻击。

Result: CONSERVAttack生成的对抗扰动能够在不确定性界限内保持一致，成功规避标准验证检查，同时有效欺骗底层机器学习模型。这揭示了现有验证框架中存在的潜在漏洞。

Conclusion: 在粒子物理（particle physics）中解释深度学习结果时，必须考虑对抗效应（adversarial effects）的鲁棒性。作者进一步提出了缓解此类漏洞的策略，强调了对抗鲁棒性在科学应用中的重要性。

Abstract: In High Energy Physics, as in many other fields of science, the application of machine learning techniques has been crucial in advancing our understanding of fundamental phenomena. Increasingly, deep learning models are applied to analyze both simulated and experimental data. In most experiments, a rigorous regime of testing for physically motivated systematic uncertainties is in place. The numerical evaluation of these tests for differences between the data on the one side and simulations on the other side quantifies the effect of potential sources of mismodelling on the machine learning output. In addition, thorough comparisons of marginal distributions and (linear) feature correlations between data and simulation in "control regions" are applied. However, the guidance by physical motivation, and the need to constrain comparisons to specific regions, does not guarantee that all possible sources of deviations have been accounted for. We therefore propose a new adversarial attack - the CONSERVAttack - designed to exploit the remaining space of hypothetical deviations between simulation and data after the above mentioned tests. The resulting adversarial perturbations are consistent within the uncertainty bounds - evading standard validation checks - while successfully fooling the underlying model. We further propose strategies to mitigate such vulnerabilities and argue that robustness to adversarial effects must be considered when interpreting results from deep learning in particle physics.

</details>


### [83] [Thermal Robustness of Retrieval in Dense Associative Memories: LSE vs LSR Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13350)
*Tatiana Petrova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛模拟探索了两种连续稠密联想记忆（DAMs）在热噪声下的检索相边界，揭示了LSE和LSR核函数在有限温度下的不同行为特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解稠密联想记忆（dense associative memories）的检索能力是否能在热噪声下存活，对于将零温度容量证明与实际推理和生物计算的有限温度条件联系起来至关重要。

Method: 使用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）在N-球面上映射两种连续稠密联想记忆的检索相边界：log-sum-exp（LSE）核和log-sum-ReLU（LSR）核，存储模式数量为指数级M = e^{αN}。

Result: 两种核函数共享零温度临界负载α_c(0)=0.5，但有限温度行为显著不同：LSE核在足够低负载下可在任意高温下维持检索，而LSR核存在有限支持阈值，低于该阈值时在任何温度下都能完美检索。

Conclusion: 对于典型锐度值，LSR核的支持阈值接近α_c，使得在整个负载范围内检索几乎完美；研究还比较了测量平衡对齐与检索盆地内分析玻尔兹曼预测的一致性。

Abstract: Understanding whether retrieval in dense associative memories survives thermal noise is essential for bridging zero-temperature capacity proofs with the finite-temperature conditions of practical inference and biological computation. We use Monte Carlo simulations to map the retrieval phase boundary of two continuous dense associative memories (DAMs) on the $N$-sphere with an exponential number of stored patterns $M = e^{αN}$: a log-sum-exp (LSE) kernel and a log-sum-ReLU (LSR) kernel. Both kernels share the zero-temperature critical load $α_c(0)=0.5$, but their finite-temperature behavior differs markedly. The LSE kernel sustains retrieval at arbitrarily high temperatures for sufficiently low load, whereas the LSR kernel exhibits a finite support threshold below which retrieval is perfect at any temperature; for typical sharpness values this threshold approaches $α_c$, making retrieval nearly perfect across the entire load range. We also compare the measured equilibrium alignment with analytical Boltzmann predictions within the retrieval basin.

</details>


### [84] [Geometric and Topological Deep Learning for Predicting Thermo-mechanical Performance in Cold Spray Deposition Process Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14478)
*Akshansh Mishra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于几何深度学习（geometric deep learning）的框架，用于预测冷喷涂（cold spray）粒子冲击响应。该框架利用有限元模拟数据，通过四种新颖算法（GraphSAGE、ChebSpectral、TDA-MLP、GAT）在特征空间图中建模，其中GraphSAGE和GAT在多数目标上取得了R平方值超过0.93的优异性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在开发一个高效的代理模型（surrogate model），用于预测冷喷涂工艺中粒子冲击的复杂响应。传统有限元模拟计算成本高昂，需要一种能够快速准确预测关键输出参数的方法，以优化冷喷涂工艺参数。

Method: 研究采用几何深度学习框架，基于自动化的Abaqus有限元模拟生成参数化数据集，涵盖粒子速度、粒子温度和摩擦系数的系统范围。实现了四种新颖算法：GraphSAGE风格的归纳图神经网络（inductive graph neural network）、Chebyshev谱图卷积网络（Chebyshev spectral graph convolution network）、拓扑数据分析增强的多层感知器（topological data analysis augmented multilayer perceptron）和几何注意力网络（geometric attention network）。每个输入样本在k最近邻特征空间图中被视为节点，使模型能够利用训练过程中工艺条件之间的空间相似性。

Result: 三维特征空间可视化和二维等高线投影证实了输入输出关系具有高度非线性和速度主导特性。定量评估显示，GraphSAGE和GAT在大多数目标上持续获得超过0.93的R平方值，其中GAT在最大塑性应变预测中达到峰值性能（R平方等于0.97）。ChebSpectral和TDA-MLP表现明显较差，在多个目标上产生负的R平方值。

Conclusion: 这些发现确立了基于空间图的邻域聚合（spatial graph-based neighbourhood aggregation）作为一种稳健且物理可解释的代理建模策略，适用于冷喷涂工艺优化。该方法能够有效捕捉工艺参数与冲击响应之间的复杂关系，为工艺参数选择提供高效预测工具。

Abstract: This study presents a geometric deep learning framework for predicting cold spray particle impact responses using finite element simulation data. A parametric dataset was generated through automated Abaqus simulations spanning a systematic range of particle velocity, particle temperature, and friction coefficient, yielding five output targets including maximum equivalent plastic strain, average contact plastic strain, maximum temperature, maximum von Mises stress, and deformation ratio. Four novel algorithms i.e. a GraphSAGE-style inductive graph neural network, a Chebyshev spectral graph convolution network, a topological data analysis augmented multilayer perceptron, and a geometric attention network were implemented and evaluated. Each input sample was treated as a node in a k-nearest-neighbour feature-space graph, enabling the models to exploit spatial similarity between process conditions during training. Three-dimensional feature space visualisations and two-dimensional contour projections confirmed the highly non-linear and velocity-dominated nature of the input-output relationships. Quantitative evaluation demonstrated that GraphSAGE and GAT consistently achieved R-square values exceeding 0.93 across most targets, with GAT attaining peak performance of R-square equal to 0.97 for maximum plastic strain. ChebSpectral and TDA-MLP performed considerably worse, yielding negative R-square values for several targets. These findings establish spatial graph-based neighbourhood aggregation as a robust and physically interpretable surrogate modelling strategy for cold spray process optimisation.

### [85] [Coupled Space Weathering: Nanophase Iron Formation by Micrometeoroid Impact and Solar Wind Sputtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14839)
*Ziyu Huang,Masatoshi Hirabayashi*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 本研究通过反应分子动力学模拟和表面结合能分析，揭示了微陨石撞击与太阳风辐照在月球表面风化过程中的耦合效应，阐明了纳米相金属铁（npFe⁰）簇形成机制及其对月球表面光学和成分成熟度的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解微陨石撞击与太阳风辐照之间的相互作用对于解释月球表面演化至关重要。这两种主导的空间风化过程如何共同影响月球表面需要深入研究。

Method: 采用反应分子动力学模拟（reactive molecular dynamics simulations）和表面结合能分析（surface binding energy analyses），研究这两种空间风化过程对由Fe₂SiO₄组成的月球风化层的耦合效应。

Result: 微陨石撞击显著改变月球表面结构，在微陨石坑形态中形成具有不同表面结合能的结构异质区域。微陨石坑底部因高密度压实而增强表面凝聚力，而坑壁和溅射物则显示结构弱化。应用Sigmund溅射理论表明Fe、Si和O的差异溅射产率，支持纳米相金属铁（npFe⁰）簇的形成和生长。

Conclusion: 选择性溅射机制支持纳米相金属铁（npFe⁰）簇的形成和生长，影响月球表面的光学和成分成熟度。这些发现推进了对月球空间风化过程的理解。

Abstract: Understanding the interplay between micrometeoroid impacts and solar wind irradiation is crucial for interpreting lunar surface evolution. Using reactive molecular dynamics simulations and surface binding energy (SBE) analyses, this study investigates the coupled effects of these two dominant space weathering processes on lunar regolith composed of Fe$_2$SiO$_4$. Our simulations reveal that micrometeoroid impacts significantly modify the lunar surface, creating structurally heterogeneous zones with varying SBEs across microcrater morphologies. Specifically, microcrater floors exhibit enhanced surface cohesion due to high-density compaction, whereas microcrater walls and ejecta show weakened structures. Applying Sigmund's sputtering theory with these SBEs indicates differential sputtering yields for Fe, Si, and O suggesting preferential retention of heavier elements like Fe. This selective sputtering mechanism supports the formation and growth of nanophase metallic iron (npFe$^0$) clusters, influencing the optical and compositional maturation of the lunar surface. These findings advance our understanding of lunar space weathering processes.
