### [86] [A numerical framework for Newtonian-noise estimation at the Einstein Telescope: 2-D simulations beyond the plane-wave approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15424)
*Patrick Schillings,Shi Yao,Johannes Erdmann,Andreas Rietbrock*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个基于谱元法（spectral-element）模拟地震波场的数值框架，用于精确估计爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）的牛顿噪声（Newtonian noise）。该框架在二维均匀介质中验证了与解析解的吻合性，并应用于30个随机表面源阵列，发现P波占比显著低于常规假设，为牛顿噪声抑制提供了新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）作为第三代地下引力波观测站，其低频灵敏度（1.7-6 Hz频段）预计将受到牛顿噪声（Newtonian noise）的限制。现有估计多基于均匀或分层介质的解析或半解析模型，忽略了地质异质性和复杂波相互作用，因此需要更精确的数值方法。

Method: 本研究提出了一个基于谱元法（spectral-element）模拟地震波场的数值框架。首先在二维均匀介质中使用单一表面源进行概念验证，将数值结果与解析平面波预测进行基准测试；随后扩展模型至30个随机表面源阵列，以近似稳态环境地震激发。

Result: 在均匀介质基准测试中，数值结果与解析预测在体波（bulk）和洞穴（cavern）贡献方面均表现出优异的一致性。更重要的是，在简单均匀情况下，模拟波场推断的P波（P-wave）占比显著低于常规假设值，这表明牛顿噪声抑制的前景可能比预期更好。

Conclusion: 该数值框架可直接应用于三维模拟，并能整合详细局部地震模型和地形数据，为特定场址的牛顿噪声估计提供了强大潜力。研究结果表明，通过更精确的波场模拟可以重新评估牛顿噪声水平，为未来引力波观测站的优化设计提供重要参考。

Abstract: The Einstein Telescope (ET) is a third-generation underground gravitational-wave observatory designed to extend the detection sensitivity down to a few Hertz. Newtonian noise is expected to limit the low-frequency sensitivity of ET, particularly in the 1.7-6 Hz band. Most existing estimates rely on analytical or semi-analytical models assuming homogeneous or layered media, neglecting geological heterogeneity and complex wave interactions. In this work, we present a numerical framework for Newtonian-noise estimation based on spectral-element simulations of a seismic wave field. As a proof of concept, we first benchmark the numerical results against analytical plane-wave predictions in a two-dimensional homogeneous medium with a single surface source, demonstrating excellent agreement for both bulk and cavern contributions. We then extend the model to an array of 30 stochastic surface sources to approximate stationary ambient seismic excitation. The P-wave fraction inferred from the simulated wave field is, in this simple homogeneous case, significantly lower than commonly assumed, indicating enhanced prospects for Newtonian-noise mitigation. The framework is readily applicable to three-dimensional simulations and to integration of detailed local seismic models and topography, offering strong potential for site-specific Newtonian-noise estimation.

This review describes the physics of detection, detailing the noise models and cross-correlation techniques required to isolate the Hellings-Downs curve. We discuss astrophysical implications, arguing that the perceived tension between current amplitudes and standard merger models is largely resolved by new insights into supermassive black hole binary populations. Beyond the stochastic background, we review the framework for multi-messenger continuous gravitational-wave searches, highlighting targeted search campaigns and rigorous detection protocols. We also examine the potential to probe New Physics, including cosmic strings and ultralight dark matter. Critical challenges are addressed, including small-scale leakage bias in anisotropy searches and the separation of deterministic signals from the GWB and pulsar noise. Finally, we outline the field's future, from rapid data combination strategies to the sensitivity gains expected from the Square Kilometre Array Observatory (SKAO) and DSA-2000.

### [88] [Informational corrections to the early-Universe radiation sector: CET Omega, WIMP freeze-out, and implications for a possible 20 GeV gamma-ray excess](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15205)
*Christian Balfagon*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Fermi-LAT伽马射线超量（gamma-ray excess）对CET Omega理论的影响，该理论预测了早期宇宙辐射能量密度的双重对数修正（doubly logarithmic correction），这种修正会影响弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）的热冻结（thermal freeze-out）过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fermi-LAT数据中发现的近球形晕状伽马射线超量（peaking at E_gamma ~ 20 GeV）可能源自暗物质湮灭（dark matter annihilation），这为探测热冻结时期（thermal freeze-out epoch）及早期宇宙膨胀率的非标准修正提供了直接观测窗口。

Method: 从理论的模量两点函数（modular two-point function）推导出修正项，论证信息扇区（informational sector）相关的起始尺度，并通过数值解计算其对冻结过程的影响；同时分析信息场Phi_Omega(x)的演化。

Result: 修正导致遗迹丰度（relic abundance）产生百分比级别的偏移，并对湮灭伽马射线通量（annihilation gamma-ray flux）的形态产生亚百分比级别的修正；参数范围10^{-4} < alpha_log < 10^{-2}与Planck、BBN和BAO约束一致，同时预测了下一代MeV-GeV任务可观测的伽马射线形态偏差。

Conclusion: CET Omega理论预测的宇宙早期辐射能量密度修正（源于重整化模量涨落，renormalized modular fluctuations）在热WIMP冻结时期变得显著，与现有宇宙学观测兼容，并为未来伽马射线观测提供了可检验的预测。

Abstract: Recent analyses of Fermi-LAT data have identified a nearly spherical, halo-like excess of gamma rays peaking at E_gamma ~ 20 GeV. If interpreted as dark matter annihilation, the excess directly probes the thermal freeze-out epoch and therefore any non-standard corrections to the early-Universe expansion rate. In this work we examine the implications of this tentative signal for CET Omega, an informational and modular extension of relativistic quantum field theory and cosmology. CET Omega predicts a universal state-dependent modification to the radiation energy density of the early Universe, characterized by a doubly logarithmic correction originating from renormalized modular fluctuations in the spectral triple of the theory. The correction is negligible during Big Bang nucleosynthesis and recombination but becomes relevant during thermal WIMP freeze-out. We derive the correction from the modular two-point function, justify the onset scale associated with the informational sector, and compute its quantitative impact on freeze-out through numerical solutions. We also analyze the evolution of the informational field Phi_Omega(x) and show that it freezes in before the freeze-out epoch and survives to the present time under gravitational advection. The resulting modification induces percent-level shifts in the relic abundance and sub-percent morphological corrections to the annihilation gamma-ray flux. We compare the scenario with Early Dark Energy, kination, and varying N_eff models, and show that the parameter range 10^{-4} < alpha_log < 10^{-2} remains consistent with Planck, BBN, and BAO constraints while predicting potentially observable deviations in the gamma-ray morphology accessible to next-generation MeV-GeV missions.

</details>


### [89] [Reconnection-driven State Transitions in Flat Spectrum Radio Quasars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14305)
*Agniva Roychowdhury*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究将Roychowdhury (2026)关于FSRQs对数流量偏度变化的工作扩展到18个FSRQs样本，发现可分为三类：大耀斑后偏度持续降低、无显著变化、变化不显著。通过统计性等离子体团模型模拟，发现系统熵在偏度变化时降低，表明耀斑增加了系统有序度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在扩展先前关于FSRQs（平谱射电类星体）对数流量偏度变化的研究，通过更大样本验证耀斑驱动的统计特性变化。同时为观测结果提供理论解释基础，探索耀斑产生机制及其对系统有序度的影响。

Method: 采用Fermo等人(2010)的统计性等离子体团模型（statistical plasmoid model），该模型通过合并过程自洽地产生大型等离子体团。进行1500次模拟运行，并下采样至18个以统计复现观测分布。计算系统集合香农熵（ensemble Shannon entropy）和功率谱密度（power spectral densities）。

Result: 18个FSRQs可分为三类：偏度持续降低、无显著变化、变化不显著。模拟下采样能统计复现观测的p值分布。系统熵在偏度变化组中均以3σ水平降低，表明耀斑增加了系统有序度。模拟光变曲线功率谱密度呈现断裂幂律（broken-power-laws），符合已知耀变体变异性特征。

Conclusion: 耀变体喷流内的随机性等离子体团模拟能自洽复现耀变体GeV光变曲线的关键可观测统计特性。结果对多个基准参数200-300%的变化具有鲁棒性，为耀斑产生机制及其对系统统计特性影响提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We extend the work of Roychowdhury (2026) on skewness variations of the logarithmic flux, driven by large GeV flares in FSRQs, to a sample of 18 FSRQs. We find that they can be categorized into three groups, one where the skewness attains a persistent lower value after a large flare, one where it does not, and those where change in skewness is not significant. To provide a theoretical ground for these results, we use the statistical plasmoid model of Fermo et al. (2010) that self-consistently produces large plasmoids through merging which, when gain energy from the reconnection event and are Doppler aligned, produce large flares. We find that a downsampling of our simulation of 1500 runs to 18 statistically reproduces the observed distribution in p-values for change in skewness. We further compute the ensemble Shannon entropy of the system and the skewness, where the entropy is found to decrease at a $3σ$ level in both the groups where skewness either increases or decreases, as a direct evidence of increase in order in the system caused by a flare. We find that the power spectral densities of the simulated light curves are broken-power-laws, resembling a white noise+red noise broken by the typical cooling timescale in our system, in accordance with known blazar variability. We find that our results are robust to a $200-300\%$ change in several fiducial parameters of the simulation. Our stochastic simulation of plasmoids inside a blazar jet self-consistently reproduces key observable statistical properties of blazar GeV light curves.

### [90] [Diverse communities promote the coexistence of closely-related strains through emergent equalization and stabilization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15052)
*Naven Narayanan Venkatanarayanan,Akshit Goyal*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 该研究结合群落生态学和统计物理学，揭示了在多样化微生物群落中，菌株共存受到群落介导的间接相互作用影响，这些相互作用产生均衡化和稳定化机制，促进菌株共存并改变其丰度相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微生物群落中存在广泛的精细尺度多样性：同一物种的密切相关的菌株与许多远缘类群共存，但菌株共存机制仍不清楚，主要因为大多数研究忽略了菌株所处的多样化群落环境。

Method: 结合群落生态学（community ecology）和统计物理学（statistical physics）来研究群落背景下的密切相关的菌株动态，并运用现代共存理论（modern coexistence theory）分析菌株间的相互作用机制。

Result: 在多样化群落中，菌株间通过周围群落成员介导的间接相互作用（indirect interactions）与直接相互作用同样强烈，这些群落介导的反馈（community-mediated feedbacks）使同种菌株表现出相关生长速率和减少的竞争。

Conclusion: 菌株动态是周围群落的涌现结果，捕捉群落反馈不需要完整的相互作用网络，仅需少量涌现参数（emergent parameters）；均衡化和稳定化机制共同促进菌株共存，并定性转变菌株丰度相关性。

Abstract: Microbial communities harbor extensive fine-scale diversity: closely-related strains of the same species coexist alongside many distantly-related taxa. Yet strain coexistence remains poorly understood, largely because most studies neglect the diverse communities in which strains are embedded. Here we combine community ecology and statistical physics to study the dynamics of closely-related strains in a community context. We demonstrate that in a diverse community, indirect interactions between strains -- mediated through the surrounding community members -- can be as strong as direct ones. These community-mediated feedbacks cause conspecific strains to behave as if they have correlated growth rates and reduced competition. Using modern coexistence theory, we show that these effects correspond to equalizing and stabilizing mechanisms which together promote strain coexistence. The same equalizing and stabilizing mechanisms also qualitatively transform strain abundance correlations: strains that compete strongly and show negative correlations in isolation instead show positive correlations in a community, appearing mutualistic despite being competitors. Our results demonstrate that strain dynamics are emergent consequences of the surrounding community, and that capturing community feedbacks does not require the full interaction network; only a small number of emergent parameters.

### [91] [The Chandrasekhar's Conditions as Equilibrium and Stability of Stars in a Universal Three-Parameter Non-Maxwell Distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15060)
*Wei Hu,Jiulin Du*

Main category: astro-ph.SR

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了钱德拉塞卡（Chandrasekhar）关于恒星平衡与稳定的条件，通过引入新的普适三参数非麦克斯韦分布（non-Maxwell distribution），推导了气体恒星和中心凝聚恒星的最大辐射压力，从而在麦克斯韦意义上推广了钱德拉塞卡条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在重新审视钱德拉塞卡（Chandrasekhar）关于恒星平衡与稳定的经典条件，通过引入更一般的非麦克斯韦分布来扩展这一理论框架，以探索更广泛的物理情形。

Method: 采用新的普适三参数非麦克斯韦分布（universal three-parameter non-Maxwell distribution），分别推导气体恒星（gas star）和中心凝聚恒星（centrally-condensed star）的最大辐射压力，并通过数值分析（numerical analyses）进行比较研究。

Result: 数值分析表明，与假设气体为麦克斯韦分布（Maxwellian distribution）的情况相比，非麦克斯韦分布通常会降低气体恒星和中心凝聚恒星的最大辐射压力（maximum radiation pressures）。

Conclusion: 研究成功推广了钱德拉塞卡条件，证明非麦克斯韦分布对恒星平衡与稳定性条件有显著影响，通常导致更低的辐射压力极限，从而扩展了经典恒星结构理论。

Abstract: The idea of the Chandrasekhar's conditions as equilibrium and stability of stars is revisited with a new universal three-parameter non-Maxwell distribution. We derive the maximum radiation pressures in the non-Maxwell distribution for a gas star and a centrally-condensed star, respectively, and thus we generalize the Chandrasekhar's conditions in a Maxwellian sense. By numerical analyses, we find that the non-Maxwellian distribution usually reduces the maximum radiation pressures in both a gas star and a central condensed star as compared with that cases if the gas is assumed to be a Maxwellian distribution.

### [92] [Adaptive tensor train metadynamics for high-dimensional free energy exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13549)
*Nils E. Strand,Siyao Yang,Yuehaw Khoo,Aaron R. Dinner*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: TT-Metadynamics通过将元动力学（metadynamics）中的高斯函数和压缩为低秩张量列车（tensor train）表示，实现了在多维集体变量（collective variables）下的高效自由能采样，计算成本随变量数量线性增长而非指数增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子动力学模拟面临的关键挑战是在相关集体变量（collective variables, CVs）上高效探索自由能景观。传统增强采样方法在超过少数几个CVs时变得极其低效，特别是广泛使用的元动力学方法，其评估和存储偏置势（bias potential）的计算成本随维度数量呈指数增长。

Method: 本文提出TT-Metadynamics方法，将原始元动力学方法中累积的高斯函数和周期性地压缩为低秩张量列车（tensor train, TT）表示。该方法采用"sketching"算法构建TT表示，计算成本随CVs数量呈线性增长，而非指数增长。

Result: 在包含多达14个CVs的基准系统中，TT-Metadynamics的准确性在长时间模拟中匹配或超过标准元动力学，特别是在具有高能垒（high barriers）的系统中。该方法实现了高效的内存使用，并防止了评估偏置势的计算成本随模拟时间增加。

Conclusion: TT-Metadynamics被确立为一种可扩展且有效的方法，用于计算作为多个CVs函数的自由能，解决了传统元动力学在多维空间中的计算效率瓶颈问题。

Abstract: A key challenge for molecular dynamics simulations is efficient exploration of free energy landscapes over relevant collective variables (CV). Common methods for enhancing sampling become prohibitively inefficient beyond only a few CVs; in the case of the widely-used metadynamics method, the computational cost of evaluating and storing the bias potential grows exponentially with the number of dimensions. Here, we introduce TT-Metadynamics, in which the accumulated sum of Gaussian functions in the original metadynamics method is periodically compressed into a low-rank tensor train (TT) representation. The TT enables efficient memory use and prevents the computational cost of evaluating the bias potential from increasing with simulation time. We present a "sketching" algorithm that allows us to construct the TT with linear scaling in the number of CVs. Applied to benchmark systems with up to 14 CVs, the accuracy of TT-Metadynamics matches or exceeds that of standard metadynamics in long simulations, particularly in systems with high barriers. These results establish TT-Metadynamics as a scalable and effective method for computing free energies that are functions of several CVs.

### [93] [Systematically Improvable Numerical Atomic Orbital Basis Using Contracted Truncated Spherical Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13995)
*Yike Huang,Zuxin Jin,Linfeng Zhang,Mohan Chen,Rui Chen,Ling Li*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过截断球面波（TSW）收缩构建数值原子轨道（NAO）基组的新方案，用于密度泛函理论中的Kohn-Sham方程求解。该方案通过最小化剩余空间中动能算符的迹来优化基组，提高了基组的可转移性和精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）框架内求解Kohn-Sham方程，需要发展数值原子轨道（numerical atomic orbital, NAO）基组的构建方法。现有方法存在基组可转移性（transferability）有限的问题，特别是在描述导带（conduction band）时表现不足。

Method: 提出了一种基于截断球面波（truncated spherical waves, TSW）收缩构建NAO基组的方案。该方法通过最小化剩余空间中动能算符的迹来优化基组，推广了先前提出的溢出最小化方案（spillage minimizing scheme）。使用TSW而非平面波作为展开基，能更有效地桥接参考态与NAO，并消除周期性镜像间的虚假相互作用。

Result: 基准测试表明，所构建的NAO基组在分子和体相系统的多种性质计算中均达到满意精度，包括总能（total energy）、键长（bond length）、原子化能（atomization energy）、晶格常数（lattice constant）、内聚能（cohesive energy）、带隙（band gap）和能级对齐（energy-level alignment）。通过包含未占据态，该方法在描述导带时展现出显著改进的可转移性。

Conclusion: 该TSW收缩方案不仅继承了先前方法的系统性可改进性，而且通过使用TSW作为展开基，更有效地桥接了参考态与NAO，消除了周期性镜像间的虚假相互作用，从而通过包含广泛的参考态实现了更好的基组可转移性，特别是在描述导带方面表现出显著优势。

Abstract: To solve the Kohn-Sham equation within the framework of density functional theory, we develop a scheme to construct numerical atomic orbital (NAO) basis sets by contracting truncated spherical waves (TSWs). The contraction minimizes the trace of the kinetic operator in the residual space, generalizing the spillage minimizing scheme [M. Chen et al., J. Phys. Condens. Matter 22, 445501 (2010); P. Lin et al., Phys. Rev. B 103, 235131 (2021)]. In addition to the systematic improvability inherited from previous schemes, the use of TSW instead of plane waves as the expansion basis bridges reference states and NAOs more effectively, and eliminates spurious interactions between periodic images, thereby enabling better transferability through the inclusion of extensive reference states. Benchmarks demonstrate that the constructed NAO achieves satisfactory precision for various properties of both molecules and bulk systems, including total energy, bond length, atomization energy, lattice constant, cohesive energy, band gap, and energy-level alignment. By incorporating unoccupied states, the improved transferability in describing the conduction band is demonstrated to be effective and substantial.

### [95] [Stochastic Collision Theory of Magnetism in Radical Fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14677)
*Yoshiaki Uchida,Ryohei Kishi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子主方程模型揭示了随机分子碰撞如何决定浓自由基溶液宏观磁性的机制：一阶交换项在碰撞平均中归零，而二阶项作为有效铁磁耦合增强磁化，解释了与传统理论不符的实验现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决物理学基本问题：随机微观事件如何产生确定性宏观性质。具体针对浓自由基溶液，其中随机分子碰撞主导系统磁性，而传统理论无法解释实验观测到的偏离现象。

Method: 开发了浓自由基溶液的量子主方程（quantum master equation）模型，该模型基于随机分子碰撞描述系统动力学，通过统计平均分析交换相互作用对宏观磁性的影响。

Result: 理论揭示了一个简单机制：一阶交换贡献在碰撞平均中归零，而二阶项作为有效铁磁耦合（ferromagnetic coupling）存活下来，从而增强磁化。该模型成功捕捉了与传统理论偏离的实验观测趋势。

Conclusion: 由于该机制源于统计平均，可能适用于更广泛的软物质（soft matter）现象，包括液晶（liquid crystals）等系统，为微观随机性与宏观确定性之间的关联提供了新见解。

Abstract: How stochastic, microscopic events generate deterministic, macroscopic properties is a fundamental question in physics. We address this question by developing a quantum master equation model for concentrated radical solutions, where random molecular collisions govern the magnetic properties of the system. Our theory reveals a simple mechanism: the first-order exchange contribution averages to zero over collisions, while the second-order term survives as an effective ferromagnetic coupling that enhances magnetization. The model captures the experimentally observed trends in magnetic behavior that deviate from conventional theories. Because the mechanism arises from statistical averaging, it may apply to a broader class of soft matter phenomena, including liquid crystals.

### [96] [Lagrangian Identity and Mass Evolution of Particle-like Objects in Nonminimally Coupled Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13408)
*S. R. Pinto,P. P. Avelino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了Nambu-Goto p-膜拉格朗日量满足恒等式$\mathcal{L}_{\rm [\it p \rm]}=T_{\rm [\it p \rm]}/(p+1)$，其中$T_{\rm [\it p \rm]}$是能量-动量张量的迹。该关系独立于引力场性质，并探讨了其在$f(R,\mathcal{L}_{\rm m})$引力理论中对宇宙弦环动力学的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Nambu-Goto p-膜拉格朗日量与能量-动量张量迹之间的基本关系，并探索这一拉格朗日恒等式在修正引力理论中对宇宙弦环动力学的物理意义。

Method: 通过数学推导证明拉格朗日恒等式$\mathcal{L}_{\rm [\it p \rm]}=T_{\rm [\it p \rm]}/(p+1)$，并应用于$f(R,\mathcal{L}_{\rm m})$引力理论中均匀各向同性宇宙的非自相交宇宙弦环动力学分析。

Result: 证明了p-膜拉格朗日量与其能量-动量张量迹之间的维度依赖关系，并发现与广义相对论不同，在$f(R,\mathcal{L}_{\rm m})$引力中宇宙弦环的固有质量可在宇宙学时间尺度上演化，与其小尺寸或张力无关。

Conclusion: 拉格朗日恒等式$\mathcal{L}_{\rm [\it p \rm]}=T_{\rm [\it p \rm]}/(p+1)$具有普适性，独立于引力场性质。该关系在修正引力理论中导致宇宙弦环质量演化，并将分析扩展到$(N+1)$维Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker时空中的闭合p-膜。

Abstract: We show that the Lagrangian of a Nambu-Goto $p$-brane satisfies the identity $\mathcal{L}_{\rm [\it p \rm]}=T_{\rm [\it p \rm]}/(p+1)$, with $T_{\rm [\it p \rm]}$ denoting the trace of the corresponding energy-momentum tensor, independently of the properties of the gravitational field. While for $p=0$ this reduces to the standard $\mathcal{L}_{\rm [0]}=T_{\rm [0]}$ relation, which determines the on-shell Lagrangian of point particles and their fluids, more generally it depends explicitly on the $p$-brane dimensionality. We explore the implications of this Lagrangian identity for the dynamics of non-self-intersecting cosmic string loops in a homogeneous and isotropic universe within $f(R,\mathcal{L}_{\rm m})$ gravity, showing that, unlike in general relativity, the proper mass of a cosmic string loop may evolve over cosmological timescales regardless of its small size or tension. Finally, we extend the analysis to the more general case of closed $p$-branes in $(N+1)$-dimensional Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker spacetimes.

### [97] [A new approach to the calculation of extreme-mass-ratio inspirals with a spinning secondary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13482)
*Viktor Skoupý*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个实用高效的计算框架，用于在极端质量比旋进（EMRI）系统中纳入次级自旋效应至第一后绝热阶，显著简化了引力波通量计算，并证明了自旋诱导相位偏移的规范无关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端质量比旋进（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）是未来空间引力波探测器（如LISA）最有前景的源之一。为充分挖掘其科学潜力，需要对具有非零自旋的偏心进动双星系统进行高精度建模，以生成参数估计所需的引力波模板。

Method: 该工作引入了一个实用高效的计算框架，将次级自旋效应纳入完全一般、偏心且非赤道的EMRIs至第一后绝热阶。利用近期发现的Kerr时空中自旋体轨迹解析解，显著简化了相应渐近引力波通量的计算。基于最近证明的通量平衡定律，使用渐近Teukolsky振幅和文献中已有的纯测地线函数来表达运动常数（包括Carter-Rüdiger常数）的变化率。

Result: 该框架在近球形旋进情况下表现良好，证明了所得自旋诱导相位偏移具有规范无关性（gauge independent）。研究开发的代码以Wolfram Mathematica实现，并公开提供在KerrSpinningFluxes包中。

Conclusion: 该研究为处理具有次级自旋的完全一般、偏心、非赤道EMRIs系统提供了一个实用高效的计算框架，显著简化了引力波通量计算，并确保了自旋效应的规范无关性，为未来空间引力波探测器的科学分析提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are among the most promising sources for future space-based gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, such as LISA. To fully leverage the scientific potential, the GW templates required for parameter estimation must be modeled with high accuracy for eccentric precessing binary systems with nonzero spins. This work introduces a practical and efficient framework for incorporating the effects of secondary spin in fully generic, eccentric, and offequatorial EMRIs to the first postadiabatic order. We utilize recently found analytic solutions for the trajectories of spinning bodies in Kerr spacetime to significantly simplify the calculation of the corresponding asymptotic GW fluxes. Furthermore, thanks to the recently proven flux-balance laws, we show how to express the rates of change of the constants of motion, including the Carter-Rüdiger constant, using asymptotic Teukolsky amplitudes and purely geodesic functions that are already established in the literature. Finally, we show how this framework performs in the case of nearly-spherical inspirals and demonstrate that the resulting spin-induced phase shifts are gauge independent. A Wolfram Mathematica implementation of the code developed in this work is publicly available in the KerrSpinningFluxes package.

Abstract: We investigated a two-dimensional superfluid model immersed in a black hole spacetime and hypothesize that if a black hole collides with a thin superfluid film, it will trigger a topological phase transition within the superfluid, characterized by the production of vortex--antivortex pairs. We adapted the 2D XY model to a curved spacetime and elucidated the topological phase transition in response to variations in the black hole's temperature. Specializing the model to a Schwarzschild--de Sitter black hole, we found a proliferation of vortex--antivortex pairs close to the event and cosmological horizons.

### [99] [Totally geodesic null hypersurfaces and constancy of surface gravity in Finsler spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13551)
*Ettore Minguzzi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了芬斯勒时空（Finsler spacetimes）中的完全测地零超曲面（totally geodesic null hypersurfaces），证明了在零收敛条件（null convergence condition）和特定引力方程下，超曲面上的里奇1-形式（Ricci 1-form）为零，从而将洛伦兹情形的重要结果推广到洛伦兹-芬斯勒框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将洛伦兹几何中关于紧致完全测地零超曲面的重要结果推广到更一般的芬斯勒时空框架。由于表面引力（surface gravity）在某些物理语境中可解释为温度，其恒定性对应热力学第零定律，这为特定芬斯勒引力方程提供了有力的物理论证。

Method: 作者定义并研究了芬斯勒时空中的完全测地零超曲面，证明了在零收敛条件和特定引力方程χ_α=0下，超曲面上的里奇1-形式为零。文中引入了一种技巧，将洛伦兹-芬斯勒分析简化为纯粹的洛伦兹研究，从而能够推广已有结果。

Result: 在所述条件下，连通紧致完全测地零超曲面具有恒定的表面引力，并获得了进一步的拓扑分类结果。研究还探讨了从主导能量条件（dominant energy condition）推导这些结果的可能性，这一策略选择了一个优雅的统一方程。

Conclusion: 里奇1-形式的消失被选为真空引力方程。由于表面引力在某些语境中可解释为温度，其恒定性表达了热力学第零定律，本研究为某些特殊的芬斯勒引力方程提供了令人信服的物理论证。

Abstract: We define and study totally geodesic null hypersurfaces in Finsler spacetimes. We prove that the null convergence condition and a certain mild gravitational equation $χ_α=0$, imply the vanishing of the Ricci 1-form on the hypersurface. This makes it possible to extend to the Lorentz-Finsler setting essentially all notable results for compact totally geodesic null hypersurfaces that hold in the Lorentzian case. In fact, we introduce a trick that reduces the Lorentz-Finsler analysis to a purely Lorentzian study. As a result, it follows that, under the stated conditions, connected compact totally geodesic null hypersurfaces admit constant surface gravity. Further topological classification results are also obtained. The possibility of deriving these results from the dominant energy condition is also explored, this strategy selecting an elegant unifying equation. In any case the vanishing of the Ricci 1-form is selected as a vacuum gravitational equation. Since surface gravity can be interpreted as temperature in some contexts, and its constancy expresses the zeroth law of thermodynamics, the present work provides a compelling physical argument in favour of some special Finslerian gravitational equations.

### [100] [One-dimensional subspaces of the $SL(n,\mathbb{R})$ Chiral Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13623)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用chiral方程方法，通过假设g=g(ξ)的ansatz，其中ξ满足广义拉普拉斯方程，将chiral方程简化为矩阵方程，从而将微分方程问题转化为代数问题求解。

Result: 成功将(n+2)维爱因斯坦场方程分解为两个方程块：主块简化为SL(n,R)群上的chiral方程，辅助块简化为关于f和α的微分方程及其复共轭。

Conclusion: 该方法能够以简单方式选择具有所需物理性质的不同爱因斯坦场方程解，为高维引力理论提供了有效的解析求解框架。

Abstract: In this work we find solutions of the ($n+2$)-dimensional Einstein Field Equations (EFE) with $n$ commuting Killing vectors in vacuum. In the presence of $n$ Killing vectors, the EFE can be separated into blocks of equations. The main part can be summarized in the chiral equation $\ (αg_{, \bar{z}} g^{-1})_{, z} + \ (αg_{, z} g^{-1})_{, \bar{z}} = 0$ with $ g\in SL(n,\mathbb{R})$. The other block reduces to the differential equation $(\ln f α^{1-1/n})_{, z} = 1/2 αtr( g_{, z} g^{-1})^2$ and its complex conjugate. We use the ansatz $g = g(ξ) $, where $ξ$ satisfies a generalized Laplace equation, so the chiral equation reduces to a matrix equation that can be solved using algebraic methods, turning the problem of obtaining exact solutions for these complicated differential equations into an algebraic problem. The different EFE solutions can be chosen with desired physical properties in a simple way.

Abstract: Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) constitute a prime target for future space-based gravitational-wave observatories such as LISA. By modeling the transition from a hadronic phase to a quark core phase, we quantify the sudden change in the tidal deformability ($Λ$) of the secondary object. Utilizing the Teukolsky formalism and Post-Newtonian expansions, we derive a strict analytical scaling law for the accumulated dephasing. We demonstrate that the Kerr spin parameter $a$ and the critical phase transition orbital velocity $v_c$ significantly amplify the dephasing effect. Our analytical framework provides a robust tool for probing the non-perturbative QCD equation of state at high baryon densities using gravitational wave astronomy.

### [102] [Multi-Field Dilaton Screening Beyond the Thin-Shell Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13986)

Method: 采用解析论证和完全耦合的数值解方法，分析膨胀子与轴子场的相互作用。研究BBQ机制（通过选择最小能量构型来抑制外部标量荷）以及薄壳直觉在多场设置中的适用性。

Result: 识别出无需精细调节即可实现完全屏蔽的机制：轴子场的反作用通过BBQ机制抑制外部标量荷，使膨胀子的梯度抵消而非局域化。同时发现薄壳直觉在多场设置中不适用，轴子表面梯度可显著重塑膨胀子轮廓，使外部标量荷基本不变甚至增强。

Abstract: We analyse screening in multi-field scalar-tensor theories, focusing on systems with a dilaton coupled to matter and an axion with a dilaton-dependent kinetic term, in the presence of both planetary and stellar density profiles. Using analytic arguments and fully coupled numerical solutions, we identify a regime in which full screening for a dark-energy-light, effectively unpinned string-dilaton, can occur without fine-tuning. The backreaction of the dilaton's partnered axion field can suppress the exterior scalar charge by selecting a minimum-energy configuration (the BBQ mechanism), yielding robust screening for generic axion gradients. In this regime screening is achieved by cancelling the dilaton's gradient rather than localising it. This reduces the exterior scalar charge and allows for gravity tests in the solar system to be passed. We then show that the more familiar thin-shell intuition need not apply in the multi-field setting. Axion surface gradients can drastically reshape the dilaton profile and drive a more localised transition without generically suppressing the fifth force. The exterior charge can remain essentially unchanged or even be enhanced as the shell is made thinner by a kinetically coupled field. Multi-field two-derivative dynamics therefore decouple localisation in thin shells from screening, evade single-field no-go arguments, and reopen viable parameter space for cosmologically light dilaton-like scalars with strong couplings to matter.

### [103] [Further Results on Null and Force-free Electromagnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14046)
*Govind Menon,Rakshak Adhikari*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文扩展了无切力电动力学（FFE）的叶状结构方法，针对零FFE解的存在性建立了两个关键条件：零平均曲率的均分和场叶分布的完整性。证明了对于任意零测地线汇，总存在局部旋转满足均分条件，且无剪切零测地线汇足以保证零场叶叶状结构的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无切力电动力学（Force-Free Electrodynamics, FFE）为致密天体磁层的建模提供了稳健框架，其中电磁场能量密度主导周围等离子体。虽然已知每个零无切力场都拥有相关的二维零测地线叶状结构，但确定哪些零测地线汇能够支持无切力解仍是一个非平凡的计算挑战。

Method: 本文扩展了基于叶状结构的方法来处理零FFE，主要解决解存在性的两个障碍：零平均曲率（null mean curvature）的均分（equipartition）和场叶分布（field sheet distribution）的完整性（involutivity）。通过证明一般存在性定理，展示了对任意给定零测地线汇，总存在局部旋转满足均分条件。

Result: 证明了无剪切（shear-free）零测地线汇足以保证存在任意三元函数，其任意选择都将生成零场叶叶状结构。每个独特的叶状结构都与一个零无切力场相关联，该场进一步包含一个任意二元函数。这些结果与剪切张量（shear tensor）的消失形式关联，为零FFE解的存在性提供了坐标无关的几何判据。

Conclusion: 研究结果在史瓦西（Schwarzschild）和克尔（Kerr）几何中通过显式示例进行了说明，并在平直时空和C度规中提出了新的非平凡精确零解。这为零无切力电动力学解的存在性提供了系统的几何框架。

Abstract: The theory of Force-Free Electrodynamics (FFE) provides a robust framework for modeling the magnetospheres of compact objects, where the electromagnetic field's energy density dominates the surrounding plasma. Central to this theory is the existence of two-dimensional integral submanifolds, or field sheets, which foliate the spacetime. While it is established that every null force-free field possesses an associated 2-D null geodesic foliation, the converse, identifying which null geodesic congruences can support a force-free solution, remains a non-trivial computational challenge. In this paper, we extend the foliation-based approach to null FFE by addressing two primary obstacles to the existence of a solution: the equipartition of null mean curvature and the involutivity of the field sheet distribution. We prove a general existence theorem demonstrating that for any given null geodesic congruence, there always exists a local rotation of a 2-D basis transverse to the geodesic congruence that satisfies the equipartition condition. Furthermore, we establish that a shear-free null geodesic congruence is sufficient to guaranty the existence of an arbitrary function of three variables such that any choice of such a function will generate a null field sheet foliation. Additionally, each unique foliation will be associated with a null force-free field that further contains an arbitrary function of two variables. These results are formally linked to the vanishing of the shear tensor, providing a coordinate-independent geometric criterion for the existence of null FFE solutions. We illustrate these theorems with explicit examples in Schwarzschild and Kerr geometries and present new, non-trivial exact null solutions in flat spacetime and for the C-metric.

The Ehrenfest equations are analytically verified demonstrating that the critical behavior corresponds to a second order phase transition. Heat engines associated with these black holes are also constructed to examine how PFDM and BI parameters influence their efficiency. Finally we analyze the geodesic structure through timelike and null trajectories using the effective potential determining conditions for stable and unstable circular orbits the innermost stable circular orbit and the photon sphere. PFDM significantly modifies the orbital structure while BI corrections are weaker.

E. Zucker*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 利用LIGO第四轮观测数据，通过三种方法在全天范围内搜索连续引力波信号，未发现统计显著信号，但建立了迄今最严格的应变上限约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过分析LIGO第四轮观测数据，搜索银河系中旋转非轴对称孤立中子星可能发出的连续引力波信号，以探测这些致密天体的物理特性。

Method: 采用三种不同分析方法处理LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组第四轮观测的前八个月数据，覆盖20 Hz至2000 Hz频率范围，并允许高达$10^{-8}$ Hz/s的频率导数变化。

Result: 未发现统计显著的周期性引力波信号，但在290 Hz附近建立了最严格的人群平均应变上限9.7×10^{-26}，在250-1700 Hz范围内与先前最佳约束相当，在高频区域改进了约1.6倍。

Conclusion: 研究结果被应用于三个天体物理场景：银河系中子星的自旋频率与椭率分布、毫秒脉冲星对银河中心GeV超量的贡献，以及小行星质量级原始双黑洞作为暗物质组分的可能性。

Abstract: We present results from an all-sky search for continuous gravitational waves, using three different methods applied to the first eight months of LIGO data from the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration s observing run. We aim at signals potentially emitted by rotating, non-axisymmetric isolated neutron star in the Milky Way. The analysis spans a frequency range from 20 Hz to 2000 Hz and accommodates frequency derivative magnitudes up to $10^{-8}$ Hz/s. No statistically significant periodic gravitational wave signals were detected. We establish 95% confidence-level (CL) frequentist upper limits on the dimensionless strain amplitudes. The most stringent population-averaged strain upper limits reach 9.7 $\times$ $10^{-26}$ near 290 Hz, matching the best previous constraints from 250 to $\sim$1700 Hz while extending coverage to a much broader spin-down range. At higher frequencies, the new limits improve upon previous results by factors of approximately $\sim$1.6. These constraints are applied to three astrophysical scenarios: 1) the distribution of galactic neutron stars as a function of spin frequency and ellipticity; 2) the contribution of millisecond pulsars to the GeV excess near the galactic center; and 3) the possible dark matter fraction composed of nearby inspiraling primordial binary black holes with asteroid-scale masses.

### [106] [CETOmega: The Causal-Informational Completion of Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14200)
*Christian Balfagon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: CETOmega是一个通过因果信息原理完成引力的统一框架，在严格四维、非局域和因果的表述中调和广义相对论与量子力学。该理论引入texon标量场作为因果连通性的有效激发，同时解释暗物质和暗能量，无需额外自由度或破坏局域性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立一个统一框架，通过因果信息原理完成引力理论，调和广义相对论（general relativity）与量子力学（quantum mechanics）之间的矛盾。研究试图在严格四维、非局域（nonlocal）和因果（causal）的表述中实现这一目标。

Method: 核心方法基于离散因果网络（discrete causal network）导出的解析延迟核K^-1(Box_R)，该核控制引力场和标量场的传播。理论引入texon标量场作为因果连通性的有效激发，该场同时解释暗物质（dark matter）和暗能量（dark energy），无需引入额外自由度或破坏局域性。

Result: 该形式体系确保了解析性（analyticity）、谱正性（spectral positivity）和全息完备性（holographic completeness）。核函数具有Stieltjes表示和正谱密度rho(mu)≥0，保证了幺正性（unitarity）和因果传播。在宇宙学尺度上，CETOmega预测了与Planck观测一致的稳定暴胀动力学。黑洞（black hole）振铃频率获得由因果尺度控制的微扰修正，在基准窗口l*（10^-5至10^-4米）内对天体物理黑洞保持次要影响。

Conclusion: CETOmega为时空动力学提供了一个完备、因果和信息的理论基础，在红外（infrared）极限下恢复爱因斯坦引力，同时将其有效性扩展到量子领域和宇宙学领域。该框架通过因果信息原理统一了引力描述，解决了暗物质和暗能量问题。

Abstract: We present CETOmega, a unified framework that completes gravity through a causal-informational principle. The theory reconciles general relativity and quantum mechanics within a strictly four-dimensional, nonlocal, and causal formulation. At its core lies an analytic and retarded kernel K^-1(Box_R), derived from a discrete causal network, which governs the propagation of the gravitational and scalar sectors. A scalar field, the texon, emerges as the effective excitation of causal connectivity and accounts simultaneously for dark matter and dark energy without introducing extra degrees of freedom or breaking locality.
  The formalism ensures analyticity, spectral positivity, and holographic completeness. The kernel admits a Stieltjes representation with positive spectral density rho(mu) greater than or equal to zero, guaranteeing unitarity and causal propagation. At cosmological scales, CETOmega predicts stable inflationary dynamics consistent with Planck observations. Black hole ringdown frequencies acquire perturbative corrections controlled by the causal scale and remain subleading for astrophysical black holes within the fiducial window l* between 10^-5 and 10^-4 meters, where l* defines the mean causal correlation length of the texonic field.
  CETOmega thus provides a complete, causal, and informational foundation for spacetime dynamics, recovering Einstein gravity in the infrared while extending its validity to the quantum and cosmological domains.

</details>


### [107] [Isomorphism between the local Poincare generalized translations group and the group of spacetime transformations (x LB1)4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14364)
*Alcides Garat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了庞加莱子群中的平移（translations）与先前研究中引入的LB1标架变换群之间存在直接关系，并将这一结果推广到局部平移（local translations）情形，其中邦迪-梅茨纳-萨克斯（Bondi-Metzner-Sachs）超平移（supertranslations）是其特例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立平移群与LB1标架变换群之间的直接关系，并推广到局部平移情形。平移群在规范理论（gauge theories）中已被广泛研究，而LB1群由SO(1;1)和两类离散变换组成，这种关系的建立具有非平凡意义。

Method: 方法包括：证明四维平移群同构于(x LB1)⁴；引入涉及阿贝尔（Abelian）、非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）、旋量（spinor）和引力场的微分方程组；构建新型局部标架（local tetrads）以简化证明过程，并利用先前获得的类似标架结果。

Result: 主要结果是证明了平移群与LB1群之间的直接关系，并成功推广到局部平移情形。特别地，邦迪-梅茨纳-萨克斯超平移子群（Bondi-Metzner-Sachs subgroup of supertranslations）作为局部平移的特例被纳入该框架。

Conclusion: 结论表明平移群与LB1标架变换群之间存在非平凡的对应关系，且这一关系可推广至局部平移。该结果为理解平移变换与标架结构之间的深层联系提供了新的几何框架，其中LB1群的特殊组成（SO(1;1)加离散变换）在这一对应中起关键作用。

Abstract: We will prove that there is a direct relationship between the Poincare subgroup of translations, and the group of tetrad transformations LB1 introduced in a previous manuscript. LB1 is the group composed by SO(1; 1) plus two kinds of discrete transformations. Translations have been extensively studied under the scope of gauge theories. By using the geometric structures built to prove this elementary result we will generalize it to the case of what we might call local translations. A special case of the latter is the Bondi-Metzner-Sachs subgroup of supertranslations. In order to accomplish this goal and since the group of translations is four-dimensional we will prove first that it is isomorphic to (x LB1)4. In order to prove this claim we will introduce a system of differential equations involving several kinds of fields. Abelian, non-Abelian, spinor, gravitational. These fields will constitute the structure needed to build local tetrads of a new kind that allow for the proof to be carried out with simplicity. Results already obtained involving similar but not equal tetrads will be useful in our constructions and demonstrations. Translations and generalized translations isomorphic to tensor products of LB1 groups are not trivial results. Because the LB1 group is composed by SO(1; 1) and two discrete transformations.

</details>


### [108] [Periodic orbits and gravitational waveforms of black holes in bumblebee gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14413)
*Zijian Shi,Xiangdong Zhang,Yunlong Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力框架下，研究黑洞时空中大质量粒子的动力学及其引力波形。分析表明，洛伦兹对称性破缺参数l和电荷Q显著影响束缚轨道参数空间，并在未带电情况下与史瓦西黑洞存在潜在可观测的周期性轨道差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力（Einstein-Bumblebee gravity）框架下黑洞时空中大质量粒子的动力学行为。主要动机是探索该理论中自发洛伦兹对称性破缺（spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking）机制对粒子轨道和引力波信号的影响。

Method: 研究方法包括分析测地线方程（geodesic equations）和有效势能，以确定束缚轨道（bound orbits）的允许参数空间。采用旋进-缩放-顶点分类法（whirl, zoom, and vertex taxonomy）对周期性轨道进行分类和表征，并使用四极公式（quadrupole formula）从这些轨道中提取引力波形。

Result: 在带电情况下，洛伦兹破缺参数l和电荷Q显著增强了势能的约束能力，从而扩大了束缚态的能量和角动量窗口。在未带电情况下，虽然径向有效势和最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）性质与史瓦西黑洞简并，但周期性轨道结构存在定性差异。引力波形计算显示，l和Q对波形产生相反的相移效应。

Conclusion: 研究表明，大黄蜂引力在引力波信号中留下了可测量的印记，这些印记可能被未来的天基引力波天文台探测到。周期性轨道结构的差异为打破与史瓦西黑洞的简并性提供了可能的观测特征。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the dynamics of massive particles and the associated gravitational waveforms in the spacetime of a black hole within the framework of Einstein-Bumblebee gravity. Our analysis encompasses both charged and uncharged black hole configurations, with a particular focus on the spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking mechanism inherent to this model, which is governed by a dimensionless coupling parameter $l$. We analyze the geodesic equations and the effective potential to determine the allowed parameter space for bound orbits, demonstrating that in the charged case, both the Lorentz-violating parameter $l$ and the electric charge $Q$ significantly enhance the confinement capacity of the potential, thereby broadening the energy and angular momentum windows for bound states. A key focus is placed on the classification and properties of periodic orbits, characterized by rational frequency ratios using the whirl, zoom, and vertex taxonomy. We demonstrate that in the uncharged case ($Q=0$), the radial effective potential and standard innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) properties are degenerate with those of a Schwarzschild black hole. However, despite this degeneracy in static potential properties, the structure of periodic orbits exhibits qualitative differences, providing a possible observational signature that can break this degeneracy. Finally, we compute the corresponding gravitational waveforms extracted from these periodic orbits using the quadrupole formula. The results reveal that $l$ and $Q$ introduce contrasting phase-shifting effects on the waveforms. This suggests that bumblebee gravity leaves measurable imprints on gravitational-wave signals that could be detected by future space-based gravitational-wave observatories.

</details>


### [109] [Cosmic anisotropic hair of nonlocal RT gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14488)
*Jiajun Zhou,Shuxun Tian,Zong-Hong Zhu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了非局域RT引力（nonlocal RT gravity）框架下各向异性Bianchi I型宇宙的动力学演化，发现与多数暗能量模型不同，该理论预测宇宙各向异性会随时间增长，这对宇宙无毛定理（cosmic no-hair theorem）提出了挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非局域RT引力能解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀且通过局域引力测试，但先前研究多假设各向同性背景，而当前观测（如Ia型超新星数据）暗示存在轻微各向异性，因此需要研究各向异性宇宙在该理论中的演化。

Method: 在非局域RT引力框架下，引入六个无量纲变量构建Bianchi I型宇宙的动力学系统，并进行详细的相空间分析（phase-space analysis）。

Result: 意外发现是：与多数暗能量模型和修正引力理论中各项异性随时间衰减不同，非局域RT引力预测宇宙各向异性会增长，这一行为对该理论框架下的宇宙无毛定理构成了挑战。

Conclusion: 非局域RT引力在各向异性宇宙背景下表现出独特的动力学行为，其预测的各向异性增长现象与标准宇宙学模型形成鲜明对比，需要进一步研究其对宇宙学观测的启示。

Abstract: Nonlocal RT gravity has proven effective in explaining the late-time cosmic acceleration while remaining consistent with local gravity tests. However, most previous cosmological studies of this theory have assumed an isotropic background, which may not fully capture the slight anisotropies suggested by current observations, such as those inferred from Type Ia supernovae data. In this paper, we investigate the dynamical evolution of an anisotropic Bianchi type I universe within the framework of nonlocal RT gravity. By introducing six dimensionless variables, we construct the corresponding dynamical system and perform a detailed phase-space analysis. An unexpected finding is that, contrary to many dark energy models and modified gravity theories in which anisotropies decay with time, nonlocal RT gravity predicts a growth of cosmic anisotropy. This behavior poses a challenge to the cosmic no-hair theorem within the nonlocal RT gravity scenario.

### [110] [Scalaron excitation by topological vortices in quadratic $f(R)$ gravity on a BTZ black hole background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14580)
*C. A. S. Almeida,F. C. E. Lima*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了三维时空中，位于静态BTZ黑洞背景下的麦克斯韦-希格斯涡旋如何激发f(R)引力理论中的标量子（scalaron）模式。在微扰近似下，曲率标量的激发呈现普适的渐近衰减行为，且该激发是线性稳定、能量有限且对背景影响可忽略的。

Method: 在微扰近似$α\ll \ell^2$下，迹方程简化为由涡旋能量-动量张量迹所驱动的曲率标量的有质量克莱因-戈尔登方程。利用径向算子的Sturm-Liouville结构构造相应的格林函数，从而获得任意局域源产生的曲率分布。

Result: 诱导的标量激发呈现普适的渐近衰减行为$R(r) \sim r^{-(1+ν)}$，与涡旋的具体结构无关。该标量激发是线性稳定的，携带有限能量，且产生参数化抑制的反作用，确保了爱因斯坦极限的平滑恢复。

Conclusion: 这些结果为理解高曲率修正如何激活三维引力中独特的局域引力自由度，以及局域源如何在黑洞时空中激发该标量模式提供了具体实现。标量子的激发行为具有普适性，且对背景时空的影响可忽略。

Abstract: In three spacetime dimensions, pure Einstein gravity admits no local propagating degrees of freedom, yet nontrivial gravitational backgrounds such as the BTZ black hole provide a natural arena to probe dynamical extensions of the theory. In quadratic $f(R)$ gravity the Ricci scalar becomes a propagating degree of freedom - the scalaron. We investigate how localized Maxwell-Higgs vortices excite this scalar mode in a static BTZ black-hole background. Working in the perturbative regime $α\ll \ell^2$, the trace equation reduces to a massive Klein-Gordon equation for the curvature scalar sourced by the trace of the vortex energy-momentum tensor. Using the Sturm-Liouville structure of the radial operator, we construct the corresponding Green function and obtain the curvature profile generated by an arbitrary localized source. The induced excitation exhibits a universal asymptotic decay $R(r) \sim r^{-(1+ν)}$, independent of the detailed vortex structure. The scalar excitation is linearly stable, carries finite energy, and produces parametrically suppressed backreaction, ensuring the smooth recovery of the Einstein limit. These results provide a concrete realization of how higher-curvature corrections activate the unique local gravitational degree of freedom in three dimensions and how localized sources excite this scalar mode in black-hole spacetimes.

### [111] [Can wormhole spacetimes in Unimodular Gravity be supported by ordinary matter? A general proof of the exotic matter requirement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14718)
*Mauricio Cataldo,Norman Cruz,Patricio Salgado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究证明在幺模引力（Unimodular Gravity）理论中，所有可穿越虫洞构型都必须依赖奇异物质（exotic matter）。这一结论源于几何的"张开条件"（flaring-out condition），该条件直接导致零能量条件（Null Energy Condition）的违反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究幺模引力理论中是否存在无需奇异物质的可穿越虫洞解。幺模引力是广义相对论的一种变体，研究者希望了解其是否能够规避广义相对论中虫洞需要奇异物质的限制。

Method: 通过建立一般性的"不可行定理"（no-go theorem），证明仅基于几何张开条件 $b'(r_0) \leq 1$ 就能推导出虫洞喉部（throat）处 $ρ(r_0) + p_r(r_0) \leq 0$。该方法不依赖于具体的形状函数（shape function）、红移函数（redshift function）或状态方程（equation of state）的选择。

Result: 研究证明幺模引力中的所有可穿越虫洞构型都必然违反零能量条件（Null Energy Condition），进而违反弱能量条件（Weak Energy Condition）和强能量条件（Strong Energy Condition）。这一结果适用于潮汐力（tidal）和零潮汐力（zero-tidal-force）两种构型，表明奇异物质需求是可穿越性条件的根本几何后果。

Conclusion: 幺模引力与广义相对论在虫洞物理方面共享相同的基本约束：可穿越虫洞的存在必然需要奇异物质。奇异物质需求不是特定解选择的产物，而是可穿越性条件的根本几何结果。

Abstract: We establish a general no--go theorem demonstrating that all traversable wormhole configurations in Unimodular Gravity necessarily require exotic matter. The proof relies solely on the geometric flaring-out condition, $b'(r_0) \leq 1$, which directly implies that $ρ(r_0) + p_r(r_0) \leq 0$ at the throat. This condition represents a violation of the Null Energy Condition and, consequently, of the Weak and Strong Energy Conditions, independently of the particular choice of shape function, redshift function, or equation of state. This result holds for both tidal and zero-tidal-force configurations, showing that the requirement of exotic matter is a fundamental geometric consequence of the traversability condition rather than an artifact of specific solution choices. Therefore, Unimodular Gravity shares this fundamental constraint with General Relativity.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索大质量标量场（可能构成所有暗物质）与引力通过非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling）相互作用时对中子星性质的影响。特别关注这种耦合如何改变中子星的结构和最大质量限制。

Conclusion: 研究表明，标量场与引力的非最小耦合能够显著改变中子星的性质，产生丰富的物理现象。这种耦合不仅允许存在大质量中子星，还导致标量场构型的多重解，为理解暗物质与中子星的相互作用提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the properties of neutron stars when a massive scalar field, which could comprise all dark matter, is non-minimally coupled to the Ricci scalar. This coupling generates additional contributions to the field's effective mass, leading to tachyonic instabilities inside neutron stars and giving rise to rich phenomenology. Within this framework, we obtain neutron-star configurations with maximum masses exceeding 2 $M_\odot$, even when hyperons, which typically soften the equation of state and significantly lower the maximum mass, are included. Furthermore, we find that larger coupling strengths lead to multiple solutions for the scalar-field configuration. We analyze the structure of the corresponding effective potential responsible for this behavior. We also investigate how the inclusion of a scalar self-interaction term, in addition to the non-minimal coupling, modifies the resulting neutron-star properties.

### [113] [Logarithmically enhanced hyperbolic square-root deformation of Starobinsky inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14743)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期精确宇宙学观测（如ACT DR6和DESI）显示标量谱指数向上偏移，并偏好偏离纯指数平台行为，这促使研究者对原始HSQRT构造进行增强。

Method: 在原始HSQRT构造基础上，引入结构最小化、量子动机的对数增强项，并发展了爱因斯坦框架的精确参数化表述，推导了慢滚可观测量（slow-roll observables）的精确解析展开。

Result: 增强模型的标量势从指数形式过渡到逆幂渐近形式，得到无参数的领头阶谱指数 $n_s \simeq 1 - 3/(2N)$ 和可调的张标比 $r \simeq 2(3β)^{1/2}/N^{3/2}$，谱指数直接落入新近偏好的观测窗口。

Conclusion: 该模型为标准暴胀e-fold持续时间提供了与最新观测数据一致的预测，同时为下一代宇宙微波背景观测提供了可行的参数控制目标。

Abstract: We propose and analyze an enhanced hyperbolic square-root (HSQRT) deformation of the Starobinsky model in the context of $f(R)$ gravity. The original HSQRT construction provided a globally regular modification of $R^2$ inflation, curing the strong-coupling singularity at negative curvatures while preserving the characteristic exponential slow-roll plateau at large positive curvatures. Motivated by recent precision cosmological observations (such as ACT DR6 and DESI) indicating an upward shift in the scalar spectral index and a preference for deviations from pure exponential plateau behavior, we introduce a structurally minimal, quantum-motivated logarithmic enhancement. This phenomenological enhancement modifies the deep ultraviolet asymptotic regime while maintaining global tachyon-free stability, ghost freedom, and the recovery of general relativity at low curvatures to preserve standard reheating. By developing an exact parametric formulation of the Einstein frame, we demonstrate that the scalar potential of the enhanced model transitions from an exponential to an inverse-power asymptotic form, $V(φ) \simeq V_0 \left[ 1 - 6β/ (κ^2φ^2) \right]$, where the strength of this deviation is governed by a single dimensionless parameter $β$. We derive exact analytic expansions for the slow-roll observables, yielding a parameter-free leading-order spectral index $n_s \simeq 1 - 3/(2N)$ and a tunable tensor-to-scalar ratio $r \simeq 2(3β)^{1/2}/N^{3/2}$. For standard inflationary e-fold durations ($N \in [50, 60]$), this model drives the spectral index directly into the newly favored observational window ($n_s \simeq 0.970\text{--}0.975$) and predicts an exceptionally small running $α_s \simeq -3/(2N^2) \in [-0.00060, -0.00042]$, while providing a viable, parameter-controlled target for next-generation cosmic microwave background observatories.

*Bo-Qiang Lu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新颖机制，直接从暴胀期间的量子涨落生成宇宙角动量。通过具有全局U(1)对称性的旁观复标量场，在非球形引力坍缩过程中将背景电荷密度与空间梯度耦合，产生可观测的黑洞自旋。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入具有全局U(1)对称性的旁观复标量场，该场通过场空间旋转存储内禀角动量。暴胀扰动产生空间梯度，在视界重入时与背景电荷密度耦合，激发体动量流。

Result: 在非球形引力坍缩过程中，动量流转化为净角动量。对于由此类坍缩形成的原初黑洞，当小尺度功率谱增强以产生可探测丰度时，无量纲自旋可达χ∼0.1-1，远超潮汐扭矩理论预测。

Conclusion: 该机制建立了暴胀、原初扰动与黑洞自旋分布之间的可检验联系，为引力波观测提供了新的理论框架，将量子涨落与宏观角动量生成直接关联。

Abstract: The origin of cosmic angular momentum is a fundamental question in structure formation. We propose a novel mechanism that generates spatial angular momentum directly from quantum fluctuations during inflation. A spectator complex scalar field with global U(1) symmetry stores internal angular momentum via field-space rotation. Inflationary perturbations create spatial gradients that, upon horizon re-entry, couple to the background charge density and source a bulk momentum flow. During nonspherical gravitational collapse, this flow converts into net angular momentum. For primordial black holes forming from such collapse, the dimensionless spin can reach \(χ\sim 0.1-1\) when the small-scale power spectrum is enhanced to produce detectable abundances-far exceeding tidal torque theory predictions. This establishes a testable link between inflation, primordial perturbations, and black hole spin distributions accessible to gravitational-wave observations.

### [115] [Spectral Bifurcations in Quasinormal Modes of Regular BTZ Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14872)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索规则BTZ黑洞中质量less标量场的准正则模谱，这类几何结构通过引入新的长度尺度ℓ解决了中心奇点问题，为研究谱分支和晚期衰落的几何机制提供了受控平台。

Method: 采用Leaver连分法（continued-fraction method）和Horowitz-Hubeny幂级数法两种方法计算标量准正则模，两种方法在整个参数空间内达到高度一致。

Result: 正则化保持线性稳定性（ω_I < 0），但随着ℓ增加，BTZ类复分支与虚轴碰撞并经历一系列分支，产生多个纯虚分支，导致模式切换和泛音（overtones）的非平凡重排。

Abstract: We study the quasinormal spectrum of massless scalar fields propagating on a family of regular BTZ black holes arising from an infinite tower of dimensionally regularized Lovelock corrections. These geometries are asymptotically AdS, reduce to the standard BTZ solution in the limit $\ell \to 0$, and resolve the central singularity by introducing a smooth core controlled by the new length scale $\ell$. The scalar quasinormal modes are computed using both Leaver's continued-fraction method and the Horowitz-Hubeny power-series method; the two approaches agree to high accuracy across the parameter space. We find that the regularization preserves linear stability ($ω_I < 0$) while qualitatively reshaping the spectrum: as $\ell$ increases, BTZ-like complex branches collide with the imaginary axis and undergo a hierarchy of bifurcations into multiple purely imaginary branches, leading to mode switching and a nontrivial reordering of overtones as functions of $\ell$ and the harmonic index $m$. Our results place regular BTZ black holes within the emerging family of bifurcating quasinormal spectra known from nearly extremal and asymptotically AdS black holes, and highlight these $(2+1)$-dimensional geometries as a controlled arena for exploring geometric mechanisms behind spectral branching and late-time ringdown in regular black hole spacetimes.

Conclusion: AIC分析表明两个模型在统计上难以区分，而贝叶斯证据显示数据对ΛCDM模型有轻微偏好。尽管如此，VHDE模型与当前晚期宇宙学观测一致，为描述晚期加速膨胀提供了可行机制。

In particular, we place constraints on the free parameters of the model using Type Ia supernovae from the PantheonPlus, Union3.0, and DES-Dovekie catalogues, the Cosmic Chronometers, and the Baryon Acoustic Oscillations from the DESI DR2. Our analysis suggests that the VHDE model fits the observational data better or similar to the $Λ$CDM for all dataset combinations considered. The value obtained for $H_0$ is similar to the $Λ$CDM, while the current matter density parameter is constrained around $Ω_{m0}\simeq 0.24$, smaller to that obtained by the $Λ$CDM. Moreover, the parameter introduced by the VHDE is found to have a mean value within the range $\fracπ{3} δ^2 \sim 0.27-0.33$. Finally, we used Akaike's Information Criterion (AIC) and Bayesian evidence to test the VHDE model against the $Λ$CDM scenario. The AIC demonstrates that the two models are statistically indistinguishable, while Bayesian evidence reveals that the data have a mild preference for the $Λ$CDM model for most of the dataset combinations considered. Nevertheless, the VHDE model remains consistent with current late-time cosmological observations and offers a feasible mechanism for describing the late-time accelerating scenario.

</details>


### [119] [Plasma impact on black hole shadow and gravitational weak lensing for Schwarzschild-like black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15241)

Abstract: This article delves into the observational properties of a Schwarzschild-like black hole (BH). Furthermore, we study the photon dynamics around the Schwarzschild-like BH in the presence of the plasma using the Hamiltonian formalism. It was found that the photon sphere radii increase under the influence of the plasma frequency and vice versa for the spacetime parameters. Further exploration is dedicated to understanding how the plasma affects the shadow of the BH, and we find that the radius of the BH shadow shrinks with the rise of the $ξ$ parameter and plasma frequency. We then turn to the getting constraint of the spacetime parameters and the plasma frequency by using the observational data released by the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) collaboration for the M87* and Sgr A*. Additionally, the research scrutinises the phenomenon of gravitational weak lensing in the vicinity of a Schwarzschild-like BH, considering both uniform and non-uniform plasma scenarios. The outcomes demonstrate that the angle of deflection increases under the influence of a uniform plasma frequency, whereas the opposite is true for non-uniform plasma. In both scenarios, a rise in the spacetime parameters results in a decrease in the deflection angle. Finally, we investigate the magnification of the gravitationally lensed image. The effect of the spacetime parameters and plasma frequencies on the total magnification are same as in the deflection angles.

### [121] [Direct Waves in Black-Hole Binary Mergers: Insights from the Backwards One Body Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15474)
*Anuj Kankani,Sean T. McWilliams*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过Backwards One Body（BOB）方法分析黑洞并合辐射，揭示了非准正则模（non-QNM）"直接波（direct wave）"成分的存在及其特性，表明该方法能高精度建模完整并合-铃降辐射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于黑洞并合辐射中非准正则模（non-QNM）"直接波（direct wave）"成分的识别，以及Backwards One Body（BOB）方法在建模完整并合-铃降辐射方面的高精度表现。研究者希望理解BOB方法如何捕获这些非QNM成分，并探究直接波频率的特性。

Result: 研究表明BOB方法自然捕获了并合辐射中的直接波成分，这解释了其在波形峰值附近的高精度。分析显示直接波频率与视界频率基本不相关，即使对于高自旋残余黑洞也是如此，而是追踪峰值News振幅时刻的News频率。

Conclusion: 该工作证实了BOB方法能够有效建模黑洞并合辐射中的非准正则模成分，揭示了直接波频率与News频率而非视界频率的相关性，为理解并合-铃降辐射的完整物理图像提供了新见解。

Abstract: The merger-ringdown radiation from a black hole binary merger is accurately modeled by a sum of linear quasinormal modes (QNMs). Recently, a non-QNM ``direct wave" component of the radiation, associated with prompt emission from a plunging perturber, has been identified. Motivated by the behavior of null geodesics perturbed from the remnant light ring, the Backwards One Body (BOB) approach has been shown to model the full merger-ringdown radiation to high accuracy, while using only a minimal number of parameters. In this work, using the Pöschl--Teller potential, we first show how the BOB amplitude evolution can be recovered from the QNM pole contributions. We then apply rational filters to isolate the non-QNM content in BOB and numerical relativity waveforms. We show that BOB naturally captures the direct wave component of the merger radiation, explaining its accuracy near the waveform peak. Finally, we use BOB to show that the direct wave frequency is largely uncorrelated with the horizon frequency, even for high spin remnants, and instead tracks the News frequency at the time of the peak News amplitude.

### [123] [Entropy Maximization and Weak Gibbsianity of Quasi-Free Fermionic States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14020)
*Vojkan Jakšić,Claude-Alain Pillet,Anna Szczepanek*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究解决了晶格费米子（lattice fermions）熵最大化问题中的两个长期疑问：证明了在特定条件下，规范不变准自由态（gauge-invariant quasi-free states）不仅是熵最大化的唯一解，而且是弱吉布斯态（weak Gibbs states）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于1972年Lanford和Robinson关于平衡态趋近的研究，他们发现晶格费米子的规范不变准自由态在固定两点函数（two-point function）的平移不变态中最大化熵，但唯一性问题未完全解决。后续研究中，唯一性问题与这些准自由态是否为弱吉布斯态的问题重新浮现。

Method: 方法是在满足特定条件的态类中进行分析：动量空间两点函数$\widehat C(k)$满足$0<\widehat C(k)<1$且属于布里渊区（Brillouin zone）的维纳代数（Wiener algebra）。证明揭示了熵最大化原理和弱吉布斯性都直接源于晶格费米子的热力学形式体系（thermodynamic formalism）。

Result: 研究结果为两个问题提供了肯定答案：在所述条件下，规范不变准自由态不仅是熵最大化的唯一解，而且是弱吉布斯态。这解决了该领域长期存在的两个理论问题。

Conclusion: 结论表明，对于晶格费米子，熵最大化原理和弱吉布斯性之间存在深刻联系，两者都可由热力学形式体系直接推导得出。这一发现统一了先前研究中分离的两个概念，深化了对平衡态统计力学基础的理解。

Abstract: In their 1972 study of approach to equilibrium, Lanford and Robinson showed that gauge-invariant quasi-free states of lattice fermions maximize entropy among all translation-invariant states with a fixed two-point function, and suggested that the maximizer is unique. In subsequent work on this topic, the uniqueness question re-emerged, together with the problem of whether such quasi-free states are weak Gibbs states. We provide a positive answer to both questions within a class of states whose momentum-space two-point function $\widehat C$ satisfies $0<\widehat C(k)<1$ and belongs to the Wiener algebra of the Brillouin zone. The proof reveals that both the entropy maximization principle and weak Gibbsianity follow directly from the thermodynamic formalism for lattice fermions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法结合了理论分析和数值模拟。理论部分证明了狄利克雷拉普拉斯算子（Dirichlet Laplacian）在本征谱阈值下方存在有限数量的离散本征值，并研究了这些本征值对椭圆几何参数的依赖性。数值模拟部分则通过计算展示了第一本征值和基态随窗口几何形状的变化。

Result: 研究结果表明，与圆形情况不同，椭圆设置会产生如本征值分裂（eigenvalue splitting）等光谱效应。数值模拟具体展示了第一本征值和基态如何随窗口几何形状变化，验证了椭圆几何参数对系统光谱特性的显著影响。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，椭圆窗口的几何结构通过打破旋转对称性和引入各向异性，显著改变了波导耦合系统的光谱特性。这种几何依赖性的理解对于设计具有特定光谱响应的波导耦合器件具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate the Dirichlet Laplacian in two spatial waveguides coupled through an elliptic window. The elliptic geometry breaks rotational symmetry and introduces anisotropy through the semi-axes of the aperture, which modifies the coupling of transverse modes and the low-lying spectrum. We prove that the operator has a finite number of discrete eigenvalues below the threshold of the essential spectrum and study their dependence on the geometric parameters of the ellipse. In contrast to the circular case, the elliptic setting gives rise to spectral effects such as eigenvalue splitting. Numerical simulations illustrate the variation of the first eigenvalues and the ground state with the window geometry.

### [125] [A new model for the quantum mechanics of the Hydrogen atom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14969)
*Joseph Bernstein,Eyal Subag*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的氢原子量子力学模型，采用四维洛伦兹二次空间中的锥体作为构型空间，使用代数微分算子和施瓦茨子空间，无需额外边界条件即可获得与物理标准模型一致的光谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在构建一个氢原子的新量子力学模型，以克服标准模型的三个主要限制：构型空间的对称性有限、算子的奇异性问题以及需要额外边界条件。

Method: 方法基于四维洛伦兹二次空间(V,q)及其对应的锥体C作为构型空间。希尔伯特空间H由锥体上的L²函数构成，可观测量由锥体上的代数微分算子代数D(C)表示。引入一个特殊的施瓦茨子空间H^∞作为D(C)-模，薛定谔算子由D(C)中的薛定谔算子族表示。

Result: 计算了施瓦茨空间H^∞中薛定谔算子族的谱，证明其与物理标准谱完全一致，且H^∞中的解对应于物理中的常规解。新模型的主要特征包括：构型空间对称性为O(q)≃O(3,1)、使用无奇异性的代数算子、以及边界条件完全编码在施瓦茨空间中。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个氢原子的新量子力学框架，在保持物理预测一致性的同时，提供了更丰富的几何对称性、无奇异性的代数算子表示，以及通过施瓦茨空间自然编码边界条件的简洁数学结构。

Abstract: In this paper we introduce a new model for the quantum-mechanical system of the hydrogen atom.
  We start with a four-dimensional Lorentzian quadratic space $(V,q)$ and let $C \subset V$ be the corresponding cone.
  The Hilbert space of our model, denoted by $H$, consists of $L^2$ functions on the cone, and observables are represented by operators in the algebra $D(C)$ of algebraic differential operators on $C$. We introduce a distinguished Schwartz subspace $H^{\infty}$ of $H$ that is naturally a $D(C)$-module. The Schrödinger operator in our system is represented by a Schrödinger family of operators in $D(C)$.
  We compute the spectrum of the Schrödinger family in the Schwartz space $H^{\infty}$ and show that it coincides with the spectrum in physics, and that solutions in $H^{\infty}$ correspond to the usual solutions in physics.
  The main differences from the standard model are as follows. First, we use the cone $C$ instead of $\mathbb{R}^3$ as our configuration space. As a result, the group of geometric symmetries of our configuration space is $O(q)\simeq O(3,1)$ rather than $O(3)\ltimes \mathbb{R}^3$. Second, we use only algebraic operators with no singularities. Third, we do not impose any specific boundary conditions on solutions of our equations; these are all encoded in the Schwartz space $H^{\infty}$.

### [126] [The Zak phase in topologically insulating chains: invariants and quaternionic constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14995)
*Federico Manzoni,Domenico Monaco,Gabriele Peluso*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了先前工作，系统分析了一维平移不变拓扑绝缘体中Zak相位在具有时间反演、粒子-空穴和/或手性对称性时的拓扑内容，构建了适应系统离散对称性的对称Bloch基，并定义了从阿贝尔Zak相位获得的Z2拓扑不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究Zak相位在一维平移不变拓扑绝缘体中的拓扑内容，特别是当系统具有时间反演（time-reversal）、粒子-空穴（particle-hole）和/或手性（chiral）对称性时。研究扩展了先前工作，分析Zak相位在多大程度上能捕捉所有Altland-Zirnbauer-Cartan（AZC）对称性类在一维情况下的拓扑特性。

Method: 基于纤维化哈密顿量（fibered Hamiltonians）和谱投影（spectral projections）框架，构建了适应系统离散对称性的对称Bloch基。通过阿贝尔Zak相位（abelian Zak phase）定义了Z2值的拓扑不变量I^(AZC-class)(H)，并分析了在具有四元数结构（即反幺正对称性平方等于负恒等）的对称性类中Zak相位的额外约束。

Result: 研究证明，在允许四元数结构的对称性类中（即反幺正对称性平方等于负恒等），Zak相位受到进一步约束，导致上述Z2不变量的消失。这凸显了Zak相位对占据能态流形（manifold of occupied energy states）额外几何结构的敏感性。作为应用，讨论了具有任意有限程跃迁和单/多手性通道的广义Kitaev链（generalized Kitaev chains）情况。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了Zak相位在一维拓扑绝缘体中的拓扑内容，建立了与AZC对称性类相关的拓扑不变量框架，并揭示了在特定对称性类中Zak相位的额外约束条件，为理解拓扑相位的几何敏感性提供了理论见解。

Abstract: In this work we investigate the topological content of the Zak phase in one-dimensional translation-invariant topological insulators endowed with time-reversal, particle-hole and/or chiral symmetries, extending results from \cite{Monaco_2023}. We analyze the extent to which the Zak phase captures the topology of all Altland--Zirnbauer--Cartan (AZC) symmetry classes in $1$D. Building on the framework of fibered Hamiltonians and spectral projections, we construct symmetric Bloch bases adapted to the discrete symmetries of the system and define a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-valued topological invariant $\mathrm{I}^{(\mathrm{AZC-class})}(H)$ obtained from the abelian Zak phase. Moreover, we demonstrate that in symmetry classes admitting a quaternionic structure, i.e. anti-unitary symmetries squaring to minus the identity, the Zak phase is further constrained, leading to the vanishing of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ invariant mentioned above. This highlights the sensitivity of the Zak phase to additional geometric structures of the manifold of occupied energy states. As an application, we discuss the case of generalized Kitaev chains with arbitrary finite-range hopping and single or multiple chiral channels.

### [127] [On uniform large genus asymptotics of Witten's intersection numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15233)
*Jindong Guo,Di Yang,Don Zagier*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究稳定代数曲线模空间（moduli space of stable algebraic curves）上psi类相交数的大亏格渐近行为，旨在建立统一的渐近公式并扩展相关结果，同时探讨其在Painlevé I方程中的应用。

Method: 基于文献[14]的思想，为原始psi类相交数构建统一的大亏格渐近公式，并以特定统一方式将结果扩展到包含零点插入的情况，同时采用文献[14]的方法为psi类相交数大亏格渐近展开的多项式性猜想提供新证明。

Result: 获得了原始psi类相交数的统一大亏格渐近公式，成功将结果扩展到包含零点插入的情况，并给出了Painlevé I方程特定形式解的具体应用，同时完成了多项式性猜想的新证明。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了psi类相交数的统一渐近理论框架，扩展了渐近公式的应用范围，验证了多项式性猜想的正确性，并为Painlevé I方程的研究提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: Following ideas from [14], we give a uniform large genus asymptotics for primitive psi-class intersection numbers on the moduli space of stable algebraic curves, and extend this result including insertions of zeros in a certain uniform way. Application to a particular formal solution of the Painlevé I equation is given. We also use a method from [14] to give a new proof of the polynomiality conjecture on large genus asymptotic expansions of psi-class intersection numbers.

</details>

### [129] [Ruijsenaars-van Diejen-Takemura Hamiltonians as rational Heun operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15595)

Result: 成功建立了最一般的Ruijsenaars-van Diejen-Takemura哈密顿量与Heun算子之间的对应关系。这些算子被明确定义为在Askey-Wilson网格上具有极点的有理函数的二阶q-差分算子。

Abstract: The most general Ruijsenaars-van Diejen-Takemura Hamiltonians are characterized as Heun operators defined as second order $q$-difference operators with a raising action on elementary rational functions with poles on the Askey-Wilson grid.

### [130] [Notes on an intuitive approach to elliptic homogenization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13661)
*Conor Rowan*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文通过物理动机推导而非摄动理论，建立了椭圆齐次化在一维和二维边界值问题中的系数，并讨论了薄曲面多尺度曲率上Laplace-Beltrami算子的齐次化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 椭圆齐次化用于确定具有小尺度特征材料的热传递和弹性粗粒化性质。现有研究大多依赖摄动理论方法，这使得对齐次化系数的直观物理理解变得困难。

Method: 基于物理动机的论证推导一维和二维椭圆边界值问题的齐次化系数，完全不依赖摄动理论。同时讨论了薄曲面多尺度曲率上Laplace-Beltrami算子的齐次化。

Result: 当材料微结构特征具有快速周期性波动时，基于"齐次化"系数场的解与基于异质材料的真实解非常相似。该方法提供了对齐次化系数更直观的物理理解。

Conclusion: 通过物理动机而非摄动理论的方法推导齐次化系数，为理解椭圆齐次化提供了更直观的途径，并扩展了薄曲面多尺度曲率问题的处理范围。

Abstract: Elliptic homogenization is used to determine coarse-grained properties of materials with features on small scales for heat transfer and elasticity. When microstructural features of a material have rapid, periodic fluctuations, the solution corresponding to a "homogenized" coefficient field closely resembles the true solution based on the heterogeneous material. Most presentations of elliptic homogenization rely on methods from perturbation theory, which can make an intuitive, physical understanding of the homogenized coefficients elusive. In this set of notes, we derive the homogenized coefficients for one- and two-dimensional elliptic boundary value problems based on arguments which are physically motivated, and with no recourse to perturbation theory. Then, we discuss homogenization of the Laplace-Beltrami operator for heat conduction on thin surfaces with multiscale curvature, an example which has seen minimal treatment in existing literature.

### [131] [Vorticity confinement for 2D incompressible flows in an infinite cylinder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13926)
*Paolo Buttà,Guido Cavallaro*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究无限圆柱中二维不可压缩流动的涡量（vorticity）约束问题，推导了Navier-Stokes和Euler方程解中涡量支撑集（support）随时间扩展的定量衰减估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维不可压缩流动在无限圆柱中涡量的约束行为，旨在理解涡量质量（vorticity mass）在初始支撑集外区域的衰减特性，为流体动力学中的涡量扩散机制提供定量分析框架。

Method: 结合迭代方案（iterative scheme）与Biot-Savart核（Biot-Savart kernel）的反对称性质（antisymmetry property）进行分析；对于Euler方程情况，进一步耦合来自[Commun. Math. Phys., 367, 1077-1093, 2019]的一阶矩估计（first-moment estimate）。

Result: 对于Navier-Stokes解，当初始涡量非负且具有紧支撑集时，涡量质量在距离初始支撑集以$\sqrt{t\log^αt}$（α>1）或$t^β$（β>1/2）速率增长的区域外分别呈现超多项式（super-polynomially）或拉伸指数（stretched-exponentially）衰减；对于Euler方程，涡量支撑集的直径增长上限为$(t\log t)^{1/3}$，优于先前文献中的$t^{1/3}\log^2 t$估计。

Conclusion: 本文建立了二维不可压缩流动中涡量约束的定量衰减估计，改进了Euler方程情况下涡量支撑集增长的边界估计，为理解涡量在流体中的扩散机制提供了更精确的数学描述。

Abstract: We study the confinement of vorticity for two-dimensional incompressible flows in an infinite cylinder. For Navier-Stokes solutions with non-negative and compactly supported initial vorticity, we derive quantitative decay estimates showing that the vorticity mass outside regions whose distance from the initial support grows like $\sqrt{t\log^αt}$ (with $α>1$) or like $t^β$ (with $β>1/2$) becomes, respectively, super-polynomially or stretched-exponentially small. The analysis combines an iterative scheme with an antisymmetry property of the Biot-Savart kernel. In the Euler case, by coupling this approach with a first-moment estimate from [Commun. Math. Phys., 367, 1077-1093, 2019], we recover the confinement bound of [Commun. Math. Phys., 367, 1077-1093, 2019] and refine it slightly: the diameter of the vorticity support grows at most like $(t\log t)^{1/3}$, rather than $t^{1/3}\log^2 t$.

</details>


### [132] [Mixing and enhanced dissipation in a time-translating shear flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14624)
*Johannes Benthaus,Giuseppe Maria Coclite,Camilla Nobili*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有平移剪切流（translating shear flow）的对流-扩散方程（advection-diffusion equation）的混合（mixing）与增强耗散（enhanced dissipation）现象。通过分析平移速度c与扩散系数ν的关系，量化了临界点（critical points）运动对衰减特性的影响，获得了介于静止剪切流与单调流之间的连续插值衰减率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文研究动机部分源于Vanneste和Byatt-Smith的工作，旨在分析具有速度场$\mathbf{u}(x,y,t)=(\sin(y-ct),0)$的对流-扩散方程。该剪切流（shear flow）剖面以速度c刚性平移，是临界点（critical points）随时间移动的典型流动示例。研究目标是量化衰减特性如何依赖于平移速度c与扩散系数ν之间的关系。

Method: 首先分析无粘输运问题（inviscid transport problem），建立$t\lesssim c^{-1}$时间尺度上的时间平均$H^{-1}$混合估计（mixing estimates）。基于这些估计，证明中等平移速度$c=c_0ν^\ell$（其中$\ell\in(1/3,3/4)$）下的增强耗散（enhanced dissipation）。混合估计依赖于精细的驻相分析（stationary phase analysis），利用临界点运动产生的抵消效应。增强耗散结果需要将静止剪切流的亚强制框架（hypocoercivity framework）适应于非自治（non-autonomous）设置，通过构造扩展能量泛函（extended energy functional）克服标准交换子层次（commutator hierarchy）闭合问题。

Result: 对于中等平移速度$c=c_0ν^\ell$（$\ell\in(1/3,3/4)$），获得衰减率$ν^{(1+2\ell)/5}$。该衰减率在静止剪切流（具有简单临界点）的尖锐速率$ν^{1/2}$与单调流（monotone flows）的$ν^{1/3}$之间连续插值，量化了增加平移速度如何逐步减弱临界点的影响。对于$c\gg 1$，证明解在固定时间区间内保持接近热方程（heat equation）的解，快速平移平均了对流效应并减弱了混合。

Conclusion: 研究量化了平移剪切流中混合与增强耗散特性对平移速度的依赖关系。中等平移速度下的衰减率在静止剪切流与单调流之间连续插值，揭示了临界点运动对衰减过程的渐进减弱效应。无粘混合与增强耗散时间尺度的启发式比较解释了$\ell=1/3$的下端点，而大平移速度分析则展示了快速平移的平均效应如何削弱混合。

Abstract: Motivated in part by the work of Vanneste and Byatt-Smith, we study mixing and enhanced dissipation for the advection-diffusion equation with velocity field $\mathbf{u}(x,y,t)=(\sin(y-ct),0)$, a shear flow whose profile translates rigidly with speed $c$. This is a prototypical example of a flow whose critical points move in time. We quantify how the decay properties depend on the relation between translation speed $c$ and diffusivity $ν$. We first analyse the inviscid transport problem and establish time-averaged $H^{-1}$ mixing estimates for $t\lesssim c^{-1}$, yielding decay rates faster than stationary estimates. Building on these estimates, we prove enhanced dissipation for moderate translation speeds $c=c_0ν^\ell$ with $\ell\in(1/3,3/4)$. In this regime we obtain decay at rate $ν^{(1+2\ell)/5}$, which interpolates continuously between the sharp rates $ν^{1/2}$ for stationary shear flows with simple critical points and $ν^{1/3}$ for monotone flows. This quantifies how increasing translation speed progressively weakens the influence of the critical points. Comparing the inviscid mixing and enhanced dissipation timescales heuristically explains the lower endpoint $\ell=1/3$. For $c\gg 1$, we show that solutions remain close to those of the heat equation on fixed time intervals, such that the rapid translation averages out advection and weakens mixing. The mixing estimate relies on a refined stationary phase analysis exploiting cancellations generated by the motion of the critical points. The enhanced dissipation result requires an adaptation of the hypocoercivity framework for stationary shear flows to the non-autonomous setting. The translating flow prevents the commutator hierarchy from closing in the standard way, which we overcome by constructing an extended energy functional. The large-$c$ analysis exploits the averaging effect of rapid translations in this regime.

</details>


### [133] [Towards a Gagliardo-Type Theory of Fractional Sobolev Spaces on Arbitrary Time Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14715)
*Hafida Abbas,Abdelhalim Azzouz*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Gagliardo方法的时标（time scales）上分数阶Sobolev空间理论，建立了相应的分数阶半范数和空间W^{α,p}_Δ(T)，证明了这些空间的Banach空间、自反性和Hilbert空间性质，并在有界混合时标上建立了Poincaré型不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立时标（time scales）上分数阶Sobolev空间的统一理论框架。动机在于将分数阶微积分理论扩展到任意时标上，从而在一个统一的框架内恢复连续、离散和混合设置。

Method: 采用Gagliardo型方法，基于Lebesgue Δ-测度和定义在非对角集Ω_T ⊂ T × T上的非局部相互作用能量（nonlocal interaction energies）。对于常数分数阶α∈(0,1)和1≤p<∞，定义了相应的分数阶半范数和空间W^{α,p}_Δ(T)。

Result: 证明了这些空间对于所有1≤p<∞是Banach空间，对于1<p<∞是自反空间，在p=2时是Hilbert空间。在有界混合时标（bounded hybrid time scales）上建立了Poincaré型不等式，表明时标的几何结构在强制性估计中起着重要作用。

Conclusion: 该构造在一个统一框架内恢复了连续、离散和混合设置。文章最后简要指出了向变阶非局部空间（variable-order nonlocal spaces）的可能扩展，这将在后续研究中单独探讨。

Abstract: We introduce a Gagliardo-type approach to fractional Sobolev spaces on arbitrary time scales, based on the Lebesgue $Δ$-measure and on nonlocal interaction energies defined on the off-diagonal set $Ω_T \subset T \times T$. For constant fractional order $α\in (0,1)$ and $1 \le p < \infty$, we define the associated fractional seminorm and the corresponding space $W^{α,p}_Δ(T)$, and we show that this construction is well posed in the measure-theoretic setting of time scales. In particular, we establish that these spaces are Banach spaces for all $1 \le p < \infty$, reflexive for $1 < p < \infty$, and Hilbert spaces in the case $p=2$. We then prove a Poincaré-type inequality on a natural class of bounded hybrid time scales, showing that the geometry of the underlying time scale enters the theory already at the level of coercive estimates. The construction recovers, within a unified framework, the continuous, discrete, and hybrid settings. We conclude by briefly indicating a possible extension to variable-order nonlocal spaces, which will be studied separately.

</details>

### [134] [Jet peak shapes based on two-particle angular correlations in lead-lead collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}$ = 5.02 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14385)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 该研究通过CMS探测器在5.02 TeV核子对质心能量下收集的铅-铅碰撞数据，实验探索了双粒子关联函数中喷注诱导峰值的纵向不变性。研究发现喷注峰形随碰撞中心度、横向动量及赝快度变化，并与质子-质子碰撞数据进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过实验探索相对论性铅-铅碰撞中双粒子关联函数喷注诱导峰值的纵向不变性。主要动机是研究喷注峰形如何随碰撞参数变化，从而深入了解喷注与介质相互作用的动力学特性。

Method: 使用CMS探测器在5.02 TeV核子对质心能量下收集铅-铅碰撞数据，积分亮度为0.607 nb⁻¹。通过事件中粒子间赝快度和方位角分离的二维分布研究长程和短程关联。分析聚焦于喷注峰形的宽度和纵向不对称性对横向动量、碰撞中心度及相关带电粒子赝快度的依赖性。

Result: 研究发现，较低横向动量粒子的喷注峰分布在赝快度和方位角上都随碰撞重叠增加而展宽，其中赝快度方向的展宽更为显著。峰值的纵向不对称性也随平均赝快度增加而增强。这些结果与相同核子-核子碰撞质心能量下收集的质子-质子碰撞数据进行了比较。

Conclusion: 该研究通过系统分析喷注峰形演化，揭示了喷注与介质相互作用的特征。赝快度方向更显著的展宽和纵向不对称性的增强表明喷注在介质中传播时受到各向异性效应影响，为理解重离子碰撞中喷注淬火机制提供了实验依据。

Abstract: The longitudinal invariance of jet-induced peaks in two-particle correlation functions from relativistic lead-lead collisions is experimentally explored. The data were collected at a center-of-mass energy per nucleon pair of 5.02 TeV in 2018 using the CMS detector. The dataset corresponds to an integrated luminosity of 0.607 nb$^{-1}$. Long- and short-range correlations are studied through two-dimensional distributions of the separations in pseudorapidity and azimuth between particles in an event. Jets manifest as a well-defined peak at small angular separations, and the shape of this peak provides insight into jet medium interactions. This Letter examines the evolution of the jet peak shape, focusing on the dependence of its width and longitudinal asymmetry on the transverse momentum, collision centrality, and pseudorapidity of the associated charged particles. The jet-peak distributions of lower transverse momentum particles broaden in both pseudorapidity and azimuth with increasing collision overlap, with the broadening in pseudorapidity being more pronounced. The longitudinal asymmetry of the peaks is also found to increase as the average pseudorapidity increases. These results are compared to proton-proton collision data that were obtained at the same nucleon-nucleon collision center-of-mass energy with an integrated luminosity of 252 nb$^{-1}$.

### [135] [Maximal green sequences for quantum and Poisson CGL extensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14376)

Result: 成功证明了对称量子与泊松CGL扩展类的所有成员的量子与经典丛代数均存在极大绿色序列，为先前许多具体族的结果提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: We prove that the quantum and classical cluster algebras for all members of the axiomatically defined classes of symmetric quantum and Poisson Cauchon-Goodearl-Letzter extensions possess maximal green sequences in the sense of Keller. Previously, maximal green sequences were constructed for explicit families of cluster algebras; many of those can be recovered from the general result for CGL extensions.
