### [136] [Probing strong coupling in core--shell nanoparticles with fast electron beams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13797)
*Annika Brandt,Christos Tserkezis,Carsten Rockstuhl,P. Elli Stamatopoulou*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究开发了分析框架，用于计算核壳纳米颗粒的电子能量损失和阴极发光谱，探究电子束参数对强耦合探测的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 集体光学激发（如金属纳米颗粒的局域表面等离激元和介质的高折射率Mie共振）在纳米尺度光-物质相互作用中起核心作用。当这些光学模式与物质中的电子跃迁在适当条件下相互作用时，可形成强耦合的杂化光-物质态。

Method: 开发了分析框架，用于计算球形核壳纳米颗粒在掠射和穿透电子轨迹下的电子能量损失谱（EEL）和阴极发光谱（CL）概率。该形式主义应用于两个代表性系统：金属壳包裹激子核，以及激子壳包裹硅核。

Result: 研究发现，电子束位置和速度显著影响强耦合的探测能力。在等离激元纳米球中，强耦合的光谱特征保持稳健；而在介质纳米球中，该特征可能显著抑制甚至完全消失。

Conclusion: 所开发的形式主义有助于深入理解电子-光-物质相互作用中的耦合机制，从而加速基于单纳米颗粒的极化激元研究进展。

Abstract: Collective optical excitations, such as localized surface plasmons in metallic nanoparticles and Mie resonances in high-index dielectrics, play a central role in nanoscale light--matter interactions. When such optical modes interact with electronic transitions in matter under suitable conditions, they can couple strongly, analogous to two coupled harmonic oscillators, forming hybrid light--matter states. In this work, we probe this coupling in core--shell nanoparticles using fast electrons in electron energy-loss (EEL) and cathodoluminescence (CL) spectroscopy. Owing to their highly localized fields, fast electrons can excite modes inaccessible with light-based spectroscopies, including higher-order nonradiative modes, which offer greater field confinement and potentially stronger coupling. Here, we develop an analytical framework to calculate the EEL and CL probabilities for spherical core--shell nanoparticles under aloof and penetrating electron trajectories. This formalism is applied to two representative systems: an excitonic core with a metallic shell, and a silicon core with an excitonic shell. Our main focus is to examine how the electron beam position and velocity affect our ability to probe this coupling. Depending on the electron beam parameters, we find that the spectral signature of strong coupling remains robust in plasmonic nanospheres. In contrast, it can be significantly suppressed or even completely obscured in dielectric nanospheres. Our developed formalism enables a deeper understanding of the coupling mechanisms in electron--light--matter interactions, thereby accelerating progress in single-nanoparticle-based polaritonic studies.

</details>

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski-space）的方法来描述双曲材料中的波传播，将各向异性嵌入到有效的洛伦兹度规（Lorentzian metric）中，为双曲界面和透镜建立了理性设计框架，并实现了超大的数值孔径和深亚衍射聚焦。

Method: 引入闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski-space）方法来描述双曲波传播，将各向异性嵌入到有效的洛伦兹度规（Lorentzian metric）中。建立了双曲界面和透镜的理性设计框架，并解析推导了其传递函数和分辨率极限。

Result: 该方法实现了超大的数值孔径（numerical apertures）和深亚衍射聚焦（deep sub-diffraction focusing）。通过设计并全波建模一个在中红外频率范围工作的平面范德华极化激元透镜（van der Waals polaritonic lens），验证了理论的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明双曲材料中的波传播复杂性本质上是几何的而非物理的，通过闵可夫斯基空间方法可以建立有效的设计框架，为双曲光学器件的理性设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The extreme anisotropy of hyperbolic materials enables extreme wave confinement, but it is also associated with an inherent misalignment between phase and energy flow, which complicates device modeling and design. Here we introduce a Minkowski-space approach to describe hyperbolic wave propagation, showing that this complexity is geometric rather than physical. By embedding anisotropy into an effective Lorentzian metric, we establish a rational design framework for hyperbolic interfaces and lenses, and analytically derive their transfer function and resolution limits, enabling ultra-large numerical apertures and deep sub-diffraction focusing. We validate our theory with the design and full-wave modeling of a planar van der Waals polaritonic lens operating in the mid-infrared frequency range.

Abstract: Optical thermodynamic theory provides distinct viewpoint to rich set of optical phenomena in multimode optical systems. The resultant nonlinear equation of state enables prediction of power localization, as well as cooling/heating in optical Joule-Thomson expansion, thus providing a unified thermodynamic perspective on nonlinear control and transport of optical waves.

Overcoming the limitations precluding the observations of laser-driven mesoscopic phenomena in the time domain with state-of-the-art amplified sources, our proposed experimental approach can be readily realized without irreversible optical damage and holds immense potential for the future development of ultrafast electrodynamics in nanogaps, applications in photochemistry and nanoscale control of quantum emitters. Our work expands the realm of quantum nanophotonics onto non-equilibrium electronic systems and facilitates the development of ultrafast methods in active plasmonics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过悬浮亚波长薄膜中的跃迁辐射干涉（transition-radiation interferences）实现类似自由电子定义的共振，并探索其与过渡金属二硫化物（transition metal dichalcogenides）中激子的相互作用。

We demonstrate that these resonances hybridize with excitonic transitions and can be tuned continuously by varying the electron energy. The resulting detuning depends on both film thickness and electron velocity, establishing the latter as an external and continuous knob for exciton-photon coupling. This approach enables tunable hybridization without structural modification and provides a free-electron-driven nanoscale platform for studying exciton-light interactions.

### [141] [Ultrafast photo-thermoelectric currents in graphene junctions in the mid-infrared](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13457)
*Nina Pettinger,Michel Panhans,Johannes Schmuck,Sebastian Loy,Xiaoyi Zhou,Chengye Dong,Joshua A. Robinson,Sergey Zherebtsov,Christoph Kastl,Frank Ortmann,Alexander W. Holleitner*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过超快泵浦-探测光电流光谱技术，证明了石墨烯在中红外波段仍保持宽带光电流响应特性，但弛豫时间随波长增加而延长，揭示了在低于光学声子能量的光子能量下，电子-电子和电子-声子散射仍能高效耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯以其超快宽带光电流响应而闻名，但其宽带超快特性在光子能量低于光学声子能量的中红外波长下是否得以保持，仍是一个未解决的问题。研究旨在探索石墨烯在中红外激发下的载流子动力学特性。

Method: 采用超快泵浦-探测光电流光谱技术（ultrafast pump-probe photocurrent spectroscopy）研究石墨烯结在中红外激发下的载流子动力学。利用双分裂栅器件证明光热电效应（photo-thermoelectric effect）在中红外飞秒激发下也能主导石墨烯的光响应。

Result: 石墨烯在中红外光谱区域仍保持宽带光电流响应，但光电流弛豫时间从8-9微米以下的约2皮秒增加到更长中红外波长下的3皮秒。室温下衰减动力学中未出现明显的声子瓶颈，表明即使在光子能量低于光学声子能量时，电子-电子和电子-声子散射仍能高效耦合。

Conclusion: 观察到的光电流弛豫时间波长依赖性与基于微观输运理论推导的能量相关理论弛豫时间一致，该理论包含Holstein-Peierls哈密顿量中的电子-声子耦合。研究证实了石墨烯在中红外波段的宽带响应特性及其弛豫机制。

Abstract: Graphene is widely recognized for its ultrafast and broadband photocurrent response, but whether the broadband ultrafast characteristics are preserved at mid-infrared wavelengths with photon energies below the optical phonon energy remains an open question. Here, we investigate the carrier dynamics in graphene junctions under mid-infrared excitation using an ultrafast pump-probe photocurrent spectroscopy. We utilize dual split gate devices to demonstrate that the photo-thermoelectric effect can dominate the photoresponse of graphene also for a mid-infrared femtosecond excitation. We observe that graphene retains its broadband photocurrent response in this spectral region, but the photocurrent relaxation time increases from ca. 2 ps below 8-9 micrometer up to 3 ps at longer mid-infrared wavelengths. The absence of a pronounced phonon bottleneck in the decay dynamics at room temperature suggests an efficient interplay of electron-electron and electron-phonon scattering even for photon energies below the optical phonon energy in graphene. The observed wavelength dependence of the photocurrent relaxation times is consistent with energy-dependent theoretical relaxation times as derived from a microscopic transport theory of graphene that includes electron-phonon coupling within a Holstein-Peierls Hamiltonian.

### [142] [Magnetic-field-induced superconductivity in hexalayer rhombohedral graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13498)
*Jinghao Deng,Jiabin Xie,Hongyuan Li,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Jie Shan,Kin Fai Mak,Xiaomeng Liu*

TL;DR: 六层菱面体石墨烯中发现了面内磁场诱导的超导现象，其转变温度随磁场增强而升高，且能承受远超传统泡利极限的强磁场，表明存在非常规的自旋极化超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超导体中，由于自旋单态配对（spin-singlet pairing），超导性通常会被外磁场抑制。本研究旨在探索面内磁场（in-plane magnetic field）能否诱导出非常规的超导现象。

Method: 在六层菱面体石墨烯（hexalayer rhombohedral graphene）中施加面内磁场$B_{\parallel}$，并通过电场调控其配对破坏行为（depairing behavior）。利用量子振荡测量（quantum oscillation measurements）分析超导态的起源。

Result: 施加小面内磁场后，在相边界窄带内出现超导态；超导区域随$B_{\parallel}$增大向高电场方向移动，转变温度随之升高。该超导态在高达14 T的$B_{\parallel}$下仍保持稳定，远超传统泡利极限（Pauli limit）。量子振荡测量显示超导性源于向列费米面重构（nematic Fermi surface reconstruction）。

Conclusion: 实验结果揭示了自旋极化超导态（spin-polarized superconducting states）的存在，其起源非常规，为探索磁场增强型超导现象提供了新平台。

Abstract: In conventional superconductors, superconductivity is generally suppressed by external magnetic fields due to spin-singlet pairing. Here, we report signatures of in-plane-magnetic-field-induced superconductivity in hexalayer rhombohedral graphene and reveal electric-field control of its depairing behavior. With the application of a small in-plane magnetic field $B_{\parallel}$, a superconducting state emerges within a narrow band along a phase boundary. Its properties evolve continuously with increasing $B_{\parallel}$: the superconducting region progressively shifts toward higher electric field as the $B_{\parallel}$ increases and the transition temperature rises with increasing $B_{\parallel}$. Remarkably, the superconducting state remains robust under $B_{\parallel}$ up to 14 T, far exceeding the conventional Pauli limit. Quantum oscillation measurements further reveal that the superconductivity emerges from nematic Fermi surface reconstruction. These results suggest a spin-polarized superconducting states with unconventional origins.

### [143] [Dissipative Nonlinear Phononics: Nonequilibrium Quasiperiodic Order in Light-Driven Spin-Phonon System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13513)
*Brayan I. Eraso-Solarte,Yafei Ren*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了耗散在非线性声子学中的非平凡作用，通过调控自旋弛豫时间，系统可从平凡极限环过渡到时间有序态，自发打破驱动施加的离散时间平移对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性声子学（nonlinear phononics）已成为通过工程化保守势能景观来非热控制量子材料的有力范式。本研究旨在探索耗散（dissipation）如何作为非线性声子学中非平衡态的额外控制参数。

Method: 研究通过分析由圆偏振光驱动的自旋-声子耦合系统（spin-phonon coupled system），探究耗散的非平凡作用。通过调节自旋弛豫时间τ_s，观察系统稳态行为的变化。

Result: 研究发现，通过调控自旋弛豫时间，系统稳态可从平凡极限环（limit cycle）过渡到时间有序态，自发打破驱动施加的离散时间平移对称性（discrete time-translation symmetry）。在此态中，自旋和声子角动量均以涌现频率Ω_s持续振荡，该频率通常与驱动频率不可通约。

Conclusion: 该时间有序态由耗散诱导的自旋与声子角动量之间的相位滞后所稳定，该滞后产生维持振荡的反馈回路。耗散控制的相变可在朗道型框架（Landau-type framework）内用赝势（pseudo-potential）描述，其中序参数具有U(1)相位对称性，其振幅与声子角动量的振荡振幅成正比。

Abstract: Nonlinear phononics has emerged as a powerful paradigm for the nonthermal control of quantum materials by engineering a conservative potential energy landscape. Here, we show that dissipation can serve as an additional control knob for nonequilibrium states in nonlinear phononics. We reveal a nontrivial role of dissipation by investigating a spin-phonon coupled system driven by circularly polarized light. By tuning the spin relaxation time $τ_s$, the steady state undergoes a transition from a trivial limit cycle to a temporally ordered state, which spontaneously breaks the discrete time-translation symmetry imposed by the drive. In this state, both the spin and phonon angular momentum exhibit persistent oscillations at an emergent frequency $Ω_s$, which is generally incommensurate with the driving frequency. This state is stabilized by a dissipation-induced phase lag between spin and phonon angular momentum that generates a feedback loop sustaining the oscillation. The dissipation-controlled transition can be described within a Landau-type framework using a pseudo-potential, where the order parameter has a $U(1)$ phase symmetry, and its amplitude is proportional to the oscillation amplitude of the phonon angular momentum.

</details>


### [144] [Overcoming intrinsic material limitations through cavity feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13515)
*M. Ebrahimi,Y. Huang,V. A. S. V. Bittencourt,A. Rashedi,A. Metelmann,J. P. Davis*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过主动微波反馈回路（active microwave feedback loop）抑制腔磁极化子（cavity-magnon polariton）的线宽，成功将极化子-声子协同性（polariton-phonon cooperativity）从C=1提升至C=150，首次实现了腔磁极化子与机械模式之间的正常模式分裂（normal-mode splitting），为光子、磁振子和声子的三模杂化（three-mode hybridization）提供了直接证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁振子（magnons）在现代技术中具有重要应用潜力，但其与声子的弱磁致伸缩相互作用（weak magnetostrictive magnon-phonon interaction）以及由磁振子耗散主导的大极化子线宽，一直将磁振子系统限制在弱耦合区域（weak-coupling regime）。材料限制的磁振子耗散率被视为这些系统中不可避免的局限性。

Method: 研究采用主动微波反馈回路来抑制腔磁极化子的线宽，从而将其有效衰减率（effective decay rate）强烈抑制至低于磁振子限制的线宽。该方法通过增强极化子-声子协同性，突破了材料特性的限制。

Result: 极化子-声子协同性从C=1显著提升至C=150，实现了腔磁极化子与机械模式之间的正常模式分裂。这为光子、磁振子和声子的三模杂化提供了直接实验证据，表明系统进入了强耦合区域（strong-coupling regimes）。

Conclusion: 反馈控制（feedback）为突破材料特性限制、进入强耦合区域提供了一条通用路径，为混合量子系统（hybrid quantum systems）中的相干控制（coherent control）开辟了新的机会。

Abstract: Magnons, the quanta of spin waves, have significant potential for use in modern technologies, especially when strongly coupled to another mode for read-out and control. However, while magnons strongly interact with microwave photons via the magnetic-dipole interaction to form hybrid cavity-magnon polariton modes, the weak magnetostrictive magnon-phonon interaction, together with large polariton linewidths dominated by magnon dissipation, has so far restricted magnonic-spheres to the weak-coupling regime. The material-limited magnon dissipation rate in particular has been regarded as an unavoidable limitation in these systems. Here, we surpass this long-standing limitation by implementing an active microwave feedback loop to suppress the linewidth of cavity-magnon polaritons and strongly suppress their effective decay rate below the magnon-limited linewidth, thereby enhancing the polariton-phonon cooperativity from C=1 to C=150. As a key milestone, we achieve normal-mode splitting between a cavity-magnon polariton and a mechanical mode, providing direct evidence of three-mode hybridization among photons, magnons, and phonons. Our results establish feedback as a general route to accessing strong-coupling regimes in systems previously thought to be limited by material properties and hence open new opportunities for coherent control in hybrid quantum systems.

### [147] [Eccentricity valley Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13801)
*Jin Cao,Shen Lai,Cong Xiao,Qian Niu,Shengyuan A. Yang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Valleytronics harnesses the valley degree of freedom -- energy-degenerate extrema in the electronic band structure -- for information storage and processing. Valley Hall effect (VHE) is a cornerstone of valleytronics, enabling electric generation of pure valley currents. While extensively studied in systems with valleys located at time-reversal-breaking points, here, we shift the paradigm to valleytronic platforms with time-reversal-invariant valleys (TRIVs), revealing a novel phenomenon: eccentricity VHE. Unlike conventional VHE, the valley Hall angle for eccentricity VHE is an intrinsic geometric property, governed solely by the eccentricity of the valley Fermi surface, rendering it highly robust against variations in temperature or carrier density. Our findings reveal a critical overlooked facet of valley Hall physics, transcend the established VHE paradigm, and significantly broadens the scope of valleytronics.

Abstract: This work combines theory and experiment to examine the mechanisms underlying the harmonic generation of magnons. Within this framework, the harmonic response arises from nonlinear magnetization dynamics localized at strongly inhomogeneous textures, such as the sample edges and domain walls, that act as anharmonic confining potentials. Scanning probe imaging confirms that the harmonic response is correspondingly nonuniform and concentrated near the sample edges. We measure an expected nonlinear power-law scaling, a systematic shift toward larger wavevector excitations at higher harmonic order, and a spin-selective response indicative of an increasingly chiral harmonic stray field. Beyond macroscopic heating metrics, the heat generation is resolved at the intra-particle level, uncovering a heterogeneous landscape of localized ''hot spots'' with nanometer spatial and nanosecond temporal resolution. The results demonstrate that grain size acts as a key experimentally tunable parameter, balancing anisotropy disorder and pinning strength, thereby controlling both the magnitude and spatio-temporal distribution of heat release within the particle. In particular, nanoflower architectures composed by larger grains deliver larger heat generation, while the smaller grains offer a deeper intra-particle pinning landscape, which effectively redistributes the heat generation over extended time windows. Together, our results provide a mechanistic framework linking nanoparticle microstructure to magnetic heating and establish design principles for optimizing nanoflowers as magnetic hyperthermia transducers.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子自旋在晶体动量上的投影被提出作为量化晶体中布洛赫态电子手性（electronic chirality）的度量标准，预期会影响磁电和光学响应等多种物理性质。然而，在整个等能面上直接实验量化这一手性度量一直难以实现。

Method: 研究采用自旋和角度分辨光电子能谱直接探测电子手性，测量了具有强自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）的手性拓扑半金属RhSi中Kramers-Weyl和Weyl锥的体自旋织构。在量化Weyl锥的自旋轨道耦合分裂后，确定不同方位角下的自旋方向，提取能量依赖的自旋-动量锁定偏离。

Result: 从自旋-动量锁定偏离（高达约40°）定义了能量依赖的归一化电子手性密度（normalized electron chirality density, NECD），这是可直接获取的体电子手性度量。在RhSi中，NECD从Kramers-Weyl点处的1下降到其下方约200 meV处的约0.8。

Conclusion: 实验验证的NECD为手性材料的磁光和输运响应提供了预测能力，以纵向Edelstein效应为例证明了其应用价值。该研究首次实现了对整个等能面电子手性度量的直接实验量化。

Abstract: Recently, the projection of the electron's spin on its crystal momentum has been proposed as a metric to quantify electronic chirality of Bloch states in crystals, which is expected to affect a wide range of physical properties, such as magnetoelectric and optical responses. However, a direct experimental quantification of this chirality metric over an entire iso-energy surface has remained elusive. Here, we have used spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy to directly probe the electronic chirality by measuring the bulk spin texture of Kramers-Weyl and Weyl cones in RhSi, a chiral topological semimetal with strong spin-orbit coupling (SOC). After quantifying the SOC splitting of Weyl cones, we determine their spin direction along different azimuthal angles to extract energy dependent the deviations (up to ~40°) from perfect parallel spin-momentum locking. From these deviations we define an energy-dependent normalized electron chirality density (NECD), a directly accessible metric of bulk electronic chirality. In RhSi, the NECD decreases from 1 at the Kramers-Weyl point to ~0.8 at ~200 meV below it. Finally, we show that this experimentally grounded NECD provides predictive power for magneto-optical and transport responses of chiral materials, exemplified by the longitudinal Edelstein effect.

</details>


### [154] [Composite boson theory of Hall crystals and their transitions to Wigner crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14680)
*Julian May-Mann,Sayak Bhattacharjee,Srinivas Raghu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解二维电子系统在垂直磁场中的结晶行为，特别是探索霍尔液体、维格纳晶体以及兼具平移对称性破缺和量子霍尔响应的霍尔晶体之间的相变机制。

Method: 采用复合玻色子理论（composite boson theory）框架，将电子系统的三种状态映射到复合玻色子的对应相：超导体、莫特绝缘体和超固态，并分析相变过程中的重整化群行为。

Result: 研究发现当ν=1霍尔液体具有足够软的旋子时，会经历一级相变形成三角晶格霍尔晶体；进一步减小旋子质量会导致从霍尔晶体到维格纳晶体的连续相变。对于分数ν=1/m霍尔液体，由于通量附着引起的动力学阻挫，在中等相互作用强度下更倾向于形成蜂窝晶格霍尔晶体而非三角晶格。

Conclusion: 复合玻色子理论为理解二维电子系统的结晶现象提供了统一框架，揭示了不同晶格结构的形成机制及其相变特性，特别是在分数霍尔液体中动力学阻挫对晶格选择的重要影响。

Abstract: We consider the crystallization of a two-dimensional electron system in a perpendicular magnetic field using composite boson theory. There are three possible states to consider: the Hall liquid, the Wigner crystal, and the Hall crystal (a state with both broken translation symmetry and a quantized Hall response). Within composite boson theory, these states map onto a superconductor, a Mott insulator, and a supersolid of composite bosons respectively. We show that when a $ν= 1$ Hall liquid has a sufficiently soft roton, there is a first order transition to a triangular lattice Hall crystal. If we continue to decrease the roton mass, there is a continuous transition from the Hall crystal to a Wigner crystal. {When the Hall crystal exhibits the integer quantum Hall effect,} this transition {is} described by a free Dirac fermion and, at the critical point, the coupling to the phonons of the crystal is irrelevant, {in the {renormalization group} sense}. We extend this analysis to fractional $ν= 1/m$ Hall liquids. There, due to kinetic frustration arising from flux attachment, honeycomb lattice Hall crystals are preferred over triangular ones at intermediate interaction strength.

Method: 研究在铁磁纳米带（ferromagnetic nanostrip）的受限几何结构中实现了时空磁子涡旋束，通过分析其相位缺陷（phase dislocations）和传播特性来表征该新型波束。

Abstract: Recent theoretical and experimental studies revealed spatiotemporal photonic, and acoustic, vortex beams in open space. Here, we report spatiotemporal magnonic vortex beams in a confined geometry of a ferromagnetic nanostrip. The spatiotemporal magnonic vortex beam contains immobile phase dislocations and the wave propagates in a zigzag-like route. It is remarkable that the transverse orbital angular momentums, carried by the phase dislocations, are spatially alternating. Our findings are in sharp contrast to the photonic and acoustic counterparts, and open a new area in the study of spatiotemporal vortex beams.

### [156] [Universal tuning of quantum electrodynamic interactions from power laws to exponential screening and logarithmic antiscreening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14780)
*Michael N. Leuenberger,Daniel Gunlycke*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种材料无关的平台，用于实现量子电动力学相互作用的普适调控，可从幂律衰减调控至指数屏蔽和对数反屏蔽。该平台基于由两个栅极可调二维导体界定的介电间隔层，通过调控反射振幅的相位/奇偶性实现相互作用范围和强度的原位电控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种能够对量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamic, QED）相互作用进行普适调控的平台，实现对相互作用范围和强度的原位电控制。传统方法通常局限于特定材料或固定相互作用形式。

Method: 方法基于介电间隔层被两个栅极可调二维导体界定的异质结构平台。从QED作用量和格林函数（Green-function）表述出发，重求和多重反射级数，证明相互作用由离散的横向腔谐波（transverse cavity harmonics）控制。

Result: 在透明极限下，相互作用简化为体材料幂律形式。在反射极限下，反射振幅的相位/奇偶性选择两个性质不同的分支：Dirichlet/PEC分支产生指数衰减的贝塞尔函数，而Neumann/PMC类分支保留无能隙模式并显著增强长程尾部。

Conclusion: 结论表明同一异质结构能够提供对介导相互作用的范围和强度的原位电控制，实现了从幂律到指数屏蔽和对数反屏蔽的普适调控，为量子电动力学相互作用的可编程设计提供了平台。

Abstract: We introduce a material-agnostic platform for \emph{universal tuning of quantum electrodynamic interactions from power laws to exponential screening and logarithmic antiscreening}, realized in a dielectric spacer bounded by two gate-tunable two-dimensional conductors. The structured electromagnetic environment is completely specified by the transverse-magnetic and transverse-electric reflection amplitudes \(r_{\mathrm{TM/TE}}(q_\perp,ω)\) of the sheets. Starting from the QED action and a Green-function formulation, we resum the multiple-reflection series and show that the interactions are governed by a discrete set of transverse cavity harmonics. In the transparent limit \(r_{\rm TM}\to 0\), the interactions reduce to bulk power laws \(U(ρ)\propto ρ^{-α}\). In the reflective limit \(|r_{\rm TM}|\to 1\), the \emph{phase/parity} of \(r_{\rm TM}\) selects two qualitatively distinct branches: a Dirichlet/PEC (screening) branch \(r_{\rm TM}\to -1\) that removes the gapless transverse mode and yields an evanescent Bessel-\(K\) function \(U(ρ)\propto e^{-πρ/d}/\sqrt{ρ/d}\) at \(ρ\gg d\), and an opposite Neumann/PMC-like (antiscreening) branch \(r_{\rm TM}\to +1\) that retains a gapless mode and can strongly enhance the long-range tail. Thus, the same heterostructure provides in situ electrical control over both the \emph{range} and the \emph{strength} of mediated interactions.

Abstract: We develop the moiré band theory for M-valley twisted square homobilayers with layer groups $P$-$42m$ and $P$-$4m2$, and propose candidate material realizations. We show that moiré ferroelectricity-originating from sliding ferroelectricity in the untwisted bilayers-provides an independent control knob for miniband engineering in addition to interlayer tunneling. Abstract: We report a detailed investigation of low-frequency resistance fluctuations (1/f noise) in chemical vapor deposition (CVD) grown graphene. These results provide key insights into the microscopic mechanism of noise in scalable graphene films and highlight the role of defect engineering in optimizing graphene for large-scale electronic applications.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子（excitons）为玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）提供了一个有前景的固态平台，能够结合强相互作用、电可调性、高转变温度和多元序参量。然而，激子凝聚的确凿证据一直难以获得，需要开发新的探测方法来验证这一量子现象。

Method: 研究采用MoSe2/hBN/WSe2电子-空穴双层结构，该异质结构支持具有四个自旋-谷（spin-valley）自由度的平衡激子流体。通过稀释制冷机中的磁光光谱（magneto-optical spectroscopy）技术，直接探测了组成电子和空穴的自旋磁化率（spin susceptibility）。

Result: 研究揭示了三种具有不同风味极化（flavor polarization）的激子凝聚相：零磁场下，多体基态是两个同时凝聚的谷内激子（intravalley exciton）风味的相干叠加；弱临界磁场下，通过一级量子相变（first-order quantum phase transition）转变为双组分谷间激子（intervalley exciton）凝聚；高磁场下转变为完全极化的单组分凝聚。双组分凝聚态在高达约1.8 K的温度下仍然存在。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了范德华电子-空穴双层结构作为探索强相互作用、多组分激子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚的通用平台，为固态系统中多组分量子凝聚态的研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Macroscopic quantum coherence emerges when bosons condense into a Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC). First observed as a single-component superfluid in helium, BECs later emerged in ultracold atomic gases at nanokelvin temperatures as weakly interacting quantum fluids, which can also host multicomponent spinor condensates with rich internal degrees of freedom. Excitons provide a promising solid-state platform for BECs that can combine strong interactions, electrical tunability, high transition temperatures, and multicomponent order. Yet, conclusive evidence for condensation has remained elusive. Here, we report evidence of two-component exciton BECs in MoSe2/hBN/WSe2 electron-hole bilayers by directly probing the spin susceptibility of constituent electrons and holes. This heterostructure hosts equilibrium exciton fluids with four spin-valley flavors. Using magneto-optical spectroscopy in a dilution refrigerator, we reveal three exciton condensate phases with distinct flavor polarizations. At zero magnetic field, the many-body ground state is a coherent superposition of two simultaneously condensed intravalley exciton flavors. Under a magnetic field, the intravalley exciton condensate first switches to a two-component intervalley exciton condensate via a first-order quantum phase transition at a weak critical field, and then turns into a fully-polarized single-component condensate at high fields. The two-component condensates persist up to ~1.8 K. Our results establish van der Waals electron-hole bilayers as a versatile platform for exploring strongly interacting, multicomponent exciton BECs.

</details>


### [162] [Umklapp-Enhanced Interlayer Valley Drag in Moiré Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15520)
*Ritajit Kundu,Mandar M. Deshmukh,Herbert A. Fertig,Arijit Kundu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了范德华材料（van der Waals materials）形成的莫尔（moiré）双层系统中，由于倒逆散射（umklapp scattering）导致的层间谷拖曳（interlayer valley drag）显著增强效应，并提出可行的实验方案进行检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔图案（moiré patterns）作为有效晶格，其面内晶胞尺寸远大于层间距离，导致独特的层间相互作用行为。研究旨在探索晶格匹配莫尔双层系统中的层间谷拖曳现象及其增强机制。

Method: 通过理论分析研究晶格匹配莫尔双层系统中的层间相互作用，特别关注倒逆散射过程对层间谷拖曳的影响。同时提出基于当前先进制造技术的实验几何构型来检测和表征该效应。

Result: 研究发现层间谷拖曳在层间相互作用的一阶项即出现，并在低温极限下保持非零值，这与传统二维系统中的拖曳现象形成鲜明对比。倒逆散射导致了该效应的显著增强。

Conclusion: 莫尔双层系统中的层间谷拖曳展现出独特性质，其在一阶相互作用下的存在和低温非零特性为研究层间耦合提供了新视角。提出的实验方案有望在现有技术条件下验证这一理论预测。

Abstract: Van der Waals materials may be combined to form moiré patterns that are effectively crystal lattices. These systems are unique in that their in-plane unit cell sizes may be orders of magnitude larger than interlayer separations, leading to unique behaviors emerging from interlayer interactions. In this work, we investigate interlayer valley drag in lattice-matched moiré bilayers, demonstrating a remarkable enhancement due to umklapp scattering. In contrast to drag phenomena in more conventional two-dimensional systems, interlayer valley drag appears at first order in the interlayer interaction, and remains non-vanishing in the low temperature limit even at this low order in the interlayer coupling. We propose an experimental geometry, feasible with current state-of-the-art fabrication techniques, to detect and characterize this effect in moiré bilayer systems.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 结果显示电流与曲率之间存在耦合，表现为陀螺矢量（gyrovector）和附加耗散张量。扩展Thiele方程中的新项导致斯格明子动力学中的额外霍尔效应（additional Hall effect）和Walker极限条件的推广。

Abstract: Curvature is a highly relevant parameter when considering nanostructures, favoring the stability and affecting the dynamics of magnetic textures. Abstract: Quantum materials constitute a novel category of substances wherein quantum effects and electron-electron (e-e) interactions give rise to unforeseen phenomena on a macroscopic scale. Of particular interest within the realm of quantum materials are flat bands, which promote heavy conduction electrons and enhance e-e correlation effects. While the engineering of such flat bands has been demonstrated in graphene and two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenides moiré superlattices and in lithography defined semiconductor moiré superlattices, conventional tear-and-stack fabrication methods face challenges due to inevitable twist-angle disorder, strain, and relaxation effects, leading to issues with reproducibility and scalability. Here, we explore the creation and modification of flat bands through vertically engineered III-V semiconductor heterostructures, without the need for twisting. These artificial quantum materials offer a reproducible and scalable means for producing high-quality flat-band materials via molecular beam epitaxy growth. Our investigation includes magnetotransport and infrared magneto-spectroscopy studies of quad-layer InAs/GaSb quantum wells, accompanied by k*p band structure calculations, which illustrate the flattening of bands in vertically designed heterostructures.

### [165] [Probing the Penetration Depth of Topological Surface States by Magnetic Impurity Scattering in V-doped Sb$_2$Te$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15601)
*Yidi Wang,Zeyu Ma,Pengcheng Chen,Shiang Fang,Yu Liu,Yau Chuen Yam,Christopher Eckberg,Joshua Samuel,Johnpierre Paglione,Mohammad Hamidian,Cyrus Hirjibehedin,Daniel T. Larson,Efthimios Kaxiras,Jennifer E. Hoffman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种直接测量拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）表面态（surface state）穿透深度（penetration depth）的新方法，通过研究磁性杂质（magnetic impurity）与表面态的相互作用，在块体晶体中实现了亚纳米尺度的穿透深度测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统测量表面态穿透深度的方法需要制备不同厚度的薄膜样品，过程繁琐且耗时。本研究旨在开发一种更直接的方法，能够在块体晶体中直接探测表面态的穿透深度。

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy）和扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）技术，研究磁性钒（vanadium）杂质与拓扑绝缘体表面态的相互作用。通过在不同深度引入钒杂质作为精确的散射探针，分析其对表面态的影响。

Result: 研究发现，即使稀疏的磁性杂质（≤0.25%钒）也能使狄拉克表面态（Dirac surface state）产生能隙（gap）。单个钒杂质仅诱导局域态（localized state），不形成杂质带（impurity band），因此在远离杂质处狄拉克色散（Dirac dispersion）得以保持。在高磁场下，观察到第0朗道能级（0th Landau level）的能量移动和狄拉克点（Dirac point）处准粒子寿命（quasiparticle lifetime）的抑制，表明表面态存在磁散射（magnetic scattering）。

Conclusion: 通过利用不同深度的钒杂质作为精确散射探针，该方法成功揭示了块体晶体中表面态的亚纳米尺度穿透深度，为拓扑绝缘体表面态穿透深度的测量提供了一种直接且高效的新途径。

Abstract: Topological insulators host Dirac surface states (SS) protected by time-reversal symmetry. Inter-surface hybridization can gap the SS and give rise to the quantum spin Hall effect in films that are sufficiently thin compared to the SS penetration depth. However, quantifying the SS penetration depth typically requires painstaking synthesis of multiple films with varying thickness. Here we introduce a direct method to probe the SS penetration depth in bulk crystals, by studying the interplay between SS and magnetic impurities in \SVT. Using scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy, we find that even sparse magnetic impurities ($\lesssim0.25\%$ vanadium) can gap the Dirac SS. However, a single V impurity induces only localized states, and does not form an impurity band, so the gapped Dirac dispersion is preserved away from the impurity. In high magnetic fields, we observe an energy shift of the $0^\text{th}$ Landau level and a suppression of quasiparticle lifetime at the Dirac point, indicating \newtext{magnetic} scattering of the SS. Crucially, by employing V impurities at different depths as precise scattering probes, we reveal the SS penetration depth on the sub-nanometer scale in a bulk crystal.

### [166] [Measuring Primitive Accumulation: An Information-Theoretic Approach to Capitalist Enclosure in PIK2, Indonesia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13715)
*Sandy Hardian Susanto Herho,Alfita Puspa Handayani,Karina Aprilia Sujatmiko,Faruq Khadami,Iwan Pramesti Anwar*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本研究采用信息几何和统计力学工具，量化分析了雅加达北部PIK2沿海大型开发项目的非平衡空间过程，揭示了其转型速度、吸收时间和空间拓扑特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模土地圈占用于投机性大型开发构成非平衡空间过程，其速度、拓扑结构和不可逆性缺乏量化研究。本研究旨在通过信息几何和统计力学工具，精确表征资本主义空间积累的运动学和拓扑特征。

Method: 使用2017-2024年Sentinel-2土地利用/土地覆盖数据（10米分辨率），将景观投影到马克思概率单纯形（Marxian probability simplex），划分为公地、农业和资本三类。采用Fisher-Rao测地距离、吸收马尔可夫链分析和渗透分析等方法。

Result: 发现2019-2020年转型脉冲速度为0.405弧度/年；耕地和树木覆盖进入建成环境的预期吸收时间分别为46.0年和38.1年；建成区自保留率为96.4%；渗透分析显示巨型连通组件在远低于随机渗透阈值的概率下持续存在，表明规划性而非随机空间增长；城市边界分形维数从1.316增至1.397。

Conclusion: 信息几何和统计力学工具能够以定量精度表征资本主义空间积累的运动学和拓扑特征，为理解大规模土地开发的空间动态提供了新的分析框架。

Abstract: Large-scale land enclosure for speculative mega-development constitutes a non-equilibrium spatial process whose velocity, topology, and irreversibility remain poorly quantified. We study the Pantai Indah Kapuk 2 (PIK2) coastal mega-development north of Jakarta, Indonesia, using eight years (2017--2024) of Sentinel-2 land-use/land-cover (LULC) data at 10-meter resolution. The landscape is projected onto a Marxian probability simplex partitioning terrestrial pixels into Commons, Agrarian, and Capital fractions. Fisher-Rao (FR) geodesic distances on this simplex identify a transformation pulse of $0.405$~rad/yr during 2019--2020, coinciding with major construction activity. Absorbing Markov chain analysis yields expected absorption times into the built environment of $46.0$~years for cropland and $38.1$~years for tree cover, with a pooled built-area self-retention rate of $96.4\%$. Percolation analysis reveals that a giant connected component containing $89$--$95\%$ of all built pixels persists at occupation probabilities $p \in [0.096, 0.162]$, far below the random percolation threshold $p_c \approx 0.593$, indicating planned rather than stochastic spatial growth. The box-counting fractal dimension of the urban boundary increases from $d_f = 1.316$ to $1.397$, consistent with increasingly irregular frontier expansion. These results suggest that information-geometric and statistical-mechanical tools can characterize the kinematic and topological signatures of capitalist spatial accumulation with quantitative precision.

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过奇异的亚普朗克几何构造可以建立非超对称弦论与M理论的对偶关系，快子凝聚机制连接了超对称与非超对称理论，而对偶对称性为分析非超对称规范理论的强耦合行为提供了新框架，特别是四维规范理论在特定膜构型上的共形固定点。

Abstract: We propose an exotic geometric M-theory dual for the weak coupling Type 0A string: compactification on a sub-Planckian $S^1\vee S^1$ (two circles connected at a point), where strong quantum effects lead to fields living on distinct resolutions of that space. Moreover we argue that tachyon condensation of the 0A theory corresponds to shrinking of one of the two circles leading to the IIA supersymmetric string. We use this and other dualities to provide an F-theoretic description of the axio-dilaton and the tachyonic field of Type 0B and argue for the existence of a strong coupling critical point of the potential using the resulting duality symmetry $Γ_0(2)\subset SL(2,\mathbb{Z})$. The existence of this critical point can also be argued using conventional M-theory dualities. If this critical point is unique it is an unstable dS vacuum. Using this we propose a strong coupling conformal fixed point for a non-supersymmetric gauge theory in four dimensions living on coincident $D3^+-D3^-$branes of 0B.

Abstract: We compute the holographic Euclidean two-point function of scalar operators in a thermal state. We work directly using the Fourier series on the thermal circle. The result is manifestly periodic and consistent with analyticity in the strip $0<\mathfrak{Re}(τ)<β$. Expanding in $τ$ we obtain all OPE coefficients, including the double-trace sector. Thus our approach has an advantage compared to recent work where double-traces were bootstrapped from stress-tensor data. Bouncing singularities appear as non-perturbative sectors in the transseries for Fourier coefficients, but their transseries parameters are all zero in the case of the Euclidean correlator.

### [169] [Quantum obstructions for $N=1$ infinite distance limits -- Part II: Kähler obstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13470)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在分析四维Type IIB/F理论紧化中复结构模空间的量子修正，特别关注F理论在Calabi-Yau四重形（Calabi-Yau fourfolds）上Kähler模的量子修正。研究动机源于理解N=1超对称理论在量子水平上的场空间结构。

Method: 研究方法采用两种独立途径：首先对纯复结构无限远极限（pure complex structure infinite distance limits）的候选EFT弦（EFT strings）的世界面理论（worldsheet theory）进行详细分析；其次在大类理论中确认BPS瞬子（BPS instantons）作用量存在显著的复结构依赖的量子修正。

Result: 分析发现纯复结构无限远极限存在量子阻碍（quantum obstruction），且BPS瞬子作用量存在显著的复结构依赖量子修正。这些量子修正在大复结构极限下变得不可控，需要Kähler模的协同标度（co-scaling）来维持微扰控制，表明经典的等效作用量无法准确描述纯大复结构区域。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在量子水平上，F理论中的复结构极限会对理论其他部分产生强烈反作用，经典的等效作用量无法准确描述纯大复结构区域。这对弦现象学（string phenomenology），特别是模型构建（model building）和模稳定化（moduli stabilisation）具有潜在影响。

Abstract: We continue our analysis of quantum corrections in the complex structure moduli space of four-dimensional Type IIB/F-theory compactifications with N=1 supersymmetry. We find that limits in the complex structure moduli space of F-theory generically induce a strong backreaction on other sectors of the theory, reflecting the non-factorisation of the field space in genuine $N=1$ theories at the quantum level. Our focus is on quantum corrections to the Kähler moduli in F-theory on Calabi-Yau fourfolds and proceeds in two independent ways: A detailed analysis of the worldsheet theory of candidate EFT strings for pure complex structure infinite distance limits reveals a mismatch with expectations based on the classical effective action and points to a quantum obstruction of the limit. Complementary to this, we confirm, in large classes of theories, the existence of significant complex structure dependent quantum corrections to the action of BPS instantons which at tree-level are governed by the Kähler moduli. As the quantum corrections become uncontrolled at large complex structure, they require a co-scaling of the Kähler moduli to maintain perturbative control. As a result, the naive, classical effective action does not provide an accurate description of pure large complex structure regimes. We comment on possible implications for string phenomenology, specifically with regard to model building and moduli stabilisation.

</details>


### [170] [State-dependent geometries from magic-enriched quantum codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13475)
*ChunJun Cao,Gong Cheng,Krishnanand Karthikeyan,Cathy Li,John Preskill*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出近似量子纠错码（approximate quantum error correction）框架，用于描述引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）与时空涌现（emergent spacetime）。通过引入类Ryu-Takayanagi熵分解，定义原面积熵（proto-area entropy）概念，揭示了非局域魔法（non-local magic）在物质-几何耦合中的关键作用。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入类Ryu-Takayanagi熵分解用于近似子系统擦除纠错码（approximate subsystem erasure-correcting codes），通过最优恢复定义体物质熵（bulk matter entropy），并将边界熵与可恢复体熵之差定义为互补的原面积熵。研究了一类通过精确码的小型非局域扰动获得的偏斜量子码（skewed quantum codes）。

Result: 对于广泛的偏斜量子码类别，原面积熵随体物质熵单调增加，与量子极值曲面（quantum extremal surfaces）行为高度一致。这种响应的根源被识别为编码映射的Choi态中的三方非局域魔法（tripartite non-local magic），该特性在稳定子码（stabilizer codes）中消失，并控制近似子系统擦除纠错码中的主导物质-几何耦合。

Conclusion: 近似量子纠错码能够有效描述引力反作用，原面积熵与体物质熵的单调关系揭示了物质与几何之间的耦合机制。非局域魔法在编码映射中的存在是实现这种耦合的关键因素，为理解涌现时空中的引力效应提供了新视角。

Abstract: Quantum error-correcting codes provide a powerful framework for emergent spacetime, yet existing holographic code models describe only quantum fields on a fixed background: in exact erasure-correcting codes, the entropic area term is state independent and cannot capture gravitational backreaction. We argue that this limitation is intrinsic to exact subsystem recovery and that incorporating backreaction instead requires approximate quantum error correction. We introduce a Ryu-Takayanagi-like entropy decomposition for approximate subsystem erasure-correcting codes, defining bulk matter entropy via optimal recovery and a complementary proto-area entropy as the difference between boundary entropy and recoverable bulk entropy. For a broad class of skewed quantum codes obtained by small nonlocal perturbations of exact codes, the proto-area increases monotonically with bulk entropy, closely aligning with the behavior of quantum extremal surfaces. We identify the origin of this response as a form of tripartite non-local magic in the Choi state of the encoding map, which vanishes in stabilizer codes and controls the leading matter-geometry coupling in approximate subsystem erasure-correcting codes.

### [171] [On the Gauge-Invariant Fermion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13684)
*Kang-Sin Choi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 对于所有规范（gauge），自能的规范依赖部分都被消除；重整化后，物理质量（physical mass）在不同缀饰下保持一致，表明缀饰的非局域性、复合性和路径依赖性并非物理障碍。

Conclusion: 狄拉克费米子缀饰等价于规范参数的移动，缀饰相关的非局域性、复合性和路径依赖性不构成物理障碍，物理质量在不同缀饰方案下保持一致性。

Abstract: We show that the Dirac dressing of the fermion is equivalent to a shift of the gauge parameter. For every gauge, the gauge-dependent part is projected out of the self-energy. After renormalization, the physical mass is the same for every dressing. The non-locality, compositeness, and path dependence associated with the dressing are therefore not physical obstructions.

Conclusion: 量子弱宇宙监督原理作为半经典陈述，比经典弱宇宙监督原理更稳健。它表明奇点的热力学一致性必然要求其被隐藏，从而为禁止裸奇点提供了基于量子信息与时空几何联系的物理机制。

Abstract: Recent work has highlighted the deep connection between quantum information and spacetime geometry. Bousso and Shahbazi-Moghaddam (Phys. Rev. Lett. 128, 231301 (2022)) proved that ``hyperentropic'' regions -- where entropy exceeds the area bound -- inevitably lead to singularity formation. In this work, we explore the converse implication: does the thermodynamic consistency of such singularities require them to be hidden? We answer in the affirmative, establishing a Quantum Weak Cosmic Censorship principle governed by Generalized Entropy. This provides a semiclassical mechanism for censorship which forbids naked singularities. Since Quantum Weak Cosmic Censorship is a semiclassical statement, it is more robust than the classical Weak Cosmic Censorship showing naked singularities are forbidden in nature even if quantum effects are taken into account.

Abstract: We compute the one-loop QED $β$-function coefficient directly from heat kernel data of the twisted Spin$^c$ Dirac operator on $S^3 \times S^1$. Using $ζ$-function regularization, the logarithmic scale dependence is encoded in the $a_4$ coefficient of the spectral expansion. The $F_{μν} F^{μν}$ term in $a_4$ yields exactly $β(e) = e^3/(12π^2)$, independent of $r$, $L$, or background, verifying spectral RG flow without flat-space propagators. The result is independent of the radii of $S^3$ and $S^1$ and of the choice of gauge background, providing a parameter-free consistency check that spectral data on compact manifolds encode renormalization group information. Beyond a mere verification of the coupling flow, this result serves as a non-trivial consistency check of the Spectral Action Principle in a curved background. It demonstrates that universal quantum corrections can be extracted purely from geometric spectral invariants, distinguishing this geometric spectral derivation from momentum-space propagator methods.

### [174] [Geometric Aspects of Covariant Phase Space Formalism: Solution Space Slicings and Surface Charge Integrability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14439)
*M. Golshani,M. M. Sheikh-Jabbari,V. Taghiloo,M. H. Vahidinia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在协变相空间形式（CPSF）框架下，建立了时空和解相空间（SPS）的严格平行几何表述，系统分析了两个空间上的微分同胚和标架变换，解决了Wald-Zoupas可积性判据的切片依赖性问题，并区分了"虚假"和"真实"通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 协变相空间形式（Covariant Phase Space Formalism, CPSF）为微分同胚不变理论中的辛结构和表面荷提供了稳健框架，但现有研究主要关注时空变换，而解相空间（Solution Phase Space, SPS）上的变换被忽视。本文旨在建立两个空间的平行几何表述，并系统分析SPS上的变换。

Method: 通过建立时空和解相空间（SPS）的严格平行几何表述，在SPS上定义并研究切片变换（changes of slicing）。利用SPS上的弗罗贝尼乌斯定理（Frobenius theorem）扩展Wald-Zoupas可积性条件，发展出切片无关的判据，并推导SPS联络、挠率和曲率等基本几何量。

Result: 证明了标准Wald-Zoupas表面荷变分可积性判据本质上是切片依赖的。通过SPS上的弗罗贝尼乌斯定理，将Wald-Zoupas条件扩展为切片无关的可积性判据。区分了"虚假"通量（pure gauge artifacts of the SPS connection）和"真实"通量（non-vanishing SPS torsion），后者与物理引力新闻张量（gravitational News tensor）直接相关。

Conclusion: 本文发展的几何框架为协变相空间形式提供了更严格的数学基础，解决了可积性判据的切片依赖性问题，区分了不同类型的表面通量，并在SPS上给出了刘维尔定理（Liouville theorem）的几何表述，为有无传播体自由度的理论提供了统一分类方案。

Abstract: The Covariant Phase Space Formalism (CPSF) provides a robust framework for deriving symplectic structures and surface charges in diffeomorphism-invariant theories. By construction, the CPSF operates on two distinct manifolds: the spacetime and the Solution Phase Space (SPS). In this paper, we advance the formalism by establishing a strictly parallel geometric formulation for both manifolds. Within this framework, we systematically analyze diffeomorphisms and frame changes on both spaces. While spacetime diffeomorphisms have been extensively studied in the literature, transformations on the SPS have been largely overlooked; we rigorously define and investigate these as changes of slicing on SPS. We demonstrate that the standard Wald-Zoupas criterion for the integrability of surface charge variations is inherently slicing-dependent. To resolve this issue, we develop the Frobenius theorem on the SPS and use it to extends the Wald-Zoupas condition into an inherently slicing-independent criterion for integrability. The Frobenius theorem on the SPS also yields a rigorous and natural definition of fundamental geometric quantities on the solution space, specifically the SPS connection, torsion, and curvature. Furthermore, this geometric machinery naturally distinguishes between fundamentally different surface fluxes: "fake" fluxes are identified mathematically as pure gauge artifacts of the SPS connection, while "genuine" fluxes manifest as non-vanishing SPS torsion, which directly relates to the physical gravitational News tensor. Finally, we present a geometric formulation of the Liouville theorem on the SPS, offering a unified classification scheme for theories with and without propagating bulk degrees of freedom.

  The further equivariant refinement of this cohomology theory reduces on A-type singularities to a form of relative 2-Cohomotopy which geometrically engineers Chern-insulator phases on $\mathrm{M5}\cap \mathrm{A}_n$, with the M-string playing the role of gapped nodal lines.

### [177] [A Holographic Model for Soft Photons and Gravitons in Four Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14499)
*Sangmin Choi,Prahar Mitra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了四维阿贝尔规范理论和引力理论红外（infrared）扇区的二维天球（celestial sphere）作用量，通过全息模型（holographic model）重现了四维理论的关键红外特性，并构造了产生红外有限散射振幅的无穷类着装态（dressed states）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于构建一个描述四维阿贝尔规范理论和引力理论红外扇区的二维天球作用量，通过全息模型系统性地重现四维理论的红外特性，包括Goldstone模式匹配条件、软定理和红外发散结构。

Method: 方法基于全息模型构建二维天球作用量，利用该模型重现四维理论中的超相位旋转（superphaserotation）和超平移（supertranslation）Goldstone模式的反极匹配条件（antipodal matching conditions）、领头软光子（soft photon）和软引力子（soft graviton）定理，以及一般着装态的振幅红外因子化（infrared factorization）。

Result: 结果显示该全息模型能够重现标准未着装振幅的红外发散（infrared divergences），并证明涉及Faddeev-Kulish着装态（Faddeev-Kulish dressed states）的振幅是红外有限的。作为推论，利用该模型构造了产生红外有限散射振幅的无穷类着装态。

Abstract: We construct a two-dimensional action on the celestial sphere that describes the infrared sector of Abelian gauge and gravitational theories in four dimensions. In particular, we use the holographic model to reproduce (1) antipodal matching conditions for the superphaserotation and supertranslation Goldstone modes in four dimensions, (2) leading soft photon and graviton theorems, and (3) infrared factorization of amplitudes with generic dressed $in$ and $out$ states. Using (3), we reproduce the infrared divergences that plague the standard undressed amplitudes, and show that amplitudes involving Faddeev-Kulish dressed states are infrared finite. As a corollary, we use our holographic model to construct an infinite class of dressed states that give rise to infrared finite scattering amplitudes.

</details>

Abstract: We discuss the semi-classical quantisation of supersymmetric membranes in holographic geometries with asymptotic AdS$_4$ and AdS$_7$ boundary conditions. In AdS$_4$ geometries this quantisation prompts the need of ensemble changes when comparing bulk and boundary observables arising from such membranes. We also discuss how supersymmetric membranes localise to loci where the background Killing spinor turns chiral, circumventing the need of evaluating their zero-mode moduli integrals. Finally, we discuss a bulk analysis of an infinite tower of membrane instantons, or giant gravitons, in AdS$_7$ geometries, whose worldvolume dynamics effectively reduces to a quantum mechanical system. This allows us to test, in a holographic setting, the emergence proposal that perturbative supergravity data may be extracted from towers of membrane instantons.

### [179] [Residual group-like symmetries in selection rules without group actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14836)

Conclusion: 尽管有限群共轭类的融合规则在圈图水平通常被破坏，但通过"群化"过程可以保留精确的残余类群对称性。这些对称性控制着圈诱导耦合的大小，并确保相关参数的自然性。群化对称性的反常现象为具有非可逆融合规则的模型提供了额外的理论约束。

Abstract: We analyze loop-induced group-like symmetries in theories where fields are labeled by basis elements of a fusion algebra constructed from the conjugacy classes of finite groups. Although the fusion rules for conjugacy classes are in general violated at loop level, residual group-like symmetries, including both Abelian and non-Abelian ones, remain exact through a procedure referred to as ``groupification''. By examining various conjugacy classes of finite groups realized in heterotic string theory on non-Abelian orbifolds, we identify an approximate discrete symmetry that controls the magnitude of loop-induced couplings. As a result, most parameters appearing in non-invertible selection rules are natural in the sense of 't Hooft. Furthermore, we discuss anomalies of the groupification symmetry, which can impose additional constraints on models with non-invertible fusion rules.

### [180] [Galois Covers of Calabi-Yau Quivers and BPS State Counting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15334)
*Johannes Aspman,Cyril Closset,Elias Furrer,Jan Manschot*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究BPS箭图（BPS quiver）的伽罗瓦覆盖（Galois cover），建立了覆盖箭图与原箭图之间的BPS不变量关系公式，特别关注于卡拉比-丘三倍体（Calabi-Yau threefold）奇点相关的CY₃箭图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BPS箭图在理解4维N=2超对称场论（4d N=2 supersymmetric field theories）和卡拉比-丘三倍体奇点处的D-膜（D-branes）中具有核心地位。这两个主题通过II型弦理论（Type II string theory）中的几何工程（geometric engineering）深度关联，其中CY₃箭图描述了奇点处的分数膜（fractional branes）。

Method: 研究任意BPS箭图Q通过有限阿贝尔群（finite abelian group）G的伽罗瓦覆盖，得到覆盖箭图Ŝ。该方法基于箭图箭头的G-分级（G-grading），可理解为轨道折叠（orbifolding）过程。研究采用超对称箭图量子力学（supersymmetric quiver quantum mechanics）语言，分析G作用在箭图表示模空间（moduli spaces of quiver representations）上的固定轨迹，以及Q和Ŝ的Kontsevich-Soibelman代数（Kontsevich-Soibelman algebras）之间的同态。

Result: 主要结果是4维N=2场论BPS不变量的显式覆盖公式：Q的有理BPS不变量（rational BPS invariant）Ω̄ᴼ(γ)可表示为覆盖箭图Ŝ的BPS不变量之和。该公式在多个特殊情况下推导得出，包括γ为原始电荷向量（primitive charge vector）的情况、无环箭图（quivers without loops）的一般电荷向量情况，以及一些简单几何（如锥形（conifold）或局部del Pezzo曲面（local del Pezzo surfaces））的CY₃箭图情况。

Conclusion: 一般公式以猜想形式提出，可在许多例子中验证。特别地，若Q是奇点X的CY₃箭图，则伽罗瓦覆盖Ŝ是轨道折叠奇点X/G的CY₃箭图，建立了箭图覆盖与几何轨道折叠之间的对应关系。

Abstract: BPS quivers are central to our understanding of BPS states in 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric field theories and of D-branes at Calabi-Yau threefold singularities. The two subjects are deeply interrelated through geometric engineering in Type II string theory, where a CY$_3$ quiver, also known as a 5d BPS quiver, describes fractional branes at a threefold singularity ${\bf X}$. We study the Galois cover ${\skew{2}\tilde Q}\rightarrow Q$ of any BPS quiver $Q$ by a finite abelian group $\mathbb{G}$, leading to a covering quiver ${\skew{2}\tilde Q}$. The Galois cover is determined by a $\mathbb{G}$-grading of the arrows of the quiver $Q$, which can be understood as an orbifolding procedure. In particular, if $Q$ is a CY$_3$ quiver for ${\bf X}$, then the Galois cover $\skew{2}\tilde Q$ is the CY$_3$ quiver for the orbifold singularity ${\bf X}/\mathbb{G}$. We explore such Galois covering procedures in the language of supersymmetric quiver quantum mechanics, in terms of fixed loci under $\mathbb{G}$ actions on moduli spaces of quiver representations, and in terms of homomorphisms between the Kontsevich-Soibelman algebras of $Q$ and ${\skew{2}\tilde Q}$. Our main result is an explicit covering formula for the BPS invariants of 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ field theories, wherein the rational BPS invariant $\barΩ^Q(γ)$ of $Q$ is expressed as a sum of BPS invariants of $\skew{2}\tilde Q$. We derive this formula in various special cases, which include the case when $γ$ is a primitive charge vector, the case of general charge vectors for quivers without loops, and the case of CY$_3$ quivers for some simple geometries such as the conifold or local del Pezzo surfaces. The general formula is presented as a conjecture that can be verified in many examples.

</details>

*Zvi Bern,Avery Jackman,Gareth Mansfield,Michael S. Ruf*

TL;DR: 该论文解释了为何在第五阶后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）近似下，卡拉比-丘（Calabi-Yau）和完全椭圆积分（complete elliptic integrals）不贡献于保守可观测量，尽管它们出现在中间计算步骤中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在阐明在引力波物理的保守部门中，某些复杂的数学结构（如卡拉比-丘和完全椭圆积分）为何最终不贡献于物理可观测量，尽管它们在中间计算中自然出现。

Method: 通过分析在维度正规化（dimensional regularization）中产生对数项（logarithm of the momentum transfer）的奇异区域，作者展示了在经典极限下，负责卡拉比-丘和完全椭圆行为的积分类别不出现于紫外奇异结构中。

Result: 研究证明，在偶数圈阶次，保守贡献与动量转移的对数项（logarithm of the momentum transfer）相关联，而这些对数项源自奇异区域；卡拉比-丘和完全椭圆积分类别在经典极限下不参与生成所需对数的紫外奇异结构。

Conclusion: 该分析不仅解释了特定阶次下数学结构的消失，还为分析偶数圈阶次保守部门中多圈积分的经典极限提供了替代策略，深化了对引力波理论中积分结构简化机制的理解。

Abstract: We explain why Calabi-Yau and complete elliptic integrals do not contribute to conservative observables at fifth post-Minkowskian order, despite appearing in intermediate steps. At even loop orders, conservative contributions are tied to terms proportional to the logarithm of the momentum transfer, which in dimensional regularization arise from singular regions. We show that in the classical limit, the integral classes responsible for Calabi-Yau and complete elliptic behavior are absent from the ultraviolet singular structures that generate the required logarithm. This perspective also suggests alternative strategies for analyzing the classical limit of multiloop integrals in the conservative sector at even loop orders.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究证实了全息Krylov复杂度在N=4 SYM库仑分支中的几何解释，揭示了复杂度振荡行为与几何奇点之间的关联，为理解量子混沌和复杂度演化提供了新的全息视角。

Abstract: We study holographic Krylov complexity in the Coulomb branch of ${\cal N}=4$ SYM. Adopting the proposal that the time derivative of the Krylov complexity is dual to the proper radial momentum of a massive particle, we investigate two probe geodesics within this geometry. For one of the radial trajectories we obtain exact analytic results, even when additional motion in the internal space is included. In cases where the geodesic avoids the interior curvature singularity, the Krylov complexity exhibits oscillatory behavior, with a frequency governed by the Coulomb scale and an amplitude determined by the UV cutoff, the Coulomb scale, and the angular momentum. This oscillatory pattern is lost, when the radial trajectory is approaching the singularity. Finally, we compare our holographic results with field-theoretic calculations, finding qualitative agreement.

### [184] [Oscillons from $Q$-balls in generalized models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15505)
*E. da Hora,Fabiano C. Simas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了具有非标准运动学（non-canonical kinematics）的扩展模型中振荡子（oscillon）与Q-球（Q-ball）的关系。通过重整化群微扰展开（RGPE）方法，证明了即使在非平凡运动学存在下，这种关系依然成立，并应用于三种有效情形。研究发现，对于高阶近似，广义振荡子与底层Q-球的关系属于不同的普适性类别（universality class）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索在包含非标准运动学的扩展模型中，振荡子与Q-球之间的关系是否依然成立。具体而言，模型包含一个实标量场，其动能项通过一个广义化函数进行扩展，旨在验证非平凡运动学是否影响这种基本关系。

Method: 研究方法采用重整化群微扰展开（Renormalization Group Perturbation Expansion, RGPE），将实标量场部分近似到簿记参数（book-keeping parameter）的三阶。对于高阶情况，分析扩展到五阶近似，并探索了奇异的φ^6-情景（φ^6-scenario）。

Result: 研究结果表明，即使在非平凡运动学存在下，振荡子与底层Q-球的关系依然成立。在三种有效情形中，解析表达式能高度精确地模拟非标准振荡子的数值演化，特别是在小到中等振幅范围内。当初始振幅增大时，数值剖面呈现调制行为，研究采用双Q-球解来种子化解析振荡子。

Conclusion: 结论指出，非标准构造允许在简单φ^2-势（φ^2-potential）下存在行为良好的振荡子，这些剖面与先前情况表现一致，属于同一普适性类别。然而，对于五阶近似下的φ^6-情景，广义振荡子与底层Q-球的关系属于不同的普适性类别。

Abstract: We study the oscillon/$Q$-ball relation in an extended model with non-canonical kinematics. The model contains a single real scalar field whose kinetic term is enlarged to include a generalizing function. We approximate the real sector up to the third order in a book-keeping parameter. In this context, we implement the Renormalization Group Perturbation Expansion (RGPE), from which we conclude that the relation between oscillons and underlying $Q$-balls holds even in the presence of nontrivial kinematics. We apply our results to the study of three different effective cases. In all of them, our expressions mimic the numerical evolution of nonstandard oscillons with great accuracy, especially for small and moderate amplitudes. As the initial amplitude increases, the numerical profile develops a modulated behavior, and we use a two $Q$-balls solution to seed our analytical oscillon. We discuss how our non-canonical construction allows the existence of a well-behaved oscillon in connection to the simplest $φ^2$-potential. This novel profile behaves in the same general way as the previous ones. So, we argue that they belong to the same universality class. Finally, we extend our analysis to consider those contributions up to the fifth order in the approximation expansion. We explore an exotic $φ^6$-scenario, and conclude that the relation between generalized oscillons and underlying $Q$-balls now belongs to a different universality class.

### [186] [Bouncing geodesics, black hole singularities, and singularities of thermal correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15598)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反弹测地线（bouncing geodesics）可作为黑洞奇点（black hole singularities）的有效探针，其在边界理论中的存在编码于关联函数（correlation functions）的解析结构中。这为分析、诊断和分类具有曲率奇点（curvature singularities）的时空提供了一个实用的全息框架（holographic framework）。

Method: 采用双曲微分方程的Hadamard理论（Hadamard theory of hyperbolic differential equations）证明，当两点可通过零测地线（null geodesic）连接时，体（bulk）和边界（boundary）推迟传播子（retarded propagators）均会发散。研究还分析了全息重整化（holographic renormalisation）对偶传播子结构的影响，并对任意时空中的反弹测地线及相关关联函数奇点进行了普遍表征。

Result: 证明了反弹测地线方法在研究黑洞奇点时的有效性及具体局限性。特别展示了一个自对偶线性轴子模型（self-dual linear axion model）中的黑洞实例，该黑洞存在曲率奇点但缺乏反弹测地线，表明反弹测地线的缺失并不必然排除奇点的存在。

Conclusion: 研究建立了黑洞奇点与边界理论关联函数解析结构之间的精确全息对应，但同时也明确了反弹测地线作为奇点探针的局限性，即某些存在曲率奇点的黑洞可能不表现出反弹测地线行为。

Abstract: Bouncing geodesics have been used as valuable probes of black hole singularities. In the dual boundary theory, the presence of bouncing geodesics is encoded in the analytic structure of correlation functions. Thus, when their existence is related to the presence of a black hole singularity, this presents a practical holographic framework to analyse, diagnose, and classify spacetimes with curvature singularities. To make this intuition precise, we use the Hadamard theory of hyperbolic differential equations to prove that both bulk and boundary retarded propagators diverge whenever two points can be connected by a null geodesic. We clarify why this statement remains valid beyond the geodesic regime (for operators of any dimension) and examine how holographic renormalisation modifies the structure of the dual propagator. We also present a general characterisation of bouncing geodesics and the associated singularities in correlation functions for arbitrary spacetimes. Furthermore, we compare the analytic structure of the correlators in position and momentum space and discuss explicit examples. Finally, we demonstrate the validity and concrete limitations of the bouncing geodesic approach to the study of black hole singularities. In particular, we show an explicit example of a black hole in the self-dual linear axion model, which has a curvature singularity despite the absence of bouncing geodesics.

</details>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [187] [Speed fluctuations of a stochastic Huxley-Zel'dovich front](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13458)
*Evgeniy Khain,Baruch Meerson,Pavel V. Sasorov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了随机Huxley-Zel'dovich反应-扩散前沿的长时间速度涨落，包括典型涨落（表现为前沿扩散）和大偏差行为。蒙特卡洛模拟验证了微扰理论预测的渐近标度关系，同时揭示了前沿粒子在达到预期扩散渐近行为前的异常动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反应-扩散前沿的实证速度会因反应和扩散的固有散粒噪声（shot noise）而产生涨落。本研究旨在探究随机Huxley-Zel'dovich前沿的长时间速度涨落特性，该前沿描述A粒子向初始空区域的入侵过程，在确定性描述中处于边缘稳定但非线性不稳定状态。

Method: 研究采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）验证微扰理论（perturbation theory）的预测。该理论模型涉及A粒子在一维晶格上的快速连续时间随机游走（continuous-time random walk）以及可逆的现场反应（on-site reactions）$2A \rightleftarrows 3A$。

Result: 模拟结果支持微扰理论的渐近预测：平均前沿速度的系统性偏移$δc$和前沿扩散系数$D_f$均按$1/N$标度，其中$N$为过渡区域的典型粒子数。同时发现前沿最初几个粒子在达到预期扩散渐近行为前存在长寿命的异常行为（long-lived anomalous behavior）。

Conclusion: 随机Huxley-Zel'dovich前沿的长时间速度涨落包含典型涨落和大偏差（large deviations）两方面。大偏差由系统的最优历史（optimal histories）主导，表现为以不同于平均速度传播的前沿，甚至可能反向传播。

Abstract: The empirical speed of travelling reaction-diffusion fronts fluctuates due to the intrinsic shot noise of the reactions and diffusion. Here we study the long-time front speed fluctuations of a stochastic Huxley-Zel'dovich front. It involves a population of particles $A$ which perform a fast continuous-time random walk on a one-dimensional lattice and undergo reversible on-site reactions $2A \rightleftarrows 3A$. This front describes an invasion of $A$-particles into an initially empty region of space which, in a deterministic description, is marginally stable but nonlinearly unstable with a zero instability threshold. Typical fluctuations of this front can be described as front diffusion in a reference frame moving with the average front speed. According to the existing perturbation theory, the shot-noise-induced systematic shift of the average front speed, $δc$, and the front diffusion coefficient, $D_f$, are both expected to scale with $N$ as $1/N$, where $N \gg 1$ is the typical number of particles in the transition region. Furthermore, $D_f$ can be determined perturbatively in the small parameter $1/\sqrt{N}$. Our Monte Carlo simulations support these asymptotic results, but also reveal a long-lived anomalous behavior of the first few particles before they reach the expected diffusion asymptotic. We also study large deviations of the empirical speed of the front at long times. These are dominated by optimal histories of the system in the form of a propagating front which travels with a speed different from the average speed, or even travel in the wrong direction.

</details>


### [188] [Energy Dynamics and Partial Consumption in Foraging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13481)
*Md Aquib Molla,Sanchari Goswami*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了觅食者在阈值能量水平下的部分食物消耗行为。研究发现，觅食者寿命随k/S比值增加而增长，存在一个临界阈值k*≈√S，在此阈值上下寿命增长速率不同。多个关键参数表现出有趣的标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索觅食者在阈值能量限制下的部分食物消耗行为。这种觅食策略允许食物不完全耗尽，从而可能延长觅食者的生存时间，研究其动态特性和标度行为。

Method: 研究方法基于觅食者模型，该觅食者具有生存时间S（无食物可存活步数）和阈值能量水平k。当觅食者能量低于阈值k时才会消耗食物，且仅部分消耗食物而非完全耗尽。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）觅食者寿命τ随k/S比值增加而增长；2）存在临界阈值k*≈√S，低于此阈值时寿命增长迅速，高于时增长缓慢；3）寿命呈现幂律行为τ∼S^β，β值在k/S=0时为4/3，随后跃升至2以上，并随k/S增加逐渐降至1.84；4）觅食者死亡后被完全或部分消耗食物的地点数量N_eat在k/S≈0.5时呈现交叉行为。

Conclusion: 研究表明，阈值能量限制下的部分食物消耗策略能有效延长觅食者寿命。该模型揭示了多个关键参数的标度行为，包括寿命、临界阈值和食物消耗地点的统计特性，为理解觅食行为中的能量管理策略提供了理论框架。

Abstract: In this work, we consider partial consumption of food by a forager in presence of a threshold energy level. The forager considered here can survive for $S$ steps without food, namely the survival time. The threshold limits the consumption of food in such a way that, the forager will only consume food, whenever its energy is below the threshold $k$. Due to partial consumption of food, a site containing food may not always be fully depleted, which in turn helps in increasing the lifetime of the forager. It has been observed that, in our case, the lifetime always increases with $k/S$, although there is a transition threshold $k^*$ below which the increase of lifetime is rapid and above is low. The transition threshold $k^* \sim \sqrt{S}$. The lifetime $τ$ shows a power law behavior as $τ\sim S^β$. For $k/S=0$, the value of $β$ is $4/3$, it then jumps above $2$ and decreases gradually to $1.84$ with increasing $k/S$. Other important quantities like number of revisits to a site, food statistics etc. have been studied and these also show some interesting scaling behavior. The collection of sites either fully or partially depleted of food after the death of the forager $N_{eat}$ shows a crossover behaviour for $k/S \sim 0.5$.

</details>


### [189] [On thermalization in many-body classical Floquet systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13631)
*Anton Kapustin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究证明了无限多经典多体Floquet系统在代数起源下，非常一般的初始态都会热化（thermalize），并指出热化的唯一障碍是存在随时间周期变化的局域可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然物理直觉预期周期性驱动的封闭多体系统会最终热化到最大熵状态，但这一性质比遍历性（ergodicity）或混合性（mixing）更强，且数学上难以严格证明。研究旨在为热化现象提供严格的数学基础。

Method: 研究描述了一类具有代数起源的无限多经典多体Floquet系统，并针对这些系统证明了非常一般初始态的热化性质。方法基于对系统动力学的代数结构分析。

Result: 证明了对于任何足够均匀的局域可微哈密顿量的吉布斯态（Gibbs state），在长时间极限下都会加热到无限温度。研究确认了物理直觉：热化的唯一障碍是存在随时间周期变化的局域可观测量。

Conclusion: 该研究为周期性驱动多体系统的热化现象提供了严格的数学证明框架，建立了代数起源系统与热化行为之间的理论联系，并明确了局域周期性可观测量是阻碍热化的关键因素。

Abstract: It is expected that a generic closed many-body system prepared in a well-behaved initial state and subjected to a periodic drive will eventually thermalize, i.e. approach the state of maximal entropy. This property, while compatible with and even demanded by the physical intuition, is much stronger than ergodicity or mixing and is difficult to justify mathematically. We describe an infinite set of classical many-body Floquet systems of algebraic origin for which thermalization of very general initial states can be proved. For example, we show that a Gibbs state of any sufficiently uniform local differentiable Hamiltonian heats up to infinite temperature at long times. We show that in agreement with the physical intuition, the only obstruction to thermalization is the existence of local observables which are periodic in time.

</details>


### [190] [Nonholonomic constraints at finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14424)
*Eduardo A. Jagla,Anthony M. Bloch,Alberto G. Rojo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非完整约束（nonholonomic constraints）系统在热浴耦合下的行为，以Chaplygin sleigh为范例。研究发现，简单的朗之万（Langevin）型方法会导致违反热力学第二定律的悖论，而通过物理上合理的粘性相互作用极限实现约束，并纳入涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relations）要求的随机力，可恢复对第二定律的遵从。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究非完整约束系统与热浴耦合时的行为，特别是当简单的朗之万型方法预测可提取有用功而违反热力学第二定律时，需要解决这一悖论并理解理想化非完整约束的物理可实现性限制。

Method: 采用两种方法：一是通过简单添加随机和耗散项到运动方程的直接朗之万型方法；二是将非完整约束作为粘性相互作用的极限情况进行物理实现，并在有限温度下纳入涨落-耗散关系所要求的接触点随机力。

Result: 直接朗之万方法预测了可提取有用功从而违反热力学第二定律的机制。然而，通过物理实现的粘性相互作用极限方法，在纳入涨落-耗散关系要求的接触点随机力后，系统恢复了对热力学第二定律的遵从。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，理想化非完整约束的物理可实现性存在基本限制。只有在适当考虑涨落-耗散关系所要求的随机力时，非完整约束系统与热浴的耦合才能与热力学第二定律保持一致。

Abstract: We investigate the behavior of dynamical systems with nonholonomic constraints when coupled to a thermal bath, focusing on the paradigmatic case of the Chaplygin sleigh. A straightforward Langevin-type approach obtained by naively adding stochastic and dissipative terms to the equations of motion predicts a regime in which useful work can be extracted, violating the second law of thermodynamics. To resolve this paradox, we resort to a physically motivated implementation of the nonholonomic constraint as the limiting case of a viscous interaction. However, at finite temperature, fluctuation-dissipation relations imply that the viscous force has to be complemented with stochastic forces acting at the contact. We show that their incorporation restores compliance with the second law. Therefore, our results place fundamental limits on the physical realizability of idealized nonholonomic constraints.

</details>


### [191] [First-return time in fractional kinetics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14487)
*M. Dahlenburg G. Pagnini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了分数动力学随机游走中首次返回时间（first-return time）的统计特性，发现当跳跃大小分布对称时，首次返回时间密度仅由等待时间分布决定，与跳跃大小分布无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解分数动力学（fractional kinetics）框架下随机游走者的首次返回时间统计特性，特别是在分数扩散（fractional diffusion）模型中，该模型基于连续时间随机游走（continuous-time random walk）理论构建。

Method: 研究方法采用连续时间随机游走框架下的非耦合表述（uncoupled formulation），使用米塔格-莱夫勒分布（Mittag-Leffler distributed）的等待时间。分析涵盖马尔可夫（Markovian）和非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）设置，以及所有对称跳跃大小分布（包括有限或无限方差的情况）。

Result: 研究结果表明，当跳跃大小分布对称时，首次返回时间密度确实与跳跃大小分布无关，仅受体现过程记忆的等待时间分布影响。分析在"先跳跃后等待"（first jump then wait）和"先等待后跳跃"（first wait then jump）两种情况下进行，提供了多个精确结果。

Conclusion: 该研究得出了分数动力学随机游走中首次返回时间的关键结论：对称跳跃大小分布不影响首次返回时间统计，过程记忆特性完全由等待时间分布决定。研究还建立了马尔可夫和非马尔可夫设置之间的关系，并比较了两种不同时序情况下的差异。

Abstract: The first-return time is the time that it takes a random walker to go back to the initial position for the first time. We study the first-return time when random walkers perform fractional kinetics, specifically fractional diffusion, that is modelled within the framework of the continuous-time random walk on homogeneous space in the uncoupled formulation with Mittag-Leffler distributed waiting-times. We consider both Markovian and non-Markovian settings, as well as any kind of symmetric jump-size distributions, namely with finite or infinite variance. We show that the first-return time density is indeed independent of the jump-size distribution when it is symmetric, and therefore it is affected only by the waiting-time distribution that embodies the memory of the process. We perform our analysis in two cases: first jump then wait and first wait then jump, and we provide several exact results, including the relation between results in the Markovian and non-Markovian settings and the difference between the two cases.

</details>


### [192] [Information-Driven Phase Transition on Weighted Graphs with Spontaneous Dimensional Sensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13896)
*Valerio Dolci*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于谱曲率（spectral curvature）$\mathcal{R}$的加权图信息流模型（FIU），发现了三个核心结果：系统在耦合参数$g_c \approx 0.023$处存在尖锐相变；节点层面存在稳定的离散泊松关系；该关系展现出对维度的自发敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索拓扑结构根据谱曲率（spectral curvature）$\mathcal{R}$演化的加权图上的信息流动。该模型旨在理解曲率依赖的耗散和长程连接形成如何影响信息传输和结构自组织。

Method: 研究方法基于FIU模型，该模型从图格林函数（graph Green function）的对角线定义谱曲率$\mathcal{R}$，通过曲率依赖的耗散传播能量，并以耦合参数$g$控制的速率在高$\mathcal{R}$节点间创建长程连接（long-range links）。

Result: 研究发现了三个主要结果：1）系统在$g_c \approx 0.023$处存在尖锐相变（sharp phase transition），局部信息通量$\sigma$与结构形成从反相关转变为强相关；2）节点层面存在稳定的离散泊松关系$\nabla^2\mathcal{R}(i) = \kappa\sigma_{\rm prev}(i)$，其中$\kappa$在参数间保持稳定；3）该关系展现出对维度的自发敏感性（spontaneous dimensional sensitivity），在2D和3D晶格中表现出不同的衰减行为。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明谱曲率$\mathcal{R}$是系统的中心自组织变量，其离散泊松关系揭示了信息流与曲率之间的基本联系。系统展现出拓扑挫折（topological frustration）和与引力维度特征的类比，表明该模型可能捕捉到复杂网络中的基本物理原理。

Abstract: We study information flow on a weighted graph whose topology evolves according to a spectral curvature measure $\mathcal{R}$. The model (FIU) defines $\mathcal{R}$ from the diagonal of the graph Green function, propagates energy with curvature-dependent dissipation, and creates long-range links between high-$\mathcal{R}$ nodes at a rate controlled by a coupling parameter $g$.
  We report three results. First, the system exhibits a sharp phase transition at $g_c \approx 0.023$: below $g_c$, local information flux $σ$ and structure formation are anti-correlated; above $g_c$, they become strongly correlated (Pearson $r \approx 0.75$, $p < 10^{-38}$), with signatures of a continuous transition and mean-field exponent $ν\approx 0.54$.
  Second, we identify a node-level discrete Poisson relation $\nabla^2\mathcal{R}(i) = κ\,σ_{\rm prev}(i)$, where $κ$ is stable across parameters (CV $= 3.1\%$ across independent configurations). Mediator analysis reveals this correlation is almost entirely mediated by $\mathcal{R}$ itself, identifying it as the central self-organizing variable.
  Third, the Poisson relation exhibits spontaneous dimensional sensitivity: in 2D lattices both signals decay for $N \gtrsim 576$, while in 3D they persist to $N \lesssim 1728$. This emerges without any dimensional parameter in the rules. The collapse mechanism is curvature homogenization at large $N$. We interpret this as topological frustration in a mesoscopic regime, and discuss analogies with dimensional signatures of gravity.

</details>


### [193] [Channel transport: gating, geometry, and heterogeneous diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13918)
*Sean D Lawley*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究推导了通道扩散通量的显式估计公式，同时考虑了随机门控（stochastic gating）、通道几何形状和异质扩散三个因素，并通过模拟验证了其准确性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通道介导的运输在生物学中普遍存在，先前理论研究试图确定扩散通量如何依赖于随机门控、通道几何形状和异质扩散，但缺乏综合考虑这三个因素的统一估计。

Method: 推导了通道扩散通量的显式估计公式，该公式同时考虑了随机门控、通道几何形状和异质扩散三个因素，并在特定参数范围内证明了估计的精确性。

Result: 研究结果显示，推导的估计公式在特定参数范围内是精确的，且通过随机模拟验证了该估计在广泛参数范围内保持准确，与物理学文献中的某些结果存在差异。

Conclusion: 该研究成功推导出综合考虑随机门控、通道几何和异质扩散的扩散通量估计公式，为通道介导运输提供了更全面的理论框架。

Abstract: Channel-mediated transport is ubiquitous in biology. A series of works by different theoreticians have sought to determine how the diffusive flux through a channel depends on (a) stochastic gating, (b) channel geometry, and (c) heterogeneous diffusion. In this paper, we derive an explicit estimate for the diffusive flux through a channel that accounts for these three factors. We show that our estimate is exact in certain parameter regimes. We further use stochastic simulations to confirm that our estimate remains accurate across a very broad range of parameters. Our estimate differs from some results in the physics literature.

### [194] [Possibilities of applying boundary functionals of random processes to nuclear safety problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14058)
*V. V. Ryazanov*

TL;DR: 该研究评估了随机风险过程的边界泛函（boundary functionals）在解决核电站核安全问题中的潜力，特别关注中子行为显著变化的特定情境，如熔盐堆（MSRs）、高温气冷堆（HTGRs）等。

Motivation: 研究动机在于评估随机风险过程的边界泛函在核电站核安全问题中的应用潜力，特别是在中子行为发生显著变化的特定运行和事故情境下，如熔盐堆、高温气冷堆、粉末燃料堆、反应堆启动和堆芯坍塌事故分析等。

Method: 研究方法基于随机风险过程的边界泛函理论，该方法能够精确计算功率分位数（power quantile），并在抽象定向渗流（directed percolation）与保护设置的工程计算之间建立数学桥梁。

Result: 研究发现，在特定核反应堆情境下，中子行为分布发生显著变化：正态分布被稳定分布和极限分布所取代，中子聚类（neutron clustering）开始发挥重要作用，而边界泛函能够为这些变化提供精确的数学描述和计算工具。

Conclusion: 边界泛函为解决核电站核安全问题提供了有效的数学工具，特别是在中子行为分布发生显著变化的复杂情境中，该方法能够精确计算功率分位数并连接抽象理论与工程实践。

Abstract: The potential for using boundary functionals of random risk processes to solve nuclear safety problems at nuclear power plants is assessed. In certain situations (MSRs (Molten Salt Reactors), High-Temperature Gas-Cooled Reactors (HTGRs), pulverized fuel reactors, reactor startups, and accident analysis (core collapse)), neutron behavior changes significantly. Neutron clustering begins to play an important role, and the distributions characterizing neutron behavior change. The normal distribution is replaced by stable, but also limiting, distributions. Boundary functionals allow for precise calculation of the power quantile and provide a mathematical bridge between abstract directed percolation and engineering calculations of protection settings.

### [195] [Intrinsic Error Thresholds in Nearly Critical Toric Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14098)
*Zack Weinstein,Samuel J. Garratt*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索通过微扰拓扑稳定子码接近连续量子相变而构建的近临界拓扑量子码中的信息保护机制。特别关注受局部泡利（Pauli）退相干影响的横场（transverse-field）环面码（toric code）。

Method: 采用相干信息（coherent information）的副本统计物理映射（replica statistical physics mapping），将退相干理解为在三维副本统计物理模型中引入二维副本间缺陷（inter-replica defect）。通过场论分析（field theoretical analysis）研究该缺陷对体临界点（bulk critical point）的影响。

Result: 场论分析表明，该副本间缺陷对体临界点是微扰无关的（perturbatively irrelevant），且无法重整化横场强度，从而导致了有限误差阈值（finite error threshold）。即使横场调至无限接近临界点，仍需要有限强度的泡利退相干才能不可逆地破坏编码信息。

Conclusion: 对于一大类近临界拓扑码（nearly critical topological codes）在各种退相干通道（decoherence channels）下，可以得出类似的定性结论，表明这类系统在接近量子临界点时仍能保持对退相干的鲁棒性。

Abstract: We study the protection of information in nearly critical topological quantum codes, constructed by perturbing topological stabilizer codes towards continuous quantum phase transitions. Our focus is on the transverse-field toric code subjected to local Pauli decoherence. Despite the strong quantum fluctuations of anyons when the transverse field is tuned infinitesimally close to the critical point, we show that a finite strength of Pauli decoherence remains necessary to irreversibly destroy information encoded in the ground-state manifold. Using a replica statistical physics mapping for the coherent information, we show that decoherence can be understood as introducing a two-dimensional inter-replica defect within a three-dimensional replica statistical physics model. A field theoretical analysis shows that this defect is perturbatively irrelevant to the bulk critical point, and cannot renormalize the transverse field strength, leading to a finite error threshold. We argue that a qualitatively similar conclusion can be drawn for a broad class of nearly critical topological codes, under a variety of decoherence channels.

### [196] [Parity superselection obstructs monogamy of mutual information in free fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14154)
*Aleksandrs Sokolovs*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明自由费米子在自旋（张量积）因子化下违反互信息单调性（monogamy of mutual information），并通过DMRG计算量化了相互作用费米子中的效应。研究强调使用I₃作为诊断工具时必须明确算子代数（operator algebra）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于澄清互信息单调性（monogamy of mutual information）在不同算子代数下的表现差异。论文旨在解决使用三重互信息I₃作为诊断工具时可能出现的模糊性，特别是在全息对偶（holographic duality）、量子混沌（quantum chaos）和费米面拓扑（Fermi surface topology）等领域的应用中。

Method: 方法基于精确的算子恒等式：不相交区域的自旋约化密度矩阵与费米子约化密度矩阵相差一个宇称插入（parity insertion）(-1)^{N_B}。同时采用严格的熵界（entropy bound）进行证明，并利用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算在t-V链上量化相互作用费米子的效应。

Result: 研究证明自由费米子在自旋因子化下违反互信息单调性：对于宽度w=1,2的三个相邻条带在所有费米动量下I₃^{spin}>0，且对所有w在z=k_F w<z^*≈1.329时成立。DMRG计算显示在中等填充下，因子化对I₃表观K依赖性的贡献超过真实相互作用贡献8倍，并解释了自旋基数值中约80%的偏差。强排斥作用（K≲0.7）在两个代数中都恢复了单调性。

Conclusion: 结论强调任何使用I₃作为诊断工具——无论是用于全息对偶、量子混沌还是费米面拓扑——都必须明确指定算子代数。没有这种规范，I₃的符号是模糊的，这凸显了算子代数选择在量子信息理论应用中的重要性。

Abstract: We prove that free fermions in the spin (tensor product) factorization violate monogamy of mutual information: $I_3^{\mathrm{spin}} > 0$ for three adjacent strips of width $w = 1, 2$ at all Fermi momenta, and for all~$w$ at $z = k_F w < z^* \approx 1.329$. The proof rests on an exact operator identity -- the fermionic and spin reduced density matrices of disjoint regions differ by the parity insertion $(-1)^{N_B}$ in the partial trace -- and a rigorous entropy bound.
  DMRG calculations on the $t$-$V$ chain quantify the effect for interacting fermions: the factorization contribution to the apparent $K$-dependence of $I_3$ exceeds the genuine interaction contribution by a factor of~8 at moderate filling, and accounts for ${\sim}80\%$ of the deviation observed in spin-basis numerics. Strong repulsion ($K \lesssim 0.7$) restores monogamy in both algebras.
  These results imply that any use of $I_3$ as a diagnostic -- whether for holographic duality, quantum chaos, or Fermi surface topology -- must specify the operator algebra; without this specification, the sign of $I_3$ is ambiguous.
