### [197] [Breakdown of Linear Response Induced by Velocity-Dependent Stochastic Resetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14164)
*Yuto Takeishi,Takuma Akimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文展示了在线性响应理论（linear response theory）中，由于状态依赖的随机重置（state-dependent stochastic resetting），物理系统对弱外力的响应可能不再成比例，导致非线性输运（nonlinear transport）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性响应理论是输运现象的基础，但该研究旨在探索这一原理在非平衡（nonequilibrium）条件下可能失效的情况。研究动机源于输运过程中快速载流子经历更频繁散射事件的现象，这启发了对速度依赖重置机制（velocity-dependent resetting mechanism）的考察。

Method: 研究考虑了一个受驱动的朗之万粒子（driven Langevin particle），其重置速率（resetting rate）随粒子速度的幂次增长。通过推导精确的稳态速度分布（steady-state velocity distribution）和建立矩平衡关系（moment balance relation），分析了外部驱动、粘性耗散和重置诱导耗散之间的关联。

Result: 研究发现响应由速度与重置速率之间的非线性耦合控制，导致非线性输运。具体而言，平均速度遵循精确的幂律关系 $\langle v\rangle \propto F^{1/(α+1)}$，其中 $α$ 表征重置速率的速度依赖性。这提供了线性响应在主导阶行为层面失效的可解示例。

Conclusion: 速度依赖的随机重置（velocity-dependent stochastic resetting）被确定为在非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady states）中产生非线性输运的最小动力学机制。该研究为线性响应理论的失效提供了可解析的范例，并揭示了状态依赖重置在输运现象中的关键作用。

Abstract: Linear response theory lies at the foundation of transport phenomena, predicting that physical systems respond proportionally to weak external forces. Here we show that this principle can break down in a minimal nonequilibrium setting due to state-dependent stochastic resetting. We consider a driven Langevin particle subject to a resetting mechanism whose rate grows as a power of the particle velocity, motivated by transport processes where faster carriers experience more frequent scattering events. We derive the exact steady-state velocity distribution and establish a moment balance relation that links external driving, viscous dissipation, and resetting-induced dissipation. This relation reveals that the response is controlled by a nonlinear coupling between the velocity and the resetting rate, leading to nonlinear transport. In particular, the mean velocity obeys the exact power law $\langle v\rangle \propto F^{1/(α+1)}$, where $α$ characterizes the velocity dependence of the resetting rate. Our results provide a solvable example in which linear response fails at the level of the leading-order behavior and identify velocity-dependent resetting as a minimal dynamical mechanism for generating nonlinear transport in nonequilibrium steady states.

### [198] [Coarsening in the long-range Persistent Voter Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14165)
*Jeferson J. Arenzon,F. Corberi,W. G. Dantas,L. Smaldone*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索长程变体持续选民模型中的粗化动力学行为，特别是分析具有两种置信水平（正常和狂热者）的代理人在不同空间维度下的演化规律。该研究旨在理解意见惯性如何影响系统动力学，并与已知的最近邻情况进行比较。

Method: 研究方法包括数值模拟和理论分析。通过数值模拟研究一维和二维系统中不同α值下的动力学行为；对于一维情况，进一步开发了理论分析方法，重现了相关长度对α的依赖关系和相关函数的函数形式。

Result: 研究结果表明，对于所有α值，该模型都属于长程伊辛模型淬火到小非零温度时的同一普适性类别（same universality class）。理论分析成功再现了一维情况下相关长度的α依赖性和相关函数的函数形式。

Conclusion: 结论确认了意见惯性（opinion inertia）的引入缓解了选民模型中存在的强界面噪声，从而恢复了伊辛模型的基本动力学机制。这些发现不仅验证了先前对最近邻情况的了解，还扩展了这种对应关系的适用性。

Abstract: We investigate the coarsening kinetics in a long-range variant of the Persistent Voter Model in space dimension $d=1$ and 2. In this model agents can hold two confidence levels, normal and zealot. If normal, agents take the opinion of others chosen at distance $r$ with probability $P(r) \propto r^{-α}$, with $α>d$. While in the zealot state, agents keep their own opinion. Normal (zealot) agents can become zealots (normal) if their opinion is equal (different) to that of the chosen neighbour. Through numerical simulations we show that, for any values of $α$, the model belongs to the same universality class of the long-range Ising model quenched to a small (non-zero) temperature, similarly to what was already known for the nearest-neighbor case. For the one-dimensional case, we further develop an analytical treatment, which reproduces the $α$-dependence of the correlation length and the functional form of the correlation function. These results not only confirm that the introduction of opinion inertia mitigates the strong interfacial noise present in the voter model, thus reinstating the basic kinetic mechanism of the Ising model, but also expand the applicability of this correspondence.

### [199] [Discrete Time Crystal Order in Spin-Chains Enabled by Floquet Flat-Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14307)
*Mahbub Rahaman,Analabha Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 提出一种基于平带（flat-band）驱动的新型协议，可在无杂质（clean）的自旋-1/2链中实现离散时间晶体（discrete time-crystal, DTC）序。该协议通过工程化完全简并的Floquet准能谱来抑制热化，并产生稳健的倍周期亚谐响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统离散时间晶体（DTC）的实现通常依赖于无序诱导的多体局域化（many-body localized, MBL）或动力学多体局域化（dynamically many-body localized, DMBL）。本研究旨在探索一种无需无序的替代方案，利用平带驱动在清洁系统中实现DTC序。

Method: 提出一种新型驱动协议：在每个驱动周期中，先进行全局自旋翻转，随后施加一个双音调平带（two-tone flat-band）段。该平带段工程化出完全简并的Floquet准能谱。通过精确时间演化（exact time evolution）分析序参量的傅里叶频谱。

Result: 在序参量的傅里叶频谱中，于驱动频率的一半处观测到显著的亚谐峰，为稳定DTC的出现提供了明确证据。该相态对系统尺寸、相互作用强度和范围不敏感，但对自旋转动误差（spin-rotation errors, εr）敏感。与MBL和DMBL DTC相比，平带协议在驱动参数上具有更广泛的调谐性。

Conclusion: 平带驱动为无杂质自旋系统中的离散时间晶体序提供了一条通用且实验相关的途径。通过引入额外的自旋-自旋相互作用，可以抑制对自旋转动误差的敏感性，从而在有限的耦合强度和驱动频率窗口内实现稳健的DTC响应。

Abstract: We propose a novel protocol to realize discrete time-crystal (DTC) order in clean, periodically driven spin-$1/2$ chains. In each drive cycle, a global spin flip is followed by a two-tone flat-band segment. This flat-band segment engineers a fully degenerate Floquet quasienergy spectrum, suppresses thermalization, and stabilizes a robust period-doubled subharmonic response. Using exact time evolution, we identify a pronounced subharmonic peak at half the drive frequency in the Fourier spectrum of the order parameter, thereby providing clear evidence for the emergence of stable DTC. The resulting phase is insensitive to system size, interaction strength, and interaction range; however, it remains sensitive to spin-rotation errors ($\varepsilon_r$), which can destabilize the subharmonic response. Compared with disorder-induced many-body localized (MBL) and disorder-free dynamically many-body localized (DMBL) DTCs, we find that the exact flat-band protocol offers a broader tunability of drive parameters, whereas MBL and DMBL based DTCs are more resistant to $\varepsilon_r$. In particular, the $\varepsilon_r$ sensitivity can be suppressed by incorporating additional spin-spin interactions that have modest deviations from the ideal flat-band protocol. This manifests itself in a robust DTC response over a finite window of spin-coupling strengths and drive frequencies. Our results establish flat-band driving as a versatile and experimentally relevant route to DTC order in disorder-free spin systems and motivate further exploration of non-equilibrium phases.

### [200] [Observation-Time-Induced Crossover in Driven Anomalous Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14685)
*Masahiro Shirataki,Takuma Akimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在强异质介质中，微弱恒定力如何通过反常输运的涨落被检测到。研究发现，力的关键特征出现在粒子位移的方差中，而非平均漂移。对于α<2的系统，响应表现出观测时间诱导的交叉现象：在固定偏压下，方差最初遵循无偏标度，仅在后期过渡到力主导的非平衡状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索在强异质介质中，微弱恒定力如何通过反常输运的涨落被检测到。传统方法关注平均漂移，但本研究揭示力的关键特征实际上体现在粒子位移的方差中，这为检测弱力提供了新视角。

Method: 研究方法采用两种代表性模型：带偏置的连续时间随机游走（continuous-time random walk, CTRW）和带偏置的淬灭陷阱模型（quenched trap model, QTM）。通过分析位移方差的力依赖性，量化涨落对弱驱动的响应，特别关注α<2的情况。

Result: 研究发现对于α<2的系统，响应表现出观测时间诱导的交叉现象。在固定偏压下，方差最初遵循无偏标度，仅在后期过渡到力主导的非平衡状态。等价地，在固定观测时间t下，存在阈值偏压ε_c(t)将类平衡状态与可检测的非平衡响应分开，该阈值随t增加而降低。淬灭无序（quenched disorder）相比CTRW进一步降低了检测阈值。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，微弱力在强异质介质中可通过涨落检测，且检测能力随观测时间增加而增强。交叉现象反映了有限观测时间与驱动异质系统本征弛豫时间之间的竞争，淬灭无序进一步降低了检测阈值，为弱力检测提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate how a weak constant force becomes detectable through fluctuations in anomalous transport in strongly heterogeneous media. Rather than focusing on the mean drift, we show that the key signature of the force appears in the variance of the particle displacement. As representative models, we study a biased continuous-time random walk (CTRW) with nearest-neighbor jumps and a biased quenched trap model (QTM) with a power-law waiting-time tail. By analysing the force dependence of the displacement variance, we quantify how fluctuations respond to weak driving. We find that for $α<2$, the response exhibits an observation-time-induced crossover: at fixed bias, the variance initially follows its unbiased scaling and only at later times crosses over to a force-dominated nonequilibrium regime. Equivalently, at fixed observation time $t$, there exists a threshold bias $\varepsilon_c(t)$ separating an apparently equilibrium-like regime from a detectable nonequilibrium response. This threshold decreases with increasing $t$, implying that weaker forces become observable over longer measurement windows. Quenched disorder further lowers the detection threshold compared with CTRW, and the crossover reflects a competition between the finite observation time and the intrinsic relaxation time of the driven heterogeneous system.

### [201] [Scaling Autoregressive Models for Lattice Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14695)
*Xiaochen Du,Juno Nam,Sulin Liu,Rafael Gómez-Bombarelli*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合任意顺序自回归模型（any-order ARMs）和边缘化模型（MAMs）的框架，用于高效学习晶格原子构型的统计分布，相比传统采样方法显著降低了计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预测材料在真实条件下的行为需要理解晶格上原子构型的统计分布，这是合金设计、催化和相变研究的核心问题。传统马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov-chain Monte Carlo）采样存在收敛慢和在相变附近临界减慢的问题，而现有自回归模型（autoregressive models, ARMs）由于固定顺序生成构型且内存和训练成本高，限制了其在真实系统中的应用。

Method: 开发了一个结合任意顺序自回归模型（any-order ARMs）和边缘化模型（marginalization models, MAMs）的框架。任意顺序ARMs通过以任意已知晶格位点子集为条件灵活生成构型，而MAMs通过单次前向传播近似任何部分构型的概率，大幅降低内存需求。该框架支持具有晶格感知位置编码（lattice-aware positional encodings）的Transformer架构，并在可管理的计算成本下实现。

Result: 基于Transformer的任意顺序MAMs在二维伊辛模型（two-dimensional Ising model）和CuAu合金上比基于多层感知机的ARMs获得了更精确的自由能，准确捕捉了相变和临界行为。该框架将系统规模从10×10扩展到20×20的伊辛系统，以及从2×2×4扩展到4×4×8的CuAu超晶胞，相比传统采样方法显著降低了计算成本。

Conclusion: 该框架结合了任意顺序ARMs的灵活性和MAMs的高效性，使在较小晶格上训练的模型能够复用于采样更大系统，同时支持具有晶格感知位置编码的Transformer架构，为材料科学中的统计分布学习提供了可扩展且计算高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Predicting how materials behave under realistic conditions requires understanding the statistical distribution of atomic configurations on crystal lattices, a problem central to alloy design, catalysis, and the study of phase transitions. Traditional Markov-chain Monte Carlo sampling suffers from slow convergence and critical slowing down near phase transitions, motivating the use of generative models that directly learn the thermodynamic distribution. Existing autoregressive models (ARMs), however, generate configurations in a fixed sequential order and incur high memory and training costs, limiting their applicability to realistic systems. Here, we develop a framework combining any-order ARMs, which generate configurations flexibly by conditioning on any known subset of lattice sites, with marginalization models (MAMs), which approximate the probability of any partial configuration in a single forward pass and substantially reduce memory requirements. This combination enables models trained on smaller lattices to be reused for sampling larger systems, while supporting expressive Transformer architectures with lattice-aware positional encodings at manageable computational cost. We demonstrate that Transformer-based any-order MAMs achieve more accurate free energies than multilayer perceptron-based ARMs on both the two-dimensional Ising model and CuAu alloys, faithfully capturing phase transitions and critical behavior. Overall, our framework scales from $10 \times 10$ to $20 \times 20$ Ising systems and from $2 \times 2 \times 4$ to $4 \times 4 \times 8$ CuAu supercells at reduced computational cost compared to conventional sampling methods.

</details>


### [202] [A Formal Physical Framework for the Origin of Life: Dissipation-Driven Selection of Evolving Replicators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15230)
*Shlomo Segal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个基于非平衡系统统计物理学的生命起源形式化物理框架，揭示了耗散历史概率偏差如何导致遗传机制的选择，并证明模板指导复制相比简单自催化具有双重指数概率优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从耗散与过程概率的已知联系（如Crooks涨落定理）过渡到系统历史概率的大偏差框架，揭示具有更大累积耗散历史的概率偏差。通过严格数学命题分析简单自催化和模板指导复制的差异。

Result: 形式化框架显示概率偏差倾向于选择遗传机制：模板指导复制通过其突变和适应能力（推导出有效适应率α），解锁了超指数增长路径，其涌现相对概率随时间呈双重指数放大，构成渐近主导的物理选择偏差。

Conclusion: 该框架描绘了从简单耗散结构到信息承载复制子的层次转变，其稳定性取决于超越保真度、动力学效率和资源供应的临界阈值。提出了精确定量可证伪的实验方案，定义了识别合成化学系统中进化过程开始的精确数学特征。

Abstract: The emergence of life from inanimate matter presents a thermodynamic challenge: the Second Law of Thermodynamics dictates a global trend towards disorder, yet life constitutes localized pockets of profound organization. This paper presents a formal physical framework for abiogenesis grounded in the statistical physics of non-equilibrium systems. We transition from the established connection between dissipation and process probability (e.g., Crooks Fluctuation Theorem) to a large-deviation framework for the likelihood of system histories. This formalism reveals a probabilistic bias towards histories with greater integrated dissipation. We then demonstrate how this bias leads to the selection of heredity. The core of our argument is a rigorous mathematical proposition showing that while simple autocatalysis leads to an exponential increase in dissipation, template-directed replication, via its capacity for mutation and adaptation (a process from which we derive an effective adaptation rate, alpha), unlocks a super-exponential growth pathway. This translates to a doubly-exponential amplification in the relative probability of its emergence over time, constituting an asymptotically dominant physical bias for its selection. This framework delineates a hierarchical transition from simple dissipative structures to information-bearing replicators, whose stability is contingent upon exceeding critical thresholds of fidelity, kinetic efficiency, and resource supply. We conclude by proposing a refined, quantitative, and falsifiable experiment, defining a precise mathematical signature for identifying the onset of evolutionary processes in synthetic chemical systems.

### [203] [Exact and limit results for the CTRW in presence of drift and position dependent noise intensity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15426)
*Marco Bianucci,Mauro Bologna,Riccardo Mannella*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究了具有漂移和位置相关跳跃的连续时间随机游走（CTRW），推导了驱动噪声的多时间关联函数精确表达式，并建立了无需扩散极限或分数标度假设的精确非局域主方程。主要发现是：在长时间极限下，该非局域主方程可被仅含瞬时更新率R(t)的普适局域主方程精确近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有漂移和位置相关跳跃的连续时间随机游走（CTRW）为描述广泛自然和工程系统提供了高度通用的框架。然而，这类模型的分析通常需要引入扩散极限、分数标度假设或闭合假设等近似。

Method: 通过分析与此类模型相关的随机微分方程（SDE），其中驱动噪声ξ(t)由尖峰（shot）事件组成。采用G-累积量（G-cumulant）形式体系推导精确结果，并在相互作用表象（interaction representation）中分析主方程结构。

Result: 获得了两个精确解析结果：1）推导了ξ(t)的n-时间关联函数（n-time correlation functions）的闭式表达式，表示为观测时间所有2^(n-1)个有序划分的和；2）建立了CTRW变量x(t)概率密度函数的精确非局域主方程（non-local master equation）。主要发现是普适局域主方程（universal local master equation）的涌现：在长时间极限下，精确非局域主方程可被仅含瞬时更新率R(t)的局域主方程精确近似。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有漂移和位置相关跳跃的CTRW提供了精确解析框架，揭示了在长时间极限下非局域主方程可被普适局域主方程精确近似的普遍规律。数值实验证实了该近似的显著准确性，即使远超出朴素时间尺度分离（time-scale separation）所能证明的范围。

Abstract: Continuous-time random walks (CTRWs) with drift and position-dependent jumps provide a highly general framework for describing a wide range of natural and engineered systems. We analyze the stochastic differential equation (SDE) associated with this class of models, in which the driving noise $ξ(t)$ consists of spike (shot) events, and we derive two exact analytical results. First, we obtain a closed-form expression for the $n$-time correlation functions of $ξ(t)$, expressed as a sum over all $2^{\,n-1}$ ordered partitions of the observation times (Proposition~2). Second, using the $G$-cumulant formalism, we derive an \emph{exact} non-local master equation (ME) for the probability density function of the CTRW variable $x(t)$, valid without invoking diffusive limits, fractional scaling assumptions, or closure hypotheses (Proposition~3). In interaction representation, this ME retains the same structural form as that of the standard CTRW without drift or position-dependent jumps. Our main result is the emergence of a \textbf{universal local master equation}: at long times, the exact non-local ME is universally and accurately approximated by a time-local ME whose only coefficient is the instantaneous renewal rate $R(t)$. This approximation reproduces the exact Poissonian ME when $R$ is constant, and numerical experiments confirm its remarkable accuracy even far beyond regimes where a naive time-scale separation would justify it.

### [204] [Glass and jamming transitions in a random organization model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15519)
*Leonardo Galliano,Ludovic Berthier*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟探索了描述非布朗悬浮液吸收相变的二维非晶格粒子模型，揭示了非平衡玻璃转变、阻塞转变与吸收相变之间的复杂关系，并发现随机组织模型与热软粒子系统在玻璃和阻塞转变方面具有深刻的物理相似性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探索描述驱动非布朗悬浮液（driven non-Brownian suspensions）中吸收相变（absorbing phase transitions）的二维非晶格粒子模型（off-lattice particle model），通过分析其相图来理解非平衡系统中的相变行为。

Method: 研究采用数值模拟方法探索(φ,ε)相图，其中φ为堆积分数（packing fraction），ε控制粒子跳跃幅度；使用二元混合物（binary mixture）抑制结晶，以区分非晶态之间的相变；通过不同制备协议（preparation protocol）研究动态冻结（dynamic arrest）对临界吸收相变的影响。

Result: 研究发现：在大φ区域，吸收相变前存在非平衡玻璃转变（non-equilibrium glass transition）到非扩散非晶态；动态冻结使临界吸收相变位置具有协议依赖性；ε→0的相变线端点定义了阻塞转变（jamming transition），其位置随制备协议连续变化；阻塞转变附近的临界指数与基于能量最小化的替代方法和平均场复制理论（mean-field replica theory）预测一致；在流体和玻璃相中观察到具有不同特征的超均匀性（hyperuniformity）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，随机组织模型（random organization models）与经历玻璃和阻塞转变的热软粒子系统（thermal soft-particle systems）具有深刻的物理相似性，微观动力学的非平衡性质对涌现的物理性质影响很小。

Abstract: We study a two-dimensional, off-lattice particle model introduced to describe absorbing phase transitions in driven non-Brownian suspensions. We numerically explore the $(φ,ε)$ phase diagram, where $φ$ is the packing fraction and $ε$ controls the amplitude of particle jumps. We use a binary mixture to suppress crystallization, which allows us to disentangle the model's distinct phase transitions between amorphous states. At large $φ$, we find that the approach to the absorbing transition is preceded by a non-equilibrium glass transition to a non-diffusive amorphous state. This dynamic arrest makes the location of the critical absorbing transitions protocol-dependent. The $ε\to 0$ end-point of the transition line defines a jamming transition whose location is shown to vary continuously with the preparation protocol, and cannot serve as a unique definition of random close packing. Near jamming, we observe a complex landscape and marginal stability, reminiscent of Gardner phases found in thermal glasses. The critical exponents characterizing packings at the jamming transition numerically agree with alternative approaches based on energy minimization, and with analytic predictions from mean-field replica theory. We analyze hyperuniformity in fluid and glass phases, where it emerges with qualitatively distinct signatures, and show that random organization dynamics does not determine the hyperuniformity observed in jammed packings, which is found to be non-universal. Our results show that random organization models share deep physical similarities with thermal soft-particle systems undergoing glass and jamming transitions, with little impact of the non-equilibrium nature of the microscopic dynamics on emerging physical properties.

### [205] [Light double-gluon hybrid states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14368)

TL;DR: 该研究采用QCD求和规则（QCD sum rules）方法，计算了由轻夸克-反夸克对和两个胶子组成的轻杂化介子（light hybrid mesons）的质量和流耦合常数，涵盖多种量子数态。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用QCD求和规则框架，使用由价轻夸克（valence light quarks）和胶子场构造的各种内插流（interpolating currents），并通过包含至维度十二的夸克和胶子凝聚算符（quark and gluon condensates）来纳入非微扰效应。

Result: 确定了$\bar{q}GGq$、$\bar{q}GGs$和$\bar{s}GGs$杂化构型的质量和流耦合常数，其中非微扰效应通过算符乘积展开（operator product expansion）中的高维凝聚项得到改进，提高了数值预测的可靠性。

Conclusion: 该研究结果为未来实验寻找轻杂化介子提供了有用输入，同时可作为研究其衰变性质及与其他强子态相互作用的基础。

Abstract: We investigate light hybrid mesons composed of a light quark-antiquark pair and two gluons within the framework of QCD sum rules. We focus on states with quantum numbers $J^{\mathrm{PC}} = 0^{++}, 0^{+-}, 0^{-+}, 0^{--}$ and $J^{\mathrm{PC}} = 1^{++}, 1^{+-}, 1^{-+}, 1^{--}$. By employing various interpolating currents constructed from valence light quarks and gluon fields, we determine the masses and current couplings of the $\bar{q}GGq$, $\bar{q}GGs$, and $\bar{s}GGs$ hybrid configurations. Nonperturbative effects are incorporated through quark and gluon condensates up to dimension twelve in the operator product expansion, improving the reliability of the numerical predictions. The results presented here may provide useful input for future experimental searches for light hybrid mesons and can also serve as a basis for studies of their decay properties and interactions with other hadronic states.

### [206] [An End-to-end Architecture for Collider Physics and Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14553)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ColliderAgent系统，采用解耦、领域无关的架构设计。系统包含分层多智能体推理层，并与统一执行后端Magnus耦合，后者负责现象学计算和模拟工具链的执行。系统仅依赖自然语言提示和标准物理符号，无需特定软件包代码。

Result: 系统在多个代表性文献重现任务中得到验证，涵盖轻夸克（leptoquark）和类轴子粒子（axion-like-particle）场景、高维有效算符（higher-dimensional effective operators）、部分子水平和探测器水平分析，以及大规模参数扫描导致的排除极限（exclusion limits）。

Conclusion: 该系统为对撞机物理、宇宙学及更广泛物理领域的研究提供了一条通向更自动化、可扩展和可重复研究的路径，展示了语言驱动智能体在复杂物理计算任务中的潜力。

Abstract: We present, to our knowledge, the first language-driven agent system capable of executing end-to-end collider phenomenology tasks, instantiated within a decoupled, domain-agnostic architecture for autonomous High-Energy Physics phenomenology. Guided only by natural-language prompts supplemented with standard physics notation, ColliderAgent carries out workflows from a theoretical Lagrangian to final phenomenological outputs without relying on package-specific code. In this framework, a hierarchical multi-agent reasoning layer is coupled to Magnus, a unified execution backend for phenomenological calculations and simulation toolchains. We validate the system on representative literature reproductions spanning leptoquark and axion-like-particle scenarios, higher-dimensional effective operators, parton-level and detector-level analyses, and large-scale parameter scans leading to exclusion limits. These results point to a route toward more automated, scalable, and reproducible research in collider physics, cosmology, and physics more broadly.

Method: 通过引入涉及惰性中微子的新相互作用来重新审视此问题。在这些新贡献修改微分衰变率的情况下，评估存在大质量惰性中微子时求和规则的违反程度。

Result: 研究发现诱导效应相对于当前实验不确定性仍然较小。新相互作用对求和规则的破坏程度有限，无法解释B介子与Λ_b衰变之间的观测差异。

Conclusion: 求和规则为实验数据提供了有用的自洽性检验。即使在存在大质量惰性中微子的情况下，求和规则仍保持有效，其违反程度不足以解释观测到的B介子衰变异常。

Abstract: We investigate the $b\to c$ semileptonic sum rule in the presence of a massive sterile neutrino. Since these decay rates are related through the sum rule, accommodating such a mismatch beyond the level of uncertainties is nontrivial. We revisit this issue by introducing new interactions involving a sterile neutrino. As the differential decay rates are modified by these new contributions, we evaluate the violation of the sum rule in the presence of a massive sterile neutrino. We find that the induced effect remains small compared with the current experimental uncertainties. Therefore, the sum rule provides a useful consistency check for the experimental data.

### [208] [Topological Gluon Mass and Shear Viscosity of the Quark--Gluon Plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13947)
*Debmalya Mukhopadhyay*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入拓扑$B\wedge F$相互作用赋予胶子规范不变质量，计算了胶子等离子体的剪切粘度，发现当拓扑质量尺度与等离子体软动量尺度相当时，粘度与熵密度比值自然落入重离子碰撞实验推断的范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）极小剪切粘度的微观起源是强相互作用物质理论中的重要问题。微扰QCD中无质量胶子交换存在红外发散，需要寻找自然红外调节机制。

Method: 采用非阿贝尔规范理论，通过拓扑$B\wedge F$相互作用赋予胶子规范不变质量（gauge-invariant mass）。利用相对论性动理学（relativistic kinetic theory）和玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann transport equation）计算等离子体剪切粘度，并推导相应的胶子散射输运截面。

Result: 拓扑胶子质量（topological gluon mass）为$t$道胶子交换提供了自然红外调节器，消除了微扰QCD中无质量胶子的发散。当拓扑质量尺度$m$与等离子体软动量尺度$gT$相当时，粘度与熵密度比值（shear viscosity to entropy density ratio）自然落入重离子碰撞实验推断的范围。

Conclusion: 拓扑质量生成（topological mass generation）可能为夸克-胶子等离子体的近完美流体性（near-perfect fluidity）提供简单的微观机制，解释了实验观测到的极小粘度现象。

Abstract: The quark--gluon plasma produced in relativistic heavy--ion collisions behaves as a nearly perfect fluid characterized by an exceptionally small shear viscosity to entropy density ratio. Understanding the microscopic origin of this small viscosity remains an important problem in the theory of strongly interacting matter. In this work we investigate the transport properties of a gluonic plasma in a non--Abelian gauge theory in which gluons acquire a gauge--invariant mass through a topological $B\wedge F$ interaction. Integrating out the antisymmetric tensor field generates an effective massive gluon propagator that modifies the infrared behaviour of gluon exchange processes. Using relativistic kinetic theory and the Boltzmann transport equation we compute the shear viscosity of the plasma and derive the corresponding transport cross section for gluon scattering. The presence of the topological gluon mass provides a natural infrared regulator for $t$--channel gluon exchange, removing the divergence that appears in perturbative QCD with massless gluons. We show that when the topological mass scale is comparable to the soft momentum scale of the plasma, $m\sim gT$, the resulting viscosity to entropy density ratio naturally falls in the range inferred from hydrodynamic analyses of heavy--ion collision experiments. These results suggest that topological mass generation may provide a simple microscopic mechanism contributing to the near--perfect fluidity of the quark--gluon plasma.

### [209] [Diagnosing Unmodeled Neutrino Physics via DUNE and T2HK Complementarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14215)
*João Paulo Pinheiro,Ushak Rahaman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理效应在未来的中微子精密测量中可能被误认为参数简并性。利用DUNE和T2HK实验的不同基线长度，通过标准三味框架分析数据可以诊断传播新物理：任何BSM效应都会导致两个实验提取参数之间出现人为张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前NOνA和T2K实验之间存在约2σ张力的现象，可能由超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理引起。在未来的精密测量时代，未建模的BSM物理可能被误认为参数简并性，因此需要开发有效的诊断工具来区分标准模型参数和新物理效应。

Method: 利用DUNE和T2HK实验在显著不同基线长度下运行的特点，在标准三味框架下解释它们的实验数据。通过分析非标准相互作用（NSI）解决方案，特别是εeμ和εeτ NSI对DUNE出现率（appearance rates）的系统性扭曲效应，研究其对大气混合八分位（octant）和CP相位δCP的误识别影响。

Result: 对于εeμ（εeτ）NSI，DUNE拟合结果会向CP守恒值（相反的CP半平面）偏移，同时偏好错误的八分位。相比之下，较短基线的T2HK实验对此效应基本不敏感。在各自收集6年数据后，DUNE和T2HK的标准拟合结果之间会产生约3σ的不兼容性。

Conclusion: DUNE和T2HK标准拟合结果之间的不兼容性为传播NSI提供了稳健的实验诊断工具。这证明了基线互补性在精密测量时代揭示新物理中的重要性，展示了如何利用不同基线实验的系统性差异来检测超出标准模型的物理效应。

Abstract: Unmodeled beyond Standard Model (BSM) physics in neutrino propagation can masquerade as parameter degeneracies in future precision measurements. Because the upcoming DUNE and T2HK experiments will operate at substantially different baselines, interpreting their data under the standard three-flavor framework provides a powerful diagnostic tool: any propagation BSM effect will inevitably manifest as an artificial tension between their extracted parameters. We demonstrate this principle using the complex non-standard interactions (NSI) currently favored to resolve the $\sim2σ$ tension between NO$ν$A and T2K. If these NSI solutions are realized, the NSI-induced interference term $\propto\sin(δ_{\rm CP}+φ)$ systematically distorts the DUNE appearance rates, leading to a correlated misidentification of the atmospheric mixing octant and the CP phase $δ_{\rm CP}$. Specifically, for $\varepsilon_{eμ}$ ($\varepsilon_{eτ}$) NSI, the DUNE fit shifts toward CP- conserving values (the opposite CP half-plane) along with a preference for the wrong octant. In contrast, the shorter-baseline T2HK experiment remains largely insensitive to this effect. The resulting $\sim3σ$ incompatibility between the DUNE and T2HK standard-fit results (after 6 years of data collection for each experiment) provides a robust experimental diagnostic for propagation NSI, illustrating how baseline complementarity is essential to uncover new physics in the precision era.

</details>


### [210] [Gauge Symmetry Beyond Perturbation Theory: BRST and anti-BRST Structure, Background Fields, and Infrared Dynamics of Yang--Mills Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15092)

The interplay between functional identities, Dyson--Schwinger equations, and lattice results is discussed in detail, highlighting how dynamical mass generation and infrared saturation naturally emerge within this framework.

An autonomous mutation layer actively prunes the expanding artifact DAG to resolve conflicting or redundant workflows, while persistent memory allows agents to continuously build upon complex epistemic states across multiple cycles. Across four autonomous investigations, peptide design for the somatostatin receptor SSTR2, lightweight impact-resistant ceramic screening, cross-domain resonance bridging biology, materials, and music, and formal analogy construction between urban morphology and grain-boundary evolution, the framework demonstrates heterogeneous tool chaining, emergent convergence among independently operating agents, and traceable reasoning from raw computation to published finding.

### [213] [Filtered Spectral Projection for Quantum Principal Component Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13441)
*Sk Mujaffar Hossain,Satadeep Bhattacharjee*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种投影优先的量子主成分分析（qPCA）框架——滤波谱投影算法（FSPA），该算法绕过显式特征值估计，直接投影到主导谱子空间，在保持谱结构的同时提高了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多量子主成分分析（quantum principal component analysis, qPCA）应用中，实际目标并非提取完整的特征值和特征向量，而是将数据投影到主导谱子空间。现有方法通常进行显式特征值估计，这可能并非必要。

Method: 本文提出滤波谱投影算法（Filtered Spectral Projection Algorithm, FSPA），该算法采用投影优先框架，绕过显式特征值估计，直接放大与主导主成分子空间的非零初始重叠。对于幅度编码的居中数据，证明其系综密度矩阵与协方差矩阵一致。

Result: FSPA算法在小间隙和近简并情况下保持鲁棒性，且不会在无偏置时引入人为对称破缺。对于未居中数据，推导了特征值交错界限来量化与标准PCA的偏差。在乳腺癌威斯康星和手写数字等基准数据集上的数值实验表明，只要投影质量得以保持，下游性能保持稳定。

Conclusion: 在广泛的qPCA设置中，谱投影是基本原语，显式特征值估计通常是不必要的。FSPA框架通过优先处理投影操作，为量子主成分分析提供了更高效且鲁棒的替代方案。

Abstract: Quantum principal component analysis (qPCA) is commonly formulated as the extraction of eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a covariance-encoded density operator. Yet in many qPCA settings, the practical objective is simpler: projecting data onto the dominant spectral subspace. In this work, we introduce a projection-first framework, the Filtered Spectral Projection Algorithm (FSPA), which bypasses explicit eigenvalue estimation while preserving the essential spectral structure. FSPA amplifies any nonzero warm-start overlap with the leading principal subspace and remains robust in small-gap and near-degenerate regimes without inducing artificial symmetry breaking in the absence of bias. To connect this approach to classical datasets, we show that for amplitude-encoded centered data, the ensemble density matrix $ρ=\sum_i p_i|ψ_i\rangle\langleψ_i|$ coincides with the covariance matrix. For uncentered data, $ρ$ corresponds to PCA without centering, and we derive eigenvalue interlacing bounds quantifying the deviation from standard PCA. We further show that ensembles of quantum states admit an equivalent centered covariance interpretation. Numerical demonstrations on benchmark datasets, including Breast Cancer Wisconsin and handwritten Digits, show that downstream performance remains stable whenever projection quality is preserved. These results suggest that, in a broad class of qPCA settings, spectral projection is the essential primitive, and explicit eigenvalue estimation is often unnecessary.

### [214] [Iterated Graph Systems (I): random walks and diffusion limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13798)

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了重整化简单随机游走在Gromov-Hausdorff-Prokhorov-Skorokhod拓扑下收敛于极限扩散过程；当电阻维度（resistance dimension）为正时，该极限扩散与布朗运动（Brownian motion）一致；利用度维度统一了局部有限和局部无限区域的对角热核估计；解决了DHL渗流簇的淬火电阻指数问题。

Conclusion: 本文系统研究了EIGS分形图上的随机游走与扩散极限，建立了多个维度间的理论联系，证明了随机游走的收敛性及其与布朗运动的关系，统一了不同区域的热核估计，并解决了文献中遗留的淬火电阻指数问题，为分形图上的随机过程研究提供了理论框架。

Abstract: This paper investigates random walks and diffusion limits on a broad class of fractal graphs generated by Edge Iterated Graph Systems (EIGS). We study random walks on combinatorial limit graphs and establish the connections among several dimensions, including the Einstein relation. Building on this, we prove that the rescaled simple random walks converge in the Gromov-Hausdorff-Prokhorov-Skorokhod topology to the limiting diffusion, which further coincides with Brownian motion when the resistance dimension is positive. Moreover, we use the degree dimension to unify the on-diagonal heat-kernel estimates in the locally finite and locally infinite (scale-free) regimes. Finally, we solve the open problem on the quenched resistance exponent for the DHL percolation cluster left in [27].

Our argument uses a recent description of the spectrum of the tight-binding model on the Bethe lattice (Aggarwal--Lopatto, 2025). By viewing the Bethe lattice as the local limit of a random regular graph, and proving several preliminary estimates, we transfer this characterization of the spectrum of the limiting model to its finite approximants.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the correlations of the celebrated Sine$_β$ point process. This point process arises as the bulk scaling limit of $β$-ensembles and has a geometric description through the Brownian carousel, as shown by Valkó and Virág (2009). We establish that the averaged $k$-point truncated correlation functions decay polynomially in the limit of large separation. We show that the decay exponent is of order $1/β$ for large $β$. This is a step towards a conjecture by Forrester and Haldane regarding the exact asymptotics of the two-point correlation function, a problem recently addressed by Qu and Valkó (2025). Our proofs, which rely on a careful analysis of the coupling of diffusions associated with the Brownian carousel, hold for all $β>0$ and $k \geq 1$, significantly extending previous results limited to specific values of $β$ or $k$.

### [217] [Sign-Indefinite Helicity and the Structure of Weak Turbulence in Inertial and Non-Hermitian Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14181)
*Shahaf Aharony Shapira,Michal Shavit*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究具有破缺时间反演对称性的不可压缩流动中，符号不定的二次不变量如何影响湍流级串。通过分析旋转欧拉流和奇粘性欧拉流，发现螺旋度守恒显著简化了弱湍流动能方程，并揭示了螺旋度在共振三波相互作用中重组级串方向的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解符号不定的二次不变量（如螺旋度）如何影响具有破缺时间反演对称性和强各向异性色散波的不可压缩流动中的湍流级串。特别关注旋转欧拉流和奇粘性欧拉流这两种典型系统。

Method: 研究方法包括：分离波分量并研究相应的弱湍流动能方程（weak-turbulence kinetic equation）；通过自然规范选择固定能量通量；在慢模能量积累的温和近似下计算主导角度依赖性；分析共振三波相互作用中螺旋度的作用；在强各向异性极限下数值评估碰撞积分。

Result: 主要结果包括：螺旋度守恒显著简化了动能方程；确定了维持从大尺度到小尺度恒定能量通量的唯一标度不变湍流谱；发现了沿慢模曲线的可积奇异性；证明了螺旋度在共振三波水平上重组级串方向，即使净级串为正向时也能产生系统性反向散射；在螺旋度确定极限下，动能方程存在与螺旋度输运相关的额外标度不变解；数值验证了强各向异性极限下的解析预测。

Conclusion: 结论表明，符号不定的螺旋度不变量通过将自身分解为各极化分支上的符号确定贡献，在湍流级串中发挥关键作用。这种分解导致共振三波相互作用表现出类似受符号确定不变量约束的行为，驱动能量向上尺度转移，即使在净级串为正向时也能产生系统性反向散射。

Abstract: We investigate how sign-indefinite quadratic invariants shape turbulent cascades in incompressible flows with broken time-reversal symmetry, where the dynamics supports strongly anisotropic dispersive waves. Focusing on rotating Euler flow and odd-viscous Euler flow, we isolate the wave component study the corresponding weak-turbulence kinetic equation. We show that helicity conservation substantially simplifies the kinetic equation. Fixing the energy flux by a natural gauge choice, we identify the turbulent spectrum as the unique scale-invariant solution that sustains a constant flux of energy from large to small scales. Under a mild approximation motivated by the accumulation of energy near slow modes, we compute the leading angular dependence and uncover an integrable singularity along the slow-mode curve, that agrees with previous results. We then demonstrate that helicity reorganizes cascade directions at the level of resonant triads. Although helicity is globally sign-indefinite, the helical decomposition splits it into sign-definite contributions on each polarization branch. Triads whose three legs lie on the same branch behave as if constrained by a sign-definite invariant and drive an upscale transfer of energy, producing systematic backscatter even when the net cascade is direct. In the helicity-definite limit (single-branch dynamics), the kinetic equation admits an additional scale-invariant solution associated with helicity transport. Finally, we validate the analytical predictions by numerically evaluating the collision integral in the strongly anisotropic limit, revealing a family of stationary solutions in that regime.

### [218] [Non-Reciprocal Capillary Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14195)
*Holly du Plessis,Pedro Cosme,Hugo França,Maziyar Jalaal*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了手性流体（chiral fluids）中毛细波（capillary waves）的非互易传播特性，发现奇粘度（odd viscosity）与表面张力（surface tension）结合会产生两种不等价的奇毛细波分支，并导致反常的斯托克斯漂移（anti-Stokes drift）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 毛细波是流体力学中的经典自由表面现象，但其在手性流体中的行为尚未被充分探索。研究旨在探究奇粘度如何影响毛细波的传播特性，以及如何利用奇偶性破缺（broken parity）与毛细作用的结合来控制流体界面处的波传播和输运。

Method: 采用线性理论（linear theory）结合完全非线性直接数值模拟（fully nonlinear direct numerical simulations）的方法进行研究。通过理论分析和数值计算来揭示奇粘度对毛细波传播特性的影响。

Result: 研究发现奇粘度破坏了毛细波的互易性（reciprocity），表面张力产生了两种不等价的奇毛细波分支：一个色散分支（dispersive branch）和一个在无毛细作用极限下不存在的准声学分支（quasi-acoustic branch）。这些波的不等传播和衰减将驻波（standing waves）转变为行波（traveling waves），并产生异常深的涡旋边界层（vortical boundary layer）。当奇粘度超过阈值时，表面附近涡度（vorticity）的非线性积累会逆转诱导的剪切流，驱动体粒子与波运动方向相反，产生传统流体中没有的反常斯托克斯漂移。

Conclusion: 研究表明，将毛细作用与奇偶性破缺结合可用于控制流体界面处的波传播和输运，为实现单向流体波导（one-way fluidic waveguiding）和手性编程界面流（chirality-programmed interfacial flows）开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Capillary waves are a classical free-surface phenomenon in fluid mechanics, yet their behavior in chiral fluids remains largely unexplored. We show that odd viscosity breaks the reciprocity of capillary waves. Using linear theory together with fully nonlinear direct numerical simulations, we find that surface tension creates two inequivalent branches of odd capillary waves: a dispersive branch and a quasi-acoustic branch absent in the capillarity-free limit. Their unequal propagation and attenuation transform standing waves into traveling waves and produce an anomalously deep vortical boundary layer. Above a threshold odd viscosity, nonlinear accumulation of vorticity near the surface reverses the induced shear current and drives bulk particles opposite to the wave motion, giving rise to an anti-Stokes drift with no counterpart in conventional fluids. Our results show how combining capillarity with broken parity can be used to control wave propagation and transport at fluid interfaces, opening a route toward one-way fluidic waveguiding and chirality-programmed interfacial flows.

</details>

### [219] [Beyond Murray's Law: Non-Universal Branching Exponents from Vessel-Wall Metabolic Costs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13687)
*Riccardo Marchesi*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: Murray立方分支定律（α=3）预测所有分层运输网络具有普适的直径标度指数，但动脉树观测值α~2.7-2.9存在差异。研究发现这种差异源于结构原因：Murray普适性是成本均匀性的假象而非生物学属性。引入经验性血管壁厚度定律h(r)=c₀rᵖ（p≈0.77）后，成本函数变为非均匀，导致分支指数非普适且满足严格边界(5+p)/2 < α*(Q) < 3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Murray立方分支定律预测所有分层运输网络具有普适的直径标度指数α=3，但动脉树的实验观测值α~2.7-2.9与此存在显著差异。研究旨在揭示这种差异的结构性起源，探究Murray定律的普适性是否真实存在。

Method: 通过引入经验性血管壁厚度定律h(r)=c₀rᵖ（p≈0.77），在成本函数中增加第三项代谢成本项∝r¹⁺ᵖ，使成本函数变为非均匀。应用柯西函数方程证明均匀性是普适分支指数存在的充要条件。通过理论分析证明所得标度相关指数满足严格边界(5+p)/2 < α*(Q) < 3。

Result: 静态壁组织机制将对称分叉指数限定在αₜ∈[2.90, 2.94]范围内，这标志着与Murray定律的一阶对称破缺，将经验差距缩小了三分之一。剩余与心血管平均值（αₑₓₚ≈2.70）的差异不是模型失败，而是数学必然性，表明脉动波动力学的独立贡献。壁成本打破了Murray的拓扑简并性，将最优分支数限定为小的有限整数。

Conclusion: Murray定律被识别为成本函数族的奇异简并特例而非普适原理。血管壁厚度定律的引入揭示了分支指数的非普适性，解释了动脉树观测值与Murray预测的差异。二进制分叉在空间约束下作为生理选择的最小值出现，为理解血管网络结构提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Murray's cubic branching law ($α=3$) predicts a universal diameter scaling exponent for all hierarchical transport networks, yet arterial trees yield $α\sim 2.7-2.9$. We show that this discrepancy has a structural origin: Murray's universality is an artifact of cost homogeneity, not a biological property. Incorporating the empirical vessel-wall thickness law $h(r)=c_0 r^p$ ($p \approx 0.77$) introduces a third metabolic cost term $\propto r^{1+p}$ that renders the cost function inhomogeneous with incommensurate scaling exponents. By Cauchy's functional equation, homogeneity is necessary and sufficient for a universal branching exponent to exist; its absence implies non-universality, and Murray's law is identified as a singular degeneracy of the cost-function family rather than a general principle. We prove that the resulting scale-dependent exponent satisfies the strict bounds $(5+p)/2 < α^*(Q) < 3$ independently of flow asymmetry (Theorem 4, Corollary 5). The static wall-tissue mechanism bounds the symmetric bifurcation exponent to $α_t \in [2.90, 2.94]$ from measured parameters, marking a first-order symmetry breaking from Murray's law that narrows the empirical gap by one-third. The remaining discrepancy with the cardiovascular mean ($α_{exp} \approx 2.70$) is not a model failure but a mathematical necessity that signals the independent contribution of pulsatile wave dynamics. Additionally, the wall cost breaks Murray's topological degeneracy, bounding the optimal branching number to small finite integers; binary bifurcation emerges as the physiologically selected minimum under steric constraints.

</details>


### [220] [A Unified Variational Principle for Branching Transport Networks: Wave Impedance, Viscous Flow, and Tissue Metabolism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14691)
*Riccardo Marchesi*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过整合血管壁亚线性缩放和代谢成本，推导出哺乳动物动脉树直径缩放指数α的理论最优值约为2.72，与实验观测值高度一致，并证明二分叉是网络刚度最大化的结构结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论无法解释哺乳动物动脉树中观察到的直径缩放指数α_exp = 2.70 ± 0.20。阻抗匹配理论（α~2）适用于脉动流，而粘性-代谢最小化理论（α=3）适用于稳态流，两者均与实验数据不符。

Method: 将血管壁亚线性缩放h(r) ∝ r^p（p=0.77）纳入三组分代谢成本模型，通过柯西函数方程严格打破Murray立方定律。构建统一的网络级拉格朗日量，平衡波反射惩罚与运输-代谢成本，并将优化问题建模为网络架构与环境间的零和博弈。

Result: 理论推导出静态最优α_t ∈ [2.90, 2.94]，而通过冯·诺依曼极小极大定理获得唯一鞍点(α*, η*)，满足精确等成本条件。对于猪冠状动脉树（G=11代），α* = 2.72，与形态测量数据差异小于0.1σ。进一步证明N=2时网络刚度比κ_eff(N)最大，推导出二分叉作为框架的结构性结果。

Conclusion: 该框架成功预测了哺乳动物动脉树的直径缩放指数，且预测仅关键依赖于组织学指数p，是从基本缩放原理推导出的零参数解。敏感性分析表明在生理代谢范围内|Δα*| < 0.01，验证了模型的稳健性。

Abstract: The branching geometry of biological transport networks is characterized by a diameter scaling exponent $α$. Two structural attractors compete: impedance matching ($α\sim 2$) for pulsatile flow and viscous-metabolic minimization ($α= 3$) for steady flow. Neither predicts the empirically observed $α_{\mathrm{exp}} = 2.70 \pm 0.20$ in mammalian arterial trees. Incorporating sub-linear vessel-wall scaling $h(r) \propto r^p$ ($p = 0.77$) into a three-term metabolic cost rigorously breaks Murray's cubic law -- via Cauchy's functional equation -- bounding the static optimum to $α_t \in [2.90, 2.94]$. We formulate a unified network-level Lagrangian balancing wave-reflection penalties against transport-metabolic costs. Because the operational duty cycle $η$ is uncertain over developmental timescales, we cast the optimization as a zero-sum game between network architecture and environment. Von Neumann's minimax theorem -- proved constructively via strict monotonicity of the cost curves -- yields a unique saddle point $(α^*, η^*)$ satisfying an exact equal-cost condition. We further prove $N = 2$ uniquely maximizes the network stiffness ratio $κ_{\mathrm{eff}}(N)$, deriving binary branching as a structural consequence of the framework. For the porcine coronary tree ($G = 11$ generations), $α^* = 2.72$, within $0.1σ$ of morphometric data. Sensitivity analysis confirms $|Δα^*| < 0.01$ across physiological metabolic ranges; the prediction depends critically only on the histological exponent $p$ -- a zero-parameter derivation from fundamental scaling principles.

</details>


### [221] [Digital unzipping of DNA through a solid-state nanopore: A theoretical study for base-by-base ratcheting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14705)
*Tomoki Ohkubo*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于双链DNA在纳米孔边缘解链的蛋白质独立棘轮机制，结合可逆保持机制实现确定性单碱基步进，为全固态纳米孔测序提供了理论可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态纳米孔DNA测序仪具有机械化学稳定性、可重用性和大规模集成性等优势，但其发展受限于缺乏蛋白质独立的DNA易位控制机制。生物系统中通常使用马达蛋白（motor proteins）实现这一功能，因此需要开发替代方案。

Method: 提出基于双链DNA在纳米孔边缘解链（unzipping）的蛋白质独立棘轮机制（ratchet mechanism），当跨膜偏压超过阈值时碱基对机械解离。引入可逆保持机制（reversible hold mechanism），通过DNA与带电纳米孔壁之间的静电吸引力暂时固定链段。使用统计力学模型（statistical-mechanical model）追踪每个棘轮周期中DNA位置的平均值和方差变化。

Result: 分析表达式显示，保持机制的亚微秒级切换能够实现碱基逐个步进（base-by-base stepping），错误率低于5%。数字解链（digital unzipping）与可逆保持机制结合理论上能够产生确定性单碱基运动。

Conclusion: 数字解链结合可逆保持机制理论上能够实现确定性单碱基运动，为全固态纳米孔测序开辟了可行的技术路径，克服了传统蛋白质依赖方法的局限性。

Abstract: Solid-state nanopore DNA sequencers present mechanical and chemical stability, reusability, and large-scale integrability. However, their development is hindered by the absence of a protein-free mechanism for controlling DNA translocation, which is accomplished by motor proteins in their biological counterparts. Here, we propose and theoretically analyze a protein-independent ratchet mechanism based on the unzipping of double-stranded DNA at the nanopore rim. When the transmembrane bias exceeds a certain threshold, the base pairs mechanically dissociate, allowing one strand to translocate while the other remains upstream. This unzipping process is known to slow DNA motion, suggesting that voltage pulses can trigger individual unzipping events at externally defined times, a concept referred to as digital unzipping. However, the intrinsic unzipping barrier is insufficient to provide the dwell times required for a reliable ionic-current readout; therefore, an additional mechanism is needed to hold the DNA in place between voltage pulses. To overcome this limitation, we introduce a reversible hold mechanism implemented via electrostatic attraction between DNA and a charged nanopore wall, which temporarily immobilizes the strand once the unzipping fork catches on the nanopore rim. Using a statistical-mechanical model, we track the evolution of the mean and variance of DNA position through each ratchet cycle. Analytical expressions for the corresponding error probabilities show that submicrosecond switching of the hold mechanism enables base-by-base stepping with an error rate <5%. These results theoretically demonstrate that digital unzipping combined with a reversible hold mechanism can yield deterministic single-base motion, thus opening a viable route toward all-solid-state nanopore sequencing.

</details>

### [222] [The ATLAS Trigger System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13409)
*Leonardo Toffolin*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: ATLAS触发系统（ATLAS Trigger system）是大型强子对撞机（LHC）ATLAS实验的关键组件，通过硬件和软件升级应对Run-3期间增加的亮度（luminosity）和堆积（pile-up）条件，支持精确测量和新物理搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ATLAS触发系统需要将质子-质子束团交叉频率（proton-proton bunch crossing frequency）从40 MHz降低到适合离线存储和分析的输出速率。在Run-3期间（2022-2026），由于亮度增加和堆积条件变化，系统需要重大升级以维持性能。

Method: 系统采用两级架构：基于硬件的Level-1（L1）触发器和基于软件的高级别触发器（High Level Trigger, HLT）。在Run-3期间对这两级系统都实施了重大升级，以应对增加的实验条件挑战。

Result: 论文总结了ATLAS触发系统的主要特性及其在Run-3期间的性能表现。系统成功实现了事件率从40 MHz到可管理水平的降低，为后续物理分析提供了合适的数据流。

Conclusion: 升级后的ATLAS触发系统在Run-3期间有效运行，为精确测量和新物理搜索（new physics searches）提供了关键支持，确保了实验数据的质量和可用性。

Abstract: The ATLAS Trigger system is a key component of the ATLAS experiment at the CERN Large Hadron Collider (LHC), designed to reduce the event rate from the 40 MHz proton-proton bunch crossing frequency to an output suitable for offline storage and analysis. During Run-3 (2022-2026), major upgrades were implemented in both the hardware-based Level-1 (L1) Trigger and the software-based High Level Trigger (HLT), to cope with increased luminosity and pile-up conditions. This paper summarises the main features of the ATLAS Trigger system, its performance in Run-3, and its role in enabling precision measurements and new physics searches.

</details>

*A. Breskin*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: PICOSEC是一种超快粒子探测器概念，结合了光电阴极涂层的切伦科夫辐射体与气体雪崩倍增器。本文提出了采用厚反射光电阴极的不同探测器配置和工作模式，以增强鲁棒性和性能，部分反射式PICOSEC探测器可在毫巴级气体压力下工作。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了采用厚反射光电阴极（thick reflective photocathodes）沉积在各种类型雪崩倍增器读出电极上的不同探测器配置。这些反射式PICOSEC（Reflective-PICOSEC）探测器部分可在毫巴（mbar）级气体压力下工作。

Result: 开发了结合厚反射光电阴极与不同类型雪崩倍增器的反射式PICOSEC探测器配置，实现了在低至毫巴级气体压力下的工作能力。

Abstract: PICOSEC is an ultrafast particle-detector concept, combining a photocathode-coated Cherenkov radiator coupled to a gas-avalanche multiplier. Particle-induced Cherenkov photons create photoelectrons emitted from an ultrathin semitransparent photocathode; they are multiplied and detected in fast gas-avalanche mode. In parallel to the constant progress made in the PICOSEC technique, we propose different detector configurations and operation modes with the aim of enhancing robustness and performance. They incorporate thick reflective photocathodes deposited on the readout electrodes of various types of avalanche multipliers. Some of these Reflective-PICOSEC detectors operate at mbar gas pressures.

Sgalaberna,A. Shaikovskiy,N. Shvarev,A. Shvartsman,Y. Shiraishi,N. Skrobova,A. Speers,M. Smy,D. Svirida,S. Tairafune,M. Tani,H. Tanigawa,A. Teklu,S. Tereshchenko,V. V. Tereshchenko,T. Tsushima,M. Tzanov,R. Van Berg,I. I. Vasilyev,T. Vladisavljevic,D. Wakabayashi,H. Wallace,A. Weber,N. Whitney,C. Wret,Y. Xu,Y. Yang,N. Yershov,A. J. P. Yrey,M. Yokoyama,Y. Yoshimoto,X. Y. Zhao,H. Zheng,H. Zhong,T. Zhu,E. D. Zimmerman,M. Zito*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: T2K实验的ND280近探测器升级了新型超精细粒度探测器（SuperFGD），该探测器由约200万个1立方厘米塑料闪烁体立方体组成，通过三正交波长位移光纤读出，显著提升了中微子-核相互作用的三维成像能力和粒子识别性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 升级T2K实验的磁化近探测器ND280旨在提高探测性能，从而更好地理解中微子-核相互作用，减少中微子振荡参数测量中的系统不确定性。

Method: 升级的核心是新型分段塑料闪烁体探测器SuperFGD，由约200万个光学隔离的1立方厘米立方体组成，通过三正交波长位移光纤（WLS fibres）读出，使用55,888个Hamamatsu多像素光子计数器（MPPCs）探测闪烁光子。

Result: SuperFGD能够通过追踪各向同性产生的未态带电粒子（包括动量阈值约330 MeV/c的质子）提供中微子相互作用的三维图像。其高光产额显著改善粒子识别，亚纳秒时间分辨率提供优异的Michel电子识别能力，并首次在中微子实验中通过精细探测器分段和亚纳秒精度飞行时间测量重建中子动能。

Conclusion: 探测器已成功安装于ND280，并于2023年使用宇宙线数据完成调试，随后使用T2K中微子束流运行。基于2023和2024年数据，探测器响应特性已得到表征，相关结果在本文中报告。

Abstract: The magnetised near detector ND280 of the long-baseline neutrino experiment T2K has been upgraded to improve its detection performance and, consequently, enhance our understanding of neutrino-nucleus interactions, reducing the systematic uncertainties in measurements of the neutrino oscillation parameters. A key component of the upgrade is a novel segmented plastic scintillator detector, called the Super Fine-Grained Detector (SuperFGD), made of approximately 2 million optically isolated 1 cm$^3$ cubes read out by three orthogonal wavelength-shifting (WLS) fibres. Scintillation photons are detected by 55,888 Hamamatsu Multi-Pixel Photon Counters (MPPCs). The SuperFGD provides 3D images of neutrino interactions by tracking the final-state charged particles produced isotropically, including protons down to a threshold of around 330 MeV/$c$. The high light yield of SuperFGD greatly improves particle identification and the sub-nanosecond time resolution provides an excellent identification of Michel electrons. The SuperFGD is also able to detect neutrons from neutrino interactions and, for the first time in a neutrino experiment, to reconstruct their kinetic energy using a fine detector segmentation and by measuring the time-of-flight with sub-nanosecond precision. In this article the details of the detector design, construction and performance are described. The detector was installed in ND280 and successfully commissioned with cosmic data in 2023 and, later, with the T2K neutrino beam. The detector response has been characterised with the 2023 and 2024 data and the results are reported in this article.

</details>

When the noble liquid is excited by particles, it scintillates vacuum ultraviolet light, which sensors then detect. A major focus of the detector development community is on producing precision light sensors for noble liquid detectors. ### [226] [Characterization of Passive CMOS Strip Detectors After Proton Irradiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15524)
*Marta Baselga,Jan-Hendrik Arling,Naomi Davis,Jochen Dingfelder,Ingrid Maria Gregor,Marc Hauser,Fabian Hügging,Karl Jakobs,Michael Karagounis,Roland Koppenhöfer,Kevin Alexander Kroeninger,Fabian Lex,Ulrich Parzefall,Simon Spannagel,Dennis Sperlich,Jens Weingarten,Iveta Zatocilova*

TL;DR: 本研究验证了在商用CMOS代工厂使用多次光刻拼接技术制造被动CMOS条带探测器的可行性，该技术能用于高能粒子探测且拼接处无不良影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用LFoundry商用代工厂的150纳米节点技术生产线，使用150微米厚浮区晶圆（FZ wafer）制造被动CMOS条带探测器。设计了三种不同几何结构以研究CMOS技术的影响，条带长度分别为2.1厘米和4.1厘米，分别对应3次和5次光刻版拼接。探测器在CERN接受24 GeV质子辐照，并通过不同测试装置进行评估。

Result: 实验结果显示，经过24 GeV质子辐照的被动CMOS条带探测器在不同测试装置中均未表现出条带拼接（strips stitching）的任何不良影响。这证明了该制造技术在高能粒子探测中的可行性。

Conclusion: 验证CMOS拼接技术可行性为未来大规模生产被动条带探测器开辟了道路，同时也为在商用CMOS代工厂制造有源条带传感器（active strip sensors）提供了可能性。

Abstract: Strip detectors are populating outer trackers of high-energy particle experiments. They are convenient for covering large areas of sensitive material since they use less power and have fewer readout channels compared to pixels sensors. Nevertheless, they are typically manufactured with a mask set that covers the full wafer, otherwise when using smaller reticles the strip implants have to be stitched. For this project, strip detectors were fabricated in a CMOS commercial foundry using different reticles to be stitched several times, proving the feasibility of this technology.

Those strip sensors have three different geometries to study different impacts of the CMOS technology. The strips have lengths of 2.1 cm and 4.1 cm, stitching 3 or 5 reticles respectively. This work shows results of 24 GeV proton irradiated passive CMOS strip detectors. The detectors were irradiated at CERN and were tested with different set-ups, not showing any effect from the strips stitching.
  Proving that this technology is feasible for detecting high-energy particles opens the door to future large productions of passive strip detectors and also to produce active strip sensors in commercial CMOS foundries.

Method: 采用75 kJ电解质电容器组驱动脉冲磁体，充电电压为400 V。磁体线圈采用Zylon增强线绕制，磁场上升时间为10 ms。集成恒温器使用4 K氦闭式循环制冷机（closed-cycle cryocooler），通过光纤耦合实现光学测量。

Conclusion: 该集成系统为磁致发光测量提供了一种有效的实验平台，通过创新的电容器组设计和低温恒温器集成，实现了高磁场与低温环境的协同工作。

Abstract: This paper presents the development of a high field pulsed magnet system combined with an optical fiber-coupled low temperature cryostat for magneto-photoluminescence measurements. A novel aspect of our system is the use of electrolyte capacitors in a 75 kJ capacitor bank to drive the pulsed magnet, enabling the generation of high magnetic fields at a relatively low charging voltage (400 V). The zylon reinforced wire wound magnet coil achieves a maximum field strength of 35 tesla with a magnetic field rise time of 10 ms. The integrated cryostat was developed to meet the specific requirements of magneto-photoluminescence experiments using a 4 K helium closed-cycle cryocooler to provide a stable low-temperature environment down to 5 K.

### [228] [Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid theory for one-dimensional attractive Fermi gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13958)
*Hai-Ying Cui,Yu-Hao Yeh,Randall G. Hulet,Han Pu,Thierry Giamarchi,Xi-Wen Guan*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文为一维吸引费米气体中的Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov（FFLO）配对态建立了统一的Tomonaga-Luttinger液体（TLL）理论，揭示了弱吸引和强吸引两种耦合区域的不同低能行为，并提出了基于超冷原子的实验验证方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一维Yang-Gaudin模型作为量子多体物理的范式，其Luther-Emery液体描述及FFLO配对态的玻色化问题尚未得到一致解决。本文旨在为跨越弱耦合和强耦合区域的FFLO态建立统一的理论框架。

Method: 通过玻色化（bosonization）方法严格推导低能有效哈密顿量，建立普适的Tomonaga-Luttinger液体理论。在弱吸引区域推导了自旋部分sine-Gordon项的重整化群方程，在强吸引区域基于有效哈密顿量分析了FFLO配对态的动力学关联函数。

Result: 理论揭示了两种不同的Luttinger液体组分：弱吸引区域表现出自旋-电荷耦合（spin-charge coupling），强吸引区域则呈现电荷-电荷分离（charge-charge separation）。弱吸引区域中sine-Gordon项存在由磁场驱动的相关-不相关相变。

Conclusion: 本文为一维吸引费米气体中的FFLO态提供了跨越不同耦合强度的统一Tomonaga-Luttinger液体描述，揭示了自旋-电荷耦合和电荷-电荷分离的微妙现象，并提出了基于超冷原子（ultracold atoms）的实验验证方案。

Abstract: The one-dimensional (1D) Yang-Gaudin model-an integrable $δ$-function interacting Fermi gas, serves as a paradigm in quantum many-body physics, encompassing phenomena from spin-charge separation to the Luther-Emery liquid. However, a consistent description of the Luther-Emery liquid and the bosonization of Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov (FFLO)-like pairing states in the 1D attractive Fermi gas remains elusive. In this work, we develop a universal Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid (TLL) theory to describe the FFLO state across both weak and strong coupling regimes. We rigorously derive the low-energy effective Hamiltonian using bosonization, revealing the emergence of a two-component Luttinger liquid: one exhibiting spin-charge coupling in the weakly attractive regime, and another featuring charge-charge separation in the strongly attractive regime. For the weakly attractive regime, we further derive the renormalization-group equations for the sine-Gordon term in the spin sector and show that this term undergoes a relevant-irrelevant phase transition driven by the magnetic field. For the strongly attractive regime, we analyze the dynamical correlation functions of the FFLO pairing state based on the derived effective Hamiltonian. Finally, we propose an experimental scheme using ultracold atoms to verify the Luther-Emery liquid behavior and the subtle phenomena of spin-charge coupling and charge-charge separation.

</details>


### [229] [Quantum simulation of the Haldane phase using open shell molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14874)
*Suman Aich,Ceren B. Dag,H. A. Fertig,Debayan Mitra,Babak Seradjeh*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究提出利用光学阱中二能级分子（dipolar molecules）构建自旋-1量子磁模型，通过微波驱动和磁场调控实现Haldane相，并探讨了MgF等大转动常数分子的实验可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学阱中的偶极分子为研究强长程相互作用下的量子多体相提供了多功能平台。本研究旨在探索特定微波驱动和磁场条件下，如何从$^2Σ$基态分子构建自旋-1量子磁模型，并研究其相图特征。

Method: 通过圆偏振微波驱动将$N=0,J=1/2,F=1$态耦合到$N=1,J=3/2,F=2$能级，并在小磁场存在下，利用$^2Σ$基态分子特有的电子自旋-轨道退耦合特性，构建自旋-1量子磁哈密顿量。采用张量网络方法（tensor network methods）计算一维情况下的相图。

Result: 计算结果显示相图中存在著名的Haldane相。即使在SU(3)修正项破坏哈密顿量SU(2)代数对称性的情况下，Haldane相仍然保持稳定。这表明该方案对对称性破坏具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该方案为利用$^2Σ$分子（如具有大转动常数的直接激光冷却分子MgF）实现自旋-1量子磁模型提供了可行路径。研究结果支持未来实验探索Haldane相及其他拓扑量子相的可能性。

Abstract: Dipolar molecules in optical traps are a versatile platform for studying many-body phases of quantum matter in the presence of strong and long-range interactions. The dipolar interactions in such setups can be enabled by microwave driving opposite parity rotational levels of the molecules. We find that the regime where the $N=0,J=1/2,F=1$ state is coupled to the $N=1,J=3/2,F=2$ manifold with circularly polarized microwaves, in the presence of a small magnetic field, can lead to spin-1 quantum magnetic Hamiltonians, due to the decoupling between electron spin and orbit, that is unique to the $^2Σ$ ground state molecules. We demonstrate that in one dimension, the phase diagram associated with this Hamiltonian, computed via tensor network methods, hosts the celebrated Haldane phase. We find that the Haldane phase persists even in the presence of SU(3) correction terms that break the SU(2) algebra of the Hamiltonian. We discuss the feasibility of the proposed scheme for $^2Σ$ molecules with large rotational constants such as the directly laser cooled molecule MgF for future experiments.

### [230] [Hierarchical structure of primary and hybridization-induced superconducting correlations in bilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13604)
*Hiroshi Watanabe,Hirofumi Sakakibara,Kazuhiko Kuroki*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过变分蒙特卡洛方法揭示了双层镍酸盐La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$中的层级配对结构，阐明了轨道杂化在多层关联超导体中的独特作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压下双层镍酸盐La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$的超导转变温度接近80K，引发了关于其微观起源的激烈争论。虽然$s_{\pm}$能隙对称性被广泛提出，但负责配对的电子自由度仍未确定。

Method: 研究采用变分蒙特卡洛方法（variational Monte Carlo method）研究双层两轨道哈伯德模型（bilayer two-orbital Hubbard model），分析镍酸盐中的配对结构。

Result: 研究发现层级配对结构：主要配对相互作用源于Ni $3d_{z^2}$轨道的成键-反键分裂（bonding--antibonding splitting），而轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）将超导关联重新分布到$d_{x^2-y^2}$通道。这种配对起源与超导关联的区分解释了为何两个轨道通道表现出可比的长程关联，且$s_{\pm}$态对费米面拓扑变化具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 研究结果调和了表面上竞争的理论方案，提供了全面理解，突显了轨道杂化在多层关联超导体中的独特作用，解释了双层镍酸盐中配对相互作用与超导关联分布的复杂关系。

Abstract: High-pressure superconductivity in the bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, with a transition temperature approaching 80 K, has stimulated intense debate regarding its microscopic origin. Although an $s_{\pm}$ gap symmetry has been widely proposed, the electronic degrees of freedom responsible for pairing remain unsettled. Here we investigate a bilayer two-orbital Hubbard model using the variational Monte Carlo method and reveal a hierarchical pairing structure in bilayer nickelates. The primary pairing interaction originates from the bonding--antibonding splitting of the Ni $3d_{z^2}$ orbitals, while orbital hybridization redistributes superconducting correlations to the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ channel despite its weak intrinsic pairing interaction. This distinction between the origin of pairing and resulting superconducting correlations explains why the two orbital channels exhibit comparable long-range correlations. The resulting $s_{\pm}$ state is robust against changes in Fermi-surface topology. These results reconcile apparently competing theoretical scenarios and provide a comprehensive understanding, highlighting the distinctive role of orbital hybridization in multilayer correlated superconductors.

</details>


### [231] [Superhydrides on the way to ambient pressure: weak localization and persistent X-ray photoconductivity in BaSiH$_{8}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14051)
*Dmitrii V. Semenok,Di Zhou,Sven Luther,Toni Helm,Hirokazu Kadobayashi,Yuki Nakamoto,Katsuya Shimizu,Kirill S. Pervakov,Andrei V. Sadakov,Oleg A. Sobolevskiy,Vladimir M. Pudalov,Simone Di Cataldo,Roman Lucrezi,Lilia Boeri,Michele Galasso,Frederico G. Alabarse,Ivan A. Troyan,Viktor V. Struzhkin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究在高压下合成了BaSiH₈超氢化物，并发现其可在减压至常压条件下保持稳定，突破了超氢化物稳定性的关键瓶颈，为氢储存应用奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降低超氢化物（superhydrides）的稳定压力是氢饱和化合物化学中最重要挑战之一。本研究旨在探索Ba-Si-H系统，以寻找可在较低压力下稳定存在的氢化物材料。

Method: 在0-142 GPa压力范围和4-317 K温度范围内，采用输运测量、¹H核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance）、单晶和粉末X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）等方法研究Ba-Si-H系统。

Result: 在18-31 GPa压力下合成了先前预测的立方BaSiH₈，并发现其可在减压至常压条件下保持稳定。在142 GPa时，Ba-Si多氢化物表现出金属性和超导性质（T_c = 9 K，B_c2(0)=13-16 T）；在低于50 GPa时，则表现为简并半导体（bandgap < 0.4 meV）或弱电子局域化的不良金属，具有负磁阻、光伏效应以及在X射线和可见光范围内的持续光电导性。

Conclusion: 该工作实现了可在减压至常压条件下保持稳定的Ba-Si多氢化物的高压合成，克服了超氢化物化学中的关键瓶颈，为氢储存的实际应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: Reducing the stabilization pressure of superhydrides represents one of the most important challenges in hydrogen-saturated compound chemistry. Moving in this direction, we studied the Ba-Si-H system at 0-142 GPa using transport measurements, 1H nuclear magnetic resonance, single-crystal and powder X-ray diffraction in the temperature range of 4-317 K. We synthesized the previously predicted cubic BaSiH$_{8}$ at pressures of 18-31 GPa. Remarkably, we demonstrate that BaSiH$_8$ remains stable upon decompression to ambient conditions and can be recovered from the diamond anvil cell. Obtained Ba-Si polyhydrides exhibit metallic and superconducting properties ($\textit{T$_c$}$ = 9 K, $\textit{B$_{c2}$}$(0)=13-16 T) at 142 GPa. However, at pressures below 50 GPa, these hydrides behave as degenerate semiconductors (bandgap < 0.4 meV) or poor metals with weak electron localization, negative magnetoresistance, photovoltaic effect, and persistent photoconductivity in the X-ray and visible range. Our work demonstrates the high-pressure synthesis of Ba-Si polyhydrides that remain stable upon decompression to ambient conditions, overcoming a critical bottleneck in superhydride chemistry and establishing a foundation for practical applications in hydrogen storage.

</details>


### [232] [The stripe state at 1/8 Ba doping hosts optimal superconductivity in La-214 cuprates under low in-plane stress](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14108)
*V. Sazgari,S. S. Islam,M. Lamotte,J. N. Graham,O. Gerguri,P. Kràl,I. Maetsu,T. Shiroka,G. Simutis,R. Khasanov,R. Sarkar,A. Steppke,N. A. Shepelin,M. Müller,M. Bartkowiak,M. Janoschek,J. Chang,H. H. Klauss,T. Adachi,G. D. Gu,J. M. Tranquada,H. Luetkens,Z. Guguchia*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过施加面内单轴应力，在La₂₋ₓBaₓCuO₄ (LBCO)的x=0.125掺杂浓度下实现了超导转变温度的巨幅提升，从5K增至37K。研究揭示了LTT相抑制和静态自旋条纹序体积分数减少对三维超导相相干性的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜酸盐体系La₂₋ₓBaₓCuO₄ (LBCO)在1/8掺杂异常附近表现出对面内单轴应力的显著敏感性，其中条纹序强烈抑制体超导性。然而，在对称选择性晶格调控下，x=0.125的共度相仍未被充分探索。

Method: 研究结合μ子自旋旋转（μSR）、交流磁化率和电阻率测量，在Cu-O键方向45°施加面内单轴应力，研究LBCO-0.125的超导性、自旋条纹序和结构响应。同时，对x=0.115和0.135的电阻率测量追踪了异常两侧的演化。

Result: 在0.5 GPa应力下，LBCO-0.125的体超导转变温度从5K巨幅提升至37K，零电阻态达到37K，超导转变起始温度高达46K。自旋条纹序起始温度仅适度下降，但磁体积分数减少约一半，局部序得以保留。与LTT相相关的电阻率峰在所有掺杂浓度下均被完全抑制。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，LTT相的抑制和静态自旋条纹序体积分数的减少对优化三维超导性的发展至关重要。条纹相关相互作用增强了配对强度，而静态条纹序主要在与超导相相干性层面竞争，而非配对本身。

Abstract: The cuprate system La$_{2-x}$Ba$_{x}$CuO$_{4}$ (LBCO) exhibits a pronounced sensitivity to in-plane uniaxial stress, particularly near the 1/8 doping anomaly, where stripe order strongly suppresses bulk superconductivity. While previous studies have focused on compositions close to 0.125, the commensurate $x$=0.125 phase remains largely unexplored under symmetry-selective lattice tuning. Here, we combine muon-spin rotation ($μ$SR), AC susceptibility, and electrical resistivity to investigate superconductivity, spin-stripe order, and structural response in LBCO-0.125 under in-plane uniaxial stress applied 45$^\circ$ to the Cu-O bond direction. Complementary resistivity measurements on $x$=0.115 and 0.135 track the evolution across both sides of the anomaly. We observe a giant enhancement of the bulk superconducting transition temperature in LBCO-0.125, increasing from 5 K to 37 K under 0.5 GPa. While the onset temperature of spin-stripe order decreases only modestly, the magnetic volume fraction is reduced by about a factor of two, with local order preserved. Simultaneously, the resistivity peak associated with the LTT phase is fully suppressed across all dopings. These results demonstrate that suppression of the LTT phase and reduction of the static spin-stripe-ordered volume fraction are crucial for the development of optimal three-dimensional superconductivity. Strikingly, the composition $x$=0.125, with the most robust stripe stability and the lowest ambient-pressure $T_{\rm c}$ develops the highest $T_{\rm c}$ under stress, reaching a zero-resistance state at 37 K and an onset of the superconducting transition as high as 46 K. This behavior indicates that stripe-related interactions enhance pairing strength, while static stripe order competes with superconductivity primarily at the level of phase coherence rather than pairing itself.

</details>


### [233] [Quantum Interference Breaks Bias Symmetry at Extended Superconducting Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14329)
*Vishal Tripathi,Goutam Sheet*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了在有限空间延伸的超导界面中，粒子-空穴对称性并不保证偏压对称输运，量子干涉效应会导致本征偏压不对称电导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为Bogoliubov-de Gennes哈密顿量的粒子-空穴对称性（particle-hole symmetry）会强制超导界面产生偏压对称输运，但作者发现这一预期在有限空间延伸的界面中普遍失效。

Method: 采用保持精确粒子-空穴对称性的紧束缚散射形式（tight-binding scattering formalism），研究电子和空穴在延伸界面中的传播过程，分析量子干涉效应。

Result: 研究发现延伸界面导致电子和空穴积累不相等相位，产生本征偏压不对称电导；界面起到有效安德烈夫干涉仪（Andreev interferometer）作用，其特征阻尼振荡源于势垒内的相干多重反射。

Conclusion: 偏压不对称性可作为干涉测量和光谱学探针，用于探测混合系统和拓扑系统中不可避免的延伸界面的非局域界面物理和超导能量尺度。

Abstract: Particle-hole symmetry of the Bogoliubov-de~Gennes Hamiltonian is widely assumed to enforce bias-symmetric transport at superconducting interfaces. We show that this expectation fails generically for interfaces with finite spatial extent due to quantum interference. Using a tight-binding scattering formalism that preserves exact particle-hole symmetry, we demonstrate that propagation through an extended interface causes electrons and holes to accumulate unequal phases, leading to intrinsic bias-asymmetric conductance. The interface thereby acts as an effective Andreev interferometer with characteristic damped oscillations arising from coherent multiple reflections within the barrier. While the asymmetry originates from normal-state interference, its bias dependence is governed by the superconducting gap, which emerges as a sharp crossover scale that can be clearly resolved even when conventional coherence peaks are weak or absent. Thus we present bias asymmetry as an interferometric, spectroscopic probe of nonlocal interface physics and superconducting energy scales in hybrid and topological systems where extended interfaces are unavoidable.

</details>


### [234] [A Unified Understanding of the Experimental Controlling of the T$_\text{c}$ of Bilayer Nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14519)
*Zeyu Chen,Jia-Heng Ji,Yu-Bo Liu,Ming Zhang,Fan Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究基于双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇的t-J∥-J⊥模型，通过结合slave-boson平均场和密度矩阵重整化群方法，统一解释了多种实验条件下超导转变温度Tc的变化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期一系列控制双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇超导转变温度（Tc）的实验引起了广泛关注，这些实验通过不同环境条件（如Sm/Nd替代、压力、压缩应变和空穴掺杂）调控Tc。研究旨在为这些实验现象提供统一的理论理解。

Method: 基于先前提出的最小单d_{x²-y²}轨道双层t-J∥-J⊥模型，采用密度泛函理论计算获取不同实验条件下的模型参数，并结合作者玻色子平均场（slave-boson-mean-field）和密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix-renormalization-group）方法求解模型。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）压力下块体Tc随Sm/Nd替代比例增加而增强；2）块体Tc-压力关系呈穹顶形曲线；3）薄膜Tc随压缩应变增强而增加；4）空穴掺杂导致Tc随掺杂水平δ增加而降低。这些Tc变化主要源于J⊥随实验条件的变化。

Conclusion: 强耦合t-J∥-J⊥模型比弱耦合随机相位近似（RPA）方法能更自然地解释实验现象。研究提出通过高价元素替代La实现电子掺杂，或进一步增强薄膜压缩应变，可有效提升Tc。

Abstract: Recently, a series of experiments which control the T$_\text{c}$ of the bilayer nickelates La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ through varying environmental conditions, including the rare-earth Sm/Nd substitution, the pressure on the bulk material, the compressive strain on the film and the hole doping through over-oxidation or alkaline earth element substitution have caught great interests. Here, we provide a unified understanding toward all these experiments based on the minimal single $d_{x^2-y^2}$-orbital bilayer $t-J_\parallel-J_\perp$ model proposed previously. With model parameters input from density-functional-theoretical calculations under varying experimental conditions, we adopt combined slave-boson-mean-field and density-matrix-renormalization-group approaches to solve the model and compare with experiments. Our results yield that, the bulk T$_\text{c}$ under pressure enhances with the Sm/Nd substitution fraction, the bulk T$_\text{c}$-pressure relation takes a dome shaped curve, the T$_\text{c}$ of the thin film enhances with compressive strain. The obtained parameters dependence of T$_\text{c}$ in these three experiments mainly originates from the variation of $J_\perp$ with experimental conditions. As for the hole doping, our results provide that T$_\text{c}$ decreases with the hole doping level $δ$, due to reduced density of state for the $d_{x^2-y^2}$-orbital. All these results are qualitatively consistent with experiments. We further conduct a comparative weak-coupling random-phase-approximation (RPA) based study on these experiments and find that our strong-coupling $t-J_\parallel-J_\perp$ model provides a more natural understanding of the experiments. We propose that electron doping implemented through substitution of La by element with higher valence, or further enhancement of the compressive strain in the film, can enhance T$_\text{c}$.

</details>


### [235] [Probing the Meissner effect in single crystals of $\mathbf{Bi_2Sr_2Ca_2Cu_3O_{10+δ}}$ via wide-field quantum microscopy under high pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15102)
*Masahiro Ohkuma,Ryo Matsumoto,Shintaro Adachi,Shinobu Onoda,Takao Watanabe,Kenji Ohta,Yoshihiko Takano,Keigo Arai*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究使用基于氮空位中心的宽场量子显微镜，比较了不同压力传递介质（cBN和KBr）对最佳掺杂Bi-2223超导体Tc压力依赖性的影响，发现介质选择显著影响高压下超导特性的保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于最佳掺杂Bi-2223的高压研究存在矛盾结果：流体介质中观察到Tc的恢复，而固体介质中则出现类绝缘转变。缺乏对不同压力传递介质效应的直接比较，因此需要系统研究介质选择对高压下超导特性的影响。

Method: 采用基于氮空位（nitrogen-vacancy）中心的宽场量子显微镜（wide-field quantum microscopy）探测高压下的磁响应。使用立方氮化硼（cBN）和溴化钾（KBr）作为压力传递介质，比较不同介质条件下超导转变的行为。

Result: 在KBr介质中，指示超导转变的近70K抗磁响应持续到23 GPa；而在cBN介质中，该响应在11 GPa和70K以上消失。这表明Bi-2223对压力环境具有高度敏感性，不同介质导致显著不同的高压行为。

Conclusion: 研究结果证明了Bi-2223超导体对压力环境的高度敏感性，并强调了静水压（hydrostatic pressure）在铜氧化物超导体中的关键作用。介质选择是高压研究中不可忽视的重要因素。

Abstract: We investigated the pressure dependence of the superconducting transition temperature ($T_{\rm c}$) in optimally doped Bi$_2$Sr$_2$Ca$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{10+δ}$ (Bi-2223) single crystals using different pressure-transmitting media. Previous high-pressure studies have reported conflicting behaviors, ranging from a resurgence of $T_{\rm c}$ of optimally doped Bi-2223 in fluid media to an insulating-like transition in solid media. However, a direct comparison of the effects of different pressure-transmitting media is lacking. Here, we employed wide-field quantum microscopy based on nitrogen-vacancy centers to probe the magnetic response under high pressure, utilizing cBN and KBr as media. We observed that a diamagnetic response near 70 K, indicative of the superconducting transition, persisted up to 23 GPa in KBr, whereas it disappeared above 11 GPa and 70 K in cBN. These results demonstrate the high sensitivity of Bi-2223 to the pressure environment and highlight the critical role of hydrostatic pressure in cuprate superconductors.

</details>


### [236] [Hidden Zeeman Field in Odd-Parity Magnets: An Ideal Platform for Topological Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15147)
*Xun-Jiang Luo,Zi-Ting Sun,Xilin Feng,Mingliang Tian,K. T. Law*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文揭示了奇宇称磁体（OPMs）中普遍存在由时间反演对称性破缺产生的隐藏塞曼场，该场从根本上重塑了能带结构。研究表明，OPMs中的非相对论性自旋劈裂（NSS）源于一种涌现规范场，表现为实空间自旋环流序。这种独特的能带结构使OPMs成为拓扑超导体（TSCs）的理想平台，支持大拓扑区域和多种马约拉纳边界模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇宇称磁体（odd-parity magnets, OPMs）作为一类基本的非常规磁性材料，其基本理解仍存在严重不足。先前研究仅关注非相对论性自旋劈裂（non-relativistic spin splitting, NSS），而忽略了磁性序本身固有的时间反演对称性破缺。本文旨在纠正这一基本误解，揭示OPMs中普遍存在的隐藏物理效应。

Method: 通过分析性f波磁体模型（analytical f-wave magnet model），研究揭示了NSS的微观起源——一种表现为实空间自旋环流序（real-space spin loop current order）的涌现规范场（emergent gauge field）。基于OPMs的能带结构，设计了一系列拓扑超导体（topological superconductors, TSCs）。

Result: 研究发现OPMs中普遍存在由时间反演对称性破缺产生的隐藏塞曼场（hidden Zeeman field），该场从根本上重塑了能带结构。大的NSS（eV尺度）使常规超导性能够与隐藏塞曼场（塞曼劈裂达数百meV）稳健共存。这种独特的能带结构使OPMs成为拓扑超导体的理想平台，支持大拓扑区域和多种马约拉纳边界模式（Majorana boundary modes），包括单向马约拉纳边缘态（unidirectional Majorana edge states）。

Conclusion: 本文纠正了关于奇宇称磁体的基本误解，揭示了其普遍存在的隐藏塞曼场效应。研究确立了OPMs作为无外场且稳健的拓扑超导体多功能平台的地位，为拓扑超导体的实现提供了新的理论框架和材料平台。

Abstract: Odd-parity magnets (OPMs) have emerged as a fundamental class of unconventional magnetisms, characterized by time-reversal-preserving non-relativistic spin splitting (NSS). Despite growing interest, the fundamental understanding of OPMs remains critically incomplete, as previous studies have focused exclusively on NSS while overlooking the intrinsically broken time-reversal symmetry ($\mathcal{T}$) inherent to magnetic order. In this work, we reveal that OPMs universally host a hidden Zeeman field rooted in this $\mathcal{T}$-breaking, which fundamentally reshapes their band structure. Through an analytical $f$-wave magnet model, we show that NSS microscopically originates from an emergent gauge field, manifesting as a real-space spin loop current order. Crucially, the large NSS (eV scale) enables conventional superconductivity to coexist robustly with the hidden Zeeman field, with Zeeman splitting reaches hundreds of meV. This unique band structure establishes OPMs as an ideal platform for topological superconductors (TSCs), supporting large topological regions. Based on OPMs, we engineer a series of TSCs hosting distinct Majorana boundary modes, including unidirectional Majorana edge states. Our work corrects a fundamental misconception about OPMs and establishes them as a versatile platform for field-free and robust TSCs.

</details>


### [237] [Quench Protection in Insulated REBCO Conductors: Design Optimization and Fast Detection via REBCO SQD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15244)
*Hajar Zgour,Walid Abdel Maksoud,Bertrand Baudouy,Antoine Guinet*

TL;DR: 本研究在法国PEPR SupraFusion项目框架下，比较了两种保护绝缘REBCO导体的方法：铜稳定剂优化和共绕REBCO超导失超检测器，旨在解决聚变能应用中高温超导体在失超事件中的可靠保护问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究比较了两种保护方法：(i)通过铜稳定剂（copper-stabilizer）优化实现导体保护；(ii)采用共绕（co-wound）的REBCO超导失超检测器（superconducting quench detector, SQD），该检测器电气隔离但热耦合，并通过故意脱氧降低临界温度（Tc）和临界电流（Ic）以实现更早的转变。使用一维THEA模型进行模拟分析。

Result: 一维THEA建模显示，选择合适的稳定剂横截面可以在失超事件期间通过将热点温度保持在安全限值内实现保护。模拟还表明，使用REBCO SQD能够在更低的温度下实现失超检测。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过优化铜稳定剂横截面或使用故意脱氧的REBCO超导失超检测器，可以有效解决绝缘REBCO导体在失超保护中的挑战，为聚变能应用中高温超导体的可靠运行提供了重要技术途径。

Abstract: This work was conducted within the framework of the exploratory French project PEPR SupraFusion, which aims to advance the field of fusion energy by developing High-Temperature Superconductor (HTS)-based demonstrators capable of storing significant energy while operating under high magnetic fields and currents. Ensuring a reliable protection during a quench in Insulated REBCO conductors is challenging\,: slow normal-zone propagation and validation delays allow the hotspot's temperature to reach damaging levels. We compare (i) conductor protection via copper-stabilizer optimization and (ii) a co-wound, REBCO superconducting quench detector (SQD) that is electrically isolated yet thermally coupled and intentionally deoxygenated to lower Tc and Ic for an earlier transition. Onedimensional THEA modeling shows that a good choice of stabilizer cross-section makes the protection possible during quench events by keeping the temperature of the hotspot within a safe limit. The simulations also demonstrate that the use of a REBCO SQD enables the quench detection at lower temperatures.

Method: 基于电子-声子耦合机制（electron-phonon coupling mechanism），系统研究准一维碳纳米管在单轴拉伸应变下的超导性。通过计算分析声子软化、电子-声子耦合强度及费米能级电子态密度等关键参数。

Abstract: Superconductivity in quasi-one-dimensional systems is an significant but undervalued research field. In this work, based on the electron-phonon coupling mechanism, we systematically investigate the superconductivity in quasi-one-dimensional carbon nanotube under uniaxial tensile strain. The calculated superconducting critical temperature attains its peak value of 162 K at a uniaxial tensile strain of 4.5\%, being drastically higher than the counterpart in the unstrained carbon nanotube. An overall softening of phonons, strong electron-phonon coupling, and an increase of electronic density of states at the Fermi level, play key roles in achieving high-temperature superconductivity in this system. Our research demonstrates that stretching is an effective approach to modulating the superconductivity one-dimensional materials, and more importantly, indicates that high-temperature superconductivity may occur in carbon nanotubes.
