### [239] [Effect of pulse duration on current-induced selective oxygen migration in high-Tc superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15509)
*Fridrich Egyenes,Daniel Stoffels,Stefan Marinkovic,Bernd Aichner,Huidong Li,Anna Palau,Milan Tapajna,Wolfgang Lang,Alejandro V. Silhanek*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究探索了脉冲长度对YBCO薄膜中电迁移起始电流的影响，发现当脉冲时间缩短至微秒级以下时，电迁移起始电流迅速增加，表明电迁移过程变得更加非热主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究主要限于毫秒或更长时间尺度的脉冲激发，热效应显著影响电迁移过程。本研究旨在探索脉冲长度对电迁移起始电流的影响，特别是在更短时间尺度下的行为。

Method: 通过测量YBa₂Cu₃O₇-δ（YBCO）桥结构在不同脉冲长度（200 ns至1 ms）下的电迁移起始电流I_EM，并结合解析和数值方法估算局部温度变化。

Result: 当脉冲长度δt减小至约10 μs以下时，电迁移起始电流I_EM呈现快速增加。温度估算表明，随着脉冲缩短，局部温度降低，使电迁移过程更加非热（athermal）主导。

Conclusion: 脉冲长度显著影响YBCO中电迁移过程的性质，短脉冲下电迁移更加非热主导。这些发现对忆阻器（memristor）操作和薄膜中热磁不稳定性效应的描述具有重要意义。

Abstract: High current densities can induce the directional diffusion of atoms in metallic films. In YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ (YBCO), this electromigration process selectively acts on oxygen atoms lying in the Cu-O chains, permitting to vary the oxygen concentration in a targeted spot of high current density. This approach has proven successful in mapping the phase diagram of the material as a function of carrier concentration or as a way to manufacture memristive devices owing to its reversibility under small bipolar excitations. Thus far, most of the investigations have been limited to pulsed excitation with current/voltage pulses on a millisecond or longer scale, for which thermal effects undeniably influence the process. In the present work, we explore the impact of pulse length $δt$ on the onset current of electromigration, $I_{\text{EM}}$, of YBCO bridges, covering the range from 200 ns to 1 ms. As $δt$ decreases below $\sim 10~μ$s, $I_{\text{EM}}$ exhibits a rapid increase. Analytical and numerical estimates of the local temperature show that as pulses shorten, the temperature decreases, making the electromigration process more athermal. These findings are relevant for the operation of memristors and should be taken into account when describing the effects of thermomagnetic instabilities in thin films.

</details>

### [240] [Measurement of the $t$-channel single top quark cross section in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 5.02 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13592)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文首次在CMS探测器上测量了质心能量5.02 TeV下质子-质子碰撞中单顶夸克t-道产生截面，测得总截面为25.4 pb，并提取了CKM矩阵元|V_tb| = 0.92 ± 0.09，结果与标准模型预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次在CMS探测器上测量质心能量5.02 TeV下质子-质子碰撞中单顶夸克t-道产生截面，填补了该能量下的测量空白，并为验证标准模型预测提供实验数据。

Method: 使用CMS探测器在2017年采集的302 pb⁻¹积分亮度数据，分析包含一个电子或μ子以及至少两个喷注的事件，其中至少一个喷注被识别为来自b夸克碎裂，从而提取单顶夸克产生截面。

Result: 测得单顶夸克和单顶反夸克产生的总截面为25.4 pb，其中tq截面为17.6 pb，t̄q截面为6.6 pb，两者比值为2.7，并提取出CKM矩阵元|V_tb| = 0.92 ± 0.09。

Conclusion: 测量结果与量子色动力学（QCD）次次领头阶精度的标准模型预测良好一致，验证了理论预测的准确性，并为基本粒子物理研究提供了重要实验依据。

Abstract: The single top quark $t$-channel production cross section is measured in proton-proton collisions at the CERN LHC at $\sqrt{s}$ = 5.02 TeV, using data recorded with the CMS detector in 2017, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 302 pb$^{-1}$, and resulting in the first CMS measurement of the process at that energy. Events with one electron or muon and two or more jets, among which at least one is identified as originating from a b quark fragmentation, are analyzed. The combined cross section of single top quark (tq) and single top antiquark ($\mathrm{\bar{t}q}$) production is $σ_{\mathrm{tq+\bar{t}q}}$ = 25.4$^{+3.6}_{-3.5}$ (stat) $^{+4.2}_{-3.9}$ (syst) $\pm$ 0.5 (lumi) pb. The individual cross sections are measured to be $σ_{\mathrm{tq}}$ = 17.6$^{+2.8}_{-2.7}$ (stat) $^{+2.6}_{-2.4}$ (syst) $\pm$ 0.3 (lumi) pb and $σ_{\mathrm{\bar{t}q}}$ = 6.6$^{+2.4}_{-1.6}$ (stat) $^{+2.1}_{-2.5}$ (syst) $\pm$ 0.1 (lumi) pb. Their ratio is measured to be $\mathcal{R}_{\mathrm{t-ch}}$ = 2.7$^{+1.5}_{-0.8}$ (stat) $^{+1.3}_{-0.3}$(syst). The absolute value of the Cabibbo$-$Kobayashi$-$Maskawa matrix element is found to be $\lvert f_{\mathrm{LV}}V_\mathrm{tb}\rvert$ = 0.92 $\pm$ 0.09 (exp) $\pm$ 0.01 (thy). The measurements are in good agreement with the standard model predictions at next-to-next-to-leading order accuracy in quantum chromodynamics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于费米国家加速器实验室（Fermi National Accelerator Laboratory）收集的完整MicroBooNE Booster Neutrino Beam数据集，包含$1.3\times 10^{21}$质子轰击靶（protons on target）。分析考虑了质子动能高于和低于可见阈值的两种情况，并提取了质子与电子的运动学（kinematics）微分截面。

Result: 结果显示，在轻子（lepton）运动学方面与大多数模型预测吻合良好，但在强子系统建模方面存在一些差异，特别是在质子角度（proton angle）的分布上。研究还通过质子与电子方向之间的角度探索了强子系统与轻子系统之间的关系。

Conclusion: 结论表明，虽然现有模型在描述轻子系统方面表现良好，但对强子系统的建模仍需改进，特别是在质子角度分布方面。这些结果为中微子相互作用模型的进一步完善提供了重要的实验约束。

Abstract: We present a new measurement of the electron neutrino charged current cross section on argon without pions in the final state. This measurement uses the full MicroBooNE Booster Neutrino Beam dataset of $1.3\times 10^{21}$ protons on target collected at Fermi National Accelerator Laboratory. Events are considered both with and without protons above the kinetic energy visibility threshold. Differential cross sections are extracted in proton and electron kinematics, including energy and angle relative to the neutrino beam direction. The relationship between the hadronic and leptonic systems is explored through the angle between the proton and electron directions. The resulting cross sections are compared to a variety of available generator predictions using different models of neutrino interactions. We find good agreement with most models in lepton kinematics and some discrepancies in the hadronic system modeling, particularly in proton angle.

Method: 研究采用技术分析方法，评估AIE在大型强子对撞机等对撞束实验典型固定延迟环境中的部署能力。具体通过向量化实现提升决策树（BDT）和卷积神经网络（CNN）两种机器学习算法来验证可行性。

Abstract: Complex, high-throughput data acquisition and processing systems, such as those used in high-energy physics experiments, are increasingly moving sophisticated pattern recognition and data compression algorithms closer to the sensors themselves. We present a technical study of a new family of such co-processors from AMD Xilinx, the Adaptive Intelligence (AI) Engine, or AIE, as part of the Versal architecture. Specifically, we focus on the deployment capabilities of AIEs in fixed latency environments such as those typically found in colliding beam experiments like those at the Large Hadron Collider. Abstract: We present here a search for WIMP dark matter using 790.8 live-days of data collected with 3269 kg of liquid argon (1266 kg fiducial) by the DEAP-3600 detector at SNOLAB, using the Profile Likelihood Ratio method. The likelihood model is based on three parameters: estimated energy, pulse-shape discrimination parameter, and reconstructed position within the detector. Using this method, the expected signal sensitivity of DEAP-3600 benefits from an increased fiducial volume and improved event selection acceptance. Alpha-decays from a small number of dust particulates circulating within the liquid argon target are the dominant source of background events and limit the sensitivity of this search. This result provides improved exclusion upper limits on the WIMP-nucleon spin-independent cross section on liquid argon for WIMP masses between 20 GeV/$c^{2}$ and 100 GeV/$c^{2}$. At 100 GeV/$c^{2}$ the observed limit is 3.4 $\times$ 10$^{-45}$ cm$^2$ at 90% confidence level.

### [244] [Dressed-State Spectroscopy of Proton Spins in Water Beyond the Rotating-Wave Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14878)

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究首次实验观测了水中质子自旋在强非共振磁场中的缀饰态（dressed states），验证了量子拉比模型（quantum Rabi model）对高阶共振的预测，为核磁共振中的精密自旋操控开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子拉比模型为描述超越旋转波近似（rotating-wave approximation）的两能级系统与强振荡场相互作用提供了理论框架。研究旨在将缀饰态光谱学扩展到质子自旋系统，为核磁共振及相关精密测量中的自旋操控提供新方法。

Method: 采用拉比型实验装置，利用强非共振磁缀饰场（magnetic dressing field）实现水中质子自旋的缀饰态。通过测量共振光谱来观测涉及多个缀饰场量子的自旋态跃迁。

Result: 测量的共振光谱显示出多个涉及数个缀饰场量子的自旋态跃迁，包括量子拉比模型预测的高阶共振。缀饰态能量与理论预期高度吻合，首次实现了质子自旋缀饰态的实验观测。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将缀饰态光谱学扩展到质子自旋系统，验证了量子拉比模型对高阶共振的预测，为核磁共振及相关精密测量中的精密自旋操控开辟了新的可能性。

Abstract: The quantum Rabi model provides the framework for describing a two-level system interacting with a strong oscillating field beyond the rotating-wave approximation. We report the first experimental observation of the resulting dressed states of proton spins in water, realized using a Rabi-type setup with a strong off-resonant magnetic dressing field. The measured resonance spectrum exhibits multiple spin-state transitions involving several dressing-field quanta, including higher-order resonances predicted by the quantum Rabi model. The dressed-state energies show excellent agreement with theoretical expectations, extending dressed-state spectroscopy to proton spins and opening new possibilities for precision spin manipulation in nuclear magnetic resonance and related precision measurements.

### [245] [Reinterpretation of searches for supersymmetry in models with variable R-parity-violating coupling strength using the full ATLAS Run 2 Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15007)
*The ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究重新解释了13项ATLAS超对称性（SUSY）搜索实验，在可变R宇称破坏（RPV）耦合强度的SUSY模型中设置质量限制，扩展了传统R宇称守恒（RPC）分析的范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超对称性（SUSY）搜索主要针对R宇称守恒（RPC）或固定R宇称破坏（RPV）模型，缺乏对可变RPV耦合强度的系统研究。本研究旨在将现有分析扩展到更广泛的RPV框架，特别是探索耦合强度如何影响最轻超对称粒子（LSP）的衰变特性（瞬时或长寿命）。

Method: 研究重新解释了13项ATLAS SUSY搜索实验，这些实验原本针对RPC和RPV SUSY模型优化。数据集基于大型强子对撞机（LHC）ATLAS探测器在2015-2018年间收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度140 fb⁻¹，质心能量√s=13 TeV。分析在可变RPV耦合强度的SUSY模型中设置95%置信水平的质量限制。

Result: 在产生顶夸克增强末态的对产生胶子模型中，无论RPV耦合值如何，胶子质量下限设定为1.8 TeV。在衰变到第一和第二代夸克的胶子模型中，根据RPV耦合λ'（λ''）的不同值，胶子质量被排除在1.6-2.2（1.6-2.5）TeV范围内。在λ''高值时，顶标夸克质量被排除高达2.4 TeV，而低中值λ''时为1.0-1.7 TeV。τ轻子质量在180-340 GeV范围内被排除，当λ耦合小于10⁻⁴时。当λ_{i33}大于4×10⁻⁵时，希格斯微子质量被排除高达800 GeV-1.0 TeV。

Conclusion: 该工作将分析范围从RPC情景扩展到广泛的RPV框架，显著提高了对多种长寿命粒子特征的敏感性。研究展示了可变RPV耦合强度对超对称粒子质量限制的显著影响，为探索超对称性提供了更全面的约束条件。

Abstract: A collection of thirteen ATLAS searches for supersymmetry (SUSY) models, optimized for R-parity-conserving (RPC) and R-parity-violating (RPV) SUSY, are reinterpreted in SUSY models with variable RPV coupling strength, which determines whether the lightest supersymmetric particle decays promptly or is long-lived. The dataset corresponds to an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collisions at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV collected between 2015 and 2018 by the ATLAS detector at the Large Hadron Collider. Limits are set at 95% confidence level on the mass of pair-produced gluinos decaying to final states enhanced or depleted with top quarks, and on the masses of pair-produced top squarks, tau-sleptons, or charginos and neutralinos. In a model of pair-produced gluinos decaying to final states enhanced with top quarks, a lower limit of 1.8 TeV on the gluino mass is set regardless of the RPV coupling value. In the gluino model with decays to first and second generation quarks, gluino masses are excluded up to 1.6-2.2 (1.6-2.5) TeV for different values of the RPV coupling $λ^{'}$ ($λ^{''}$). Top-squark masses up to 2.4 TeV are excluded at high values of $λ^{''}$, compared to 1.0-1.7 TeV for low and intermediate $λ^{''}$. Tau-slepton masses between 180 GeV and 340 GeV are excluded for $λ$ couplings smaller than $10^{-4}$. Higgsino masses up to 800 GeV-1.0 TeV are excluded when $λ_{i33}$ is larger than $4\times10^{-5}$. This work extends the analyses beyond RPC scenarios to a broad class of RPV frameworks and achieves significantly improved sensitivity to a diverse range of long-lived particle signatures.

### [246] [A Simulation-Based Inference Evaluation of Tension Between MicroBooNE and MiniBooNE Results in a 3+1 Sterile Neutrino Global Fit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15322)
*Julia P. Woodward,Joshua Villarreal,John M. Hardin,Austin Schneider,Janet M. Conrad*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文开发了基于模拟推理（SBI）的框架来评估3+1惰性中微子（sterile neutrino）全局拟合中不同数据集间的兼容性（compatibility），并以MiniBooNE和MicroBooNE实验数据为例，量化了它们之间的张力（tension）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在3+1惰性中微子全局拟合中，不同数据集间长期存在的张力表明该模型无法充分解释观测数据，尽管相比标准三中微子模型有显著改进。评估更复杂模型目前计算成本过高，因此需要开发降低计算成本的框架。

Method: 本文是开发基于模拟推理（Simulation-Based Inference, SBI）框架系列工作的第三篇，旨在形式化定义SBI框架内的张力。作为示例，对来自同一束流的MiniBooNE实验的带电电流准弹性（charged-current quasi-elastic）中微子数据和MicroBooNE实验的包容性（inclusive）中微子数据进行完整的3+1拟合。

Result: 使用SBI程序拟合时，发现MiniBooNE和MicroBooNE数据分别以3.6σ和1.8σ支持3+1模型，而两者间的张力为3.3σ。在修正MicroBooNE νμ样本中数据与蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo）的归一化差异后，张力降至2.2σ，表明分歧减小但仍不可忽略。

Conclusion: 观测到的张力可能反映了3+1模型在描述数据集方面的局限性，以及系统性效应（systematic effects）对不同实验的影响差异。这为考虑更复杂模型提供了依据，但当前计算成本仍是主要限制因素。

Abstract: Compatibility between different datasets in a global fit is essential for determining whether a chosen model adequately describes the data. In a 3+1 sterile neutrino global fit, long-standing tensions between datasets sensitive to $ν_e$ appearance and $ν_e/ν_μ$ disappearance indicate a failure of the model to explain the observed data, despite an overall $> 5σ$ improvement over the $3ν$ Standard Model (SM) based on a $χ^2$ fit. Overall, a global preference for the 3+1 sterile-neutrino hypothesis with significant tension between experiments motivates consideration of more complex models, but these are currently computationally prohibitive to evaluate. This paper is the third in a series aimed at reducing computational cost by developing a Simulation-Based Inference (SBI) framework for global fits. Previous papers focused on rapidly fitting the data sets using frequentist (Feldman-Cousins) and Bayesian approaches, while in this work, we formalize a definition of tension within the SBI framework.
  As an example, we perform a full 3+1 fit to the charged-current quasi-elastic neutrino data from the MiniBooNE experiment and the inclusive neutrino data from the MicroBooNE experiment, located on the same beamline. Using experiment-supplied systematics as is, we find these data sets favor 3+1 at $3.6σ$ and $1.8σ$ respectively, while the tension between the two is $3.3σ$, when fit with the SBI procedure. After correcting for normalization differences between data and Monte Carlo in the MicroBooNE $ν_μ$ samples, the tension relaxes to $2.2σ$, indicating reduced but non-negligible disagreement. The observed tension may reflect both limitations of the 3+1 model in describing the datasets and the presence of systematic effects that impact the experiments differently.

</details>

*Jacopo Fanini,Gerardo Ganis,Marcello Maggi*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文提出将LEP实验数据迁移至EDM4hep标准化格式，以支持FCC-ee物理潜力评估和长期数据保存，并已成功开发概念验证工作流应用于ALEPH数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LEP数据作为最精确的高能电子-正电子对撞数据集，其长期保存符合FAIR数据原则至关重要。这些数据在FCC-ee物理潜力评估中具有关键作用，因其质心能量重叠可为探测器性能和物理分析提供宝贵基准。

Method: 开发概念验证工作流（proof of concept workflow），将LEP数据迁移至EDM4hep标准化事件数据格式，该格式是HEP软件生态系统Key4hep中正在开发的标准格式。

Result: 迁移工作流已成功开发并应用于ALEPH数据，验证了技术可行性。迁移至EDM4hep不仅能支持未来研究，还能显著降低数据丢失风险，提高可访问性和互操作性。

Conclusion: 将LEP数据迁移至EDM4hep格式对于实现长期数据保存、支持FCC-ee物理评估至关重要，已开发的工作流为全面数据迁移提供了技术基础。

Abstract: The LEP data represents the most precise and highest centre-of-mass energy sample of $e^+e^-$ collision data collected to date. Numerous scientific articles have been published since the conclusion of the experiments, underscoring the ongoing relevance of this dataset and the need to secure its long-term availability according to FAIR data preservation principles. These data could also play a crucial new role in the context of the evaluation of the physics potential of FCC-ee, due to the overlapping centre-of-mass energies, offering a valuable benchmark for detector performance and physics analyses. To fulfill this role, the data should be made available in EDM4hep, the standardized event data format currently developed in the context of the common HEP software ecosystem Key4hep. Migrating to EDM4hep would not only beneficial to future studies but also significantly mitigate the risk of data loss, increase accessibility and interoperability, hence facilitate long-term data preservation. A proof of concept workflow to perform the migration has been developed and successfully applied to ALEPH data.

### [248] [Search for the rare decays of $D\to h(h^{(')})e^{+}e^{-}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15575)
*BESIII collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII实验基于20.3 fb⁻¹的e⁺e⁻对撞数据，对15种D介子稀有衰变道D→h(h')e⁺e⁻进行搜索，未发现显著信号，首次测量了5个衰变道的分支比上限，并对8个衰变道的结果改进了至少4倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在搜索D介子到强子伴随电子-正电子对（D→h(h')e⁺e⁻）的15种稀有衰变道，这些过程在标准模型（Standard Model）中受到高度抑制，对超出标准模型（beyond Standard Model）的新物理敏感。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的20.3 fb⁻¹ e⁺e⁻对撞数据，质心能量为3.773 GeV，对15个稀有衰变道进行系统搜索，并基于无显著信号观测确定分支比上限。

Result: 所有15个衰变道均未观测到显著信号，灵敏度达到10⁻⁶∼10⁻⁷水平。首次测量了D⁺→ρ⁺e⁺e⁻等5个衰变道的分支比上限，对D⁰→π⁰e⁺e⁻等8个衰变道的上限改进了至少4倍，其中D⁰→ρ⁰e⁺e⁻和D⁰→φe⁺e⁻的上限分别设为0.7×10⁻⁶和4.6×10⁻⁶。

Conclusion: 该研究为D介子稀有衰变提供了迄今为止最严格的实验限制，这些结果对检验标准模型和探索新物理具有重要意义，并为未来更高精度的实验测量奠定了基础。

Abstract: We search for 15 rare decays of $D$ mesons to hadrons accompanied by an electron-positron pair $D\to h(h^{(')})e^{+}e^{-}$, based on 20.3 fb$^{-1}$ of $e^+ e^-$ collision data collected at the center-of-mass energy of 3.773 GeV with the BESIII detector at BEPCII. No significant signals are observed, and the corresponding upper limits on the branching fractions at the 90\% confidence level are determined. The sensitivities of the results are at the level of $10^{-6}$ $\sim$ $10^{-7}$. The upper limits on the branching fractions for the $D^+\to ρ^{+} e^+ e^-$, $D^+\to K^{*+} e^+ e^-$, $D^0\to K_S^0 K_S^0 e^+ e^-$, $D^0\to π^0 π^0 e^+ e^-$ and $D^0\to η^{\prime} e^+ e^-$ decay channels are measured for the first time. For the $D^0\to π^0 e^+ e^-$, $D^0\to ηe^+ e^-$, $D^0\to ωe^+ e^-$, $D^0\to K_S^0 e^+ e^-$, $D^+\to π^+ π^0 e^+ e^-$, $D^+\to K^+ π^0 e^+ e^-$, $D^+\to π^+ K_S^0 e^+ e^-$ and $D^+\to K^+ K_S^0 e^+ e^-$ decay channels, the upper limits on the branching fractions are determined, with an improvement of at least a factor of four compared to previous searches. The upper limits on the branching fractions for the $D^0\to ρ^{0} e^+ e^-$ and $D^0\to φe^+ e^-$ decay channels are set at $0.7 \times 10^{-6}$ and $4.6 \times 10^{-6}$, respectively.

### [249] [Optimality and annealing path planning of dynamical analog solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13778)
*Shu Zhou,K. Y. Michael Wong,Juntao Wang,David Shui Wing Hui,Daniel Ebler,Jie Sun*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于动力学系统的模拟求解器（如伊辛机）在大规模组合优化中展现出潜力，但该领域缺乏对求解器最优性保证的深入理解，以及参数调度如何影响动力学和结果的机制分析。

Method: 研究开发了一个动力学平均场（dynamical mean-field）框架来分析伊辛机动力学过程，特别针对求解Sherrington-Kirkpatrick(SK)自旋玻璃模型的基态能量问题。该方法能够识别实现快速收敛至近最优解的内在机制。

Result: 对于固定的目标能量密度Ec，解通常可在O(1)次矩阵向量乘法内达到，表明具有常数时间复杂度。研究还揭示了不同参数调度轨迹的理论限制，并证明了温度退火（temperature-only annealing）对相干伊辛机（Coherent Ising Machine）的显著优势。

Conclusion: 基于这些发现，研究提出了设计优化参数调度的通用框架，从而提高了伊辛机在复杂优化任务中的实际有效性。动力学求解器的优越性能通过达到SK模型的基态能量得到了验证。

Abstract: Recently proposed analog solvers based on dynamical systems, such as Ising machines, are promising platforms for large-scale combinatorial optimization. Yet, given the heuristic nature of the field, there is very limited insight on optimality guarantees of the solvers, as well as how parameter schedules shape dynamics and outcomes. Here, we develop a dynamical mean-field framework to analyze Ising-machine dynamics for finding the ground state energy of the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick(SK) model of spin glasses and identify mechanisms that enable rapid convergence to provenly near-optimal energies. For a fixed target energy density Ec, we show that solutions are typically reached within O(1) matrix vector multiplications, indicating constant time complexity. We further delineate theoretical limitations arising from different parameter-scheduling trajectories and demonstrate a pronounced benefit of temperature-only annealing for the Coherent Ising Machine. Building on these insights, we propose a general framework for designing optimized parameter schedules, thereby improving the practical effectiveness of Ising machines for complex optimization tasks. The superior performance of the dynamical solvers is illustrated by the attainment of the ground state energy of the SK model.

### [250] [Learning Associations in Reconfigurable Particle Packings via Local Cyclic Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14534)
*Wenjing Guo,Vidyesh Rao Anisetti,Kairui Zhang,Shabeeb Ameen,Ananth Kandala,Menachem Stern,Nidhi Pashine,Joseph D. Paulsen,J. M. Schwarz,Tao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究在可重构颗粒堆积系统中实现了联想记忆行为，通过纯局部循环驱动编程，利用颗粒接触网络的重组形成有效的机械耦合权重更新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索无热驱动颗粒介质中实现联想记忆功能的最小物理要素，区别于具有固定架构的传统物理学习系统，关注通过可重构物质实现基于关联的功能性。

Method: 采用二维双分散Lennard-Jones颗粒组装体，在周期性边界条件下进行无热准静态松弛演化。训练阶段固定输入颗粒循环驱动，输出颗粒通过区域驱动规则实时选择并按预定流动模式驱动；检索阶段仅驱动输入颗粒。

Result: 根据任务难度识别出三种机制：简单任务中固有机械响应已能产生正确运动；困难任务中期望映射与主导集体漂移冲突，训练增益有限；中间四极任务中重新定位输入-输出几何结构可稳定期望响应。引入间歇松弛循环可减少训练-检索失配并提高性能。

Conclusion: 研究确定了无热驱动颗粒介质中实现联想记忆功能的最小物理要素，并提出了可重构物质的联想学习相图（association learning phase diagram）概念，为可编程物质系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: We investigate associative-memory behavior in a reconfigurable particle packing programmed by purely local cyclic driving. The system is a two-dimensional bidisperse Lennard--Jones particle assembly with periodic boundaries evolved under athermal quasistatic relaxation. During training, a fixed set of input particles is driven cyclically while output particles are selected on-the-fly by a region-driving rule and driven according to a prescribed flow pattern; during retrieval, only the inputs are driven. Associative-memory performance is quantified by the cosine similarity between realized and target output displacement directions. Unlike physical learning systems with fixed architecture, learning here arises through emergent weight updates: localized rearrangements modify the contact network and reshape the effective mechanical couplings between inputs and outputs. Across task difficulty we identify three regimes. In an easy setting, the intrinsic mechanical response already produces coherent motion in the right-hand region under input-only driving, yielding high performance without training. In a hard setting, the desired mapping conflicts with the dominant collective drift, resulting in low baseline performance and only modest training gains; introducing intermittent relaxation cycles reduces train--retrieval mismatch and improves performance. In an intermediate quadrupolar task, repositioning the input--output geometry stabilizes the desired response and converts initially stochastic trajectories into reproducible learned motions. Together these results identify minimal physical ingredients for association-based functionality in athermally driven particulate media and motivate an association learning phase diagram for reconfigurable matter.

</details>


### [251] [Rigorous Asymptotics for First-Order Algorithms Through the Dynamical Cavity Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14573)
*Yatin Dandi,David Gamarnik,Francisco Pernice,Lenka Zdeborová*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文形式化（formalize）了动力学空腔方法（dynamical cavity method），并利用该方法为广义一阶方法（General First Order Methods）的动力学平均场理论（DMFT）方程提供了新的证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动力学平均场理论（Dynamical Mean Field Theory, DMFT）为某些无序系统（disordered systems）中宏观可观测量（macroscopic observables）的动力学提供了渐近描述，但物理学家主要使用的动力学空腔方法（dynamical cavity method）一直缺乏严格的数学基础。

Method: 本文形式化了动力学空腔方法，并将其应用于广义一阶方法（General First Order Methods）这一广泛类别，该类方法包含了梯度下降（Gradient Descent）和近似消息传递（Approximate Message Passing）等算法。

Result: 通过形式化动力学空腔方法，本文为广义一阶方法的DMFT方程提供了新的证明，为这一原本非严格（non-rigorous）的物理方法建立了数学基础。

Conclusion: 本文首次为动力学空腔方法提供了严格的数学形式化，并成功应用于证明广义一阶方法的DMFT方程，弥合了物理学启发方法与现有数学形式化方法之间的差距。

Abstract: Dynamical Mean Field Theory (DMFT) provides an asymptotic description of the dynamics of macroscopic observables in certain disordered systems. Originally pioneered in the context of spin glasses by Sompolinsky and Zippelius (1982), it has since been used to derive asymptotic dynamical equations for a wide range of models in physics, high-dimensional statistics and machine learning. One of the main tools used by physicists to obtain these equations is the dynamical cavity method, which has remained largely non-rigorous. In contrast, existing mathematical formalizations have relied on alternative approaches, including Gaussian conditioning, large deviations over paths, or Fourier analysis. In this work, we formalize the dynamical cavity method and use it to give a new proof of the DMFT equations for General First Order Methods, a broad class of dynamics encompassing algorithms such as Gradient Descent and Approximate Message Passing.

</details>


### [252] [Machine learning for sustainable geoenergy: uncertainty, physics and decision-ready inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14907)
*Hannah P. Menke,Ahmed H. Elsheikh,Lingli Wei,Nanzhe Wang,Andreas Busch*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文分析了地热能源（geoenergy）项目中存在的四个关键瓶颈，并提出匹配这些挑战的机器学习（ML）方法及其在四个核心应用领域的应用，最后为可重现且可靠的ML应用制定了实用议程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地热能源项目（包括CO2封存、地热能、地下氢气生成/储存等）面临从筛选评估到运营监测的全流程挑战。这些项目需要在有限且异质的观测数据下，在严格的物理和地质约束条件下做出风险可控的运营决策，这些决策直接影响部署速度、资本成本以及气候减缓声明的可信度。

Method: 论文提出了匹配地热能源项目现实挑战的机器学习方法，包括混合物理-ML（hybrid physics-ML）、概率不确定性量化（probabilistic uncertainty quantification）、结构感知表示（structure-aware representations）以及多保真度/持续学习（multi-fidelity/continual learning）。这些方法被应用于四个核心领域：成像到过程的数字孪生、多相流和近井一致性、监测和反问题（包括变形和微地震监测）、以及盆地尺度的投资组合管理。

Result: 论文识别了限制地热能源项目进展的四个关键瓶颈：稀缺且有偏的标签与有限的现场性能数据；不确定性被事后处理而非作为交付成果；从孔隙到盆地尺度的弱尺度桥接（包括耦合的化学-流动-地质力学）；以及面向监管部署的质量保证、可审计性和治理不足。

Conclusion: 论文最后提出了一个实用议程，包括基准测试、验证、报告标准以及政策支持，这些是实现可持续地热能源领域中可重现且可靠的机器学习应用所必需的。该议程旨在解决当前存在的质量保证和治理不足问题，推动地热能源项目的可信部署。

Abstract: Geoenergy projects (CO2 storage, geothermal, subsurface H2 generation/storage, critical minerals from subsurface fluids, or nuclear waste disposal) increasingly follow a petroleum-style funnel from screening and appraisal to operations, monitoring, and stewardship. Across this funnel, limited and heterogeneous observations must be turned into risk-bounded operational choices under strong physical and geological constraints - choices that control deployment rate, cost of capital, and the credibility of climate-mitigation claims. These choices are inherently multi-objective, balancing performance against containment, pressure footprint, induced seismicity, energy/water intensity, and long-term stewardship. We argue that progress is limited by four recurring bottlenecks: (i) scarce, biased labels and few field performance outcomes; (ii) uncertainty treated as an afterthought rather than the deliverable; (iii) weak scale-bridging from pore to basin (including coupled chemical-flow-geomechanics); and (iv) insufficient quality assurance (QA), auditability, and governance for regulator-facing deployment. We outline machine learning (ML) approaches that match these realities (hybrid physics-ML, probabilistic uncertainty quantification (UQ), structure-aware representations, and multi-fidelity/continual learning) and connect them to four anchor applications: imaging-to-process digital twins, multiphase flow and near-well conformance, monitoring and inverse problems (monitoring, measurement, and verification (MMV), including deformation and microseismicity), and basin-scale portfolio management. We close with a pragmatic agenda for benchmarks, validation, reporting standards, and policy support needed for reproducible and defensible ML in sustainable geoenergy.

</details>


### [253] [Extreme-Value Criticality and Gain Decomposition at the Integer Quantum Hall Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15290)
*Wei-Han Li,Abbas Ali Saberi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了开放量子系统中量子临界点处极值波函数振幅的统计特性，发现极值涨落可分解为全局增益因子和本征极值分量，并提出了极值矩标度方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强关联和开放条件下，量子临界点处的极值涨落（extreme-value fluctuations）仍缺乏深入理解。研究旨在探索开放Chalker-Coddington网络中整数量子霍尔转变（integer quantum Hall transition）的极值统计特性。

Method: 通过分析开放Chalker-Coddington网络模型，将最大波函数振幅分解为全局增益因子A和本征极值分量$|\tildeψ|_{\max}$。引入极值矩标度（extreme-moment scaling）方法研究$|ψ|_{\max}$的统计特性。

Result: 发现$|ψ|_{\max}$的指数函数$τ_{\max}(q)$在中等q值范围内近似为抛物线型，而$\ln|ψ|_{\max}$在研究尺寸范围内呈现几乎高斯分布。增益因子接近对数正态分布，对原始极值起主要控制作用。

Conclusion: 增益归一化（gain normalization）会重组统计特性：$\tildeτ_{\max}(q)$发生质变，且$|\tildeψ|_{\max}$在可及尺寸窗口内不支持标准中心化/标度下的单参数广义极值塌缩。极值可观测量为开放量子系统中的关联临界性提供了稳健探针。

Abstract: Extreme-value fluctuations at quantum critical points remain poorly understood in the presence of strong correlations and openness. At the integer quantum Hall transition in the open Chalker--Coddington network, we show that the maximal wave-function amplitude separates into a global gain and an intrinsic extreme component, $|ψ|_{\max}=A\,|\tildeψ|_{\max}$. We introduce extreme-moment scaling for $|ψ|_{\max}$ and observe an approximately parabolic exponent function $τ_{\max}(q)$ over moderate $q$, while $\ln|ψ|_{\max}$ displays an almost Gaussian bulk over the studied sizes. The gain factor is close to log-normal and largely controls the raw extremes. Gain normalization reorganizes the statistics: $\tildeτ_{\max}(q)$ changes qualitatively and $|\tildeψ|_{\max}$ does not support a single-parameter generalized extreme-value collapse under standard centering/scaling in the accessible size window. Extreme observables thus provide a robust probe of correlated criticality in open quantum systems.

</details>


### [254] [Controlled Langevin Dynamics for Sampling of Feedforward Neural Networks Trained with Minibatches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15367)
*Alessandro Zambon,Francesca Caruso,Riccardo Zecchina,Guido Tiana*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种伪朗之万（pseudo-Langevin, pL）动力学方法，用于高效地对前馈神经网络进行玻尔兹曼（Boltzmann）采样。该方法利用小批量（minibatch）梯度噪声的统计特性，通过调整虚拟质量和摩擦系数确保有效采样目标平衡分布，可扩展到百万参数规模的网络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统精确采样方法如混合蒙特卡洛（hybrid Monte Carlo, hMC）在真实数据集上计算成本过高，需要重复评估全批量梯度。需要开发一种能够利用小批量进行可控采样的高效方法，以探索大规模神经网络的解空间。

Method: 提出伪朗之万（pseudo-Langevin, pL）动力学方法，通过利用小批量梯度噪声的统计特性，调整虚拟质量（fictitious masses）和摩擦系数（friction coefficients），确保诱导的随机过程能够高效采样期望的平衡分布。

Result: 数值验证表明pL方法的平衡统计量与精确hMC采样结果一致。性能基准测试显示，随着网络规模增大，hMC迅速变得低效，而pL方案保持高计算扩散性，可良好扩展到超过百万参数的神经网络。

Conclusion: 在中间温度下采样可获得与随机梯度下降（SGD）相当的最优泛化性能，无需验证集或早停（early stopping）过程。受控小批量朗之万动力学成为探索和利用大规模神经网络解空间的实用且可扩展工具。

Abstract: Sampling the parameter space of artificial neural networks according to a Boltzmann distribution provides insight into the geometry of low-loss solutions and offers an alternative to conventional loss minimization for training. However, exact sampling methods such as hybrid Monte Carlo (hMC), while formally correct, become computationally prohibitive for realistic datasets because they require repeated evaluation of full-batch gradients. We introduce a pseudo-Langevin (pL) dynamics that enables efficient Boltzmann sampling of feed-forward neural networks trained with large datasets by using minibatches in a controlled manner. The method exploits the statistical properties of minibatch gradient noise and adjusts fictitious masses and friction coefficients to ensure that the induced stochastic process samples efficiently the desired equilibrium distribution. We validate numerically the approach by comparing its equilibrium statistics with those obtained from exact hMC sampling. Performance benchmarks demonstrate that, while hMC rapidly becomes inefficient as network size increases, the pL scheme maintains high computational diffusion and scales favorably to networks with over one million parameters. Finally, we show that sampling at intermediate temperatures yields optimal generalization performance, comparable to SGD, without requiring a validation set or early stopping procedure. These results establish controlled minibatch Langevin dynamics as a practical and scalable tool for exploring and exploiting the solution space of large neural networks.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种基于扩散的生成式机器学习模型，仅基于初始微观结构嵌入进行条件化预测。模型在单裂纹系统的分子动力学模拟数据上进行训练，用于预测原子尺度裂纹扩展过程。

Result: 模型实现了显著的计算加速，同时准确预测了动态断裂过程，包括应力驱动的裂纹萌生、裂纹分支和原子尺度桥接韧带。模型展现出固有的物理保真度，能够再现材料内在机制并忽略周期性边界伪影，且可泛化到未见的多裂纹构型。

Conclusion: 验证表明该模型无需辅助应力或能量数据即可捕捉复杂断裂物理，实现了对裂纹介导失效的快速探索，为半导体可靠性优化提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Predicting atomic-scale crack propagation in aluminum nitride (AlN) is critical for semiconductor reliability but remains prohibitively expensive via molecular dynamics (MD). We develop a diffusion-based generative machine learning model to predict atomic-scale crack propagation in AlN, a critical semiconductor material, by conditioning solely on initial microstructure embeddings. Trained on MD simulations of single-crack systems, the model achieves a significant speedup while accurately forecasting dynamic fracture processes, including stress-driven crack initiation, crack branching, and atomic-scale bridging ligaments. Crucially, it demonstrates inherent physical fidelity by reproducing material-intrinsic mechanisms while disregarding periodic boundary artifacts, and generalizes to unseen multi-crack configurations. Validation against MD ground truth confirms the capability of the model to capture complex fracture physics without auxiliary stress or energy data, enabling rapid exploration of crack-mediated failure for semiconductor reliability optimization.

### [256] [Accurate electronic and optical properties of bulk antiferromagnet CrSBr via a tuned hybrid density functional with on-site corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13494)
*Ashwin Ramasubramaniam,Daniel Hernangómez Pérez,Javier Junquera,María Camarasa-Gómez*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CrSBr作为一种层状反铁磁体（layered antiferromagnet），是探索低维光学与磁性强耦合的重要平台。然而，该材料可靠的从头算结果仅限于自洽多体微扰理论（self-consistent, many-body perturbation theory）领域，这种方法计算成本高昂且技术挑战大。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于广义Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论的替代方法，该方法计算要求较低。通过使用一个最小化的双参数集，可以调整参数以复现已知的实验和/或理论基准，如基本带隙（fundamental gap）和光学带隙（optical gap）。

Result: 经过参数调整后的泛函展现出优异的预测能力，能够准确预测CrSBr的电子结构、光学吸收谱以及激子与磁序的定量耦合。该方法在保持准确性的同时显著降低了计算复杂度。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法具有广泛适用性，可应用于其他磁性半导体材料，为当前建模方法提供了补充和简化。这种替代方案有望在保持预测精度的同时，显著降低计算资源需求和技术门槛。

Abstract: CrSBr, a layered antiferromagnet, is emerging as a versatile platform for exploring strong coupling between optical and magnetic properties in low dimensions. While experimental research on this material has progressed at a rapid pace, reliable results on the ab initio front are limited to the domain of self-consistent, many-body perturbation theory, which is both computationally expensive and technically challenging. We present an alternate, less-demanding approach -- rooted in generalized Kohn-Sham density functional theory -- that can deliver accurate electronic structure and optical absorption spectra of CrSBr, as well as quantitively accurate predictions of coupling of excitons to magnetic order in CrSBr. Using a minimal two-parameter set that can be tuned to reproduce a couple of well-known experimental and/or theoretical benchmarks, such as fundamental and optical gaps, we demonstrate excellent predictive capability for the tuned functional. The approach presented here can potentially be applied broadly to other magnetic semiconductors, complementing and simplifying current approaches to modeling these materials.

### [257] [Smoothed Boundary Method Framework for Electrochemical Simulation of Li-ion Battery Cathode with Complex Microstructure: Model, Formulation and Parameterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13527)
*Hui-Chia Yu,Bernardo Orvananos,Scott Cronin,Martin Bazant,Scott Barnett,K. Thornton*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于平滑边界法（smoothed-boundary method, SBM）的电化学模拟框架，用于分析复杂电池电极微观结构的电化学动力学。该方法利用实验重建的3D微观结构图像作为输入几何，在均匀笛卡尔网格上求解重构的控制方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可充电电池电极具有高度复杂的微观结构，包括不均匀的电极颗粒、曲折的电解质通道和不规则的颗粒-电解质界面。这些几何和机理的复杂性使得使用传统方法在微观结构层面进行电化学模拟面临挑战。

Method: 引入平滑边界法（SMB）电化学模拟框架，将传统控制方程重构为SBM版本，并在均匀笛卡尔网格上求解。模拟使用基于图像的实验重建3D微观结构作为输入几何，并采用实验测量的物理参数。

Result: 通过模拟揭示了复杂阴极微观结构的详细动力学。对两种锂化机制模型（固溶体模型和两相模型）的比较表明，使用菲克扩散（Fick's diffusion）模拟两相锂化会高估电极性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的模拟框架为探索微观结构层面的电化学动力学提供了一条创新途径，能够有效处理复杂电极微观结构的几何和机理复杂性。

Abstract: Rechargeable battery electrodes have highly complex microstructures, consisting of nonuniform electrode particles, tortuous electrolyte channels, and irregular particle-electrolyte interfaces. Moreover, the electrochemical processes involve several coupled physical mechanisms, including mass transport in the electrode particles and electrolyte, current continuity in the solid and liquid, and electrochemical surface reactions. These geometric and mechanistic complexities create a challenging barrier of electrochemical simulations at the microstructural level using conventional methods. In this paper, we introduce a smoothed-boundary method (SBM) electrochemical simulation framework for modeling the electrochemical dynamics of complex battery electrode microstructures. The conventional governing equations are reformulated into SBM versions, and are solved using uniform Cartesian grids. The simulations utilize an image-based, experimentally reconstructed 3D microstructure as the input geometry, and the physical parameters acquired from experimental measurements. Two models of lithiation mechanisms, solid-solution and two-phase, are examined under potentiostatic discharging of a Li$_x$CoO$_2$ composite cathode. Detailed dynamics of the complex cathode microstructure are revealed through the simulations. The comparison between the two models indicates that modeling two-phase lithiation with Fick's diffusion will overestimate the electrode's performance. The presented simulation framework provides an innovative avenue in exploring the electrochemical dynamics at the microstructural level.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁电材料的发展需要化学设计策略，将结构极性与能够支持竞争性自旋相互作用的磁性晶格相结合。本研究旨在探索极性褶皱蜂窝磁体作为实现磁电耦合的新平台。

Method: 研究采用磁化率和热容测量来表征材料的磁性行为，同时使用二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation）测量来探测晶体对称性变化与磁相变之间的关联。

Result: Co2SeO3Cl2表现出强磁各向异性和四个连续的磁相变（25.4K、16.8K、11K和3K）。通过有序区域恢复的磁熵仅为预期值2Rln(2)的一半，表明存在持续的自旋涨落（spin fluctuations）。二次谐波测量显示在11K、17K和26K处有三个显著的强度异常，与磁相变重合，同时表明晶体对称性得以保持。

Conclusion: 极性褶皱蜂窝磁体为磁电材料中磁偶极子与电偶极子的耦合提供了非常规相空间（unconventional phase space），展示了将结构极性与磁性晶格整合的设计策略的有效性。

Abstract: The development of magnetoelectric materials requires chemical design strategies that integrate structural polarity with magnetic lattices capable of supporting competing spin interactions. Here, we demonstrate such an approach in the polar, buckled honeycomb magnet Co2SeO3Cl2. Magnetization and heat-capacity measurements reveal strong magnetic anisotropy and four successive magnetic transitions at 25.4, 16.8, 11, and 3 K. The recovered magnetic entropy through the ordering regime is only around half of the expected 2Rln(2), indicating persistent spin fluctuations. Second-harmonic generation measurements show three pronounced intensity anomalies at 11, 17, and 26 K that coincide with magnetic transitions while revealing that the crystallographic symmetry is preserved. Together, these results demonstrate that polar, buckled honeycomb magnets offer an unconventional phase space for coupling magnetic and electric dipoles in magnetoelectric materials.

### [259] [Analyzing coherent phonon mode-conversion in gradient superlattices with atomistic wave-packet simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13572)
*Evan Wallace Doe,Theodore Maranets,Yan Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过原子声子波包模拟，探究了基于不同周期尺寸有序排列的梯度超晶格中相干声子（coherent phonons）和声子传输的表现。研究发现梯度超晶格的相干声子行为介于完全有序和无序结构之间，且长程无序对相干模式转换（coherent mode-conversion）的影响远大于短程有序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索梯度超晶格（gradient superlattices）中相干声子的表现及其传输特性，重点关注这类准周期结构（quasi-periodic structures）中相干模式转换如何随三个关键结构参数变化，并与周期性及非周期性超晶格进行比较。

Method: 采用原子声子波包模拟（atomistic phonon wave-packet simulations）方法，系统研究梯度超晶格中三个结构参数的影响：(1)不同周期尺寸的数量，(2)每个特定周期尺寸的周期数，(3)周期尺寸按升序或降序排列的方式。

Result: 梯度超晶格中的相干声子通常表现出介于完全有序和无序结构之间的中间态行为。短程有序（short-range order）的变化对传输影响不显著，表明长程无序（long-range disorder）对相干模式转换更为重要。

Conclusion: 调控界面的长程无序可能是定制超晶格结构声子热导率（phonon thermal conductivity）的有效策略，为声子传输的工程控制提供了新途径。

Abstract: In this study, we have used atomistic phonon wave-packet simulations to investigate the manifestation of coherent phonons and phonon transmission in gradient superlattices (SL) based on ordered arrangements of varied SL period sizes. We specifically explore how coherent mode-conversion in these quasi-periodic structures changes as function of three key structural parameters: (1) the number of distinct period sizes, (2) the number of periods present for each distinct period size, and (3) the arrangement of period sizes in either an ascending or descending arrangement. Comparisons to periodic SLs and aperiodic SLs are highlighted, revealing that coherent phonons in gradient SLs generally exhibit behaviors characteristic of intermediate states between the fully ordered and disordered structures. Interestingly, changes to the short-range order of GMLs does not significantly influence transmission, indicating that long-range disorder is far more important to coherent mode-conversion. Our results indicate that manipulating the long-range disorder of interfaces could be an effective strategy to tailor phonon thermal conductivity of SL architectures.

### [260] [Competing Magnetic Ground States in Copper-Doped Pb$_{10}$P$_{6}$O$_{25}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13650)
*Lin Hou,Kevin Allen,Christopher Lane,Jian-Xin Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）和多体微扰理论（many-body perturbation theory），揭示了铜掺杂Pb₁₀(PO₄)₆O的电子与磁学特性。费米能级处的平带半填充电子态导致非公度反铁磁不稳定性，铜原子间的海森堡交换耦合约为1 meV，表明磁性局域于杂质铜位点且无长程有序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究铜掺杂Pb₁₀(PO₄)₆O的电子与磁学性质，旨在理解铜杂质在磷灰石基质中的磁性行为。通过分析费米能级处的电子态和磁性不稳定性，探究铜掺杂对该材料磁学特性的影响机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）与多体微扰理论（many-body perturbation theory）相结合的计算方法。在随机相位近似（random phase approximation）框架下分析磁性不稳定性，并估算相邻铜原子间的海森堡交换耦合（Heisenberg exchange coupling）。

Result: 费米能级处的平带半填充电子态导致非公度反铁磁不稳定性，波矢为(0.28π,±0.47π,π)，主要源于铜的d_{yz}和d_{xz}轨道。相邻铜原子间的海森堡交换耦合约为1 meV，磁性局域于杂质铜位点，无长程有序（long-range ordering）。

Conclusion: 铜掺杂Pb₁₀(PO₄)₆O中的磁性行为表现为局域于杂质铜位点的磁杂质特性，支持铜在磷灰石基质中作为磁性杂质（magnetic impurity）的物理图像。该研究为理解掺杂磷灰石材料的磁学性质提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate the electronic and magnetic properties of copper-doped Pb$_{10}$(PO$_4$)$_6$O using a combination of density functional theory and many-body perturbation theory. The flat half-filled electronic band at the Fermi level is found to give way to an incommensurate antiferromagnetic instability with wave vector $(0.28π,\pm 0.47π,π)$ within the random phase approximation arising predominantly from Cu-$d_{yz}$ and Cu-$d_{xz}$ orbitals. Moreover, the Heisenberg exchange coupling between neighboring copper atoms is estimated to be $\sim 1$ meV. Our results suggest that magnetism in copper-doped Pb$_{10}$(PO$_4$)$_6$O is localized on the impurity copper site, with no long-range ordering. These findings support the picture that copper behaves as a magnetic impurity within the Pb-apatite matrix.

### [261] [Revealing Hydroxide Ion Transport Mechanisms in Commercial Anion-Exchange Membranes at Nano-Scale from Machine-learned Interatomic Potential Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13705)
*Jonas Hänseroth,Muhammad Nawaz Qaisrani,Mostafa Moradi,Karl Skadell,Christian Dreßler*

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学模拟（large-scale molecular dynamics simulations）结合精细调优的机器学习原子间势函数（machine-learned interatomic potentials），在数十纳秒和十纳米尺度上对商用膜中的氢氧根迁移性提供原子尺度洞察。

Abstract: Hydroxide ion transport in anion-exchange membranes fundamentally limits the efficiency of alkaline water electrolysis for green hydrogen production, yet the atomic-scale transport mechanisms remain poorly understood due to the computational challenges associated with modeling ion dynamics. Given that anion-exchange membranes enable alkaline electrolysis with abundant catalysts while avoiding perfluoroalkyl and polyfluoroalkyl materials, a deeper mechanistic understanding of hydroxide transport in these systems is essential for advancing sustainable hydrogen production. Here, we show that large-scale molecular dynamics simulations with fine-tuned machine-learned interatomic potentials provide atomistic insight into hydroxide mobility in a commercial membrane over tens of nanoseconds and over ten nanometer. We find that increasing water content transforms isolated water clusters into a connected hydrogen-bond network that enables long-range proton transfer. Under dry conditions hydroxide ions are trapped near positively charged groups and transport is strongly hindered, whereas well-hydrated membranes exhibit extended proton migration and diffusion coefficients approaching those of dilute aqueous solutions. The simulations reproduce experimental trends in diffusion and activation energies. Our results establish a direct link between nano-scale structure and macroscopic transport. Beyond mechanistic insight, the presented simulation framework enables predictive, simulation-guided optimization of membrane chemistry and architecture, opening a pathway toward the rational design of more efficient anion-exchange membranes for green hydrogen technologies.

### [263] [Vacuum Wannier Functions for First-Principles Scattering and Photoemission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14105)
*Tyler Wu,Tomás Arias*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究建立了统一紧束缚（tight-binding）和近自由电子（nearly-free-electron）描述的真空中万尼尔函数（vacuum Wannier functions）第一性原理理论，实现了无需半经验真空势的预测性光电子发射计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在发展统一固体-真空界面描述的万尼尔函数理论，克服传统方法依赖半经验真空势的局限，为预测性光电子发射计算提供理论基础。

Method: 建立了真空中万尼尔函数的第一性原理理论，推导了任意维度规范万尼尔函数（canonical Wannier functions）的解析解和一维解纠缠函数（disentangled functions），提出并数值验证了三维万尼尔密堆积原理（Wannier close-packing principle）。

Result: 实现了界面处完整玻恩级数散射态（full Born-series scattering states）的密集k空间构造，应用于石墨烯和六方氮化硼（h-BN）体系，揭示了超越一级玻恩近似（first-Born approximation）的修正效应。

Conclusion: 该理论框架统一了固体-真空界面的紧束缚和近自由电子描述，为无半经验参数的预测性光电子发射计算提供了可靠方法，并在实际材料体系中验证了其超越传统近似的修正能力。

Abstract: We establish a first-principles theory of vacuum Wannier functions unifying tight-binding and nearly-free-electron descriptions across solid-vacuum interfaces. Analytic solutions for canonical Wannier functions in arbitrary dimension and disentangled functions in 1D motivate a numerically verified 3D Wannier close-packing principle, enabling dense k-space construction of full Born-series scattering states at interfaces and thus predictive photoemission calculations without semiempirical vacuum potentials. Applications to graphene and h-BN reveal corrections beyond the first-Born approximation.

Unlike previously reported mechanisms relying on external magnetic fields or strain, our approach exploits intrinsic compositional tuning to stabilize a non-coplanar magnetic ground state for realizing a strong full-space AHE in antiferromagnets, providing another viable pathway toward high-performance, low-power spintronic devices.

This substantially facilitates knowledge accumulation and material discovery with desired functionalities to realize versatile applications. In recent years, with the advent of artificial intelligence (AI) techniques, the attention of AI towards scientific research is soaring. The trials of implementing AI in various disciplines are endless, with great potential to revolutionize the research diagram. Despite the success in natural language processing and computer vision, how to effectively integrate AI with natural science is still a grand challenge, bearing in mind their fundamental differences. Inspired by these observations and limitations, we delve into the current research paradigm dictated by the classical material tetrahedron and propose two new paradigms to stimulate data-driven and AI-augmented research. Conclusion: 氮空位导致缺陷介导的铁磁性（defect-mediated ferromagnetism），使居里温度从68 K提升至82 K。观察到的磁行为可通过束缚磁极化子（bound magnetic polaron, BMP）模型很好描述，证实氮空位是铁磁有序的关键贡献者，同时保留了GdN固有的软磁特性。该研究强调了缺陷工程在优化GdN薄膜用于自旋电子学应用中的关键作用。

Abstract: Among rare-earth nitrides (RENs), gadolinium nitride (GdN) stands out as a promising material for spintronics owing to its distinctive combination of semiconducting behavior, strong exchange interactions, and intrinsically soft ferromagnetism. Its relatively high Curie temperature and large saturation magnetization make it an attractive candidate for device concepts such as non-volatile memory elements and spin-based transistors, motivating efforts toward low-cost, uniform, and compositionally controlled thin-film growth. In this work, we deposited GdN thin films on SiO2/AlN substrates using DC sputtering under reactive nitridation conditions, with thicknesses varying from 18 to 180 nm, and systematically investigated their structural and magnetic properties. The films exhibit soft ferromagnetic ordering, characterized by a coercive field of approximately 200 Oe and a Curie temperature (Tc) near 70 K. Structural analysis reveals lattice distortions and local strain associated with nitrogen-vacancy defects, whose concentration varies with film thickness. Our theoretical studies establish a direct correlation between the observed Raman modes of the GdN lattice and the reduced magnetization induced by nitrogen vacancies. These vacancies give rise to defect-mediated ferromagnetism, leading to a measurable enhancement of Tc from 68 K to 82 K across the studied thickness range. The observed magnetic behavior is well described by the bound magnetic polaron (BMP) model, confirming that nitrogen vacancies are key contributors to ferromagnetic ordering while preserving the soft-magnetic character intrinsic to GdN. This study underscores the pivotal role of defect engineering in optimizing GdN thin films for spintronics applications.

Method: 通过新颖的局域化程序（localization procedure），将高维空间中相应的物理相互作用通过切割投影方法映射到准晶中。采用密度泛函理论（DFT++）公式化，使切割投影方法能够处理准晶中的薛定谔方程。

Abstract: Cut-and-project from a symmetric structure in a higher-dimensional space is a standard method for describing the structure of a large class of quasicrystals. By means of a novel localization procedure, we now show how local physical interactions within these quasicrystals are also accurately described by cut-and-project, from corresponding physical interactions in the higher-dimensional space. A density functional theory (DFT++) formulation allows the cut-and-project method to handle the Schroedinger equation for interactions in quasicrystals. The theory is both rigorous and computationally tractable. The resulting ab initio approach specifies quasicrystalline quantum states, in contrast to previous approaches which only worked with crystalline approximants of the quasi-periodic structures.

Abstract: Cold metals are a class of metals with an intrinsic energy gap located close to the Fermi level, which enables cold-carrier injection for steep-slope transistors and is therefore promising for low-power electronic applications. High-throughput screening has revealed 252 three-dimensional (3D) cold metals in the Materials Project database, but database searches are inherently limited to known compounds. Here we present an inverse-design workflow that generates 3D cold metals using MatterGPT, a conditional autoregressive Transformer trained on SLICES, an invertible and symmetry-invariant crystal string representation. We curate a training set of 26,309 metallic structures labeled with energy above hull and a unified band-edge distance descriptor that merges p-type and n-type cold-metal characteristics to address severe label imbalance. Property-conditioned generation targeting thermodynamic stability and 50-500 meV band-edge distances produces 148,506 unique candidates; 92.1% are successfully reconstructed to 3D structures and down-selected by symmetry, uniqueness and novelty filters, followed by high-throughput DFT validation. We identify 257 cold metals verified as novel with respect to the Materials Project database, with gaps around the Fermi level spanning 50-500 meV. First-principles phonon, electronic-structure, and work-function calculations for representative candidates confirm dynamical stability and contact-relevant work functions. Our results demonstrate that SLICES-enabled generative transformers can expand the chemical space of cold metals beyond high-throughput screening, providing a route to low-power electronic materials discovery.

*Igor Evangelista,Abdul Saboor,Muhammad Zubair,Intuon Chatratin,Ruiqi Hu,Dai Q. Ho,Shoaib Khalid,Ioanna Fampiou,Anderson Janotti*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过含自旋轨道耦合的杂化密度泛函计算，研究了单层1H相过渡金属二硫化物（MX₂）在单轴应变下的能带结构演化，揭示了应变导致能带间隙减小、能谷漂移及间接带隙形成的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在准确描述单层过渡金属二硫化物（transition-metal dichalcogenides）在单轴应变下的准粒子带隙（quasiparticle band gap）演化，而非激子光学带隙，为光电子和量子缺陷应用提供能带结构调控的定量指导。

Method: 采用包含自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的杂化密度泛函计算（hybrid density functional calculations），计算了MX₂（M=Mo, W; X=S, Se, Te）单层材料在单轴应变下的能带结构演化，并构建了最小紧束缚模型（minimal tight-binding model）解释能谷漂移现象。

Result: 研究发现：沿扶手椅或锯齿方向的单轴拉伸应变导致基本带隙显著减小，导带边（conduction-band edge）对应变更敏感；导带电子能谷和价带空穴能谷在应变下保持简并，但会从高对称K点漂移（valley drift），形成间接带隙；MoS₂的间接性随拉伸应变增强，解释了实验中观察到的光致发光强度下降现象。

Conclusion: 研究结果为通过应变工程调控过渡金属二硫化物的能带结构提供了定量指导，有助于优化其在光电子和量子缺陷应用中的性能，特别是解释了单轴变形下光致发光强度降低的实验观察。

Abstract: Using hybrid density functional calculations including spin-orbit coupling, we compute the strain evolution of the band structure of monolayer 1H-phase transition-metal dichalcogenides, MX$_2$ (M= Mo, W; X= S, Se, Te), emphasizing an accurate reproduction of the quasiparticle band gap (as opposed to the excitonic optical gap). We show that tensile uniaxial strain applied along either the armchair or zigzag directions leads to a pronounced reduction of the fundamental gap, with the conduction-band edge generally exhibiting the stronger strain response. Both the conduction-band electron valleys (CBM) and the valence-band hole valleys (VBM) remain degenerate under uniaxial strain, while simultaneously drifting away from the high-symmetry $K$ point under strain ("valley drift"), such that the band extrema occur at nearby off-symmetry wave vectors. A minimal tight-binding model rationalizes the valley drift and the unequal electron- and hole-valley drift rates in the presence of strain, leading to indirect band gaps. In particular, for MoS$_2$ the indirectness increases with tensile strain, providing a natural explanation for the experimentally observed decrease in photoluminescence intensity under uniaxial deformation. These results provide quantitative guidance for tailoring band structures for optoelectronic and quantum-defect applications.

</details>


### [272] [Digital Hydrogen Platform (DigHyd): A Rigorously Curated Database for Hydrogen Storage Materials Empowered by AI-Assisted Literature Mining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14139)
*Seong-Hoon Jang,Di Zhang,Xue Jia,Hung Ba Tran,Linda Zhang,Ryuhei Sato,Yusuke Hashimoto,Toyoto Sato,Kiyoe Konno,Shin-ichi Orimo,Hao Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 研究人员开发了Digital Hydrogen Platform (DigHyd)数据库，包含超过30,000个数据条目，用于固态储氢材料的数据驱动发现。该数据库通过AI辅助文献挖掘结合人工验证构建，重点关注热力学参数而非单一温度下的平衡压力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态储氢材料是安全紧凑储氢的有前景候选材料，但该领域的数据驱动发现受到大规模、高质量数据集可用性的限制。需要构建经过严格整理的热力学数据库来支持系统性的材料探索。

Method: 通过AI辅助文献挖掘结合人工验证（human-in-the-loop validation）构建了包含超过4,000个实验文献源和30,000个数据条目的数据库。热力学参数通过手动分析多温度压力-组成-温度（PCT）数据并使用范特霍夫分析（van't Hoff analysis）获得。

Result: DigHyd数据库覆盖了质量储氢密度（w）以及氢化反应相关的焓变（ΔH）和熵变（ΔS）。统计分析揭示了不同材料类别间热力学参数的明显分布差异。物理可解释的符号回归（symbolic regression）和黑盒XGBoost模型对w和室温平衡压力（P_eq,RT）具有相当的预测性能。

Conclusion: DigHyd提供了一个经过严格整理的热力学数据集，可作为储氢材料数据驱动分析的可靠基础，并支持结构-性能关系的系统性探索。该平台通过关注ΔH和ΔS而非固定单一温度下的平衡压力，实现了应用特定操作条件下平衡行为的灵活评估。

Abstract: Solid-state hydrogen storage materials are promising candidates for safe and compact hydrogen storage; however, data-driven discovery in this field remains limited by the availability of large-scale, well-curated datasets. Here, we present the Digital Hydrogen Platform (DigHyd: www.dighyd.org), a rigorously curated database comprising $>4,000$ experimental literature sources and $>30,000$ data entries on hydrogen storage materials, constructed through AI-assisted literature mining combined with human-in-the-loop validation. In addition to gravimetric hydrogen storage density ($w$), DigHyd also covers thermodynamic parameters, specifically the enthalpy ($ΔH$) and entropy ($ΔS$) changes associated with hydrogenation reactions, primarily defined as $M + \frac{1}{2} {\rm H}_2 \rightleftarrows M{\rm H}$. These parameters were obtained by manually analyzing multi-temperature pressure-composition-temperature (PCT) data using van't Hoff analysis. By focusing on $ΔH$ and $ΔS$ rather than fixing equilibrium pressure at a single temperature, DigHyd enables flexible evaluation of equilibrium behavior under application-specific operating conditions. Statistical analyses reveal distinct distributions of thermodynamic parameters across material classes, together with broad compositional variability within representative hydride systems. Furthermore, both physically interpretable symbolic regression and black-box XGBoost models achieve comparable predictive performance for $w$ and equilibrium pressure at room temperature ($P_{\rm eq,RT}$), demonstrating internal consistency and learnable composition-property relationships within the curated dataset. Overall, DigHyd provides a rigorously curated thermodynamic dataset that serves as a reliable basis for data-driven analyses of hydrogen storage materials and supports systematic exploration of structure-property relationships.

</details>


### [273] [Emergent giant topological Hall effect in twisted Fe3GeTe2 metallic system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14192)
*Hyuncheol Kim,Kai-Xuan Zhang,Yu-Hang Li,Giung Park,Ran Cheng,Je-Geun Park*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 在保持全局反演对称性的扭曲Fe3GeTe2金属系统中，发现了仅在特定"魔角"范围（0.45°-0.75°）内出现的巨大拓扑霍尔效应，该效应源于局部反演对称性破缺诱导的斯格明子晶格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑霍尔效应（topological Hall effect）通常作为探测磁性材料拓扑性质的重要探针，但传统上需要全局反演对称性破缺的系统。本研究旨在探索在保持全局反演对称性的扭曲范德华（van der Waals）磁体中实现拓扑霍尔效应的可能性。

Method: 研究采用扭曲Fe3GeTe2金属系统作为平台，通过调节扭曲角度在0.45°至0.75°的"魔角"范围内进行实验观测。同时使用微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）分析拓扑霍尔效应的物理起源。

Result: 在保持全局反演对称性的扭曲Fe3GeTe2系统中，仅在特定扭曲角度窗口内观测到巨大的拓扑霍尔效应。微磁模拟表明该效应源于局部反演对称性破缺诱导的交替面内和层间Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用所稳定的斯格明子晶格（skyrmion lattice）。

Conclusion: 扭曲Fe3GeTe2系统为在金属性扭曲范德华磁体中工程化和控制拓扑磁性结构提供了多功能平台，为下一代自旋电子器件开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The topological Hall effect, driven by the exchange interaction between conduction electrons and topological magnetic textures such as skyrmions, is a powerful probe for investigating the topological properties of magnetic materials. Typically, this phenomenon arises in systems with broken global inversion symmetry, where Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions stabilize such textures. Here, we report the discovery of an emergent giant topological Hall effect in the twisted Fe3GeTe2 metallic system, which notably preserves the general global inversion symmetry. This effect manifests exclusively within a narrow window of "magic" twist angles ranging from 0.45° to 0.75°, while it is absent identically outside of that range, highlighting its unique and emergent nature. Micromagnetic simulations reveal that this topological Hall effect originates from a skyrmion lattice induced by alternating in-plane and layer-contrasting Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions that result from local inversion symmetry breaking. Our findings underscore twisted Fe3GeTe2 as a versatile platform for engineering and controlling topological magnetic textures in metallic twisted van der Waals magnets, thereby opening up new avenues for next-generation spintronic devices.

*Woojoo Lee,Qiang Gao,Yufei Zhao,Hui Li,Albert Tsui,Yichao Zhang,Yunhe Bai,Haoran Lin,Khanh Duy Nguyen,Gabriele Berruto,Gangbin Yan,Jianchen Dang,Tongyao Wu,Hossein Rokni,Thomas S. Method: 采用精确的逐层生长技术，实现了地毯状形貌的宏观尺度生长。通过多模态光谱学和显微技术，结合光子能量依赖的光电子能谱、时间分辨光电子能谱以及扫描隧道谱，系统表征了材料的电子结构和拓扑性质。

Conclusion: 该研究定义了一个可扩展的材料平台，其大反转带隙支持接近室温的工作条件，为下一代低损耗量子器件和节能器件的发展奠定了基础。

Abstract: Quantum spin Hall insulators, or synonymously known as 2D topological insulators, are crucial 2D systems hosting topologically protected edge states. The working temperature of this topological quantum phase is dictated by the inverted bandgap. However, the previously identified large-gap 2D topological insulators are either extremely chemically unstable, or cannot be made with atomistic precision over macroscopic scales. Here, we establish two-quintuple-layer Bi2Te3 and MnBi2Te4/Bi2Te3 heterostructures as atomically controlled, millimeter-scale 2D topological insulators, enabled by precision layer-by-layer growth that yields a carpet-like morphology extending coherently over macroscopic distances. This carpet-like growth mode renders the films amenable to mechanical exfoliation and subsequent wet or dry transfer. Multimodal spectroscopies and microscopies reveal the integer-layer tuned electronic structure of (Bi2Te3)n with excellent agreement to theory. Photon-energy-dependent photoemission and time-resolved photoemission identify band inversion and band dynamics, respectively, while scanning tunneling spectroscopy resolves topological edge states, characteristic of the 2D topological insulator phase. Thickness- and photon-energy-dependent photoemission further validates MnBi2Te4/Bi2Te3 as a robust 2D topological insulator. The large inverted gaps of ~100 meV in (Bi2Te3)2 and ~150 meV in MnBi2Te4/Bi2Te3 suggest operation near ambient temperature. These results define a scalable materials platform for next-generation, low-loss quantum and energy-efficient devices.

### [275] [Evolution of Phonon Transport Across Structural Phase Transitions in MgAgSb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14213)
*Luman Shang,Yu Wu,Yufan Liu,Shuming Zeng,Gang Tang,Chenhan Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理计算系统分析了MgAgSb三种相（α、β、γ）的晶格热导率，揭示了其随相变递增的趋势（α<β<γ）。研究发现四声子散射显著抑制β和γ相的粒子状热导率，而α相中相干声子隧穿贡献高达44%的波状热导率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MgAgSb作为一种有前景的热电材料，经历可逆相变会显著改变其热输运行为。理解不同相中热导率的差异及其物理机制对于优化热电性能至关重要。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）系统研究了MgAgSb三种相（α、β、γ）的晶格热导率。分析涵盖了粒子状热导率（κ_p）和波状热导率（κ_c）的贡献，并考虑了四声子散射（four-phonon scattering）和电子-声子散射（electron-phonon scattering）机制。

Result: 晶格热导率呈现α<β<γ的递增趋势。四声子散射显著抑制β和γ相的粒子状热导率，电子-声子散射提供次要的额外降低。α相中相干声子隧穿产生的波状热导率最高，贡献达44%。不同相的热导率温度依赖性存在根本差异：β相中弱κ_p变化源于Grüneisen参数随温度降低；α相中κ_c随温度强烈上升抵消了κ_p的衰减。

Conclusion: 研究建立了MgAgSb热输运的全面图像，强调了粒子状和波状声子贡献之间的相依赖性相互作用。这些发现对于理解相变材料的热输运机制和优化热电性能具有重要意义。

Abstract: MgAgSb, a promising thermoelectric material, undergoes reversible phase transitions that drastically alter its thermal transport behavior. Using first-principles calculations, we systematically investigate the lattice thermal conductivity ($κ_L$) of its three phases: $α$, $β$, and $γ$, revealing a progressive increase following $α< β< γ$. This trend originates from distinct scattering mechanisms. Four-phonon scattering substantially suppresses the particle-like conductivity ($κ_p$) in the $β$ and $γ$ phases, while electron-phonon scattering provides a minor additional reduction. In contrast, the wave-like conductivity ($κ_c$) from coherent phonon tunneling is highest in the complex $α$ phase, contributing up to 44\% of $κ_L$. Notably, the temperature dependence of $κ_L$ differs fundamentally between phases: in $β$, the weak $κ_p$ variation arises from a decreasing Grüneisen parameter with temperature; in $α$, the strong rise in $κ_c$ with temperature counteracts the decay of $κ_p$. Our findings establish a comprehensive picture of thermal transport in MgAgSb, highlighting the phase-dependent interplay between particle-like and wave-like phonon contributions.

### [276] [Diagonal Curvature in Second Order Jahn Teller Theory Can Be Negative: An Analytic Proof with First-Principles Confirmation in NH3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14291)
*Zhian Li,Hanxiang Mi,Xiyue Cheng,Jurgen Kohler,Shuiquan Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究推翻了二阶Jahn-Teller理论（SOJTT）中关于对角曲率（diagonal curvature）必须为正的基本假设，证明其可为负值，并揭示了对称性自发破缺（spontaneous structural symmetry breaking）需要验证鞍点（saddle point）存在，而非假设对角曲率正定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二阶Jahn-Teller理论（SOJTT）长期以来假设对角曲率为正，但该研究旨在验证这一基本假设的量子力学基础，探究对称性自发破缺的真实物理机制。

Method: 采用冻结声子多体展开（frozen-phonon many-body expansion）方法，并在Kohn-Sham框架下重新表述问题；通过第一性原理计算（first principles calculations）分析NH3分子，并应用Schwarz不等式上界分析（Schwarz-inequality upper-bound analysis）量化不同贡献。

Result: 发现对角曲率可为负值，NH3的D3h参考构型位于A2"鞍点；HOMO-LUMO混合贡献仅占总能量下降的<0.2%，而99.8%来自驱动N(2s-2pz)电子重分布的对角电子-核项（diagonal electron-nuclear term）。

Conclusion: 研究推翻了SOJTT的核心信条，确立了自发结构对称破缺需要先验证鞍点存在，而非假设对角曲率的正定性，从根本上修正了该理论框架。

Abstract: We demonstrate that the diagonal curvature in second-order Jahn-Teller theory (SOJTT) can be negative, invalidating its foundational positivity assumption. Using a frozen-phonon many-body expansion, we show no quantum-mechanical principle enforces its positivity; recasting into the Kohn-Sham framework further reveals that phonon-induced eigen-energy changes arise solely from electron-nuclear, Hartree, and exchange-correlation terms, with kinetic-energy contributions canceling identically. First principles calculations on NH3 place the D3h reference configuration at an A2" saddle point; Schwarz-inequality upper-bound analysis confines the HOMO-LUMO mixing contribution to < 0.2% of the total energy drop,while 99.8% originates from the diagonal electron-nuclear term driving N (2s-2pz) electron redistribution. These findings overturn a core SOJTT tenet and establish that spontaneous structural symmetry breaking demands prior verification of a saddle point, not assumed positivity of the diagonal curvature.

### [277] [Self-Assembled H2NC Molecular Lattices as a Platform for Substrate-Tunable Quantum Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14446)
*Adrian Bahri,Zhibo Kang,Ziyan Zhu,Eric I. Altman,Yu He,Chunjing Jia*

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory），辅以角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）和扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy），对比分析了自由支撑H2Nc单层与贵金属基底上组装H2Nc晶格的电子结构。

Result: 自由薄膜中识别出近局域的分子态和色散能带，可用各向异性紧束缚哈密顿量描述。吸附在Ag(100)上导致强轨道杂化、电荷转移和C2对称性破缺，产生部分填充的基底介导色散态，使分子晶格金属化。H2Nc/Au(111)的角分辨光电子能谱实验定性验证了预测的色散和部分填充。

Abstract: Compared to van der Waals moiré systems, molecular assembly has emerged as an exciting alternative platform for superlattice engineering via heterointegration. The electronic properties of the self-assembled square lattice monolayer molecular crystal of metal-free naphthalocyanine (H2Nc), in particular the electronic band dispersion and their tunability by metal substrates, remain less explored. Using density functional theory, supported by angle-resolved photoemission and scanning tunneling microscopy, we compare the electronic structure of a free-standing H2Nc monolayer with that of H2Nc lattice assembled on noble metal substrates. In the freestanding film, we identify both nearly flat, molecule-localized states and more dispersive bands, and we show that each can be compactly described by an anisotropic tight-binding Hamiltonian that yields band-resolved hopping anisotropies. We further reveal wide tunability in the Coulomb interaction and inter-site hopping based on different molecular orbitals. Adsorption on Ag(100) drives strong orbital hybridization, charge transfer, and C2 symmetry breaking, producing partially filled, substrate-mediated dispersive states that metallize the molecular lattice. Orbital analysis identifies C2-even and C2-odd components and maps the spatial pattern of charge redistribution tied to symmetry breaking. Complementary ARPES on H2Nc/Au(111) qualitatively corroborates the predicted dispersion and partial filling. These results clarify how metal substrates convert H2Nc from isolated molecules into a tunable 2D lattice and highlight molecular superlattices as a versatile platform to simulate anisotropic lattice models.

### [278] [Role of ionic quantum-anharmonic fluctuations on the bond length alternation and giant piezoelectricity of conjugated polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14472)
*Stefano Paolo Villani,Lorenzo Monacelli,Paolo Barone,Francesco Mauri*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 功能化共轭聚合物（functionalized conjugated polymers）因其预测的巨大压电性（giant piezoelectricity）而成为有前景的机电应用材料，这种压电性源于异常大的动态有效电荷（dynamical effective charges）以及在二聚化相变（dimerization phase transition）附近的增强响应。本研究旨在评估量子离子涨落对压电性的影响。

Method: 采用随机自洽谐振近似（stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation）结合Rice-Mele双原子链模型（Rice-Mele diatomic chain model），该模型参数化以复现典型卡拜（carbyne）的杂化泛函第一性原理计算（hybrid-functional first-principles calculations）。模型准确性通过有无量子非谐效应（quantum-anharmonic effects）的第一性原理计算进行了验证。

Result: 离子涨落强烈影响结构性质，使二聚化相变边界偏移34%。尽管键长的量子涨落幅度与平均值相当，但强压电响应仍然存在。有效电荷的拓扑增强保持稳健，并因量子诱导的电子带隙（electronic gap）收缩而增强约20%。压电系数仍由内部弛豫主导并保持类形态特性（morphotropic-like character），在重整化边界附近达到最大值，量子非谐性主要改变最佳增强窗口的位置。

Conclusion: 量子离子涨落显著改变功能化共轭聚合物的结构性质，但强压电响应和有效电荷的拓扑增强机制保持稳健，压电系数在重整化相变边界附近仍能达到最大值，表明这些材料在量子涨落存在下仍具有优异的机电性能潜力。

Abstract: Functionalized conjugated polymers are promising materials for electromechanical applications due to predicted giant piezoelectricity, arising from anomalously large dynamical effective charges and an enhanced response in the proximity of the dimerization phase transition. In this work, we assess the impact of quantum ionic fluctuations on piezoelectricity using the stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation with a Rice-Mele diatomic chain model, parametrized to reproduce hybrid-functional first-principles calculations of prototypical carbyne. The model's accuracy is validated against first-principles calculations both with and without quantum-anharmonic effects. We find that ionic fluctuations strongly impact the structural properties, with the boundary of the dimerization phase transition shifted by $34\%$. Despite quantum fluctuations in the bond length reaching magnitudes comparable to the average, the strong piezoelectric response persists. The topological enhancement of the effective charges remains robust and is even enhanced by about $\sim20\%$ thanks to a quantum-induced shrinking of the electronic gap. The piezoelectric coefficient remains dominated by the internal relaxation and retains a morphotropic-like character, reaching maximum values near the renormalized boundary, with quantum anharmonicity mainly shifting the optimal enhancement window.

</details>


### [279] [Gas sensing potential of stacked graphene/h-BN structures: a DFT-based investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14530)
*Martin Siebel,Pavel Rubin,Raivo Jaaniso*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过周期性密度泛函理论（periodic DFT）分析了NO₂、NH₃和O₃在石墨烯/六方氮化硼（graphene/h-BN）异质结上的吸附行为，揭示了该材料作为气体传感器的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索石墨烯/六方氮化硼（graphene/h-BN）异质结作为气体传感器材料的性能。六方氮化硼（h-BN）覆盖层既作为活性吸附表面，又作为保护层以减少不可逆过程（如石墨烯氧化）。

Method: 采用周期性密度泛函理论（periodic DFT）研究两种模型系统：扩展的石墨烯/h-BN双层结构（B₃₆N₃₆C₇₂）和部分覆盖较小h-BN岛的石墨烯片（B₁₁N₁₁C₇₂）。分析比较了它们在狄拉克点（Dirac point）附近的电子结构差异。

Result: 两种系统的电子结构存在显著差异：扩展双层中费米能级（Fermi level）与原始石墨烯对齐，表明电荷转移可忽略；而岛覆盖系统中费米能级向低能移动，反映电子从石墨烯转移到h-BN。NO₂在B₁₁N₁₁C₇₂上结合更强并形成化学键，O₃在该表面解离但在扩展双层中保持完整，NH₃在岛系统中异常地作为电子受体。NO₂和O₃显著增加石墨烯电导率，而NH₃引起的变化较弱。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明石墨烯/六方氮化硼（graphene/h-BN）异质结在气体传感方面具有潜力，不同气体分子在两种结构上的吸附行为差异显著，这为设计高性能气体传感器提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Using periodic DFT, we examined the adsorption of NO2, NH3, and O3 on the h-BN side of a graphene/h-BN heterostructure designed as a model gas sensor material. The h-BN overlayer serves both as an active adsorption surface and as protection that may reduce irreversible processes such as graphene oxidation. Two model systems were considered: an extended graphene/h-BN bilayer (B36N36C72) and a graphene sheet partially covered by a smaller h-BN island (B11N11C72). Their electronic structures differ strongly near the Dirac point. In the extended bilayer, the Fermi level remains aligned with that of pristine graphene, indicating negligible charge transfer. In the island-covered system, the Fermi level shifts to lower energies, reflecting electron transfer from graphene to h-BN. These differences lead to distinct adsorption behavior. NO2 binds much more strongly to B11N11C72, forming a chemical bond, while O3 dissociates on this surface but remains intact on the extended bilayer. NH3 unusually acts as an electron acceptor in the island system. Overall, NO2 and O3 substantially increase graphene conductivity, whereas NH3 induces much weaker changes. These results highlight the potential of graphene/h-BN heterostructures for gas sensing.

Abstract: Polyamide 6,6 (PA66) is a key engineering polymer, whose unique mechanical properties arise from strong interchain hydrogen bonding. However, its hygroscopic nature makes it highly sensitive to water uptake, which markedly alters its thermomechanical behavior. Contrary to traditional experimental approaches, this study uses atomistic molecular dynamics (MD) simulations to investigate the role of water in modifying the glass transition temperature (Tg) and the viscoelastic response of amorphous PA66. Simulations capture a nonmonotonic dependence of Tg on water content. At low water concentrations, isolated water molecules bind to amide groups and restrict chain mobility, while beyond ~2.5 wt %, water clustering disrupts the hydrogen bond network and causes a pronounced Tg depression. Analysis of amide group fluctuations reveals a master correlation between local segmental dynamics and bulk density, verifying the known temperature humidity equivalence in terms of density variation. The computed Young's modulus exhibits systematic softening with increasing temperature and water content, consistent with experimental trends, albeit a more pronounced impact of water at low temperatures. Time temperature superposition behavior is observed for both dry and hydrated systems. This work provides molecular scale information on the hygromechanical coupling in PA66 and demonstrates the ability of MD simulations to predict water induced transitions that govern the macroscopic behavior of polyamides.

### [281] [Radiation-induced segregation in dilute Fe-Cr: A rate-theory framework for the Cr enrichment-depletion transition at the grain boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14574)
*Russell Oplinger,Mukesh Bachhav,Karim Ahmed,Sourabh Bhagwan Kadambi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过基于物理的速率理论模型，结合自洽平均场理论得到的昂萨格输运系数，研究了稀Fe-(0.1 at.%) Cr合金中晶界处的辐射诱导偏析现象，揭示了在对称点缺陷条件下Cr偏析的温度依赖性转变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 辐射诱导偏析（radiation-induced segregation, RIS）对铁素体Fe-Cr合金的机械完整性和晶间腐蚀敏感性构成严重威胁，但目前对Cr偏析机制的理解仍不完整，需要建立更准确的预测模型。

Method: 采用基于物理的速率理论模型，参数化使用自洽平均场理论（self-consistent mean field theory）推导的昂萨格输运系数（Onsager transport coefficients），研究稀Fe-(0.1 at.%) Cr合金晶界处的RIS现象。

Result: 在空位和自填隙原子（self-interstitial atoms, SIA）产生率相等且被体相位错等量吸收的对称条件下，模型成功模拟了实验观察到的Cr从低温富集向高温贫化的转变；温度依赖性输运性质决定偏析方向，而剂量率、晶粒尺寸和位错密度仅影响偏析幅度和空间范围。

Conclusion: 仅基于输运系数的RIS预测仅在对称点缺陷通量条件下有效，损伤级联中的优先空位产生和/或体相位错的优先SIA吸收等偏置效应必须被考虑才能获得准确预测；该工作为理解铁素体合金RIS提供了机制框架，并为先进核系统合金设计提供指导。

Abstract: Radiation-induced segregation (RIS) poses a significant challenge for ferritic Fe-Cr alloys under irradiation, as it can compromise mechanical integrity and increase susceptibility to intergranular corrosion. Yet, the mechanisms governing Cr segregation remain incompletely understood. In this study, We present a physics-based rate-theory model parameterized using self-consistent mean field theory-based Onsager transport coefficients to investigate RIS at the grain boundary (GB) in dilute Fe-(0.1 at.%) Cr. Under equal production rates of vacancies and self-interstitial atoms (SIA), and their equal absorption rates by bulk dislocations, the model simulates the experimentally observed transition from Cr enrichment at low temperatures to depletion at higher temperatures. Under these unbiased conditions, systematic investigation reveals that while temperature-dependent transport properties dictate the segregation direction, dose rate, grain size, and dislocation density only influence the magnitude and spatial extent of Cr segregation. However, under more realistic conditions of preferential vacancy production within damage cascade and/or preferential SIA absorption by bulk dislocations, the enrichment-to-depletion transition shifts to lower temperatures. Our findings demonstrate that RIS predictions based solely on transport coefficients are valid only under symmetric point defect flux conditions, and that biases in defect production and absorption must be considered for accurate predictions. This work provides a mechanistic framework for understanding RIS in ferritic alloys and informs alloy design for advanced nuclear systems.

### [282] [Sequential Quenching to Predict Semiconductor Defect Concentrations from Formation & Migration Energies: The Case of CdTe:As Doping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14618)
*Khandakar Aaditta Arnab,Intuon Chatratin,Anderson Janotti,Michael Scarpulla*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种新的缺陷计算方法——顺序淬火（sequential quenching），用于模拟半导体材料在有限冷却速率下缺陷浓度的演化，解决了传统平衡或瞬时淬火假设的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体中的缺陷浓度受生长和冷却过程中热历史的强烈影响，但传统缺陷计算通常假设瞬时淬火或完全平衡两种极端情况，这与实际冷却过程不符。需要建立更符合物理实际的缺陷演化模型。

Method: 提出了顺序淬火（sequential quenching, SQ）方法，利用缺陷形成能和迁移能，模拟有限冷却速率下受扩散限制动力学的缺陷浓度演化。该方法中每个缺陷在特征温度下冻结，该温度由其扩散速率、与源/汇的距离以及冷却速率决定。

Result: 在As掺杂CdTe的示例中，SQ计算显示快速扩散缺陷（如Cd间隙原子）在较低温度下仍保持移动性，并在较大特征距离下冻结，导致快速冷却或块体样品中出现强补偿和n型行为。较慢冷却和较小特征距离则抑制施主冻结并增强p型激活。

Conclusion: 顺序淬火（SQ）提供了一个物理透明且计算高效的框架，能够将冷却条件、样品几何形状和缺陷动力学与CdTe及相关材料中的掺杂剂激活联系起来，填补了传统平衡和完全淬火计算之间的空白。

Abstract: Defect concentrations in semiconductors are strongly influenced by thermal history during growth and cooldown, yet most defect calculations assume either instantaneous quenching from high temperature or that full-equilibrium is maintained - two limiting cases rarely approached in reality. Here, we introduce sequential quenching (SQ) as a 3rd type of defect calculation utilizing defect formation and migration energies to model defect concentrations subject to diffusion-limited kinetics in samples cooled at finite rates. In SQ, the concentration of each defect is frozen at a characteristic temperature determined by its diffusion rate, distance to sources/sinks, and cooling rate. Because different charge-states interact through charge neutrality but freeze at different temperatures, the sequence of freeze-in events is non-commuting. Critically, not all room-temperature SQ solutions can be predicted from full equilibrium (EQ) or full-quenching (FQ) calculations - erroneous predictions are likely without SQ. We illustrate SQ using the example of As-doped CdTe, for which experimental data show differences in doping with cooling rate and between polycrystalline thin-films for photovoltaics and bulk crystals. SQ calculations reveal that fast-diffusing defects such as Cd-interstitials remain mobile to lower temperatures and freeze-in at larger characteristic distances, leading to strong compensation and n-type behavior in rapidly cooled or bulk samples. Slower cooling and reduced characteristic distances suppress donor freeze-in and enhance p-type activation. These results establish SQ as a physically transparent and computationally efficient framework for connecting cooling conditions, sample geometry, and defect kinetics to dopant activation in CdTe and related materials.
